pādāḥ tu svarṇa jāla paricchadāḥ jārāsaṃdhim haya śreṣṭhāḥ sahadevam udāvahan ye tu puṣkara nālasya sama varṇāḥ haya uttamāḥ jave śyena samāḥ citrāḥ sudāmānam udāvahan śaśa lohita varṇāḥ tu pāṇḍura udgata rājayaḥ pāñcālyam gopateḥ putram siṃhasenam udāvahan pāñcālānām nara vyāghraḥ yaḥ khyātaḥ janamejayaḥ tasya sarṣapa puṣpāṇām tulya varṇāḥ haya uttamāḥ māṣa varṇāḥ tu javanāḥ bṛhantaḥ hema mālinaḥ dadhi pṛṣṭhāḥ candra mukhāḥ pāñcālyam avahan drutam śūrāḥ ca bhadrakāḥ ca eva śara kāṇḍa nibhāḥ hayāḥ padma kiñjalka varṇa ābhāḥ daṇḍadhāram udāvahan rāsabha aruṇa varṇa ābhāḥ pṛṣṭhatas mūṣaka prabhāḥ harayaḥ kālakāḥ citrāḥ citra mālya vibhūṣitāḥ sudhanvānam nara vyāghra pāñcālyam samudāvahan indra aśani sama sparśāḥ indragopaka saṃnibhāḥ kośaiḥ citra antarāḥ citrāḥ citrāyudham udāvahan bibhrataḥ hema mālāḥ ca cakravāka udarāḥ hayāḥ śabalāḥ tu bṛhantaḥ aśvāḥ dāntāḥ jāmbūnada srajaḥ yuddhe satyadhṛtim kṣaimim avahan prāṃśavaḥ śubhāḥ aśvaiḥ ca dhanuṣā ca eva śuklaiḥ śuklaḥ nyavartata aśvāḥ śaśāṅka sadṛśāḥ candradevam udāvahan nīlotpala savarṇāḥ tu tapanīya vibhūṣitāḥ śaibyam citra ratham yuddhe citra mālyāḥ avahan hayāḥ kalāya puṣpa varṇāḥ tu śveta lohita rājayaḥ rathasenam haya śreṣṭhāḥ samūhuḥ yuddha durmadam yam tu sarva manuṣyebhyaḥ prāhuḥ śūrataram nṛpam tam paṭaccara hantāram śuka varṇāḥ avahan hayāḥ ūhuḥ kiṃśuka puṣpāṇām tulya varṇāḥ haya uttamāḥ yodhāḥ ca bhadrakārāḥ ca śaradaṇḍa anudaṇḍa jāḥ śveta aṇḍāḥ kukkuṭa aṇḍa ābhāḥ daṇḍaketum udāvahan bhinne kapāṭe pāṇḍyānām vidruteṣu ca bandhuṣu bhīṣmāt avāpya ca astrāṇi droṇāt rāmāt kṛpāt tathā astraiḥ sama tvam saṃprāpya rukmikarṇa arjuna acyutaiḥ iyeṣa dvārakām hantum kṛtsnām jetum ca medinīm nivāritaḥ tatas prājñaiḥ suhṛdbhiḥ hita kāmyayā sa sāgara dhvajaḥ pāṇḍyaḥ candra raśmi nibhaiḥ hayaiḥ vaiḍūrya jāla saṃchannaiḥ vīrya draviṇam āśritaḥ divyam visphārayan cāpam droṇam abhyapatat balī āṭarūṣaka puṣpa ābhāḥ hayāḥ pāṇḍya anuyāyinām nānā rūpeṇa varṇena nānā ākṛti mukhāḥ hayāḥ bharatānām sametānām utsṛjya ekaḥ matāni yaḥ lohita akṣam mahā bāhum bṛhantam tam vara dhvajam nānā dhvaja patākena nānā kavaca vājinā suvarṇa varṇāḥ dharma jñam anīkastham yudhiṣṭhiram rāja śreṣṭham haya śreṣṭhāḥ sarvatas pṛṣṭhatas anvayuḥ varṇaiḥ ca uccāvacaiḥ divyaiḥ sat aśvānām prabhadrakāḥ te yattāḥ bhīmasenena sahitāḥ kāñcana dhvajāḥ atyarocata tān sarvān dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ samāgatān uvāca atīva śuśubhe tasya dhvajaḥ kṛṣṇa ajina uttaraḥ kamaṇḍaluḥ mahā rāja jātarūpa mayaḥ śubhaḥ bhrājamānam mahā siṃham rājatam dṛṣṭavān aham dṛṣṭavān asmi sauvarṇam somam graha gaṇa anvitam śarabham pṛṣṭha sauvarṇam nakulasya mahā dhvajam haṃsaḥ tu rājataḥ śrīmān dhvajaḥ ghaṇṭā patākavān pañcānām draupadeyānām pratimā ratha bhūṣaṇam dharma māruta śakrāṇām aśvinoḥ ca mahātmanoḥ abhimanyoḥ kumārasya śārṅgapakṣī hiraṇmayaḥ aśvāḥ ca kāma gāḥ tasya rāvaṇasya yathā purā trailokya rakṣaṇa arthāya brahmaṇā sṛṣṭam āyudham vaiṣṇavam nakulāya atha sahadevāya ca aśvijam pañcānām draupadeyānām bhārata raudram dhanuḥ varam śreṣṭham yam lebhe rohiṇī sutaḥ tam tuṣṭaḥ pradadau rāmaḥ saubhadrāya mahātmane ete ca anye ca bahavaḥ dhvajāḥ hema vibhūṣaṇāḥ dadṛśuḥ tatra śūrāṇām dviṣatām śoka vardhanāḥ droṇa anīkam mahā rāja paṭe citram iva arpitam śuśruvuḥ nāma gotrāṇi vīrāṇām saṃyuge tadā droṇam ādravatām rājñ svayaṃvare iva āhave uvāca saṃprayuktaḥ kila eva ayam diṣṭaiḥ bhavati pūruṣaḥ tasmin eva tu sarva arthāḥ dṛśyante vai pṛthagvidhāḥ dīrgham viproṣitaḥ kālam araṇye jaṭilaḥ ajinī ajñātaḥ ca eva lokasya vijahāra yudhiṣṭhiraḥ saḥ eva mahatīm senām samāvartayat āhave dyūta vyasanam āsādya kleśitaḥ hi yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ardham me kekayāḥ labdhāḥ kāśikāḥ kosalāḥ ca ye cedayaḥ ca apare vaṅgāḥ mām eva samupāśritāḥ pṛthivī bhūyasī tāta mama pārthasya no tathā madhye rājñām mahā bāhum sadā yuddha abhinandinam sarva astra pāragam droṇam katham mṛtyuḥ upeyivāḥ samanuprāpta kṛcchraḥ aham saṃmoham paramam gataḥ bhīṣma droṇau hatau śrutvā na aham jīvitum utsahe yat mā kṣattā bravīt tāta prapaśyan putra gṛddhinam nṛśaṃsam tu param tat syāt tyaktvā duryodhanam yadi putra śeṣam cikīrṣeyam kṛcchram na maraṇam bhavet avaśeṣam na paśyāmi kakude mṛdite sati katham syāt avaśeṣam hi dhuryayoḥ abhyatītayoḥ yau nityam anujīvāmaḥ kṣamiṇau puruṣa ṛṣabhau tasmāt bhayam naḥ bhūyiṣṭham bhrātṛvyāt ca viśeṣataḥ yathā āsīt ca nivṛtteṣu pāṇḍaveṣu ca saṃjaya mama sainya avaśeṣasya saṃnipātaḥ su dāruṇaḥ māmakānām ca ye śūrāḥ kān tatra samavārayan uvāca mahat bhairavam āsīt naḥ saṃnivṛtteṣu pāṇḍuṣu dṛṣṭvā droṇam chādyamānam taiḥ bhāskaram iva ambudaiḥ tatas hatam amanyāma droṇam dṛṣṭi pathe hate tān tu śūrān mahā iṣvāsān krūram karma cikīrṣataḥ dṛṣṭvā duryodhanaḥ tūrṇam sva sainyam samacūcudat yathāśakti yathotsāham yathāsattvam narādhipāḥ vārayadhvam yathāyogam pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm krūram dṛṣṭvā tu te putram bhīmasenaḥ abhyavartata ārāt dṛṣṭvā kiran bāṇaiḥ icchan droṇasya jīvitam tam bāṇaiḥ avatastāra kruddhaḥ mṛtyum iva āhave tam ca bhīmaḥ atudat bāṇaiḥ tadā āsīt tumulam mahat te īśvara samādiṣṭāḥ prājñāḥ śūrāḥ prahāriṇaḥ bāhyam mṛtyu bhayam kṛtvā pratyatiṣṭhan parān yudhi kṛtavarmā śineḥ putram droṇa prepsum viśām pate paryavārayat āyāntam śūram samiti śobhanam tam śaineyaḥ śara vrātaiḥ kruddhaḥ kruddham avārayat saindhavaḥ kṣatradharmāṇam āpatantam śara oghinam ugra dhanvā mahā iṣvāsam yattaḥ droṇāt avārayat vivyādha kṣatradharmāṇam raṇe sarva āyasaiḥ śaraiḥ yuyutsum pāṇḍava arthāya yatamānam mahā ratham subāhuḥ bhrātaram śūram yattaḥ droṇāt avārayat subāhoḥ sa dhanuḥ bāṇau asyataḥ parigha upamau yuyutsuḥ śita pītābhyām kṣurābhyām acchinat bhujau duḥśāsanaḥ tu saṃyāntam droṇāya nakulam yudhi savya dakṣiṇam asyantam śūraḥ śūram nyavārayat rājānam pāṇḍava śreṣṭham dharma ātmānam yudhiṣṭhiram velā iva sāgaram kṣubdham madra rāj samavārayat madra īśaḥ tam catuḥṣaṣṭyā śaraiḥ viddhvā anadat bhṛśam kṣurābhyām pāṇḍava śreṣṭhaḥ tatas uccukruśuḥ janāḥ tathā eva rājā vāhlīkaḥ rājānam drupadam śaraiḥ ādravantam saha anīkam saha anīkaḥ nyavārayat vinda anuvindau āvantyau virāṭam matsyam ārcchatām matsyānām kekayaiḥ sārdham abhīta aśva ratha dvipam nākulim tu śatānīkam bhūtakarmā sabhāpatiḥ asyantam iṣu jālāni yāntam droṇāt avārayat cakre vibāhu śirasam bhūtakarmāṇam āhave droṇāya abhimukham vīram viviṃśatiḥ avārayat viviṃśatim śaraiḥ viddhvā na abhyavartata daṃśitaḥ śālvaḥ bhīma rathaḥ śūram śrutasenam mahā āhave droṇāya abhimukham yāntam śara ogheṇa nyavārayat atha bhīmarathaḥ śālvam āśugaiḥ āyasaiḥ śitaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ sa aśva niyantāram anayat yama sādanam śrutakarmāṇam āyāntam mayūra sadṛśaiḥ hayaiḥ śaraiḥ ca draupadī putram citrasenaḥ samāvṛṇot śrutakarmāṇam āyāntam dauḥśāsaniḥ avāyat tiṣṭhantam agratas dṛṣṭvā prativindhyam tam āhave drauṇiḥ mānam pituḥ kurvan mārgaṇaiḥ samavārayat tam kruddhaḥ prativivyādha prativindhyaḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ siṃha lāṅgūla lakṣmāṇam pituḥ arthe vyavasthitam ārjunim śrutakīrtim ca draupadeyam mahā ratham droṇāya abhimukham yāntam dauḥśāsaniḥ avārayat tasya kṛṣṇa samaḥ kārṣṇiḥ tribhiḥ bhallaiḥ su saṃśitaiḥ dhanuḥ dhvajam ca sūtam ca chittvā droṇa antikam yayau tam paṭaccara hantāram lakṣmaṇaḥ samavārayat sa lakṣmaṇasya iṣvasanam chittvā lakṣma ca bhārata lakṣmaṇe śara jālāni visṛjan bahu aśobhata ārjuniḥ kṛtinam śūram lakṣmaṇam samayodhayat vikarṇaḥ tu mahā prājñaḥ yājñasenim śikhaṇḍinam paryavārayat āyāntam yuvānam samare yuvā tatas tam iṣu jālena yājñaseniḥ samāvṛṇot vidhūya tat bāṇa jālam babhau te sutaḥ balī droṇāya abhimukham yāntam vatsadantaiḥ avārayat sa saṃprahāraḥ tumulaḥ tayoḥ puruṣa siṃhayoḥ sainikānām ca sarveṣām tayoḥ ca prīti vardhanaḥ aṅgadam pañcabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ avidhyat sa paraṃtapaḥ aṅgadaḥ daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ punar enam avākirat vīrāṇām jaya kāṅkṣāṇām atīva bala pauruṣāt durmukhaḥ tu mahā iṣvāsaḥ vīram purujitam balī droṇāya abhimukham yāntam kuntibhojam avārayat droṇāya abhimukham yātān śara varṣaiḥ avārayat te ca enam bhṛśa saṃkruddhāḥ śara vrātaiḥ avākiran sa ca tān chādayām āsa śara jālaiḥ punar punar na eva karṇaḥ na te pañca dadṛśuḥ bāṇa saṃvṛtāḥ sa aśva sūta dhvaja rathāḥ paraspara śara ācitāḥ nīlam kāśyam jayam śūrāḥ trayaḥ trīn pratyavārayan siṃha vyāghra tarakṣūṇām yathā ibha mahiṣa ṛṣabhaiḥ dhṛṣṭadyumna sutān vīrān putrāḥ te samavārayan droṇāya abhimukham yāntam śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ tatakṣatuḥ siṃhasya dvipa mukhyābhyām prabhinnābhyām yathā vane rājānam tu tathā ambaṣṭham ekam yuddha abhinandinam cedi rājaḥ śarān asyan kruddhaḥ droṇāt avārayat sa tyaktvā sa śaram cāpam rathāt bhūmim atha apatat vārdhakṣemim tu vārṣṇeyam kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ śaraiḥ akṣudraḥ kṣudrakaiḥ droṇāt kruddha rūpam avārayat yudhyantau kṛpa vārṣṇeyau ye apaśyan citra yodhinau punar patākām sūtam ca chatram ca apātayat rathāt atha āplutya rathāt tūrṇam yūpaketuḥ amitra hā sa aśva sūta dhvaja ratham tam cakarta vara asinā ratham ca svam samāsthāya dhanuḥ ādāya ca aparam svayam yacchan hayān rājan vyadhamat pāṇḍavām camūm pāṇḍyam indram iva āyāntam asurān prati jaghnivasam samarthaḥ sāyaka oghena dvīpam sindhuḥ iva āvṛṇot gadā parigha nistriṃśa paṭṭiśa āyodhana upalaiḥ kaḍaṅgaraiḥ bhuśuṇḍībhiḥ prāsa tomara sāyakaiḥ tasya sindhupateḥ vāhān vyadhamat pāṇḍya rāj svayam vīraḥ vīreṇa saṃkruddhaḥ droṇāya abhimukham vrajan mṛga ṛkṣa yuddhe tiṣṭhantam rathe vīraḥ ratheṣubhiḥ tām pāṇḍavīm mahā senām deva senā upamām raṇe pārtham indram iva āyāntam droṇam prati nijaghnivasam sa nṛpam sa aśva yantāram arāti ghnam arāti hā amṛdnāt tam pṛṣatkena duryodhanam ariṃdamam sa jyām mṛdnat pṛṣatkena spṛṣṭvā vṛkṣam iva aśaniḥ vṛka ṛkṣa yukte tiṣṭhantam rathe vīraḥ vara iṣubhiḥ pāṃsu vāta agni salilaiḥ bhasma loṣṭha tṛṇa drumaiḥ senām vibhīṣayan āyāt droṇa prepsuḥ ghaṭotkacaḥ tam tu nānā praharaṇaiḥ nānā yuddha viśeṣaṇaiḥ rākṣasam rākṣasaḥ kruddhaḥ samājaghne hi alambuṣaḥ tādṛś yādṛś purā vṛttam śambara amararājayoḥ bhāradvājaḥ tu senānyam dhṛṣṭadyumnam mahā ratham mahatā śara jālena kirantam śatru vāhinīm avārayat mahā rāja sa amātyam sa padānugam tathā anye pārthivāḥ rājan bahu tvāt na anukīrtitāḥ hayaiḥ hayāḥ samājagmuḥ kuñjaraiḥ eva kuñjarāḥ padātayaḥ padātaiḥ ca rathaiḥ eva ratha ṛṣabhāḥ akurvan ārya karmāṇi tatra te puruṣa ṛṣabhāḥ kula vīrya anurūpāṇi saṃsṛṣṭāḥ ca parasparam evam dvaṃdva śatāni āsan ratha vāraṇa vājinām padātīnām ca bhadram te tava teṣām ca saṃkulam na etādṛśaḥ dṛṣṭa pūrvaḥ saṃgrāmaḥ na eva ca śrutaḥ droṇasya abhāva bhāveṣu prasaktānām yathā bhavat uvāca teṣu evam saṃnivṛtteṣu pratyudyāteṣu bhāgaśas katham yuyudhire pārthāḥ māmakāḥ ca tarasvinaḥ saṃśaptakāḥ vā pārthasya kim akurvata saṃjaya uvāca tathā teṣu nivṛtteṣu pratyudyāteṣu bhāgaśas sa nāgaḥ iva nāgena go vṛṣeṇa iva go vṛṣaḥ samāhūtaḥ svayam rājñā nāga anīkam upādravat sa yuddha kuśalaḥ pārthaḥ bāhu vīryeṇa ca anvitaḥ abhinat kuñjara anīkam acireṇa eva māriṣa te gajāḥ giri saṃkāśāḥ kṣarantaḥ sarvatas madam bhīmasenasya nārācaiḥ vimukhāḥ vimadīkṛtāḥ vidhamet abhra jālāni yathā vāyuḥ samantataḥ sa teṣu visṛjan bāṇān bhīmaḥ nāgeṣu aśobhata te bhīma bāṇaiḥ śataśas saṃsyūtāḥ vibabhuḥ gajāḥ tathā gajānām kadanam kurvāṇam anilātmajam tatas kṣaṇena kṣitipam kṣataja pratima īkṣaṇaḥ kṣayam ninīṣuḥ niśitaiḥ bhīmaḥ vivyādha pattribhiḥ sa śara arpita sarva aṅgaḥ kruddhaḥ vivyādha pāṇḍavam bhallābhyām kārmukam ca eva kṣipram ciccheda pāṇḍavaḥ duryodhanam pīḍyamānam dṛṣṭvā bhīmena māriṣa cukṣobhayiṣuḥ abhyāgāt aṅgaḥ mātaṃgam āsthitaḥ kumbha antare bhīmasenaḥ nārācena ārdayat bhṛśam śiraḥ ciccheda bhallena kṣiprakārī vṛkodaraḥ tasmin nipatite vīre saṃprādravata sā camūḥ saṃbhrānta aśva dvipa rathā padātīn avamṛdnatī prāgjyotiṣaḥ tatas bhīmam kuñjareṇa samādravat śravaṇābhyām atho padbhyām saṃhatena kareṇa ca vyāvṛtta nayanaḥ kruddhaḥ pradahan iva pāṇḍavam vṛkodara ratham sa aśvam aviśeṣam acūrṇayat padbhyām bhīmaḥ api atho dhāvan tasya gātreṣu alīyata jānan añjalikā vedham na apākrāmata pāṇḍavaḥ gātra abhyantara gaḥ bhūtvā kareṇa atāḍayat muhur lālayām āsa tam nāgam vadha ākāṅkṣiṇam avyayam nāga ayuta balaḥ śrīmān kālayānaḥ vṛkodaram bhīmam kareṇa avanamya jānubhyām abhyapātayat grīvāyām veṣṭayitvā enam sa gajaḥ hantum aihata punar gātrāṇi nāgasya praviveśa vṛkodaraḥ bhīmaḥ api nāga gātrebhyaḥ viniḥsṛtya apayāt javāt hā hā vinihataḥ bhīmaḥ kuñjareṇa iti māriṣa tena nādena vitrastā pāṇḍavānām anīkinī tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā hatam matvā vṛkodaram bhagadattam sa pāñcālaḥ sarvatas samavārayat bhīmaḥ api dorbhyām nāga indram nipīḍya amocayat balī tam rathaiḥ rathinām śreṣṭhāḥ parivārya samantataḥ avākiran śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas sa vighātam pṛṣatkānām aṅkuśena samācaran gajena pāṇḍu pāñcālān vyadhamat parvateśvaraḥ tathā vṛddhasya caritam kuñjareṇa viśām pate tatas rājā daśārṇānām prāgjyotiṣam upādravat tiryagyātena nāgena sa madena āśu gāminā prāgjyotiṣa pateḥ nāgaḥ saṃnipatya apavṛtya ca pārśve daśārṇa adhipateḥ bhittvā nāgam apātayat tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ dṛṣṭvā daśārṇa adhipatim hatam upasṛtya tu rājānam bhagadattam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ maṇḍalam sarvatas śliṣṭam rathinām ugra dhanvinām kiratām śara varṣāṇi sa nāgaḥ paryavartata tatas prāgjyotiṣaḥ rājā parigṛhya dvipa ṛṣabham preṣayām āsa sahasā yuyudhāna ratham prati āpatantam tu saṃprekṣya nāgam sātvata puṃgavaḥ avidhyat pañcabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ śitaiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ vyavartata paritrāsāt maṇḍalāni śara arditaḥ bṛhataḥ saindhavān aśvān samutthāpya tu sārathiḥ tasthau sātyakim āsādya saṃplutaḥ tam ratham punar niścakrāma tatas sarvān paricikṣepa pārthivān te tu āśu gatinā tena trāsyamānāḥ nara ṛṣabhāḥ tam ekam dviradam saṃkhye menire śataśas nṛpāḥ airāvata sthena yathā devarājena dānavāḥ teṣām pradravatām bhīmaḥ pāñcālānām itas tatas gaja vāji kṛtaḥ śabdaḥ su mahān samajāyata bhagadattena samare kālyamāneṣu pāṇḍuṣu tasya abhidravataḥ vāhān hasta muktena vāriṇā tatas tam abhyayāt tūrṇam ruciparva ākṛtīsutaḥ samukṣan śara varṣeṇa ratha sthaḥ antaka saṃnibhaḥ tatas ruciraparvāṇam śareṇa nata parvaṇā te enam śara dhārābhiḥ dhārābhiḥ iva toyadāḥ siṣicuḥ bhairavān nādān vinadantaḥ jighāṃsavaḥ tatas pārṣṇi aṅkuśa aṅguṣṭhaiḥ kṛtinā coditaḥ dvipaḥ prasārita karaḥ prāyāt stabdha karṇa īkṣaṇaḥ drutam saḥ adhiṣṭhāya padā vāhān yuyutsoḥ sūtam ārujat ratham babhañja saṃkruddhaḥ caṇḍa vātaḥ yathā drumam tatas pāṇḍava yodhāḥ te nāga rājam śaraiḥ drutam sa kuñjara sthaḥ visṛjan iṣūn ariṣu pārthivaḥ sa bhīmena atha bahudhā dantābhyām avapīḍayan mokṣitaḥ yuddha śauṇḍena nāga ayuta balaḥ gajaḥ tam ārjuniḥ dvādaśabhiḥ yuyutsuḥ daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ cekitānaḥ catuḥṣaṣṭyā sa uttara āyudhikam punar niyantuḥ śilpa yatnābhyām preṣitaḥ ari śara arditaḥ paricikṣepa tān nāgaḥ sa ripūn savya dakṣiṇam gopālaḥ iva daṇḍena yathā paśu gaṇān vane āveṣṭayata tām senām bhagadattaḥ tathā muhur kṣipram śyena abhipannānām vāyasānām iva svanaḥ sa reṇu mārgaḥ viyati bhāti daṇḍaḥ iva utthitaḥ samucchritaḥ bhṛśa ārtāyā senāyā su bhujaḥ yathā babhūva pāṇḍaveyānām bhṛśam vidravatām svanaḥ sa nāga rājaḥ pravara aṅkuśa āhataḥ purā sapakṣaḥ adri varaḥ yathā nṛpa bhayam tathā ripuṣu samādadhat bhṛśam vaṇij gaṇānām kṣubhitaḥ yathā arṇavaḥ kṣitim viyat dyām vidiśaḥ diśaḥ tathā sa tena nāga pravareṇa pārthivaḥ bhṛśam jagāhe dviṣatām anīkinīm tam eka nāgam gaṇaśas yathā gajāḥ samantataḥ drutam iva menire janāḥ uvāca yat mām pārthasya saṃgrāme karmāṇi paripṛcchasi tat śṛṇuṣva mahā rāja pārthaḥ yat akarot mṛdhe rajaḥ dṛṣṭvā samudbhūtam śrutvā ca gaja nisvanam bhajyatām bhagadattena kaunteyaḥ kṛṣṇam abravīt yathā prāgjyotiṣaḥ rājā gajena madhusūdana indrāt an avaraḥ saṃkhye gaja yāna viśāradaḥ prathamaḥ vā dvitīyaḥ vā pṛthivyām iti mama matiḥ sa ca api dvirada śreṣṭhaḥ sadā pratigajaḥ yudhi sarva śabda atigaḥ saṃkhye kṛta karmā jita klamaḥ sahaḥ śastra nipātānām agni sparśasya ca anagha sa pāṇḍava balam vyaktam adya ekaḥ nāśayiṣyati siṃhanādam mahat kṛtvā dhanuḥ bāṇa ravaiḥ saha vidrāvyamāṇam saṃpaśya hata bhūyiṣṭha nāyakam dṛṣṭvā vinadya sahasā mama senām pramṛdnati na ca āvābhyām ṛte anyaḥ asti śaktaḥ tam pratibādhitum tvaramāṇaḥ tatas yāhi yatas prāgjyotiṣa adhipaḥ vacanāt atha kṛṣṇaḥ tu prayayau savyasācinaḥ dāryate bhagadattena yatra pāṇḍava vāhinī tam prayāntam tatas paścāt āhvayantaḥ mahā rathāḥ saṃśaptakāḥ samārohan sahasrāṇi caturdaśa daśa eva tu sahasrāṇi trigartānām narādhipa catvāri tu sahasrāṇi vāsudevasya ye anugāḥ dāryamāṇām camūm dṛṣṭvā bhagadattena māriṣa āhūyamānasya ca taiḥ abhavat hṛdayam dvidhā ekaḥ ratha sahasrāṇi nihantum vāsavī raṇe sa tu saṃvartayām āsa dvaidhībhāvena pāṇḍavaḥ rathena tu ratha agryāṇām akarot tām mṛṣā tadā tatas śata sahasrāṇi śarāṇām nata parvaṇām vyasṛjan arjune rājan saṃśaptaka mahā rathāḥ na eva kuntī sutaḥ pārthaḥ na eva kṛṣṇaḥ janārdanaḥ na hayāḥ na rathaḥ rājan dṛśyante sma śaraiḥ citāḥ dṛśyante śara varṣeṇa prabaleṇa samāvṛtāḥ tatas tena śara oghena mahatā samavāstṛtaḥ yadā moham anuprāptaḥ sa svedaḥ ca janārdanaḥ tatas tān prāyaśas pārthaḥ vajra astreṇa nijaghnivān śataśas pāṇayaḥ chinnāḥ sa iṣu jyā tala kārmukāḥ ketavaḥ vājinaḥ sūtāḥ rathinaḥ ca apatan kṣitau druma acala agra ambudharaiḥ sama rūpāḥ su kalpitāḥ hata ārohāḥ kṣitau petuḥ dvipāḥ pārtha śara āhatāḥ vipraviddha kutha valgāḥ chinna bhāṇḍāḥ parāsavaḥ sa ārohāḥ turagāḥ petuḥ mathitāḥ pārtha mārgaṇaiḥ sa ṛṣṭi carma asi nakharāḥ sa mudgara paraśvadhāḥ saṃchinnāḥ bāhavaḥ petuḥ nṛṇām bhallaiḥ kirīṭinā bāla āditya ambuja indūnām tulya rūpāṇi māriṣa saṃchinnāni arjuna śaraiḥ śirāṃsi urvīm prapedire jajvāla alaṃkṛtaiḥ senā patribhiḥ prāṇa bhojanaiḥ kṣobhayantam tadā senām dviradam nalinīm iva dhanaṃjayam bhūta gaṇāḥ sādhu sādhu iti apūjayan dṛṣṭvā tat karma pārthasya vāsavasya iva mādhavaḥ yugapad ca eva saṃgrāme śataśas atha sahasraśas patitāḥ eva me dṛṣṭāḥ saṃśaptaka mahā rathāḥ tatas saṃśaptakān hatvā bhūyiṣṭham ye vyavasthitāḥ bhagadattāya yāhi iti pārthaḥ kṛṣṇam acodayat uvāca yiyāsataḥ tatas kṛṣṇaḥ pārthasya aśvān manojavān apraiṣīt hema saṃchannān droṇa anīkāya pāṇḍurān tam prayāntam kuru śreṣṭham svān trātum droṇa tāpitān suśarmā bhrātṛbhiḥ sārdham yuddha arthī pṛṣṭhatas anvayāt tatas śvetahayaḥ kṛṣṇam abravīt ajitam jayaḥ eṣa mām bhrātṛbhiḥ sārdham suśarmā āhvayate acyuta dvaidhībhūtam manaḥ mama adya kṛtam saṃśaptakaiḥ idam kim nu saṃśaptakān hanmi svān rakṣāmi ahita arditān yena trigarta adhipatiḥ pāṇḍavam samupāhvayat tatas arjunaḥ suśarmāṇam viddhvā sapta āśugaiḥ dhvajam dhanuḥ ca asya tathā kṣurābhyām samakṛntata trigarta adhipateḥ ca api bhrātaram ṣaḍbhiḥ āyasaiḥ sa aśvam sa sūtam tvaritaḥ pārthaḥ praiṣīt yama kṣayam tatas bhujaga saṃkāśām suśarmā śaktim āyasīm cikṣepa arjunam ādiśya vāsudevāya tomaram śaktim tribhiḥ śaraiḥ chittvā tomaram tribhiḥ arjunaḥ suśarmāṇam śara vrātaiḥ mohayitvā nyavartata tam vāsavam iva āyāntam bhūri varṣa śara oghinam rājñ tāvaka sainyānām na ugram kaḥ cit avārayat na aśaknuvan te saṃsoḍhum sparśam agneḥ iva prajāḥ saṃveṣṭayan anīkāni śara varṣeṇa pāṇḍavaḥ suparṇa pāta vat rājñ āyāt prāgjyotiṣam prati yat tadā anāmayat jiṣṇuḥ bharatānām apāyinām dhanuḥ kṣema karam saṃkhye dviṣatām aśru vardhanam kṛte kṣatra vināśāya dhanuḥ āyacchat arjunaḥ tathā vikṣobhyamāṇā sā pārthena te vāhinī matim kṛtvā raṇe kruddhāḥ vīrāḥ jaya parājaye yathā naḍavanam kruddhaḥ prabhinnaḥ ṣaṣṭihāyanaḥ mṛdnīyāt tadvat āyastaḥ pārthaḥ amṛdnāt camūm te tam rathena nara vyāghraḥ pratyagṛhṇāt abhīta vat kalpitābhyām yathāśāstram rathena ca gajena ca tatas jīmūta saṃkāśāt nāgāt indraḥ sa ca api śara varṣam tat śara varṣeṇa vāsaviḥ saṃnyavārayat asya āśu laghu tvāt pākaśāsanaḥ vavarṣa śara varṣam tu punar eva dhanaṃjayaḥ tatas prāgjyotiṣaḥ rājā śara varṣam nivārya tat śaraiḥ jaghne mahā bāhum pārtham kṛṣṇam ca bhārata codayām āsa tam nāgam vadhāya acyuta pārthayoḥ tam āpatantam dviradam dṛṣṭvā kruddham iva antakam saṃprāptam api na iyeṣa parāvṛttam mahā dvipam sa āroham mṛtyusāt kartum smaran dharmam dhanaṃjayaḥ sa tu nāgaḥ dvipa rathān hayān ca ārujya māriṣa uvāca prāgjyotiṣaḥ vā pārthasya tat me śaṃsa yathātatham uvāca prāgjyotiṣeṇa saṃsaktau ubhau dāśārha pāṇḍavau tathā hi śara varṣāṇi pātayati aniśam prabho atha kārṣṇāyasaiḥ bāṇaiḥ pūrṇa kārmuka niḥsṛtaiḥ avidhyat devakīputram hema puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ agni sparśa samāḥ tīkṣṇāḥ bhagadattena coditāḥ nirbhidya devakīputram kṣitim jagmuḥ śarāḥ tatas tasya pārthaḥ dhanuḥ chittvā śarāvāpam nihatya ca saḥ arka raśmi nibhān tīkṣṇān tomarān vai caturdaśa viśīrṇa varmā sa gajaḥ śaraiḥ su bhṛśam arditaḥ babhau śirasi mātaṃgo tatas prāgjyotiṣaḥ śaktim hema daṇḍām ayasmayīm tatas chatram dhvajam ca eva chittvā rājñaḥ arjunaḥ śaraiḥ bhagadattaḥ tatas kruddhaḥ pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥ vyasṛjat tomarān mūrdhani śvetāśvasya unnanāda ca parivṛttam kirīṭam tam yamayan eva phalgunaḥ su dṛṣṭaḥ kriyatām loke iti rājānam abravīt evam uktaḥ tu saṃkruddhaḥ śara varṣeṇa pāṇḍavam tasya pārthaḥ dhanuḥ chittvā tūṇīrān saṃnikṛtya ca abhimantrya aṅkuśam kruddhaḥ vyasṛjat pāṇḍava urasi tat astram udyatam dṛṣṭvā vāsudevaḥ pratāpavān arjunaḥ pṛṣṭhatas kṛtvā pratijagrāha vīryavān urasā pratijagrāha pārtham saṃchādya keśavaḥ jvalana arka indu varṇa āḍhyā tāraka ujjvala pāvakā tayā padma abhiśobhinyā vāyu kampita lolayā śobhate abhyadhikam śauriḥ atasī puṣpa saṃnibhaḥ keśavaḥ keśimathanaḥ śārṅgadhanvā arimardanaḥ sandhyā abhraiḥ iva saṃchannaḥ prāvṛṣ kāle naga uttamaḥ tatas arjunaḥ klānta manāḥ keśavam pratyabhāṣata iti uktvā puṇḍarīkākṣa pratijñām svām na rakṣasi kimartham puruṣa vyāghra svayam pratigṛhītavān yadi aham vyasanī vā syām aśaktaḥ vā nivāraṇe sa bāṇaḥ sa dhanuḥ ca aham sa sura asura mānavān śaktaḥ lokān imān jetum tat ca api viditam tava śṛṇu guhyam idam pārtha yathā vṛttam purā anagha yā iyam loka dharā devī sarva bhūta dharā dharā sa kāmā lokakartāram nārāyaṇam upasthitā sā vavre viṣṇu sadṛśam putram astram ca vaiṣṇavam babhūva ca sutaḥ tasyām narakaḥ nāma viśrutaḥ astram ca vaiṣṇavam tasmai dadau nārāyaṇaḥ svayam tasmāt prāgjyotiṣam prāptam sarva śastra vighātanam uvāca tasmāt mayā kṛtam hi etat mā te abhūt buddhiḥ anyathā anunīya tu dāśārhaḥ pāṇḍavam tvaritaḥ abravīt jahi prāgjyotiṣam kṣipram vākya śeṣam ca me śṛṇu caturmūrtiḥ aham śaśvat loka trāṇa artham udyataḥ ātmānam pravibhajya iha lokānām hitam ādadhe ekā mūrtiḥ tapaḥ caryām kurute mama bhuvi sthitā aparā paśyati jagat kurvāṇam sādhu asādhunī aparā kurute karma mānuṣam lokam āśritā śete caturthā tu aparā nidrām varṣa sahasrikām vara arhebhyaḥ varān śreṣṭhān tasmin kāle dadāti sā tam tu kālam anuprāptam viditvā pṛthivī tadā prāyācata varam yam mām naraka arthāya tam śṛṇu devānām asurāṇām ca avadhyaḥ tanayaḥ astu me upetaḥ vaiṣṇava astreṇa tat me tvam dātum arhasi evam varam aham śrutvā jagatyāḥ tanaye tadā amogham astram adadam vaiṣṇavam tat aham purā narakasya abhirakṣā artham na enam kaḥ cit vadhiṣyati anena astreṇa te guptaḥ sutaḥ para bala ardanaḥ bhaviṣyati durādharṣaḥ sarva lokeṣu sarvadā tathā iti uktvā gatā devī kṛta kāmā manasvinī vyajāyata dharā devī putram putra śata avaram sa ca api āsīt durādharṣaḥ narakaḥ śatru tāpanaḥ tasmāt prāgjyotiṣam prāptam tat astram pārtha māmakam sarvān samāgatān hanyāt kim punar tvām dhanaṃjaya bhoginām ca eva durdharṣam mayā dattam sura asuraiḥ jahi prāgjyotiṣam pārtha purā sarvān hinasti saḥ na asya avadhyaḥ asti lokeṣu sa indra rudreṣu māriṣa yathā aham jaghnivān pūrvam hita artham narakam tathā yathā aham narakam loka hita artham ahanam purā evam uktaḥ tatas pārthaḥ keśavena mahātmanā bhagadattam śitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ sahasā samavākirat ghaṇṭām kāñcana saṃchannām viśvakarma vinirmitām kāñcana śṛṅkhalā naddhām savyām ciccheda pāṇḍavaḥ sā hatā śara ghātena vajra niṣpeṣa saṃnibhā dakṣiṇā api hatā rājan ghaṇṭā bāṇaiḥ kirīṭinaḥ papāta dūram adhvānam gatvā sūryaḥ iva kṣitau tatas pārthaḥ mahā bāhuḥ asambhrāntaḥ mahā manāḥ tatas saṃdhāya viśikham dīpyamānam iva analam samāsādya tu tam nāgam bāṇaḥ vajraḥ iva acalam sa karī bhagadattena preryamāṇaḥ punar punar syandamānam tatas nāgam caraṇābhyām anodayat sa tu viṣṭabhya gātrāṇi dantābhyām avanim yayau nadan ārta svaram prāṇān utsasarja mahā dvipaḥ tatas gāṇḍīvadhanvānam abhyabhāṣata keśavaḥ ayam mahattaraḥ pārtha palitena samāvṛtaḥ valī saṃchanna nayanaḥ śūraḥ parama durjayaḥ akṣṇoḥ unmīlana arthāya baddha paṭṭaḥ sadā nṛpaḥ deva vākyāt praciccheda śareṇa bhṛśam arjunaḥ tatas candra ardha bimbena śareṇa nata parvaṇā rājñā balavatā tena jānubhyām dhāritaḥ raṇe evam yuddham tadā tena rājñā tena durātmanā kirīṭī ca ardha bimbena śareṇa ānata parvaṇā bibheda hṛdayam rājñaḥ bhagadattasya pāṇḍavaḥ sa bhinna hṛdayaḥ rājā bhagadattaḥ kirīṭinā śarāsanam śarān ca eva gatāsuḥ pramumoca ha śirasaḥ tasya vibhraṣṭaḥ papāta ca vara aṅkuśaḥ nāla tāḍana vibhraṣṭam palāśam nalināt iva sa hema mālī tapanīya bhāṇḍāt papāta nāgāt giri saṃnikāśāt su puṣpitaḥ māruta vega rugṇaḥ mahīdhara agrāt iva karṇikāraḥ tatas aparān te jaya kāṅkṣiṇaḥ narān babhañja vāyuḥ balavān drumān iva uvāca hatvā prāgjyotiṣam pārthaḥ pradakṣiṇam avartata pūrva daityam mahā vīram bhagadattam mahā balam kṛṣṇau daśārha bībhatsū jaghnatuḥ yudhi durjayam nāga ayuta bala prāṇam śūram āhava śobhinam vaiṣṇava astreṇa saṃyuktaḥ aṃkuśena ca vīryavān bhagadattam raṇe śūram nihanyāt kaḥ arjunam vinā arjunaḥ api mahā vīryaḥ hatvā pitṛ sakham raṇe tam āditya samam kāntyā bhūmau nipatitam divaḥ prasamīkṣya tadā pārthaḥ reṇunā tu avaguṇṭhitam ārchetām arjunam saṃkhye bhrātarau vṛṣaka acalau avidhyetām mahā vegaiḥ niśitaiḥ āśugaiḥ bhṛśam vṛṣakasya hayān sūtam dhanuḥ chatram ratham dhvajam tilaśas vyadhamat pārthaḥ saubalasya śitaiḥ śaraiḥ tatas arjunaḥ śara vrātaiḥ nānā praharaṇaiḥ api gāndhārān vyākulān cakre saubala pramukhān punar tatas pañcaśatān vīrān gāndhārān udyata āyudhān prāhiṇot mṛtyu lokāya kruddhaḥ bāṇaiḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ hata aśvāt tu rathāt tūrṇam avatīrya mahā bhujaḥ tau eka ratham ārūḍhau bhrātarau vṛṣaka acalau śara varṣeṇa bībhatsum avidhyetām punar punar syālau tava mahātmānau rājñau vṛṣaka acalau bhṛśam nijaghnatuḥ pārtham indram vṛtra balau iva labdha lakṣyau tu gāndhārau ahatām pāṇḍavam punar nidāgha vārṣikau māsau lokam gharmāmbuṣu yathā saṃśliṣṭa aṅgau sthitau rājñ jaghāna eka iṣuṇā arjunaḥ tau rathāt siṃha saṃkāśau lohita akṣau mahā bhujau gatāsū petatuḥ vīrau sodaryau eka lakṣaṇau yaśaḥ daśa diśaḥ puṇyam gamayitvā vyavasthitau dṛṣṭvā vinihatau saṃkhye mātulau apalāyinaḥ bhṛśam mumucuḥ aśrūṇi putrāḥ te viśām pate nihatau bhrātarau dṛṣṭvā māyā śata viśāradaḥ kṛṣṇau saṃmohayan māyām vidadhe śakuniḥ tatas laguḍa ayaḥ guḍa aśmānaḥ śataghnyaḥ ca sa śaktayaḥ gadā parigha nistriṃśa śūla mudgara paṭṭiśāḥ sa kampana ṛṣṭi nakharāḥ musalāni paraśvadhāḥ kṣurāḥ kṣurapra nālīkāḥ vatsadantāḥ trisaṃdhinaḥ cakrāṇi viśikhāḥ prāsāḥ vividhāni āyudhāni ca khara uṣṭra mahiṣāḥ siṃhāḥ vyāghrāḥ sṛmara cillikāḥ ṛkṣāḥ śālāvṛkāḥ gṛdhrāḥ kapayaḥ atha sarīsṛpāḥ vividhāni ca rakṣāṃsi kṣudhitāni arjunam prati visṛjan iṣu jālāni sahasā tāni atāḍayat te hanyamānāḥ śūreṇa pravaraiḥ sāyakaiḥ dṛḍhaiḥ viruvantaḥ mahā rāvān vineśuḥ sarvatas hatāḥ tasmāt ca tamasaḥ vācaḥ krūrāḥ pārtham abhartsayan tat tamaḥ astreṇa mahatā jyotiṣeṇa arjunaḥ avadhīt hate tasmin jala oghāḥ tu prādurāsan bhayānakāḥ ambhasaḥ tasya nāśa artham āditya astram atha arjunaḥ prāyuṅkta ambhaḥ tatas tena prāyaśas astreṇa śoṣitam evam bahuvidhāḥ māyāḥ saubalasya kṛtāḥ kṛtāḥ durdyūta devin gāndhāre na akṣān kṣipati gāṇḍivam jvalitān niśitān tīkṣṇān śarān kṣipati gāṇḍivam tathā hatāsu māyāsu trastaḥ arjuna śara āhataḥ apāyāt javanaiḥ aśvaiḥ śakuniḥ prākṛtaḥ yathā abhyavarṣat śara ogheṇa kauravāṇām anīkinīm sā hanyamānā pārthena putrasya te vāhinī dvaidhībhūtā mahā rāja gaṅgā iva āsādya parvatam ke cit duryodhanam rājan ardyamānāḥ kirīṭinā gāṇḍīvasya ca nirghoṣaḥ śrutaḥ dakṣiṇatas mayā śaṅkha dundubhi nirghoṣam vāditrāṇām ca nisvanam gāṇḍīvasya ca nirghoṣaḥ vyatikramya aspṛśat divam tatas punar dakṣiṇatas saṃgrāmaḥ citra yodhin yaudhiṣṭhirāṇi anīkāni pradahanti tatas tatas nānāvidhāni anīkāni putrāṇām tava bhārata arjunaḥ vyadhamat kāle divi iva abhrāṇi mārutaḥ tam vāsavam iva āyāntam bhūri varṣa śara oghinam mahā iṣvāsam nara vyāghram na ugram kaḥ cit avārayat te hanyamānāḥ pārthena tvadīyāḥ vyathitāḥ bhṛśam te arjunena śarāḥ muktāḥ kaṅka pattrāḥ tanu chidaḥ śalabhāḥ iva saṃpetuḥ saṃvṛṇvānāḥ diśaḥ daśa turagam rathinam nāgam padātim api māriṣa na ca dvitīyam vyasṛjat kuñjara aśva nareṣu saḥ pṛthak eka śara ārugṇāḥ nipetuḥ te gatāsavaḥ hataiḥ manuṣyaiḥ turagaiḥ ca sarvatas śara abhivṛṣṭaiḥ dviradaiḥ ca pātitaiḥ tadā vicitram āyodha śiraḥ babhūva ha pitā sutam tyajati suhṛd varam suhṛd tathā eva putraḥ pitaram śara āturaḥ sva rakṣaṇe kṛta matayaḥ tadā janāḥ tyajanti vāhān api pārtha pīḍitāḥ uvāca teṣu anīkeṣu bhagneṣu pāṇḍu putreṇa saṃjaya calitānām drutānām ca katham āsīt manaḥ hi vaḥ anīkānām prabhagnānām vyavasthānam a paśyatām atas param raṇe sūta kim akurvanta māmakāḥ duṣkaram pratisaṃdhānam tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya uvāca tathā api tava putrasya priya kāmāḥ viśām pate yaśaḥ pravīrāḥ lokeṣu rakṣantaḥ droṇam anvayuḥ samudyateṣu śastreṣu saṃprāpte ca yudhiṣṭhire sātyakeḥ ca eva śūrasya dhṛṣṭadyumnasya ca abhibho droṇam droṇam iti krūrāḥ pāñcālāḥ samacodayan droṇam droṇam iti hi eke mā droṇam iti ca apare kurūṇām pāṇḍavānām ca droṇa dyūtam avartata yam yam sma bhajate droṇaḥ pāñcālānām ratha vrajam tatra tatra sma pāñcālyaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ atha dhīyate vīrāḥ samāsadan vīrān agacchan bhīravaḥ parān akampanīyāḥ śatrūṇām babhūvuḥ tatra pāṇḍavāḥ akampayan tu anīkāni smarantaḥ kleśam ātmanaḥ te tu amarṣa vaśam prāptāḥ hrīmantaḥ sattva coditāḥ tyaktvā prāṇān nyavartanta ghnantaḥ droṇam mahā āhave ayasām iva saṃpātaḥ śilānām iva ca abhavat dīvyatām tumule yuddhe prāṇaiḥ amita tejasām dṛṣṭa pūrvam mahā rāja śruta pūrvam atha api vā prākampata iva pṛthivī tasmin vīra avasādane pravartatā bala oghena mahatā bhāra pīḍitā samāsādya tu pāṇḍūnām anīkāni sahasraśas droṇena caratā saṃkhye prabhagnāni śitaiḥ śaraiḥ teṣu pramathyamāneṣu droṇena adbhuta karmaṇā paryavārayat āsādya droṇam senāpatiḥ svayam tat adbhutam abhūt yuddham droṇa pāñcālyayoḥ tadā śara sphuliṅgaḥ cāpa arciḥ dahan kakṣam iva analaḥ tam dahantam anīkāni droṇaputraḥ pratāpavān pūrva abhibhāṣī su ślakṣṇam smayamānaḥ abhyabhāṣata nīla kim bahubhiḥ dagdhaiḥ te yodhaiḥ śara arciṣā vyākośa padma ābha mukham nīlaḥ vivyādha sāyakaiḥ droṇāyaneḥ śiraḥ kāyāt dhartum aicchat patatri vat tasya udyata aseḥ su nasam śiraḥ kāyāt sa kuṇḍalam bhallena apāharat drauṇiḥ smayamānaḥ iva anagha saṃpūrṇa candra ābha mukhaḥ padma pattra nibha īkṣaṇaḥ tatas pravivyathe senā pāṇḍavā bhṛśam ākulā cintayan ca te sarve pāṇḍavānām mahā rathāḥ dakṣiṇena tu senāyāḥ kurute kadanam balī saṃśaptaka avaśeṣasya nārāyaṇa balasya ca uvāca pratighātam tu sainyasya na amṛṣyata vṛkodaraḥ saḥ abhinat bāhlikam ṣaṣṭyā karṇam ca daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ tasya droṇaḥ śitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ tīkṣṇa dhāraiḥ ayasmayaiḥ ānantaryam abhiprepsuḥ ṣaḍviṃśatyā samārpayat punar ca agni sama sparśaiḥ āśīviṣa viṣa upamaiḥ karṇaḥ dvādaśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ aśvatthāmā ca sapta droṇam pañcāśatā iṣūṇām karṇam ca daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ duryodhanam dvādaśabhiḥ drauṇim ca aṣṭabhiḥ āśugaiḥ ārāvam tumulam kurvan abhyavartata tān raṇe tasmin saṃtyajati prāṇān mṛtyu sādhāraṇīkṛte ajātaśatruḥ tān yodhān bhīmam trāta iti acodayat yuyudhāna prabhṛtayaḥ mādrī putrau ca pāṇḍavau te sametya su saṃrabdhāḥ sahitāḥ puruṣa ṛṣabhāḥ mahā iṣvāsa varaiḥ guptam droṇa anīkam bibhitsavaḥ samāpetuḥ mahā vīryāḥ bhīma prabhṛtayaḥ rathāḥ tān pratyagṛhṇāt avyagraḥ droṇaḥ api rathinām varaḥ mahā balān atirathān vīrān samara śobhinaḥ bāhyam mṛtyu bhayam kṛtvā tāvakāḥ pāṇḍavān yayuḥ āsīt śakti asi saṃpātaḥ yuddham āsīt paraśvadhaiḥ nikṛṣṭam asi yuddham ca babhūva kaṭuka udayam kuñjarāṇām ca saṃpātaḥ babhūva kaṭuka udayaḥ kuñjarāṇām ca saṃghātaiḥ yuddham āsīt su dāruṇam apatat kuñjarāt anyaḥ hayāt anyaḥ tu avākśirāḥ naraḥ bāṇena nirbhinnaḥ rathāt anyaḥ ca māriṣa śiraḥ pradhvaṃsayām āsa vakṣasi ākramya kuñjaraḥ apare api aparān jaghnuḥ vāraṇāḥ patitān narān viṣāṇaiḥ ca avanim gatvā vyabhindan rathinaḥ bahūn nara antraiḥ ke cit apare viṣāṇa ālagna saṃsravaiḥ babhramuḥ śataśas nāgāḥ mṛdnantaḥ śataśas narān kāṃsya āyasa tanutrāṇān nara aśva ratha kuñjarān patitān pothayām cakruḥ dvipāḥ sthūla naḍān iva anīkānām prabhagnānām avasthānam a paśyatām duṣkaram pratisaṃdhānam bhuvi ca āsīt tadā nṛpa gṛdhra patra adhivāsāṃsi śayanāni narādhipāḥ hrīmantaḥ kāla saṃpakvāḥ su duḥkhāni adhiśerate yuga ardham chinnam ādāya pradudrāva tathā hayaḥ sa asiḥ bāhuḥ nipatitaḥ śiraḥ chinnam sa kuṇḍalam gajena ākṣipya balinā rathaḥ saṃcūrṇitaḥ kṣitau rathinā tāḍitaḥ nāgaḥ nārācena apatat vyasuḥ sa ārohaḥ ca apatat vājī gajena ātāḍitaḥ bhṛśam hā tāta hā putra sakhe kva asi tiṣṭha kva dhāvasi upāśāmyat rajaḥ bhaumam bhīrūn kaśmalam āviśat cakreṇa cakram āsādya vīraḥ vīrasya saṃyuge atīta iṣu pathe kāle jahāra gadayā śiraḥ āsīt keśa parāmarśaḥ muṣṭi yuddham ca dāruṇam nakhaiḥ dantaiḥ ca śūrāṇam a dvīpe dvīpam icchatām sa dhanuḥ ca aparasya api sa śaraḥ sa aṅkuśaḥ tathā anyaḥ prāptasya ca anyasya śiraḥ kāyāt apāharat śabdam abhyadravat ca anyaḥ śabdāt anyaḥ adravat bhṛśam svān anyaḥ atha parān anyaḥ jaghāna niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ bhītaḥ ca anyaḥ udakrośat anyaḥ bhītaḥ upādravat asaṃprāptasya tam deśam anyaḥ jīvitam ādade giri śṛṅga upamaḥ ca atra nārācena nipātitaḥ mātaṃgaḥ nyapatat bhūmau nadī rodhe iva uṣṇage adhyatiṣṭhat padā bhūmau saha aśvam saha sārathim śūrān praharataḥ dṛṣṭvā kṛtāstrān rudhira ukṣitān bahūn api āviśat mohaḥ bhīrūn hṛdaya durbalān tatas senāpati śīghram ayam kālaḥ iti bruvan nitya abhitvaritān eva tvarayām āsa pāṇḍavān kurvantaḥ śāsanam tasya pāṇḍaveyāḥ yaśasvinaḥ gṛhṇīta adravata anyonyam vibhītāḥ vinikṛntata tatas droṇaḥ kṛpaḥ karṇaḥ drauṇiḥ rājā jayadrathaḥ te tu ārya dharma saṃrabdhāḥ durnivāryāḥ durāsadāḥ śara ārtāḥ na juhuḥ droṇam pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha tatas droṇaḥ abhisaṃkruddhaḥ visṛjan śataśas śarān cedi pāñcāla pāṇḍūnām akarot kadanam mahat tasya jyā tala nirghoṣaḥ śuśruve dikṣu māriṣa vajra saṃghāta saṃkāśaḥ trāsayan pāṇḍavān bahūn etasmin antare jiṣṇuḥ hatvā saṃśaptakān balī abyayāt tatra yatra sma droṇaḥ pāṇḍūn pramardati tam śara ogha mahā vartam śoṇita udam mahā hradam tīrṇaḥ saṃśaptakān hatvā pratyadṛśyata phalgunaḥ dīpyamānam apaśyāma tejasā vānaradhvajam sa pāṇḍava yuga anta arkaḥ kurūn api abhyatītapat pradadāha kurūn sarvān arjunaḥ śastra tejasā tāḍyamānāḥ kṣitim jagmuḥ mukta śastrāḥ śara arditāḥ pārtha bāṇa hatāḥ ke cit nipetuḥ vigata asavaḥ teṣām utpatatām kān cit patitān ca parāṅmukhān te viśīrṇa ratha aśva ibhāḥ prāyaśas ca parāṅmukhāḥ kuravaḥ karṇa karṇa iti hā hā iti ca vicukruśuḥ tam ādhirathiḥ ākrandam vijñāya śaraṇa eṣiṇām sa bhārata ratha śreṣṭhaḥ sarva bhārata harṣaṇaḥ rāma śiṣyaḥ mahā bāhuḥ dhanvinām māna hā sadā śara oghān śara jālena vidudhāva dhanaṃjayaḥ astram astreṇa saṃvārya prāṇadat visṛjan śarān dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca bhīmaḥ ca sātyakiḥ ca mahā rathaḥ arjuna astram tu rādheyaḥ saṃvārya śara vṛṣṭibhiḥ teṣām trayāṇām cāpāni ciccheda viśikhaiḥ tribhiḥ te nikṛtta āyudhāḥ śūrāḥ nirviṣāḥ bhujagāḥ iva ratha śaktīḥ samutkṣipya bhṛśam siṃhāḥ iva anadan tāḥ bhuja agraiḥ mahā vegāḥ visṛṣṭāḥ bhujaga upamāḥ dīpyamānāḥ mahā śaktyaḥ jagmuḥ ādhirathim prati nanāda balavān karṇaḥ pārthāya visṛjan śarān arjunaḥ ca api rādheyam viddhvā sapta āśugaiḥ karṇāt avarajam bāṇaiḥ jaghāna niśitaiḥ tribhiḥ tatas śatruṃjayam hatvā pārthaḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ ajihmagaiḥ paśyatām dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām ekena eva kirīṭinā vara asinā karṇa pakṣān jaghāna daśa pañca ca punar sva ratham āsthāya dhanuḥ ādāya ca aparam vivyādha daśabhiḥ karṇam sūtam aśvān ca pañcabhiḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ api asi varam carma ca ādāya bhāsvaram jaghāna candravarmāṇam bṛhatkṣatram ca pauravam tatas sva ratham āsthāya pāñcālyaḥ anyat ca kārmukam ādāya karṇam vivyādha trisaptatyā nadan raṇe sūtaputram catuḥṣaṣṭyā viddhvā siṃhaḥ iva anadat bhallabhyām sādhu muktābhyām chittvā karṇasya kārmukam punar karṇam tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ bāhuvoḥ urasi ca arpayat nimajjamānam rādheyam ujjahruḥ sātyaka arṇavāt patti aśva ratha mātaṃgāḥ tvadīyāḥ śataśas apare karṇam eva abhyadhāvanta trāsyamānāḥ prahāriṇaḥ nakulaḥ sahadevaḥ ca sātyakim jugupuḥ raṇe evam eṣa mahā raudraḥ kṣaya artham sarva dhanvinām tāvakānām pareṣām ca tyaktvā prāṇān abhūt raṇaḥ padāti ratha nāga aśvaiḥ gaja aśva ratha pattayaḥ saṃsaktāḥ samadṛśyanta pattayaḥ ca api pattibhiḥ evam su kalilam yuddham āsīt kravyāda harṣaṇam mahadbhiḥ taiḥ abhītānām yama rāṣṭra vivardhanam kurūṇām pāṇḍavānām ca droṇa arjuna samāgame nirasta jihvā daśana īkṣaṇāḥ kṣitau kṣayam gatāḥ pramathita varma bhūṣaṇāḥ vipothitāḥ haya gaja pāda tāḍitāḥ bhṛśa ākulāḥ ratha khura nemibhiḥ hatāḥ pramodane śvāpada pakṣi rakṣasām jana kṣaye vartati tatra dāruṇe mahā balāḥ te kupitāḥ parasparam niṣūdayantaḥ praviceruḥ ojasā mahā indra sadma atithi tām yiyāsavaḥ uvāca rajasvalā bhṛśa udvignā vīkṣamāṇā diśaḥ daśa avahāram tatas kṛtvā bhāradvājasya saṃmate labdha lakṣyaiḥ paraiḥ dīnāḥ bhṛśa avahasitāḥ raṇe ślāghamāneṣu bhūteṣu phalgunasya amitān guṇān abhiśastāḥ iva abhūvan dhyāna mūka tvam āsthitāḥ nistejasaḥ vimanasaḥ nirvīryāḥ niṣparākramāḥ ye pradhānāḥ hatāḥ teṣām vairāgyam samupāśritāḥ na arjunaḥ ca samaḥ vīrye ślāghyamānāḥ punar punar rājānaḥ rāja putrāḥ ca sarve duryodhana ādayaḥ tatas duryodhanaḥ rājā droṇam dīnaḥ abhyabhāṣata praṇayāt abhimānāt ca dviṣat vṛddhyā ca durmanāḥ śṛṇvatām sarva bhūtānām saṃrabdhaḥ vākya kovidaḥ kṛpa karṇa mukha ādīnām praṇayāt niṣṭhuram vacaḥ tathā hi na agrahīḥ prāptam samīpe adya yudhiṣṭhiram jighṛkṣataḥ rakṣyamāṇaḥ sa amaraiḥ api pāṇḍavaiḥ varam dattvā mama prītaḥ paścāt vikṛtavān asi āśā bhaṅgam na kurvanti bhaktasya āryāḥ katham cana na arhase mā anyathā jñātum ghaṭamānam tava priye sa sura asura gandharvāḥ sa yakṣa uraga rākṣasāḥ na alam lokāḥ raṇe jetum pālyamānam kirīṭinā viśvasṛj yatra govindaḥ pṛtanāriḥ adya eṣām pravaram vīram pātayiṣye mahā ratham na hi ajñātam asādhyam vā tasya saṃkhye asti kim cana droṇena vyāhṛte tu evam saṃśaptaka gaṇāḥ punar āhvayan arjunam saṃkhye dakṣiṇām abhitas diśam tatra arjunasya atha paraiḥ sārdham samabhavat raṇaḥ tādṛśaḥ yādṛśaḥ na anyaḥ śrutaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ api vā kva cit sa kṛtvā duṣkaram karma hatvā vīrān sahasraśas mahā ratham śalya putram lakṣmaṇam ca te priyam ṣaṭsu vīreṣu saṃsaktaḥ dauḥśāsani vaśam gataḥ nihataḥ puruṣa vyāghraḥ putraḥ gāṇḍīvadhanvinaḥ saubhadraḥ pṛthivīpāla jahau prāṇān paraṃtapa vayam parama saṃhṛṣ pāṇḍavāḥ śoka karśitāḥ uvāca raṇe vinihatam śrutvā bhṛśam mama dīryate manaḥ dāruṇaḥ kṣatra dharmaḥ ayam vihitaḥ dharma kartṛbhiḥ yatra rājya īpsavaḥ śūrāḥ bāle śastram apātayan bibhitsatā ratha anīkam saubhadreṇa amita ojasā vikrīḍitam yathā saṃkhye tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya uvāca tat te kārtsnyena vakṣyāmi śṛṇu rājan samāhitaḥ vikrīḍitam kumāreṇa yathā anīkam bibhitsatā ārugṇāḥ ca yathā vīrāḥ duḥsādhyāḥ ca api viplave dāva agni abhiparītānām bhūri gulma tṛṇa drume vanaukasām iva araṇye tvadīyānām abhūt bhayam uvāca samare ati ugra karmāṇaḥ karmabhiḥ vyañjita śramāḥ sa kṛṣṇāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ pañca devaiḥ api durāsadāḥ sattva karma anvayaiḥ buddhyā prakṛtyā yaśasā śriyā na eva bhūtaḥ na bhavitā kṛṣṇa tulya guṇaḥ pumān sadā eva tridivam prāptaḥ rājā kila yudhiṣṭhiraḥ yuga ante ca antakaḥ rājan jāmadagnyaḥ ca vīryavān raṇa sthaḥ bhīmasenaḥ ca kathyante sadṛśāḥ trayaḥ pratijñā karma dakṣasya raṇe gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ upamām na adhigacchāmi pārthasya sadṛśīm kṣitau nakule aprātirūpyam ca śauryam ca niyatāni ṣaḍ śruta gāmbhīrya mādhurya sattva vīrya parākramaiḥ sadṛśaḥ devayoḥ vīraḥ sahadevaḥ kila aśvinoḥ ye ca kṛṣṇe guṇāḥ sphītāḥ pāṇḍaveṣu ca ye guṇāḥ abhimanyau kila ekasthāḥ dṛśyante guṇa saṃcayāḥ uvāca vaiśaṃpāyanaḥ abhimanyum hatam śrutvā dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ janeśvaraḥ uvāca mahantam bandhu nāśam te kathayiṣyāmi tat śṛṇu cakravyūhaḥ mahā rājaḥ ācāryeṇa abhikalpitaḥ tatra śakra upamāḥ sarve rājānaḥ viniveśitāḥ aṇu sthāneṣu vinyastāḥ kumārāḥ sūrya varcasaḥ kesarāṇi ca padmasya sukumārāṇi bhārata kumārāḥ rāja lokasya nikṣiptāḥ kesara upamāḥ saṃghātaḥ rāja putrāṇām sarveṣām abhavat tadā kṛta abhisamayāḥ sarve suvarṇa vikṛta dhvajāḥ rakta ambara dharāḥ sarve sarve rakta vibhūṣaṇāḥ te ratha aśva varāḥ sarve sarve rakta vibhūṣaṇāḥ candana aguru digdha aṅgāḥ sragviṇaḥ sūkṣma vāsasaḥ sahitāḥ paryadhāvanta kārṣṇim prati yuyutsavaḥ teṣām daśa sahasrāṇi babhūvuḥ dṛḍha dhanvinām karṇa duḥśāsana kṛpaiḥ vṛtaḥ rājā mahā rathaiḥ devarāja upamaḥ śrīmān śveta chatra abhisaṃvṛtaḥ sindhurājaḥ tathā atiṣṭhat śrīmān meruḥ iva acalaḥ sindhurājasya pārśva sthāḥ aśvatthāma purogamāḥ sutāḥ te mahā rāja triṃśat tridaśa saṃnibhāḥ gāndhāra rājaḥ kitavaḥ śalyaḥ bhūriśravāḥ tathā pārśvatas sindhurājasya vyarājanta mahā rathāḥ tāvakānām pareṣām ca mṛtyum kṛtvā nivartanam uvāca tat anīkam anādhṛṣyam bhāradvājena rakṣitam sātyakiḥ cekitānaḥ ca dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca pārṣataḥ ārjuniḥ kṣatradharmā ca bṛhatkṣatraḥ ca vīryavān cedipaḥ dhṛṣṭaketuḥ ca mādrī putrau ghaṭotkacaḥ yudhāmanyuḥ ca vikrāntaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca aparājitaḥ uttamaujāḥ ca durdharṣaḥ virāṭaḥ ca mahā rathaḥ draupadeyāḥ ca saṃrabdhāḥ śaiśupāliḥ ca vīryavān kekayāḥ ca mahā vīryāḥ sṛñjayāḥ ca sahasraśas ete ca anye ca sa gaṇāḥ kṛtāstrāḥ yuddha durmadāḥ samavetān tu tān sarvān bhāradvājaḥ api vīryavān asambhrāntaḥ śara ogheṇa mahatā samavārayat droṇam te na abhyavartanta velām iva jalāśayāḥ pīḍyamānāḥ śaraiḥ rājan droṇa cāpa viniḥsṛtaiḥ na śekuḥ pramukhe sthātum bhāradvājasya pāṇḍavāḥ yat enam na abhyavartanta pāñcālāḥ sṛñjayaiḥ saha tam āyāntam abhikruddham droṇam dṛṣṭvā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ bahudhā cintayām āsa droṇasya prativāraṇam aśakyam tu tam anyena droṇam matvā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ aviṣahyam gurum bhāram saubhadre samavāsṛjat tvam vā arjunaḥ vā kṛṣṇaḥ vā bhindyāt pradyumnaḥ eva vā abhimanyo varam tāta yācatām dātum arhasi pitṝṇām mātulānām ca sainyānām ca eva sarvaśas kṣipram astram samādāya droṇa anīkam viśātaya śṛṇu rājñ mahā bāho vacanam mama suvrata mukhāt kṛṣṇasya rāja indra śrutam asmi mayā prabho tasmāt vyūham praviśyāmi cakra ākhyam nṛpa sattama pitṝṇām jayam ākāṅkṣan avagāhe bhinadmi ca uvāca bhindhi anīkam yudhā śreṣṭha dvāram saṃjanayasva naḥ vayam tvā anugamiṣyāmaḥ yena tvam tāta yāsyasi dhanaṃjaya samam yuddhe tvām vayam tāta saṃyuge praṇidhāya anuyāsyāmaḥ rakṣantaḥ sarvatomukhāḥ uvāca aham tvā anugamiṣyāmi dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ atha sātyakiḥ pāñcālāḥ kekayāḥ matsyāḥ tathā sarve prabhadrakāḥ sakṛt bhinnam tvayā vyūham tatra tatra punar punar vayam pradhvaṃsayiṣyāmaḥ nighnamānāḥ varān varān yātaḥ aham arjunāt rājan subhadrāyām tathā eva ca mahā balena saṃpūrṇam paśyadhvam pauruṣam mama sarvān haniṣyāmi kurūn droṇa mukhyān narādhipa yaiḥ kṛtam duṣkṛtam karma pāṇḍavānām mahātmanām jyeṣṭhā mātā madīyā yat sabhām nītā durāsadaiḥ duḥśāsanena ca tadā pāpena duṣṭa karmaṇā pāñcālām prati rāja indra yat kṛtam duṣṭa kāribhiḥ tat sarvam ca adya tad vyūhe darśayiṣyāmi lāghavāt aham etat pravekṣyāmi droṇa anīkam durāsadam tat karma adya kariṣyāmi hitam yat vaṃśayoḥ dvayoḥ śiśunā ekena saṃgrāme kālyamānāni saṃghaśas na aham pārthena jātaḥ syām na ca jātaḥ subhadrayā uvāca evam te bhāṣamāṇasya balam saubhadra vardhatām rakṣitam puruṣa vyāghraiḥ mahā iṣvāsaiḥ prahāribhiḥ uvāca sumitra aśvān raṇe kṣipram droṇa anīkāya codaya uvāca acodayata yantāram droṇa anīkāya bhārata tena saṃcodyamānaḥ tu yāhi yāhi iti sārathiḥ atibhāraḥ ayam āyuṣman āhitaḥ tvayi pāṇḍavaiḥ ācāryaḥ hi kṛtī droṇaḥ parama astre kṛta śramaḥ droṇaḥ hi kṛtavan yatnam śastra astra kṛta niśramaḥ tvam tu bālaḥ sa balavān saṃgrāmāṇām akovidaḥ sārathe kaḥ nu ayam droṇaḥ samagram kṣatram eva vā airāvata gatam śakram saha amara gaṇaiḥ aham athavā rudram īśānam sarva bhūta gaṇaiḥ vṛtam na mama etat dviṣat sainyam kalām arhati ṣoḍaśīm evam api ucyamānaḥ sa sārathiḥ tam punar punar api viśvajitam viṣṇum mātulam prāpya sūtaja pitaram ca arjunam saṃkhye na bhī mām upayāsyati tatas abhimanyuḥ tām vācam kadarthīkṛtya sāratheḥ yāhi iti eva abravīt enam droṇa anīkāya māciram tatas saṃcodayām āsa hayān asya tri hāyanān na ati hṛṣṭa manāḥ sūtaḥ hema bhāṇḍa paricchadān te preṣitāḥ sumitreṇa droṇa anīkāya vājinaḥ tam udīkṣya tathā āyāntam sarve droṇa purogamāḥ abhyavartanta kauravyāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ ca tam anvayuḥ yuyutsayā droṇa mukhān mahā rathān samāsadat siṃha śiśuḥ yathā gajān te viṃśati pade yattāḥ saṃprahāram pracakrire āsīt gāṅgaḥ iva āvartaḥ muhūrtam udadheḥ iva śūrāṇām yudhyamānānām nighnatām itaretaram saṃgrāmaḥ tumulaḥ rājan prāvartata su dāruṇaḥ droṇasya miṣataḥ vyūham bhittvā prāviśat ārjuniḥ tat abhedyam anādhṛṣyam droṇa anīkam su durjayam tam praviṣṭam parān ghnantam śatru madhye mahā balam nānā vāditra ninadaiḥ kṣveḍita utkruṣṭa garjitaiḥ huṃkāraiḥ siṃhanādaiḥ ca tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti nisvanaiḥ ghoraiḥ halahalā śabdaiḥ mā gāḥ tiṣṭha ehi mām iti bṛṃhitaiḥ śiñjitaiḥ hāsaiḥ khura nemi svanaiḥ api teṣām āpatatām vīraḥ pūrvam śīghram atho dṛḍham te hanyamānāḥ ca tathā nānā liṅgaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ tatas teṣām śarīraiḥ ca śarīra avayavaiḥ ca saḥ saṃtastāra kṣitim kṣipram kuśaiḥ vedim iva adhvare baddha godhā aṅguli trāṇān sa śarāvara kārmukān sa asi carma aṅkuśa abhīśūn sa tomara paraśvadhān sa guḍa ayomukha prāsān sa ṛṣṭi tomara paṭṭiśān sa bhindipāla parighān sa śakti vara kampanān sa mudgara kṣepaṇīyān sa pāśa parigha upalān sa keyūra aṅgadān bāhūn hṛdya gandha anulepanān saṃciccheda ārjuniḥ vṛttān tvadīyānām sahasraśas taiḥ sphuradbhiḥ mahā rāja śuśubhe lohita ukṣitaiḥ pañcāsyaiḥ pannagaiḥ chinnaiḥ garuḍena iva māriṣa su nāsā ānana keśāntaiḥ avraṇaiḥ cāru kuṇḍalaiḥ saṃdaṣṭa oṣṭha puṭaiḥ krodhāt kṣaradbhiḥ śoṇitam bahu cāru sraj mukuṭa uṣṇīṣaiḥ maṇi ratna virājitaiḥ vināla nalina ākāraiḥ divākara śaśi prabhaiḥ dviṣat śirobhiḥ pṛthivīm avatastāra phālguniḥ samāsthitān yodha varaiḥ dānta aśvān sādhu sārathīn vipatākā dhvaja chattrān vitūṇīra āyudhān api visūta aśva ratha abhīśūn viśamya āyoktra daṇḍakān vīṣāmukhān vitriveṇūn vyasta daṇḍaka bandhurān vijaṅgha kūbara akṣān ca vinemīn anarān api praśātita upakaraṇān hata yodhān sahasraśas śaraiḥ viśakalīkurvan dikṣu sarvāsu adṛśyata tūṇān varmāṇi atho kakṣyāḥ graiveyān atha kambalān ghaṇṭāḥ śuṇḍān viṣāṇa agrān kṣura pālān padānugān śaraiḥ niśita dhārā agraiḥ śātravāṇām aśātayat vanāyu jān pārvatīyān kāmboja āraṭṭa bāhlikān sthira vāladhi karṇa akṣān javanān sādhu vāhinaḥ su ārūḍhān śikṣitaiḥ yodhaiḥ śakti ṛṣṭi prāsa yodhibhiḥ vidhvasta cāmara kuthān viprakīrṇa prakīrṇakān nirasta jihvā nayanān niṣkīrṇa antra yakṛt ghanān hata ārohān bhinna bhāṇḍān kravyāda gaṇa modanān nikṛtta varma kavacān śakṛt mūtra asṛj āplutān nipātayan aśva varān tāvakān saḥ abhyarocata ekaḥ viṣṇuḥ iva acintyaḥ kṛtvā prāk karma duṣkaram kṛtvā karma raṇe asahyam paraiḥ ārjuniḥ āhave evam ekena tām senām saubhadreṇa śitaiḥ śaraiḥ bhṛśam viprahatām dṛṣṭvā skandena iva āsurīm camūm tvadīyāḥ tava putrāḥ ca vīkṣamāṇāḥ diśaḥ daśa saṃśuṣka āsyāḥ calat netrāḥ prasvinnāḥ loma harṣaṇāḥ palāyana kṛta utsāhāḥ nirutsāhāḥ dviṣat jaye hatān putrān tathā pitṝn suhṛd saṃbandhi bāndhavān uvāca tām prabhagnām camūm dṛṣṭvā saubhadreṇa amita ojasā tatas rājānam āvṛttam saubhadram prati saṃyuge dṛṣṭvā droṇaḥ abravīt yodhān paryāpnuta narādhipam purā abhimanyuḥ lakṣyam naḥ paśyatām hanti vīryavān tam ādravata mā bhaiṣṭa kṣipram rakṣata kauravam saubhadraḥ ayam āyātaḥ asmān jetum mahā balaḥ tatas kṛtajñāḥ balinaḥ suhṛdaḥ jita kāśinaḥ trāsyamānāḥ bhayāt vīram parivavruḥ te ātmajam droṇaḥ drauṇiḥ kṛpaḥ karṇaḥ kṛtavarmā ca saubalaḥ bṛhadbalaḥ madra rājaḥ bhūriḥ bhūriśravāḥ śalaḥ pauravaḥ vṛṣasenaḥ ca visṛjantaḥ śitān śarān saubhadram śara varṣeṇa mahatā samavākiran āsyāt grāsam iva ākṣiptam mamṛṣe na arjuna ātmajaḥ tān śara ogheṇa mahatā sa aśva sūtān mahā rathān tasya nādam tatas śrutvā siṃhasya iva āmiṣa eṣiṇaḥ na amṛṣyanta su saṃrabdhāḥ punar droṇa mukhāḥ rathāḥ te enam koṣṭhakīkṛtya ratha vaṃśena māriṣa vyasṛjan iṣu jālāni nānā liṅgāni saṃghaśas tatas rathāḥ padāti oghāḥ kuñjarāḥ sādinaḥ ca ha tatas te kopitāḥ tena śaraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ śūrāṇām yudhyamānānām nighnatām itaretaram abhimanyoḥ pareṣām ca na āsīt kaḥ cit parāṅmukhaḥ duḥśāsanaḥ dvādaśabhiḥ kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ tribhiḥ droṇaḥ tu saptadaśabhiḥ śaraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ viviṃśatiḥ tu viṃśatyā kṛtavarmā ca sapta bṛhadbalaḥ tathā aṣṭābhiḥ aśvatthāmā ca sapta bhūriśravāḥ tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ madra īśaḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ āśugaiḥ dvābhyām śarābhyām śakuniḥ tribhiḥ duryodhanaḥ nṛpaḥ nṛtyan iva mahā rāja cāpa hastaḥ pratāpavān abhyadravata tam kārṣṇim aśmaka indraḥ kṛta tvaraḥ dāntaiḥ aśmaka dāyādam tvaramāṇaḥ abhyahārayat vivyādha ca enam daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ tiṣṭha iti ca bravīt tasya abhimanyuḥ daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ sūtam hayān dhvajam bāhū dhanuḥ śiraḥ ca urvyām smayamānaḥ abhyapātayat saṃcacāla balam sarvam palāyana parāyaṇam tatas karṇaḥ kṛpaḥ droṇaḥ drauṇiḥ gāndhāra rāj śalaḥ śalyaḥ bhūriśravāḥ krāthaḥ somadattaḥ viviṃśatiḥ vṛṣasenaḥ suṣeṇaḥ ca kuṇḍabhedī pratardanaḥ śaram ādatta karṇāya para kāya avabhedanam tasya bhittvā tanutrāṇam deham nirbhidya ca āśugaḥ prāviśat dharaṇīm rājan valmīkam iva pannagaḥ saṃcacāla raṇe karṇaḥ kṣiti kampe yathā acalaḥ atha anyaiḥ niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ suṣeṇam dīrgha locanam karṇaḥ tam pañcaviṃśatyā nārācānām samarpayat aśvatthāmā ca viṃśatyā kṛtavarmā ca sapta sa śara ardita sarva aṅgaḥ kruddhaḥ śakrātmaja ātmajaḥ vicaran dṛśyate sainye pāśa hastaḥ iva antakaḥ śalyam ca bāṇa varṣeṇa samīpa stham avākirat udakrośat mahā bāhuḥ tava sainyāni bhīṣayan tam hi viddham tathā dṛṣṭvā saubhadreṇa yaśasvinā saṃprādravat camūḥ sarvā bhāradvājasya paśyataḥ prekṣantaḥ tam mahā bāhum rukma puṅkhaiḥ samāvṛtam tvadīyāḥ ca palāyante mṛgāḥ siṃha arditāḥ iva ekaḥ anekān jaghāna āśu prāṇinām antakaḥ yathā kālāgni sadṛśaḥ vīrye mātariśvā iva vai jave yudhyamānaḥ mahā bāhuḥ śakra tulya parākramaḥ jaghāna samare sarvān nānā śastra viśāradān iti iva teṣām samare mahātmā pratāpavān nītivatām variṣṭhaḥ cakāra sarvān iṣubhiḥ pradagdhān saubhadra śara nirbhiṇṇāḥ samare amara vikramāḥ sa tu raṇa yaśasā abhipūjyamānaḥ pitṛ sura cāraṇa siddha yakṣa saṃghaiḥ uvāca tathā pramathamānam tam mahā iṣvāsam ajihmagaiḥ ārjunim māmakāḥ sarve ke tu enam samavākiran uvāca śṛṇu rājan kumārasya raṇe vikrīḍitam mahat madra īśam sāditam dṛṣṭvā saubhādreṇa āśugaiḥ raṇe śalyāt avarajaḥ kruddhaḥ kiran bāṇān samabhyayāt sa viddhvā daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ sa aśva yantāram ārjunim udakrośat mahā śabdam tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt tasya ārjuniḥ śiraḥ grīvam pāṇi pādam dhanuḥ hayān chatram dhvajam niyantāram triveṇum śamī upaskaram cakre yuga īṣām tūṇīrān anukarṣam ca sāyakaiḥ patākām cakragoptārau sarva upakaraṇāni ca sa papāta kṣitau kṣīṇaḥ praviddha ābharaṇa ambaraḥ anugāḥ ca asya vitrastāḥ prādravan sarvatodiśam ārjuneḥ karma tat dṛṣṭvā praṇeduḥ ca samantataḥ nādena sarva bhūtāni sādhu sādhu iti bhārata śalya bhrātari atha ārugṇe bahuśas tasya sainikāḥ kula adhivāsa nāmāni śrāvayantaḥ arjuna ātmajam rathaiḥ aśvaiḥ gajaiḥ ca anye pādātaiḥ ca bala utkaṭāḥ huṃkāraiḥ kṣveḍita utkruṣṭaiḥ siṃhanādaiḥ sa garjitaiḥ tān tathā bruvataḥ dṛṣṭvā saubhadraḥ prahasan iva yaḥ yaḥ sma prāharat pūrvam tam tam vivyādha pattribhiḥ saṃdarśayiṣyan astrāṇi citrāṇi ca laghūni ca ārjuniḥ samare śūraḥ mṛdu pūrvam ayudhyata vāsudevāt upāttam yat yat astram ca dhanaṃjayāt adarśayata tat kārṣṇiḥ kṛṣṇābhyām aviśeṣayan dūram asyan gurum bhāram sādhayan ca punar punar saṃdadhat visṛjan ca iṣūn nirviśeṣam adṛśyata cāpa maṇḍalam eva asya visphurat dikṣu adṛśyata jyā śabdaḥ śuśruve tasya tala śabdaḥ ca dāruṇaḥ hrīmān amarṣī saubhadraḥ māna kṛt priya darśanaḥ saṃmimānayiṣuḥ vīrān iṣvāsān ca api ayudhyata mṛduḥ bhūtvā mahā rāja dāruṇaḥ samapadyata varṣa abhyatītaḥ bhagavān śaradi iva divākaraḥ śarān vicitrān mahataḥ rukma puṅkhān śilā śitān kṣurapraiḥ vatsadantaiḥ ca vipāṭhaiḥ ca mahā yaśāḥ tān tathā dravataḥ dṛṣṭvā saubhadraḥ prahasan iva avākirat ratha anīkam bhāradvājasya paśyataḥ uvāca dvaidhībhavati me cittam hriyā tuṣṭyā ca saṃjaya vistareṇa eva me śaṃsa sarvam gāvalgaṇe punar uvāca ekasya ca bahūnām ca yathā āsīt tumulaḥ raṇaḥ abhimanyuḥ kṛta utsāhaḥ kṛta utsāhān ariṃdamān droṇam karṇam kṛpam śalyam drauṇim bhojam bṛhadbalam nānā nṛpān nṛpa sutān sainyāni vividhāni ca alāta cakra vat sarvān caran bāṇaiḥ samabhyayāt tat dṛṣṭvā caritam tasya saubhadrasya amita ojasaḥ atha abravīt mahā prājñaḥ bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān harṣeṇa utphulla nayanaḥ kṛpam ābhāṣya sa tvaram ghaṭṭayan iva marmāṇi te putrasya māriṣa abhimanyum raṇe dṛṣṭvā tadā raṇa viśāradam nandayan suhṛdaḥ sarvān rājānam ca yudhiṣṭhiram nakulam sahadevam ca bhīmasenam ca pāṇḍavam bandhūn saṃbandhinaḥ ca anyān madhyasthān suhṛdaḥ tathā droṇasya prīti saṃyuktam śrutvā vākyam te ātmajaḥ ārjunim prati saṃkruddhaḥ droṇam dṛṣṭvā smayan iva duḥsāsanam madra rājam tān tān ca anyān mahā rathān sarva mūrdhāvasiktānām ācāryaḥ brahma vittamaḥ tasmāt saṃpaśyataḥ tasya droṇa ācāryasya dhīmataḥ arjunasya sutam tu eṣa śiṣya tvāt abhirakṣati putrāḥ śiṣyāḥ ca dayitāḥ tat apatyam ca dharmiṇām saṃrakṣyamāṇaḥ droṇena manyate vīryam ātmanaḥ ātma saṃbhāvitaḥ mūḍhaḥ tam pramathnīta māciram evam uktāḥ tu te rājñā sātvatīputram abhyayus saṃrabdhāḥ tam jighāṃsantaḥ bhāradvājasya paśyataḥ abravīt kuru śārdūlaḥ duryodhanam idam vacaḥ duḥśāsanaḥ tu saṃrabdham jñātvā bhrātaram agrajam aham enam haniṣyāmi mahā rāja bravīmi te miṣatām pāṇḍu putrāṇām pāñcālānām ca paśyatām utkruśya ca abravīt vākyam kuru rājam idam punar śrutvā kṛṣṇau mayā grastam saubhadram atimāninau gamiṣyataḥ preta lokam jīva lokāt na saṃśayaḥ tau ca śrutvā mṛtau vyaktam pāṇḍoḥ kṣetra udbhavāḥ sutāḥ eka ahnā sa suhṛd vargāḥ klaibyāt dhāsyanti jīvitam śivena dhyāhi mā rājan eṣa hanmi ripum te abhimanyuḥ śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ ṣaḍviṃśatyā samarpayat duḥśāsanaḥ tu saṃkruddhaḥ prabhinnaḥ iva kuñjaraḥ tau maṇḍalāni citrāṇi rathābhyām savya dakṣiṇam caramāṇau ayudhyetām ratha śikṣā viśāradau atha paṇava mṛdaṅga dundubhīnām kṛkara mahānaka bherī jharjharāṇām uvāca tasmin kāle mahā bāhuḥ saubhadraḥ para vīra hā sa śaram kārmukam chittvā lāghavena nyapātayat duḥśāsanam śaraiḥ ghoraiḥ saṃtatakṣa samantataḥ abhimanyuḥ smayan dhīmān duḥśāsanam atha abravīt diṣṭyā paśyāmi saṃgrāme māninam śatrum āgatam niṣṭhuram tyakta dharmāṇam ākrośana parāyaṇam yat sabhāyām tvayā rājñaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya śṛṇvataḥ akṣakūṭam samāśritya saubalasya bhavat balam śṛṇu mama vacanam tāta pitṛvyaḥ asi mahāmate sauhṛdam pṛṣṭhatas kṛtvā sarvaiḥ eva durātmabhiḥ bhuktam rājyam idam mūḍhaiḥ sarva dharma bahiṣkṛtaiḥ mithyābhūtam ca tat sarvam suhṛdbhiḥ varjitam tadā yūyam pāpiṣṭhāḥ pāpa vañcakāḥ teṣām tvam agraṇī pāpa yena sā drupada ātmajā ānītā ca sabhām sādhvī tasya idam karmaṇaḥ phalam darśayiṣyāmi sarveṣām kurūṇām ca durātmanām kopitaḥ paruṣaiḥ vākyaiḥ dharmarājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ akṣakūṭam samāśritya saubalena durātmanā pitṝṇām mama rājyasya haraṇasya ugra dhanvinām śāsitā asmi adya te bāṇaiḥ sarva sainyasya paśyataḥ amarṣitāyāḥ kṛṣṇāyāḥ kāṅkṣitasya ca me pituḥ evam uktvā mahā bāhuḥ bāṇam duḥśāsana antakam duḥśāsanaḥ mahā rāja kaśmalam ca āviśat mahat sārathiḥ tvaramāṇaḥ tu duḥśāsanam acetasam raṇa madhyāt apovāha saubhadra śara pīḍitam pāṇḍavāḥ draupadeyāḥ ca virāṭaḥ ca samīkṣya tam pāñcālāḥ kekayāḥ ca eva siṃhanādam atha anadan vāditrāṇi ca sarvāṇi nānā liṅgāni sarvaśas prāvādayanta saṃhṛṣṭāḥ pāṇḍūnām tatra sainikāḥ paśyantaḥ smayamānāḥ ca saubhadrasya viceṣṭitam atyanta vairiṇam dṛptam dṛṣṭvā śatrum parājitam dharma māruta śakrāṇām āśvinoḥ pratimāḥ tathā dhārayantaḥ dhvaja agreṣu draupadeyāḥ mahā rathāḥ sātyakiḥ cekitānaḥ ca dhṛṣṭadyumna śikhaṇḍinau kekayāḥ dhṛṣṭaketuḥ ca matsya pāñcāla sṛṃjayāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ ca mudā yuktāḥ yudhiṣṭhira purogamāḥ jayam ākāṅkṣamāṇānām śūrāṇām anivartinām paśya duḥśāsanam vīram abhimanyu vaśam gatam pratapantam iva ādityam nighnantam śātravān raṇe atha ca ete su saṃrabdhāḥ siṃhāḥ iva bala utkaṭāḥ saubhadram udyatāḥ trātum abhidhāvanti pāṇḍavāḥ enam vadhiṣyāmi ripum yathā vṛtram śacīpatiḥ evam uktvā tu rādheyaḥ ratha ārūḍhaḥ mahā rathaḥ yayau yoddhum mahā vīraḥ kurūṇām tatra paśyatām dhanuṣā pūryamāṇena maurvī guṇa vibhūṣiṇā śaraiḥ agni śikhā ākāraiḥ āśīviṣa sama prabhaiḥ tatas karṇaḥ śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ abhimanyum durāsadam tasya ca anucarān tīkṣṇaiḥ vivyādha parama iṣubhiḥ avajñā pūrvakam vīraḥ saubhadrasya raṇa ajire tam tadā na aśakat kaḥ cit droṇāt vārayitum raṇe ārujantam ratha śreṣṭhān vajrahastam iva asurān saubhadram śataśas avidhyat uttama astrāṇi darśayan saḥ astraiḥ astra vidām śreṣṭhaḥ rāma śiṣyaḥ pratāpavān sa tathā pīḍyamānaḥ tu rādheyena astra vṛṣṭibhiḥ samare amara saṃkāśaḥ saubhadraḥ na vyaṣīdata tatas śilā śitaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ bhallaiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ chittvā dhanūṃṣi śūrāṇām ārjuniḥ karṇam ārdayat dhanuḥ maṇḍala nirmuktaiḥ śaraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ karṇaḥ api ca asya cikṣepa bāṇān saṃnata parvṇaḥ asambhrāntaḥ ca tān sarvān agṛhṇāt phalguna ātmajaḥ tatas muhūrtāt karṇasya bāṇena ekena vīryavān tasmai cikṣepa niśitam śaram parama saṃhitam sa dhvajam kārmukam ca asya chittvā bhūmau nyapātayat tatas kṛcchra gatam karṇam dṛṣṭvā karṇāt anantaraḥ saubhadram abhyayāt tūrṇam dṛḍham udyamya kārmukam tatas uccukruśuḥ pārthāḥ teṣām ca anucarāḥ janāḥ vāditrāṇi ca saṃjaghnuḥ saubhadram ca api tuṣṭuvuḥ uvāca saḥ abhigarjan dhanuṣpāṇiḥ jyām vikarṣan punar punar pitṛpaitāmaham karma kurvāṇam atimānuṣam dṛṣṭvā arditam śaraiḥ kārṣṇim tvadīyāḥ hṛṣitāḥ abhavan śiraḥ pracyāvayām āsa sa rathāt prāpatat bhuvi karṇikāram iva uddhūtam vātena mathitam nagāt karṇa anujam ca saṃprekṣya tāvakāḥ vyathitāḥ abhavan bhrātaram nihatam dṛṣṭvā rājñ karṇaḥ vyathām yayau punar karṇam pravivyādha śaraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ vivyādha daśabhiḥ śūraḥ abhimanyum mahā balam rādheyam viratham kṛtvā saubhadraḥ vākyam abravīt bhṛtyaḥ asi sūtaputraḥ asi baiḍālavratikaḥ sadā pāṇḍavaiḥ saha paiśunyam nitya tvam kṛtavān asi sabhām nītvā ca pāñcālī vivastrā kāritā tvayā tad tad rūpāṇi anekāni vāsāṃsi su bahūni ca dṛṣṭāni tatra yuṣmābhiḥ kurubhiḥ ca durātmabhiḥ yuṣmābhiḥ ca kṛtaḥ adya eva cakra vyūhaḥ durātmabhiḥ kulīnāḥ ye ca rājānaḥ dharmiṣṭhāḥ satya saṃgarāḥ cakra ākhyam ca na kurvanti vyūham pāpiṣṭha kāritam krauñcāḥ suparṇāḥ haṃsāhvāḥ musalāḥ gāruḍāḥ tathā ete vyūhāḥ ca śūrāṇām dharmiṣṭhānām mahātmanām yūyam daitya aṃśa saṃbhūtāḥ sarve tatra na saṃśayaḥ iti evam uktvā sa tadā mahātmā karṇam subhadrā tanayaḥ mahā balaḥ mahā balaḥ satyavatām variṣṭhaḥ vimukhīkṛtya karṇam tu saubhadraḥ kaṅka pattribhiḥ anyān api mahā iṣvāsān tūrṇam eva abhidudruve jhaṣaḥ kruddhaḥ iva abhindat abhimanyuḥ mahā yaśāḥ tiṣṭha karṇa mahā iṣvāsa kṛpa duryodhana iti ca śalabhaiḥ iva ca ākāśe dhārābhiḥ iva ca āvṛte abhimanyoḥ śaraiḥ rājan na prājñāyata kim cana tāvakānām tu yodhānām vadhyatām niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ saubhadraḥ tu tatas śaṅkham pradhmāpya puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ śīghram abhyapatat senām bhāratām bharata ṛṣabha sa kakṣe agniḥ iva utsṛṣṭaḥ nirdahan tarasā ripūn ratha nāga aśva manujān ardayan niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ sa praviśya akarot bhūmim kabandha gaṇa saṃkulām svān eva abhimukhān ghnantaḥ prādravan jīvita arthinaḥ te ghorāḥ raudra karmāṇaḥ vipāṭhāḥ pṛthavaḥ śitāḥ nighnantaḥ ratha nāga aśvān jagmuḥ āśu vasuṃdharām sa āyudhāḥ sa aṅguli trāṇāḥ sa khaḍgāḥ sa aṅgadāḥ raṇe dṛśyante bāhavaḥ chinnāḥ hema ābharaṇa bhūṣitāḥ śarāḥ cāpāni khaḍgāḥ ca śarīrāṇi śirāṃsi ca sa kuṇḍalāni sragvīṇi bhūmau āsan sahasraśas apaskaraiḥ adhiṣṭhānaiḥ īṣā daṇḍaka bandhuraiḥ śakti cāpa āyudhaiḥ ca api patitaiḥ ca mahā dhvajaiḥ carma cāpa dharaiḥ ca api vyavakīrṇaiḥ samantataḥ nihataiḥ kṣatriyaiḥ aśvaiḥ vāraṇaiḥ ca viśām pate agamya kalpā pṛthivī kṣaṇena āsīt su dāruṇā vadhyatām rāja putrāṇām krandatām itaretaram prādurāsīt mahā śabdaḥ bhīrūṇām bhaya vardhanaḥ sa śabdaḥ bharata śreṣṭha diśaḥ sarvāḥ vyanādayat vyacarat sa diśaḥ sarvāḥ pradiśaḥ ca āhitān rujan tam tadā na anupaśyāma sainyena rajasā āvṛtam ādadānam gaja aśvānām nṛṇām ca āyūṃṣi bhārata kṣaṇena bhūyas apaśyāma sūryam madhyaṃdine yathā abhimanyum mahā rāja pratapantam dviṣat gaṇān sa vāsava samaḥ saṃkhye vāsavasya ātmaja ātmajaḥ yathā purā vahni sutaḥ sura sainyeṣu vīryavān uvāca gāhamānam anīkāni sat aśvaiḥ tam tri hāyanaiḥ uvāca yudhiṣṭhiraḥ bhīmasenaḥ śikhaṇḍī sātyakiḥ yamau dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ virāṭaḥ ca drupadaḥ ca sa kekayaḥ dhṛṣṭaketuḥ ca saṃrabdhaḥ matsyāḥ ca anvapatan raṇe tena eva tu pathā yātāḥ pitaraḥ mātulaiḥ saha abhyadravan parīpsantaḥ vyūḍha anīkāḥ prahāriṇaḥ tān dṛṣṭvā dravataḥ śūrān tvadīyāḥ vimukhāḥ abhavan jāmātā tava tejasvī viṣṭambhayiṣuḥ ādravat vārddhakṣatriḥ upāsedhat pravaṇāt iva kuñjarān uvāca yat ekaḥ pāṇḍavān kruddhān putra gṛddhīn avārayat tat asya brūhi me vīryam karma ca agryam mahātmanaḥ kim dattam hutam iṣṭam vā su taptam atha vā tapaḥ devam katamam ārādhya viṣṇum īśānam agni jam na evam kṛtam mahat karma tathā uvāca mānāt sa taptavān rājā vara arthī su mahat tapaḥ indriyāṇi indriya arthebhyaḥ priyebhyaḥ saṃnivartya saḥ kṣudh pipāsā ātapa sahaḥ kṛśaḥ dhamani saṃtataḥ uvāca praṇataḥ rudram prāñjaliḥ niyata ātmavān pāṇḍaveyān aham saṃkhye bhīma vīrya parākramān sa tu vavre varam tatra pāṇḍaveyān aham raṇe viṣṇu sahasra mūrdhānam sa kṛṣṇaḥ pāti phālgunam dhārayiṣyasi saṃgrāme caturaḥ pāṇḍu nandanān eka aham iti rāja indra tatra eva adarśanam gataḥ ekaḥ saṃdhārayām āsa pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm tasya jyā tala ghoṣeṇa kṣatriyān bhayam āviśat dṛṣṭvā tu kṣatriyāḥ bhāram saindhave sarvam arpitam uvāca śṛṇu tat sarvam ākhyāsye yathā pāṇḍūn ayodhayat tam ūhuḥ sāratheḥ vaśyāḥ saindhavāḥ sādhu vāhinaḥ vikurvāṇāḥ bṛhantaḥ aśvāḥ śvasana upama raṃhasaḥ tasya abhyaśobhayat ketuḥ vārāhaḥ rājataḥ mahān sa visphārya mahat cāpam kiran iṣu gaṇān bahūn tat khaṇḍam pūrayām āsa yat vyadārayat ārjuniḥ sa sātyakim tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ aṣṭabhiḥ ca vṛkodaram dhṛṣṭadyumnam tathā ṣaṣṭyā virāṭam daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ drupadam pañcabhiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ daśabhiḥ ca śikhaṇḍinam kekayān pañcaviṃśatyā draupadeyān tribhiḥ tribhiḥ yudhiṣṭhiram ca saptatyā tatas śeṣān apānudat atha asya śita pītena bhallena ādiśya kārmukam akṣṇoḥ nimeṣa mātreṇa saḥ anyat ādāya kārmukam vivyādha daśabhiḥ pārtha tān ca eva anyān tribhiḥ tribhiḥ tasya tat lāghavam jñātvā bhīmaḥ bhallaiḥ tribhiḥ punar saḥ anyat ādāya balavān sajyam kṛtvā ca kārmukam bhīmasya apothayat ketum dhanuḥ aśvān ca māriṣa tatas tvadīyāḥ saṃhṛṣṭāḥ sādhu sādhu iti cukruśuḥ vivyadhuḥ śara varṣeṇa samantāt nṛpa sattamāḥ saṃchādyamānaḥ bahubhiḥ pāṇḍavānām mahā rathaiḥ chittvā ca tān śarān rājan śara varṣaiḥ pṛthagvidhaiḥ chādayām āsa tān sarvān tat abhūt roma harṣaṇam saṃkruddhān pāṇḍavān ekaḥ yat dadhāra astra tejasā pāṇḍūnām darśitaḥ pathī saindhavena nivāritaḥ yatamānāḥ tu te vīrāḥ matsya pāñcāla kekayāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ ca anvapadyanta pratyaikaśyena saindhavam yaḥ yaḥ hi yatate bhettum droṇa anīkam tava ahitaḥ uvāca saindhavena niruddheṣu jaya gṛddhiṣu pāṇḍuṣu praviśya tu ārjuniḥ senām satya saṃdhaḥ durāsadām vyakṣobhayata tejasvī makaraḥ sāgaram yathā tam tathā śara varṣeṇa kṣobhayantam ariṃdamam yathā pradhānāḥ saubhadram abhyayus kuru sattamāḥ teṣām tasya ca saṃmardaḥ dāruṇaḥ samapadyata sṛjatām śara varṣāṇi prasaktam amita ojasām tasya vivyādha balavān śaraiḥ aśvān ajihmagaiḥ vātāyamānaiḥ atha taiḥ aśvaiḥ apahṛtaḥ raṇāt ratha vrajāḥ tatas hṛṣṭāḥ sādhu sādhu iti cukruśuḥ ārāt āyāntam abhyetya vasātīyaḥ abhyayāt drutam saḥ abhimanyum śaraiḥ ṣaṣṭyā rukma puṅkhaiḥ avākirat tam ayasmaya varmāṇam iṣuṇā āśu pātinā nihatam dṛṣṭvā kruddhāḥ kṣatriya puṃgavāḥ parivavruḥ tadā rājan tava pautram jighāṃsavaḥ visphārayantaḥ cāpāni nānā rūpāṇi anekaśas teṣām śarān sa iṣvasanān śarīrāṇi śirāṃsi ca sa kuṇḍalāni sragvīṇi kruddhaḥ ciccheda phālguniḥ sa khaḍgāḥ sa aṅguli trāṇāḥ sa paṭṭiśa paraśvadhāḥ adṛśyanta bhujāḥ chinnāḥ hema ābharaṇa bhūṣitāḥ apaskaraiḥ adhiṣṭhānaiḥ īṣā daṇḍaka bandhuraiḥ anukarṣaiḥ patākābhiḥ tathā sārathi vājibhiḥ rathaiḥ ca bhagnaiḥ nāgaiḥ ca hataiḥ kīrṇā abhavat mahī nihataiḥ kṣatriyaiḥ śūraiḥ nānā janapada īśvaraiḥ jaya gṛddhaiḥ vṛtā bhūmiḥ dāruṇā samapadyata kāñcanam yat yat asya āsīt varma ca ābharaṇāni ca dhanuṣaḥ ca śarāṇām ca tat apaśyāma kevalam tam tadā na aśakat kaḥ cit cakṣurbhyām abhivīkṣitum uvāca ādadānaḥ tu śūrāṇām āyūṃṣi abhavat ārjuniḥ antakaḥ sarva bhūtānām prāṇān kāle iva āgate sa śakraḥ iva vikrāntaḥ śakra sūnoḥ sutaḥ balī satyaśravasi ca ākṣipte tvaramāṇāḥ mahā rathāḥ aham pūrvam aham pūrvam iti kṣatriya puṃgavāḥ spardhamānāḥ samājagmuḥ jighāṃsantaḥ arjuna ātmajam kṣatriyāṇām anīkāni pradrutāni abhidhāvatām jagrāsa timiḥ āsādya kṣudra matsyān iva arṇave mahā grāha gṛhītā iva vāta vega bhaya arditā samakampata sā senā vibhraṣṭā nauḥ iva arṇave saṃtrastā vāhinī te nauḥ iva āsīt mahā arṇave trastām āśvāsayan senām atrastaḥ vākyam abravīt alam trāseṇa vaḥ śūrāḥ na eṣa kaḥ cit mayi sthite aham enam grahīṣyāmi jīva grāham na saṃśayaḥ sa tasya iṣvasanam chittvā phālguṇiḥ savya dakṣiṇau dṛṣṭvā rukmaratham rugṇam putram śalyasya māninam jīva grāham jighṛkṣantam saubhadreṇa yaśasvinā saṃgrāma durmadāḥ rājan rāja putrāḥ prahāriṇaḥ vayasyāḥ śalya putrasya suvarṇa vikṛta dhvajāḥ tāla mātrāṇi cāpāni vikarṣantaḥ mahā rathāḥ ārjunim śara varṣeṇa samantāt paryavārayan śūraiḥ śikṣā bala upetaiḥ taruṇaiḥ ati amarṣaṇaiḥ dṛṣṭvā ekam samare śūram saubhadram aparājitam chādyamānam śara vrātaiḥ hṛṣṭaḥ duryodhanaḥ abhavat adṛśyam ārjunim cakruḥ nimeṣāt te nṛpa ātmajāḥ sa sūta aśva dhvajam tasya syandanam tam ca māriṣa ācitam samapaśyāma śvāvidham śalalaiḥ iva ekaḥ sa śatadhā rājan dṛśyate sma sahasradhā bibheda śatadhā rājñ śarīrāṇi mahīkṣitām bhinna anīkāḥ ca diś mūḍhāḥ bhūyas saṃtrasta cetasaḥ prāṇāḥ prāṇabhṛtām saṃkhye preṣitāḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ rājan prāpuḥ amum lokam śarīrāṇi avanim yayuḥ dhanūṃṣi aśvān niyantṝn ca dhvajān bāhūn ca sa aṅgadān śirāṃsi ca śitaiḥ bhallaiḥ teṣām ciccheda phālguniḥ cūta ārāmaḥ yathā bhagnaḥ pañca varṣa phala upagaḥ kruddha āśīviṣa saṃkāśān su kumārān sukha ucitān ekena nihatān dṛṣṭvā bhītaḥ duryodhanaḥ abhavat rathinaḥ kuñjarān aśvān padātīn ca avamarditān dṛṣṭvā duryodhanaḥ kṣipram upāyāt tam amarṣitaḥ tayoḥ kṣaṇam iva āpūrṇaḥ saṃgrāmaḥ samapadyata atha abhavat te vimukhaḥ putraḥ śara śata arditaḥ uvāca saṃgrāmam tumulam ghoram jayam ca eva mahātmanaḥ kim tu na ati adbhutam teṣām yeṣām dharmaḥ vyapāśrayaḥ mūlam hi sarva dharmāṇām daivatam svarga vāsinām sa kṛṣṇaḥ daivatam yeṣām kim teṣām duḥkha sambhavaḥ karmaṇām pratipanne arthe kālena pariṇāmite kā cintā mahatī bhūpa cintayā bādhyate jaḍaḥ kriyā upakramitaḥ pūrvam pariṇāma dṛśaḥ sukham tyāgam vinā mahā rāja samādhānam na vidyate bhavān tad rahitaḥ rājan śṛṇuṣva ācarite phalam uvāca tāvakāḥ te putrāḥ ca vīkṣamāṇāḥ parasparam saṃśuṣka āsyāḥ calat netrāḥ prasvinnāḥ loma harṣiṇaḥ palāyana kṛta utsāhāḥ nirutsāhāḥ dviṣat jaye hatān bhrātṝn pitṝn putrān suhṛd saṃbandhi bāndhavān tān prabhagnān tathā dṛṣṭvā droṇaḥ drauṇiḥ bṛhadbalaḥ kṛpaḥ duryodhanaḥ karṇaḥ kṛtavarmā atha saubalaḥ tathā vinihatām dṛṣṭvā te senām anātha vat te api pautreṇa te rājan prāyaśas vimukhīkṛtāḥ tam te abhiṣiṣicuḥ bāṇaiḥ meghāḥ girim iva ambuṣu pautram tu tava durdharṣam lakṣmaṇam priya darśanam pituḥ samīpe tiṣṭhantam śūram udyata kārmukam āsasāda raṇe kārṣṇiḥ mattaḥ mattam iva dvipam abravīt lakṣmaṇaḥ kruddham ārjunim paramām āstra vid śṛṇu vākyam mahā bāho abhimanyo mahā bala gaccha tvam pāṇḍavān śīghram mā yuddham kuru suvrata gamiṣyāmi ciram bhrātar sarvān etān nihatya vai pāṇḍavān prati ca adya eva iti satyam vadāmi te siṃha śāvaḥ vane yadvat puṇḍarīka śiśum yathā śaraiḥ su niśitaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ bāhuvoḥ urasi ca arpitaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ vai mahā bāhuḥ daṇḍa āhataḥ iva uragaḥ su dṛṣṭaḥ kriyatām lokaḥ amum lokam gamiṣyasi paśyatām bāndhavānām tvām nayāmi yama sādanam tasya ca atikramam dṛṣṭvā lakṣmaṇaḥ yuddha kovidaḥ tayoḥ yuddham atīva āsīt budha aṅgārakayoḥ iva lakṣmaṇaḥ niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ daśabhiḥ ca stanāntare pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ nijaghne ratha vājinaḥ sārathim iṣuṇā ekena dhvajam ca eka iṣuṇā ahanat tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ dhanuḥ chittvā ārjuniḥ su mahā balaḥ su nasam subhru keśāntam śiraḥ ahārṣīt sa kuṇḍalam lakṣmaṇam nihatam dṛṣṭvā hā hā iti uccukruśuḥ janāḥ sa bhrātṝn rāja putrān ca kumārasya anuyāyinām jaghāna bāṇaiḥ saubhadraḥ sahasrāṇi caturdaśa aṣṭau ratha sahasrāṇi sapta nāga śatāni ca tatas droṇaḥ kṛpaḥ karṇaḥ droṇa putraḥ bṛhadbalaḥ kṛtavarmā ca hārdikyaḥ ṣaṭ rathāḥ paryavārayan sa tān viddhvā śitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ vimukhīkṛtya ca ārjuniḥ āvavruḥ tasya panthānam gaja anīkena daṃśitāḥ kaliṅgāḥ ca niṣādāḥ ca krātha putraḥ ca vīryavān tat prasaktam iva atyartham yuddham āsīt viśām pate tatas tat kuñjara anīkam vyadhamat dhṛṣṭam ārjuniḥ yathā nityagatiḥ jaladān śataśas ambare tatas krāthaḥ śara vrātaiḥ ārjunim samavākirat atha itare saṃnivṛttāḥ punar droṇa mukhāḥ rathāḥ parama astrāṇi dhunvānāḥ saubhadram abhidudruvuḥ tān nivārya ārjuniḥ bāṇaiḥ krāthaputram atha ardayat śara ogheṇa aprameyeṇa tvaramāṇaḥ jighāṃsayā sa dhanuḥ bāṇa keyūrau bāhū sa mukuṭam śiraḥ chatram dhvajam niyantāram aśvān ca asya nyapātayat kula śīla śruta balaiḥ kīrtyā ca astra balena ca uvāca tathā praviṣṭam taruṇam saubhadram aparājitam kula anurūpam kurvāṇam saṃgrāmeṣu apalāyinam plavamānam iva ākāśe ke śūrāḥ samavārayan uvāca abhimanyuḥ praviśya eva tāvakān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ akarot vimukhān sarvān pārthivān pāṇḍu nandanaḥ tam tu droṇaḥ kṛpaḥ karṇaḥ drauṇiḥ ca sa bṛhadbalaḥ kṛtavarmā ca hārdikyaḥ ṣaṭ rathāḥ paryavārayan dṛṣṭvā tu saindhave bhāram atimātram samāhitam tāla mātrāṇi cāpāni vikarṣantaḥ mahā rathāḥ tān tu sarvān mahā iṣvāsān sarva vidyāsu niṣṭhitān vyaṣṭambhayat raṇe bāṇaiḥ saubhadraḥ para vīra hā droṇam pañcāśatā viddhvā viṃśatyā ca bṛhadbalam aśītyā kṛtavarmāṇam kṛpam ṣaṣṭyā śilīmukhaiḥ avidhyat daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ aśvatthāmānam ārjuniḥ sa karṇam karṇinā karṇe pītena niśitena ca phālguniḥ dviṣatām madhye vivyādha parama iṣuṇā pātayitvā kṛpasya aśvān tathā ubhau pārṣṇisārathī tatas vṛndārakam vīram kurūṇām kīrti vardhanam putrāṇām te vīrāṇām paśyatām avadhīt balī tam drauṇiḥ pañcaviṃśatyā kṣudrakāṇām samarpayat varam varam amitrāṇām ārujantam abhīta vat sa tu bāṇaiḥ śitaiḥ tūrṇam pratyavidhyata māriṣa paśyatām dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām aśvatthāmānam ārjuniḥ ṣaṣṭyā śarāṇām tam drauṇiḥ tigma dhāraiḥ su tejanaiḥ tasmin droṇaḥ bāṇa śatam putra gṛddhī nyapātayat aśvatthāmā tathā aṣṭau ca parīpsan pitaram raṇe karṇaḥ dvāviṃśatim bhallān kṛtavarmā caturdaśa bṛhadbalaḥ tu pañcāśat kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ daśa tān tu pratyavadhīt sarvān daśabhiḥ daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ taiḥ ardyamānaḥ saubhadraḥ sarvatas niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ tam kosalānām adhipaḥ karṇinā atāḍayat hṛdi sa tasya aśvān dhvajam cāpam sūtam ca apātayat kṣitau iyeṣa phālguneḥ kāyāt śiraḥ hartum sa kuṇḍalam sa kosalānām bhartāram rāja putram bṛhadbalam babhañja ca sahasrāṇi daśa rājan mahātmanām sṛjatām aśivāḥ vācaḥ khaḍga kārmuka dhāriṇām viṣṭambhayan mahā iṣvāsān yodhān te śara ambuṣu uvāca sa karṇam karṇinā karṇe punar vivyādha phālguniḥ śaraiḥ pañcāśatā ca enam avidhyat kopayan bhṛśam karṇaḥ api vibabhau śūraḥ śaraiḥ citraḥ asṛj āplutaḥ saṃdhyā anugata paryantaḥ śaradi iva divākaraḥ babhūvatuḥ mahātmanau puṣpitau iva kiṃśukau atha karṇasya sacivān ṣaṭ śūrān citra yodhinaḥ atha itarān mahā iṣvāsān daśabhiḥ daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ māgadhasya punar putram hatvā ṣaḍbhiḥ ajihmagaiḥ sa aśvam sa sūtam taruṇam aśva ketum apātayat mārtikāvatakam bhojam tatas kuñjara ketanam kṣurapreṇa samunmathya nanāda visṛjan śarān sūtam ekena vivyādha daśabhiḥ ca arjuna ātmajam tatas dauḥśāsanim kārṣṇiḥ viddhvā sapta āśugaiḥ pitā te āhavam tyaktvā gataḥ kāpuruṣaḥ yathā diṣṭyā tvam api jānīṣe yoddhum na tu adya mokṣyase nārācam visasarja asmai tam drauṇiḥ tribhiḥ ācchinat tam śalyaḥ navabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ gārdhra pattraiḥ atāḍayat tasya ārjuniḥ dhvajam chittvā ubhau ca pārṣṇisārathī tam vivyādha āyasaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ saḥ apakrāmat ratha antaram ca pañca etān hatvā vivyādha saubalam atha abravīt tadā droṇam karṇaḥ vaikartanaḥ vṛṣā purā sarvān pramathnāti brūhi asya vadham āśu naḥ tatas droṇaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ sarvān tān pratyabhāṣata śīghra tām nara siṃhasya pāṇḍaveyasya paśyata dhanuḥ maṇḍalam eva asya ratha mārgeṣu dṛśyate saṃdadhānasya viśikhān śīghram ca eva vimuñcataḥ vikarṣataḥ dhanuḥ śreṣṭham na antaram dṛśyate hi vai ārujan iva me prāṇān mohayan api sāyakaiḥ praharṣayati mā bhūyas saubhadraḥ para vīra hā antaram yasya saṃrabdhāḥ na paśyanti mahā rathāḥ na viśeṣam prapaśyāmi raṇe gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ atha karṇaḥ punar droṇam āha ārjuni śara arditaḥ sthātavyam iti tiṣṭhāmi pīḍyamānaḥ abhimanyunā tejasvinaḥ kumārasya śarāḥ parama dāruṇāḥ kṣiṇvanti hṛdayam me adya ghorāḥ pāvaka tejasaḥ hrīmat tvāt kṣitipālānām paśyatām adya ca dvija na me aṅga hīyate kim cit na vai vāc eti mām tathā vicinvadbhiḥ iva asūn me śarīram na vibhāvyate tam ācāryaḥ abravīt karṇam śanakais prahasan iva abhedyam asya kavacam yuvā ca āśu parākramaḥ upadiṣṭā mayā asya pituḥ kavaca dhāraṇā tām eṣa nikhilām vetti dhruvam parapuraṃjayaḥ jyā lakṣaṇam mayā ca iha na upadiṣṭam tu phalgune śakyam tu asya dhanuḥ chettum jyām ca bāṇaiḥ samāhitaiḥ abhīśavaḥ hayāḥ ca eva tathā ubhau pārṣṇisārathī atha enam vimukhīkṛtya paścāt praharaṇam kuru vilakṣa karaṇam vā nādam vimuñcan agratas nṛpa saṃdhāna kṛta lakṣasya kim cit vyākṣipta cetasaḥ puras sthitena kena api duḥśakyaḥ jetum ārjuniḥ naṣṭa lakṣaḥ kumāraḥ ayam hanyatām hanyatām iti aśvān asya avadhīt bhojaḥ gautamaḥ pārṣṇisārathī śeṣāḥ tu chinna dhanvānam śara varṣaiḥ avākiran tvaramāṇāḥ tvarā kāle viratham ṣaṭ mahā rathāḥ śara varṣaiḥ akaruṇāḥ bālam ekam avākiran khaḍga carma dharaḥ śrīmān utpapāta vihāyasam maṇḍalāni su śikṣābhiḥ gata pratyāgatāni ca ārjuniḥ vyacarat vyomni bhṛśam vai pakṣirāj iva mayi eva nipatati eṣa sa asiḥ iti ūrdhva dṛṣṭayaḥ vivyadhuḥ tam mahā iṣvāsāḥ samare chidra darśiṇaḥ kṣurapreṇa mahā tejāḥ tvaramāṇaḥ sapatna jit vyasi carman iṣu pūrṇa aṅgaḥ saḥ antarikṣāt punar kṣitim sa cakra reṇu ujjvala śobhita aṅgaḥ babhau atīva unnata cakra pāṇiḥ raṇe abhimanyuḥ kṣaṇadā subhadraḥ sa vāsubhadra anukṛtim prakurvan sruta rudhira kṛta eka rāga vaktraḥ bhrukuṭi puṭa akuṭilaḥ ati siṃhanādaḥ uvāca viṣṇoḥ svasā ānandi karaḥ sa viṣṇu āyudha bhūṣitaḥ rarāja atirathaḥ saṃkhye janārdanaḥ iva aparaḥ māruta uddhūta keśāntam udyata ari vara āyudham vapuḥ samīkṣya pṛthvīśāḥ duḥsamīkṣyam suraiḥ api yadi pāṇi talāt etat cakram mucyeta phālguneḥ vara dānāt mātulasya viṣṇoḥ cakram iva āpatet tat cakram bhṛśam udvignāḥ saṃcicchiduḥ anekadhā mahā rathaḥ tatas kārṣṇiḥ saṃjagrāha mahā gadām vidhanuḥ syandana asiḥ taiḥ vicakraḥ ca aribhiḥ kṛtaḥ abhimanyuḥ gadā pāṇiḥ aśvatthāmānam ādravat sa gadām udyatām dṛṣṭvā jvalantīm aśanīm iva apākrāmat rathopasthāt vikramān trīn nara ṛṣabhaḥ tasya aśvān gadayā hatvā tathā ubhau pārṣṇisārathī śara ācita aṅgaḥ saubhadraḥ śvāvidh vat pratyadṛśyata jaghāna ca asya anucarān gāndhārān saptasaptatim punar brahma vasātīyān jaghāna rathinaḥ daśa kekayānām rathān sapta hatvā ca daśa kuñjarān dauḥśāsani ratham sa aśvam gadayā samapothayat tatas dauḥśāsaniḥ kruddhaḥ gadām udyamya māriṣa abhidudrāva saubhadram tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt tau udyata gadau vīrau anyonya vadha kāṅkṣiṇaḥ tau anyonyam gadā agrābhyām saṃhatya patitau kṣitau tatas mahī talāt kārṣṇiḥ viṣa pītaḥ iva skhalan samabhyadhāvat daṣṭa oṣṭhaḥ dauḥśāsanim atha kṣitau kiṃcid śvāsaḥ tu saubhadraḥ dauḥśāsanim atāḍayat dauḥśāsaniḥ atha utthāya kurūṇām kīrti vardhanaḥ deva kalpaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ kṣatram dagdhvā mahā yaśāḥ prottiṣṭhamānam saubhadram gadayā mūrdhani atāḍayat pauruṣam ca samālambya kim cit mūrchām avāpa saḥ evam tadā mahā vīraḥ kuru vaṃśa vivardhanaḥ yudhyamānaḥ tṛṣā ākrāntaḥ su kumāraḥ mahā balaḥ kṣudhā saṃpīḍitaḥ rājan īṣat mūrchām avāpa saḥ īṣat bhramamāne te cakṣuṣī samadṛśyata kṣaṇa upaviṣṭaḥ atha tadā vākyam ca idam uvāca ha śṛṇvantu kauravāḥ sarve vākyam dharma artha saṃhitam kṛṣṇasya ca aham durmedhāḥ yathā kāpuruṣaḥ tadā subhadrā nandanaḥ bhūtvā kim ca api na kṛtam mayā sarve yūyam jīvamānāḥ mad droṇa ha parāyaṇāḥ evam bruvāṇaḥ sa tadā abhimanyuḥ pratāpa yuktaḥ api raṇe pranaṣṭaḥ dhṛtyā gṛhītaḥ sa tadā mahātmā mūrchā anvitaḥ vihvala tām jagāma hatvā tān su bahūn vīrān lakṣmaṇa ādīn mahā balaḥ koṭim hatvā rathānām ca gajānām ca tathā eva ca hayānām arbudam pūrṇam kharvam ekam padātinām kṣobhayitvā camūm sarvām nalinīm iva kuñjaraḥ tam tathā patitam śūram tāvakāḥ paryavārayan dāvam dagdhvā yathā śāntam pāvakam śiśirātyaye vimṛdya taru śṛṅgāṇi saṃnivṛttam iva anilam astam gatam iva ādityam taptvā bhārata vāhinīm upaplutam yathā somam saṃśuṣkam iva sāgaram pūrṇa candra ābha vadanam kākapakṣa vṛta akṣakam kākapakṣa āklipta keśam paugaṇḍam iti saṃjñitam tam bhūmau patitam dṛṣṭvā tāvakāḥ te mahā rathāḥ mudā paramayā yuktāḥ cukruśuḥ siṃha vat muhur āsīt paramakaḥ harṣaḥ tāvakānām viśām pate itareṣām tu vīrāṇām netrebhyaḥ prāpatat jalam abhikrośanti bhūtāni antarikṣe viśām pate dṛṣṭvā nipatitam vīram cyutam candram iva ambarāt droṇa karṇa mukhaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ dhārtarāṣṭraiḥ mahā rathaiḥ dyauḥ yathā pūrṇa candreṇa nakṣatra gaṇa mālinī rukma puṅkhaiḥ ca saṃpūrṇā rudhira ogha pariplutā uttamāṅgaiḥ ca vīrāṇām bhrājamānaiḥ sa kuṇḍalaiḥ vicitraiḥ ca paristomaiḥ patākābhiḥ ca saṃvṛtā ratha aśva nara nāgānām alaṃkāraiḥ ca su prabhaiḥ cāpaiḥ ca viśikhaiḥ chinnaiḥ śakti ṛṣṭi prāsa kampanaiḥ vividhaiḥ āyudhaiḥ ca anyaiḥ saṃvṛtā bhūḥ aśobhata vājibhiḥ ca api nirjīvaiḥ svapadbhiḥ śoṇita ukṣitaiḥ sa ārohaiḥ viṣamā bhūmiḥ saubhadreṇa nipātitaiḥ sa aṅkuśaiḥ sa mahāmātraiḥ sa varma āyudha ketubhiḥ pṛthivyām anukīrṇaiḥ ca vyaśva sārathi yodhibhiḥ padāti saṃghaiḥ ca hataiḥ vividha āyudha bhūṣaṇaiḥ bhīrūṇām trāsa jananī ghora rūpā bhavat mahī tam dṛṣṭvā patitam bhūmau candra arka sadṛśa dyutim tāvakānām parā prītiḥ pāṇḍūnām ca abhavat vyathā saṃprādravat camūḥ sarvā dharmarājasya paśyataḥ dīryamāṇam balam dṛṣṭvā saubhadre vinipātite ajātaśatruḥ svān vīrān idam vacanam abravīt astam gataḥ ayam dyumaṇiḥ tāpayitvā mahā balaḥ evam bruvāṇaḥ nṛpatiḥ sainyena mahatā vṛtaḥ vyūha dvāram samāsādya bāṣpa pūrya ākula īkṣaṇaḥ svargam eṣa gataḥ śūraḥ yaḥ hataḥ na parāṅmukhaḥ saṃstambhayata mā bhaiṣṭa vijeṣyāmaḥ raṇe ripūn iti evam sa mahā tejāḥ duḥkhitebhyaḥ mahā dyutiḥ dharmarājaḥ yudhām śreṣṭhaḥ bruvan duḥkham apānudat yuddhe hi āśīviṣa ākārān rāja putrān raṇe bahūn pūrvam nihatya saṃgrāme paścāt ārjuniḥ anvagāt hatvā daśa sahasrāṇi kausalyam ca mahā ratham kṛṣṇa arjuna samaḥ kārṣṇiḥ śakra sadma gataḥ dhruvam ratha aśva nara mātaṃgān vinihatya sahasraśas a vitṛptaḥ sa saṃgrāmāt a śocyaḥ puṇya karma kṛt gataḥ puṇya kṛtām lokān bhāsvarān puṇya nirjitān kim mayā jīvitena arthaḥ saubhadreṇa vinā bhuvi akṣayām gatim āsādya sa gataḥ śāśvatīḥ samāḥ vayam tu pravaram hatvā teṣām taiḥ śara pīḍitāḥ niveśāya abhyupāyāma sāyāhne rudhira ukṣitāḥ nirīkṣamāṇāḥ tu vayam pare ca āyodhanam śanais apayātāḥ mahā rāja glānim prāptāḥ vicetasaḥ tatas niśāyāḥ divasasya ca aśivaḥ śivā rutaḥ saṃdhiḥ avartata adbhutaḥ vara asi śakti ṛṣṭi varūtha carmaṇām vibhūṣaṇānām ca samākṣipan prabhām divam ca bhūmim ca samānayan iva priyām tanum bhānuḥ upaiti pāvakam mahā abhra kūṭa acala śṛṅga saṃnibhaiḥ gajaiḥ anekaiḥ iva vajra pātitaiḥ mahā rathaiḥ bhūḥ śuśubhe vicūrṇitaiḥ puraiḥ iva amitra hataiḥ narādhipa ratha aśva vṛndaiḥ saha sādibhiḥ hataiḥ praviddha bhāṇḍa ābharaṇaiḥ pṛthagvidhaiḥ praviddha varma ābharaṇāḥ vara āyudhāḥ vipanna hasti aśva ratha anugāḥ narāḥ mahārha śayyā āstaraṇa ucitāḥ sadā kṣitau anāthāḥ iva śerate hatāḥ atīva hṛṣṭāḥ śva sṛgāla vāyasāḥ suparṇāḥ ca vṛkāḥ tarakṣavaḥ vayāṃsi asṛkpāni atha rakṣasām gaṇāḥ piśāca saṃghāḥ ca su dāruṇāḥ raṇe vapām vilumpanti hasanti gānti ca prakarṣamāṇāḥ kuṇapāni anekaśas śarīra saṃghāṭa vahā asṛj jalā ratha uḍupā kuñjara śaila saṃkaṭā manuṣya śīrṣa upala māṃsa kardamā uvāha madhyena raṇa ajiram bhṛśam bhaya āvahā jīva mṛta pravāhinī pibanti ca aśnanti ca yatra durdṛśāḥ piśāca saṃghāḥ vividhāḥ su bhairavāḥ su nanditāḥ prāṇabhṛtām bhayaṃkarāḥ samāna bhakṣāḥ śva sṛgāla pakṣiṇaḥ tathā tat āyodhanam ugra darśanam niśā mukhe pitṛpati rāṣṭra saṃnibham nirīkṣamāṇāḥ śanakais jahuḥ narāḥ samutthita aruṇḍa kula upasaṃkulam apeta vidhvasta mahārha bhūṣaṇam nipātitam śakra samam mahā ratham raṇe abhimanyum dadṛśuḥ tadā janāḥ vyapoḍha havyam sadasi iva pāvakam uvāca vimukta ratha saṃnāhāḥ sarve nikṣipta kārmukāḥ upopaviṣṭāḥ rājānam parivārya yudhiṣṭhiram tat eva duḥkham dhyāyantaḥ saubhadra gata mānasāḥ tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā vilalāpa su duḥkhitaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ eṣa karṇam kṛpam śalyam rājānam ca suyodhanam droṇam drauṇim mahā iṣvāsam tathā eva anyān mahā rathān droṇa anīkam asaṃbādham mama priya cikīrṣayā hatvā śatru gaṇān vīraḥ eṣa śete nipātitaḥ kṛtāstrān yuddha kuśalān mahā iṣvāsān mahā balān kula śīla guṇaiḥ yuktān śūrān vikhyāta pauruṣān a dṛṣṭa pūrvam asmābhiḥ padmam cakra āyudha priyaḥ cikrīḍitam raṇe tena nighnatā vai parān varān yasya śūrāḥ mahā iṣvāsāḥ pratyanīka gatāḥ raṇe atyanta śatruḥ naḥ yena duḥśāsanaḥ śaraiḥ kṣipram hi abhimukhaḥ saṃkye visaṃjñaḥ vimukhīkṛtaḥ sa tīrtvā dustaram vīraḥ droṇa anīka mahā arṇavam śūra grāha ākulam bhīmam tīrtvā ca enam abhīta vat prāpya dauḥśāsanim kārṣṇiḥ yātaḥ vaivasvata kṣayam subhadrām vā mahābhāgām priyam putram a paśyatīm hata vatsām yathā dhenum tad darśana kṛta unmukhīm tau ubhau prativakṣyāmaḥ hṛṣīkeśa dhanaṃjayau priya kāmaḥ jaya ākāṅkṣī kṛtavan idam apriyam madhu lipsuḥ hi na apaśyam prapātam idam īdṛśam bhūṣaṇeṣu ca saḥ asmābhiḥ bālaḥ yudhi puraskṛtaḥ katham hi bālaḥ taruṇaḥ yuddhānām a viśāradaḥ bībhatsoḥ kopa dīptasya dagdhāḥ kṛpaṇa cakṣuṣā alubdhaḥ matimān hrīmān kṣamāvān rūpavān balī vapuṣmān māna kṛt vīraḥ priyaḥ satya parāyaṇaḥ yasya ślāghanti vibudhāḥ karmāṇi ūrjita karmaṇaḥ nivāta kavacān jaghne kālakeyān ca vīryavān akṣṇoḥ nimeṣa mātreṇa paulomāḥ sa gaṇāḥ hatāḥ bhayam tu su mahat prāptam dhārtarāṣṭram mahat balam pārthaḥ putra vadhāt kruddhaḥ kauravān śoṣayiṣyati kṣudraḥ
