nihate yuddhe katham jīveta mādṛśaḥ śyāmaḥ yuvā guḍākeśaḥ darśanīyaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ laghu astraḥ citra yodhī ca praviṣṭaḥ tāta bhāratīm tat na jānāmi vārṣṇeya yadi jīvati vā na vā kurūṇām ca api tat sainyam sāgara pratimam mahat ekaḥ eva ca bībhatsuḥ praviṣṭaḥ tāta bhāratīm aviṣahyām mahā bāhuḥ suraiḥ api mahā mṛdhe yugapad ca sametānām kāryāṇām tvam vicakṣaṇaḥ na aham śocāmi dāśārham goptāram jagantaḥ prabhum sa hi śaktaḥ raṇe tāta trīn lokān api saṃgatān prajahyāt samare prāṇān tasmāt vindāmi kaśmalam tasya tvam padavīm gaccha gaccheyuḥ tvādṛśāḥ yathā tādṛśasya īdṛśe kāle mādṛśeṇa abhicoditaḥ tvādṛśāḥ tādṛśam gaccheḥ tādṛśam gaccha satyaka raṇe vṛṣṇi pravīrāṇām dvau eva atirathau smṛtau pradyumnaḥ ca mahā bāhuḥ tvam ca sātvata viśrutaḥ astre nārāyaṇa samaḥ saṃkarṣaṇa samaḥ bale vīra tāyām nara vyāghra dhanaṃjaya samaḥ hi asi na anyathā tām mahā bāho saṃprakartum iha arhasi parityajya priyān prāṇān raṇe vicara vīra vat na hi śaineya dāśārhāḥ raṇe rakṣanti jīvitam bhīrūṇām asatām mārgaḥ na eṣa dāśārha sevitaḥ tava arjunaḥ guruḥ tāta dharma ātmā śini puṃgava vāsudevaḥ guruḥ ca api te pārthasya dhīmataḥ praviśa etat balam tāta dhārtarāṣṭrasya durmateḥ praviśya ca yathānyāyam saṃgamya ca mahā rathaiḥ yathārham ātmanaḥ karma raṇe sātvata darśaya uvāca prīti yuktam ca hṛdyam ca madhura akṣaram eva ca kāla yuktam ca citram ca svatayā ca abhibhāṣitam dharmarājasya tat vākyam niśamya śini puṃgavaḥ sātyakiḥ bharata śreṣṭha pratyuvāca yudhiṣṭhiram evaṃvidhe tathā kāle madṛśam prekṣya saṃmatam na me dhanaṃjayasya arthe prāṇāḥ rakṣyāḥ katham cana kuśalī aham kuśalinam samāsādya dhanaṃjayam avaśyam tu mayā sarvam vijñāpyaḥ tvam narādhipa dṛḍham tu abhiparītaḥ aham arjuna punar punar āryām yuddhe matim kṛtvā yāvat dhanmi jayadratham tvayi vā aham mahā bāho pradyumne vā mahā rathe saḥ evam vai vinikṣiptaḥ nikṣepaḥ savyasācinā jānīṣe hi raṇe droṇam rabhasam śreṣṭha saṃmatam pratijñā ca api te nityam śrutā droṇasya mādhava śaktaḥ ca api raṇe droṇaḥ nigṛhītum yudhiṣṭhiram sa tvam adya raṇe yattaḥ rakṣa mādhavaiḥ pāṇḍavam dharmarājam yathā droṇaḥ nigṛhṇīyāt raṇe balāt nigṛhīte nara śreṣṭhe bhāradvājena mādhava evam gate nara śreṣṭha pāṇḍave satya vādini yadi droṇaḥ raṇe kruddhaḥ nigṛhṇīyāt yudhiṣṭhiram jaya artham ca yaśaḥ artham ca rakṣa rājānam āhave sa bhavān mayi nikṣepaḥ nikṣiptaḥ savyasācinā bhāradvājāt bhayam nityam paśyamānena te prabho tasya api ca mahā bāho nityam paśyati saṃyuge na anyam hi pratiyoddhāram raukmiṇeyāt ṛte prabho mām vā api manyate yuddhe bhāradvājasya dhīmataḥ saḥ aham saṃbhāvanām ca etām ācārya vacanam ca tat pṛṣṭhatas na utsahe kartum tvām vā tyaktum mahīpate ācāryaḥ laghu hasta tvāt abhedya kavaca āvṛtaḥ upalabhya raṇe krīḍet yathā śakuninā śiśuḥ yadi kārṣṇiḥ dhanuṣpāṇiḥ iha syāt makara dhvajaḥ tasmai tvām visṛjeyam vai sa tvām rakṣet yathā arjunaḥ yaḥ pratīyāt raṇe droṇam yāvat gacchāmi pāṇḍavam udīcyāḥ dākṣiṇātyāḥ ca ye ca anye api mahā rathāḥ ye ca karṇa mukhāḥ rājan ratha udārāḥ prakīrtitāḥ ete arjunasya kruddhasya kalām na arhanti ṣoḍaśīm udyuktā pṛthivī sarvā sa sura asura mānuṣā sa rākṣasa gaṇā rājan sa kiṃnara mahā uragā jaṅgamāḥ sthāvaraiḥ sārdham na alam pārthasya saṃyuge evam jñātvā mahā rāja vyetu te bhī dhanaṃjaye yatra vīrau mahā iṣvāsau kṛṣṇau satya parākramau daivam kṛtāstra tām yogam amarṣam api ca āhave kṛtajña tām dayām ca eva bhrātuḥ tvam anucintaya droṇe citra astra tām saṃkhye rājñ tvam anucintaya ācāryaḥ hi bhṛśam rājan nigrahe tava gṛdhyati pratijñām ātmanaḥ rakṣan satyām kartum ca bhārata na hi aham tvā mahā rāja a nikṣipya mahā āhave śaktam yam manyase rājan goptāram prati pāṇḍava dṛṣṭvā śreyaḥ param buddhyā tatas rājñ praśādhi mām uvāca na tu me śudhyate bhāvaḥ śvetāśvam prati māriṣa kariṣye parama yatnam ātmanaḥ rakṣaṇam prati ātma saṃrakṣaṇam saṃkhye gamanam ca arjunam prati sa tvam ātiṣṭha yānāya yatra yātaḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ pṛṣṭhatas puruṣa vyāghra bhīmaḥ tvā anugamiṣyati mama api rakṣaṇam bhīmaḥ kariṣyati mahā balaḥ pārṣataḥ ca sa sodaryaḥ pārthivāḥ ca mahā balāḥ draupadeyāḥ ca mām tāta rakṣiṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ kekayāḥ bhrātaraḥ pañca rākṣasaḥ ca ghaṭotkacaḥ virāṭaḥ drupadaḥ ca eva śikhaṇḍī ca mahā rathaḥ dhṛṣṭaketuḥ ca balavān kuntibhojaḥ ca māriṣa nakulaḥ sahadevaḥ ca pāñcālāḥ sṛñjayāḥ tathā ete samāhitāḥ tāta rakṣiṣyanti na saṃśayaḥ samāsādayitum śaktaḥ na ca mām dharṣayiṣyati dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca samare droṇam kruddham paraṃtapaḥ yatra sthāsyati saṃgrāme pārṣataḥ para vīra hā eṣa droṇa vināśāya samutpannaḥ hutāśanāt kavacī sa śarī khaḍgī dhanvī ca vara bhūṣaṇaḥ pāñcālaḥ sahitaḥ sarvaiḥ pāṇḍavānām ca dhanvibhiḥ viśrabdhaḥ gaccha śaineya mā kārṣīḥ mayi saṃbhramam dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ raṇe kruddhaḥ droṇam āvārayiṣyati uvāca dharmarājasya tat vākyam niśamya śini puṃgavaḥ pārthāt ca bhayam āśaṅkan parityāgāt mahīpateḥ apavādam hi ātmanaḥ ca lokāt rakṣan viśeṣataḥ na mām bhīta iti brūyuḥ āyāntam phalgunam prati na ati vyaktam iva ābhāṣya dharmarājam mahā yaśāḥ śoka gadgadayā vācā śoka upahata cetanaḥ yathā idānīm iti dhyātvā dharmarājam atha abravīt kṛtām ced manyase rakṣām svasti te astu viśām pate anuyāsyāmi bībhatsum kariṣye vacanam te na hi me pāṇḍavāt kaḥ cit triṣu lokeṣu vidyate tasya aham padavīm yāsye saṃdeśāt te mānada yathā hi me guroḥ vākyam viśiṣṭam dvipadām vara tathā tava api vacanam viśiṣṭataram eva me priye hi tava vartete bhrātarau kṛṣṇa pāṇḍavau te ājñām śirasā gṛhya pāṇḍava artham aham prabho droṇa anīkam viśāmi eṣa kruddhaḥ jhaṣaḥ iva arṇavam tatra yāsyāmi yatra asau rājñ rājā jayadrathaḥ yatra senām samāśritya bhītaḥ tiṣṭhati pāṇḍavāt guptaḥ ratha vara śreṣṭhaiḥ drauṇi karṇa kṛpa ādibhiḥ itas tri yojanam manye tam adhvānam viśām pate ā saindhava vadhāt rājan su dṛḍhena antarātmanā an ādiṣṭaḥ tu guruṇā kaḥ nu yudhyeta mānavaḥ ādiṣṭaḥ tu tvayā rājan kaḥ na yudhyeta mādṛśaḥ abhijānāmi tam deśam yatra yāsyāmi aham prabho yatra tiṣṭhati rājā asau saindhavaḥ bāla ghātakaḥ huḍa śakti gadā prāsa khaḍga carma ṛṣṭi tomaram iṣvastra vara sambādham kṣobhayiṣye bala arṇavam yat etat kuñjara anīkam sāhasram anupaśyasi kulam añjanakam nāma yatra ete vīrya śālinaḥ āsthitāḥ bahubhiḥ mlecchaiḥ yuddha śauṇḍaiḥ prahāribhiḥ nāgāḥ megha nibhāḥ rājan kṣarantaḥ iva toyadāḥ anyatra hi vadhāt eṣām na asti rājan parājayaḥ ete rukmarathāḥ nāma rāja putrāḥ mahā rathāḥ ratheṣu astreṣu nipuṇāḥ nāgeṣu ca viśām pate dhanurvede gatāḥ pāram muṣṭi yuddhe ca kovidāḥ gadā yuddha viśeṣa jñāḥ niyuddha kuśalāḥ tathā khaḍga praharaṇe yuktāḥ saṃpāte ca asi carmaṇoḥ śūrāḥ ca kṛtavidyāḥ ca spardhante ca parasparam nityam ca samare rājan vijigīṣanti mānavān karṇena vijitāḥ rājan duḥśāsanam anuvratāḥ etān tu vāsudevaḥ api ratha udārān praśaṃsati satatam priya kāmāḥ ca karṇasya ete vaśe sthitāḥ tasya eva vacanāt rājan nivṛttāḥ śvetavāhanāt te na kṣatāḥ na ca śrāntāḥ dṛḍha āvaraṇa kārmukāḥ mad artham viṣṭhitāḥ nūnam dhārtarāṣṭrasya śāsanāt prayāsyāmi tatas paścāt padavīm savyasācinaḥ yān tu etān aparān rājan nāgān sapta śatāni ca prekṣase varma saṃchannān kirātaiḥ samadhiṣṭhitān kirāta rājaḥ yān prādāt gṛhītaḥ savyasācinā su alaṃkṛtān tathā preṣyān icchan jīvitam ātmanaḥ āsan ete purā rājan tava karmakarāḥ dṛḍham teṣām ete mahāmātrāḥ kirātāḥ yuddha durmadāḥ ete vinirjitāḥ sarve saṃgrāme savyasācinā etān bhittvā śaraiḥ rājan kirātān yuddha durmadān ye tu ete su mahā nāgāḥ añjanasya kula udbhavāḥ karkaśāḥ ca vinītāḥ ca prabhinna karaṭāmukhāḥ jāmbūnada mayaiḥ sarvaiḥ varmabhiḥ su vibhūṣitāḥ labdha lakṣyāḥ raṇe rājñ airāvaṇa samāḥ yudhi uttarāt parvatāt ete tīkṣṇaiḥ dasyubhiḥ āsthitāḥ āsthitāḥ dasyubhiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ śūraiḥ uttama pārvataiḥ karkaśaiḥ pravaraiḥ yodhaiḥ kārṣṇāyasa tanucchadaiḥ aneka yonayaḥ ca anye tathā mānuṣa yonayaḥ mlecchānām pāpa kartṝṇām himavat durga vāsinām kṛpam ca saumadattim ca droṇam ca rathinām varam sindhurājam tathā karṇam avamanyata pāṇḍavān bhīṣmam droṇam kṛpam karṇam āvantyau atha saindhavam drauṇim ca saumadattim ca pāṇḍavān atimanyate kṛtārtham atha ca ātmānam manyate kāla coditaḥ tena saṃbhāvitā nityam para vīrya upajīvinā vināśam upayāsyanti mad śara ogha nipīḍitāḥ ye tu ete rathinaḥ rājan dṛśyante kāñcana dhvajāḥ ete durvāraṇāḥ nāma kāmbojāḥ yadi te śrutāḥ śūrāḥ ca kṛtavidyāḥ ca dhanurvede ca niṣṭhitāḥ saṃhatāḥ ca bhṛśam hi ete anyonyasya hita eṣiṇaḥ akṣauhiṇyaḥ ca saṃrabdhāḥ dhārtarāṣṭrasya bhārata yattāḥ mad artham tiṣṭhanti kuru vīra abhirakṣitāḥ apramattāḥ mahā rāja mām eva pratyupasthitāḥ tān tu aham pramathiṣyāmi tṛṇāni iva hutāśanaḥ tasmāt sarvān upāsaṅgān sarva upakaraṇāni ca yathā upadiṣṭam ācāryaiḥ kāryaḥ pañcaguṇaḥ rathaḥ kāmbojaiḥ hi sameṣyāmi kruddhaiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ nānā śastra samāvāpaiḥ vividha āyudha yodhibhiḥ kirātaiḥ ca sameṣyāmi viṣa kalpaiḥ prahāribhiḥ lālitaiḥ satatam rājñā duryodhana hita eṣibhiḥ śakaiḥ ca api sameṣyāmi śakra tulya parākramaiḥ tri yojana gatasya aham padavīm savyasācinaḥ yāsyāmi rathinām śreṣṭham pravaram ca dhanuṣmatām sūrya udaya gatasya aham pāṇḍavasya gatim caran apareṇa gate sūrye gamiṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ tasmāt vai vājinaḥ mukhyāḥ viśrāntāḥ śubha lakṣaṇāḥ upāvṛttāḥ ca pītāḥ ca punar yujyantu me rathe tasya sarvān upāsaṅgān sarva upakaraṇāni ca rathe prāsthāpayat rājā śastrāṇi vividhāni ca tatas tān sarvatas muktvā sat aśvān caturaḥ janāḥ rasavat pāyayām āsuḥ pānam mada samīriṇam pīta upavṛttān snātān ca jagdha annān samalaṃkṛtān vinīta śalyān turagān caturaḥ hema mālinaḥ tān yattān rukma varṇa ābhān vinītān śīghra gāminaḥ pāṇḍura abhra prakāśābhiḥ patākābhiḥ alaṃkṛte yojayām āsa vidhivat hema bhāṇḍa vibhūṣitān dārukasya anujaḥ bhrātā sūtaḥ tasya priyaḥ sakhiḥ tatas snātaḥ śuciḥ bhūtvā kṛta kautukamaṅgalaḥ snātakānām sahasrasya svarṇa niṣkān adāpayat āśīrvādaiḥ pariṣvaktaḥ sātyakiḥ śrīmatām varaḥ tatas sa madhuparka arhaḥ pītvā kailāvatam madhu ālabhya vīra kāṃsyam ca harṣeṇa mahatā anvitaḥ dviguṇīkṛta tejāḥ hi prajvalan iva pāvakaḥ utsaṅge dhanuḥ ādāya sa śaram rathinām varaḥ lājaiḥ gandhaiḥ tathā mālyaiḥ kanyābhiḥ ca abhinanditaḥ yudhiṣṭhirasya caraṇau abhivādya kṛtāñjaliḥ āśiṣaḥ vipulāḥ śrutvā dharmarāja mukha udgatāḥ tatas te vājinaḥ hṛṣṭāḥ su puṣṭāḥ vāta raṃhasaḥ yathā śakra ratham rājan ūhuḥ te harayaḥ purā prāyāt sātyakinā sārdham abhivādya yudhiṣṭhiram tau dṛṣṭvā pravivikṣantau te senām ariṃdamau saṃyattāḥ tāvakāḥ sarve tasthuḥ droṇa purogamāḥ saṃnaddham anugacchantam dṛṣṭvā bhīmam sa sātyakiḥ abhinandya abravīt vīraḥ tadā harṣa karam vacaḥ atha harṣa parīta aṅgaḥ sātyakiḥ bhīmam abravīt tvam bhīma rakṣa rājānam etat kāryatamam hi te āyatau ca tadātve ca śreyaḥ rājñaḥ abhirakṣaṇam jānīṣe mama vīryam tvam te ca aham ariṃdama aham rājñaḥ kariṣyāmi rakṣām puruṣa sattama evam uktaḥ pratyuvāca bhīmasenam sa mādhavaḥ nihate saindhave pāpe pāṇḍavena mahātmanā pariṣvajiṣye rājānam dharma ātmānam na saṃśayaḥ apramādaḥ ca te kāryaḥ droṇam prati mahā ratham etāvat uktvā bhīmam tu visṛjya ca mahāmanāḥ saṃpraikṣat tāvakam sainyam vyāghraḥ mṛga gaṇān iva tam dṛṣṭvā pravivikṣantam sainyam te janādhipa bhūyas eva abhavat mūḍham su bhṛśam ca api akampata tatas prayātaḥ sahasā sainyam te sa sātyakiḥ didṛkṣuḥ arjunam rājan dharmarājasya śāsanāt uvāca dharmarājaḥ mahā rāja svena anīkena saṃvṛtaḥ prāyāt droṇa ratha prepsuḥ yuyudhānasya pṛṣṭhatas tatas pāñcāla rājasya putraḥ samara durmadaḥ prākrośat pāṇḍava anīke vasudānaḥ ca pārthivaḥ senāpati vacaḥ śrutvā pāṇḍaveyāḥ samantataḥ bāṇa śabda ravān kṛtvā vimiśrān śaṅkha nisvanaiḥ yuyudhāna ratham dṛṣṭvā tāvakāḥ abhidudruvuḥ tatas śabdaḥ mahān āsīt yuyudhāna ratham prati sātvatena mahā rāja śatadhā abhivyadīryata tasyām vidīryamāṇāyām śineḥ pautraḥ mahā rathaḥ sapta vīrān mahā iṣvāsān agra anīke vyapothayat atha anyān api rāja indra nānā janapada īśvarān śaraiḥ anala saṃkāśaiḥ ninye vīrān yama kṣayam śatam ekena vivyādha śatena ekam ca pattriṇām dvipa ārohān dvipān ca eva haya ārohān hayān tathā rathinaḥ sa aśva sūtān ca jaghāna īśaḥ paśūn iva tam tathā adbhuta karmāṇam śara sampāta varṣiṇam te bhītāḥ mṛdyamānāḥ ca pramṛṣṭāḥ dīrgha bāhunā āyodhanam jahuḥ vīrāḥ dṛṣṭvā tam ati mānuṣam saṃgrāma kovidam vīram vicarantam abhīta vat rathaiḥ vimathita akṣaiḥ ca bhagna nīḍaiḥ ca māriṣa anukarṣaiḥ patākābhiḥ śirastrāṇaiḥ sa kāñcanaiḥ bāhubhiḥ candana ādigdhaiḥ sa aṅgadaiḥ ca viśām pate ūrubhiḥ pṛthivī channā manujānām nara uttama śaśāṅka saṃnikāśaiḥ ca vadanaiḥ cāru kuṇḍalaiḥ patitaiḥ vṛṣabha akṣāṇām babhau bhārata medinī gajaiḥ ca bahudhā chinnaiḥ śayānaiḥ parvata upamaiḥ rarāja ati bhṛśam bhūmiḥ vikīrṇaiḥ iva parvataiḥ gatasattvāḥ mahīm prāpya pramṛṣṭāḥ dīrgha bāhunā nānāvidhāni sainyāni te hatvā tu sātvataḥ praviṣṭaḥ tāvakam sainyam drāvayitvā camūm bhṛśam iyeṣa sātyakiḥ gantum tatas droṇena vāritaḥ bharadvājam samāsādya yuyudhānaḥ tu māriṣa nivārya tu raṇe droṇaḥ yuyudhānam mahā ratham vivyādha niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ pañcabhiḥ marma bhedibhiḥ sātyakiḥ tu raṇe droṇam rājñ vivyādha sapta hema puṅkhaiḥ śilā dhautaiḥ kaṅka barhiṇa vājitaiḥ tam ṣaḍbhiḥ sāyakaiḥ droṇaḥ sa aśva yantāram ārdayat sa tam na mamṛṣe droṇam yuyudhānaḥ mahā rathaḥ siṃhanādam tatas kṛtvā droṇam vivyādha sātyakiḥ daśabhiḥ sāyakaiḥ ca anyaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ aṣṭabhiḥ eva ca yuyudhānaḥ punar droṇam vivyādha daśan śaraiḥ tam droṇaḥ sa aśva yantāram sa ratha dhvajam āśugaiḥ tvaran prācchādayat bāṇaiḥ śalabhānām iva vrajaiḥ tam tathā śara jālena pracchādya mahatā punar tava ācāryaḥ raṇam hitvā gataḥ kāpuruṣaḥ yathā yudhyamānam hi mām hitvā pradakṣiṇam avartata yadi mām tvam raṇe hitvā na yāsi ācārya vat drutam uvāca dhanaṃjayasya padavīm dharmarājasya śāsanāt ācārya anugataḥ mārgaḥ śiṣyaiḥ anvāsyate sadā tasmāt evam vrajāmi āśu yathā mama sa guruḥ gataḥ uvāca etāvat uktvā śaineyaḥ ācāryam parivarjayan prayātaḥ sahasā rājñ sārathim ca idam abravīt droṇaḥ kariṣyate yatnam sarvathā mama vāraṇe yattaḥ yāhi raṇe sūta śṛṇu ca idam vacaḥ param asya anantarataḥ tu etat dākṣiṇātyam mahā balam bāhlika abhyāśataḥ yuktam karṇasya api mahat balam deśa sākalyam āsādya dṛśyate su mahat balam etat antaram āsādya codaya aśvān prahṛṣṭa vat bāhlikāḥ yatra dṛśyante nānā praharaṇa udyatāḥ dākṣiṇātyāḥ ca bahavaḥ sūtaputra purogamāḥ hasti aśva ratha saṃbādham yat ca anīkam vilokyate nānā deśa samutthaiḥ ca padātibhiḥ adhiṣṭhitam tatas śakyaḥ mahā vyūhaḥ bhettum sma sahasā raṇe tam deśam tvaritāḥ yāmaḥ mṛdantaḥ yudhi śātravān tatra ete saṃprahṛṣṭa tvāt na asmān prati yuyutsavaḥ etāvat uktvā yantāram brahmānam parivarjayan yatra ete parama kruddhāḥ dākṣiṇātyāḥ mahā rathāḥ uvāca yuyudhāna vacaḥ śrutvā yuyudhānasya sārathiḥ sa ca sainyam mahat bhittvā dākṣiṇātya balam ca tat prāviśat bhāratīm senām aparyantām sa sātyakiḥ amarṣī kṛtavarmā tu sātyakim paryavārayat tam āpatantam viśikhaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ āhatya sātyakiḥ caturbhiḥ caturaḥ asya aśvān ājaghāna āśu vīryavān tatas punar ṣoḍaśabhiḥ nata parvabhiḥ āśugaiḥ sātyakiḥ kṛtavarmāṇam pratyavidhyat stanāntare sātvatena mahā rāja kṛtavarmā na cakṣame ākṛṣya rājñ ākarṇāt vivyādha urasi sātyakim sa tasya deha āvaraṇam bhittvā deham ca sāyakaḥ sa pattra puṅkhaḥ pṛthivīm viveśa rudhira ukṣitaḥ sa mārgaṇa guṇam rājan kṛtavarmā śarāsanam tatas praśīrṇe dhanuṣi śaktyā śaktimatām varaḥ abhyahan dakṣiṇam bāhum sātyakiḥ kṛtavarmaṇaḥ tatas anyat su dṛḍham vīraḥ dhanuḥ ādāya sātyakiḥ vyasṛjat viśikhān tūrṇam śataśas atha sahasraśas te śarāḥ sātvatena astāḥ kṛtavarmāṇam āhave chādayām cakrire vṛkṣam śalabhāḥ iva ghoṣiṇaḥ sa ratham kṛtavarmāṇam samantāt paryavākirat chādayitvā raṇe atyartham hārdikyam tu sa sātyakiḥ atha asya bhallena śiraḥ sāratheḥ samakṛntata sa papāta hataḥ sūtaḥ hārdikyasya mahā rathāt sātyakiḥ ca abhyagāt tasmāt sa tu bhīmam upādravat yuyudhānaḥ api rāja indra droṇa anīkāt viniḥsṛtaḥ prayayau tvaritaḥ tūrṇam kāmbojānām mahā camūm sa tatra bahubhiḥ śūraiḥ saṃniruddhaḥ mahā rathaiḥ na cacāla tadā rājan sātyakiḥ satya vikramaḥ saṃdhāya ca camūm droṇaḥ bhoje bhāram niveśya ca tathā tam anudhāvantam yuyudhānasya pṛṣṭhatas nyavārayanta saṃkruddhāḥ pāṇḍu sainye bṛhattamāḥ samāsādya tu hārdikyam rathānām pravaram ratham pāñcālāḥ vigata utsāhāḥ bhīmasena purogamāḥ vikramya vāritāḥ rājan vīreṇa kṛtavarmaṇā yatamānān tu tān sarvān īṣat vigata cetasaḥ abhitas tān śara ogheṇa klānta vāhān avārayat nigṛhītāḥ tu bhojena bhoja anīka īpsavaḥ raṇe atiṣṭhan ārya vat vīrāḥ prārthayantaḥ mahat yaśaḥ hārdikyam samare yattāḥ na śekuḥ prativīkṣitum uvāca vyūḍham evam yathānyāyam evam bahu ca saṃjaya nityam pūjitam asmābhiḥ abhikāmam ca naḥ sadā prauḍham ati adbhuta ākāram purastāt dṛḍha vikramam na ati vṛddham abālam ca na kṛśam na ati pīvaram laghu vṛtta āyata prāṇam sāra gātram anāmayam śastra grahaṇa vidyāsu bahuṣu pariniṣṭhitam nāgeṣu aśveṣu bahuśas ratheṣu ca parīkṣitam parīkṣya ca yathānyāyam vetanena upapāditam na goṣṭhyā na upacāreṇa na saṃbandha nimittataḥ kulīna ārya jana upetam tuṣṭa puṣṭam anuddhatam asmān abhisṛtaiḥ kāmāt sa balaiḥ sa padānugaiḥ mahā udadhim iva āpūrṇam āpagābhiḥ samantataḥ apakṣaiḥ pakṣi saṃkāśaiḥ rathaiḥ aśvaiḥ ca saṃvṛtam yodha akṣayya jalam bhīmam vāhana ūrmi taraṃgiṇam kṣepaṇī asi gadā śakti śara prāsa jhaṣa ākulam dhvaja bhūṣaṇa saṃbādham ratna paṭṭena saṃcitam droṇa gambhīra pātālam kṛtavarma mahā hradam gate sainya arṇavam bhittvā tarasā pāṇḍava ṛṣabhe tatra śeṣam na paśyāmi praviṣṭe savyasācini sindhurājam ca saṃprekṣya gāṇḍīvasya iṣu gocare kim tadā kuravaḥ kṛtyam vidadhuḥ kāla coditāḥ dāruṇa ekāyane kāle katham vā pratipedire grastān hi kauravān manye mṛtyunā tāta saṃgatān vikramaḥ hi raṇe teṣām na tathā dṛśyate adya vai akṣatau saṃyuge tatra praviṣṭau kṛṣṇa pāṇḍavau bhṛtāḥ ca bahavaḥ yodhāḥ parīkṣya eva mahā rathāḥ pūjitāḥ hi yathāśaktyā dāna māna āsanaiḥ mayā tathā putraiḥ ca mama tāta jñātibhiḥ ca sa bāndhavaiḥ te ca prāpya eva saṃgrāme nirjitāḥ savyasācinā śaineyena parāmṛṣṭāḥ kim anyat bhāgadheyataḥ rakṣyate yaḥ ca saṃgrāme ye ca saṃjaya rakṣiṇaḥ ekaḥ sādhāraṇaḥ panthāḥ rakṣyasya saha rakṣibhiḥ arjunam samare dṛṣṭvā saindhavasya agratas sthitam putraḥ mama bhṛśam mūḍhaḥ kim kāryam pratyapadyata sātyakim ca raṇe dṛṣṭvā praviśantam abhīta vat dṛṣṭvā kām vai dhṛtim yuddhe pratyapadyanta māmakāḥ dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇam tu dāśārham arjuna arthe vyavasthitam śinīnām ṛṣabham ca eva manye śocanti putrakāḥ dṛṣṭvā senām vyatikrāntām sātvatena arjunena ca palāyamānān ca kurūn manye śocanti putrakāḥ vidrutān rathinaḥ dṛṣṭvā nirutsāhān dviṣat jaye palāyane kṛta utsāhān manye śocanti putrakāḥ śūnyān kṛtān rathopasthān sātvatena arjunena ca hatān ca yodhān saṃdṛśya manye śocanti putrakāḥ vyaśva nāga rathān dṛṣṭvā tatra vīrān sahasraśas dhāvamānān raṇe vyagrān manye śocanti putrakāḥ vivīrān ca kṛtān aśvān virathān ca kṛtān narān tatra sātyaki pārthābhyām manye śocanti putrakāḥ mahā nāgān vidravataḥ dṛṣṭvā arjuna śara āhatān patitān patataḥ ca anyān manye śocanti putrakāḥ haya oghān nihatān dṛṣṭvā drāvyamāṇān tatas tatas raṇe sātvata pārthābhyām manye śocanti putrakāḥ patti saṃghān raṇe dṛṣṭvā dhāvamānān ca sarvaśas nirāśāḥ vijaye sarve manye śocanti putrakāḥ kṣaṇena dṛṣṭvā tau vīrau manye śocanti putrakāḥ saṃmūḍhaḥ asmi bhṛśam tāta śrutvā kṛṣṇa dhanaṃjayau praviṣṭau māmakam sainyam sātvatena saha acyutau tasmin praviṣṭe pṛtanām śinīnām pravare rathe bhoja anīkam vyatikrānte katham āsan hi kauravāḥ tathā droṇena samare nigṛhīteṣu pāṇḍuṣu droṇaḥ hi balavān śūraḥ kṛtāstraḥ dṛḍha vikramaḥ pāñcālāḥ tam mahā iṣvāsam pratyayudhyan katham raṇe baddhavairāḥ tathā droṇe dharmarāja jaya eṣiṇaḥ bhāradvājaḥ tathā teṣu kṛta vairaḥ mahā rathaḥ uvāca ātma aparādhāt saṃbhūtam vyasanam bharata ṛṣabha prāpya prākṛta vat vīra na tvam śocitum arhasi purā yat ucyase prājñaiḥ suhṛdbhiḥ vidura ādibhiḥ mā ahārṣīḥ pāṇḍavān rājan iti tat na tvayā śrutam suhṛdām hita kāmānām vākyam yaḥ na śṛṇoti ha yācitaḥ asi purā rājan dāśārhena śamam prati na ca tam labdhavān kāmam tvattaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ mahā yaśāḥ tava nirguṇa tām jñātvā pakṣapātam suteṣu ca dvaidhībhāvam tathā dharme pāṇḍaveṣu ca matsaram te jihmam abhiprāyam viditvā pāṇḍavān prati ārta pralāpān ca bahūn manuja adhipa sattama ātma aparādhāt su mahān prāptaḥ te vipulaḥ kṣayaḥ dṛśyate pṛṣṭhatas ca eva tvad mūlaḥ hi parājayaḥ ārta pralāpān iha yān idānīm kuruṣe nṛpa tasmāt adya sthiraḥ bhūtvā jñātvā lokasya nirṇayam śṛṇu yuddham yathā vṛttam ghoram devāsura upamam bhīmasena mukhāḥ pārthāḥ pratīyuḥ vāhinīm te āgacchataḥ tān sahasā kruddha rūpān saha anugān dadhāra ekaḥ raṇe pāṇḍūn kṛtavarmā mahā rathaḥ udvṛttam sāgaram yadvat velā vārayate sadā pāṇḍu sainyam tathā saṃkhye hārdikyaḥ samavārayat yat enam sahitāḥ pārthāḥ na aticakramuḥ āhave tatas bhīmaḥ tribhiḥ viddhvā kṛtavarmāṇam āyasaiḥ śaṅkham dadhmau mahā bāhuḥ harṣayan sarva pāṇḍavān sahadevaḥ tu viṃśatyā dharmarājaḥ ca pañcabhiḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ tribhiḥ ca api kṛtavarmāṇam ārdayat virāṭaḥ drupadaḥ ca eva yājñaseniḥ ca pañcabhiḥ śikhaṇḍī ca api hārdikyam viddhvā pañcabhiḥ āśugaiḥ punar vivyādha viṃśatyā sāyakānām hasan iva kṛtavarmā tatas rājan sarvatas tān mahā rathān atha enam chinna dhanvānam tvaramāṇaḥ mahā rathaḥ ājaghāna urasi kruddhaḥ saptatyā niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ bhīmasenam tathā dṛṣṭvā dharmarāja purogamāḥ visṛjantaḥ śarān ghorān kṛtavarmāṇam ārdayan tam tathā koṣṭhakīkṛtya ratha vaṃśena māriṣa vivyadhuḥ sāyakaiḥ hṛṣṭāḥ rakṣā artham māruteḥ mṛdhe pratilabhya tatas saṃjñām bhīmasenaḥ mahat balaḥ śaktim jagrāha samare hema daṇḍām ayasmayīm cikṣepa ca rathāt tūrṇam kṛtavarma ratham prati kṛtavarmāṇam abhitas prajajvāla su dāruṇā tām āpatatīm sahasā yuga anta agni sama prabhām dvābhyām śarābhyām hārdikyaḥ nicakarta dvidhā tadā sā chinnā patitā bhūmau śaktiḥ kanaka bhūṣaṇā śaktim vinihatām dṛṣṭvā bhīmaḥ cukrodha vai bhṛśam atha enam pañcabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ ājaghāna stanāntare bhojaḥ tu kṣata sarva aṅgaḥ bhīmasenena māriṣa śikhaṇḍinaḥ tatas kruddhaḥ kṣurapreṇa mahā rathaḥ śikhaṇḍī tu tatas kruddhaḥ chinne dhanuṣi sa tvaram bhrāmayitvā mahā carma cāmīkara vibhūṣitam tam asim preṣayām āsa kṛtavarma ratham prati nistriṃśam ca mahā prabham sa tasya sa śaram cāpam chittvā saṃkhye mahān asiḥ abhyagāt dharaṇīm rājñ cyutam jyotiḥ iva ambarāt etasmin eva kāle tu tvaramāṇāḥ mahā rathāḥ vivyadhuḥ sāyakaiḥ gāḍham kṛtavarmāṇam āhave viśīrṇam bharata śreṣṭha hārdikyaḥ para vīra hā śikhaṇḍinam ca vivyādha tribhiḥ pañcabhiḥ eva ca śikhaṇḍinam tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ viddhvā ciccheda kārmukam dhanuḥ anyat samādāya śikhaṇḍī tu mahā yaśāḥ avārayat kūrma nakhaiḥ āśugaiḥ hṛdika ātmajam tatas kruddhaḥ raṇe rājan hṛdikasya ātmasaṃbhavaḥ bhīṣmasya samare rājan mṛtyoḥ hetum mahātmanaḥ vidarśayan balam śūraḥ śārdūlaḥ iva kuñjaram tau diśāgaja saṃkāśau jvalitau iva pāvakau vidhunvānau dhanuḥ śreṣṭhe saṃdadhānau ca sāyakān tāpayantau śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ anyonyam tau mahā rathau kṛtavarmā tu rabhasam yājñasenim mahā ratham viddhvā iṣūṇām trisaptatyā punar vivyādha sapta visṛjan sa śaram cāpam mūrchayā abhipariplutaḥ tam viṣaṇṇam rathe dṛṣṭvā tāvakāḥ bharata ṛṣabha hārdikyam pūjayām āsuḥ vāsāṃsi ādudhuvuḥ ca ha śikhaṇḍinam tathā jñātvā hārdikya śara pīḍitam apovāha raṇāt yantā tvaramāṇaḥ mahā ratham sāditam tu rathopasthe dṛṣṭvā pārthāḥ śikhaṇḍinam parivavruḥ rathaiḥ tūrṇam kṛtavarmāṇam āhave tatra adbhutam param cakre kṛtavarmā mahā rathaḥ yat ekaḥ samare pārthān vārayām āsa sa anugān pārthān jitvā ajayat cedīn pāñcālān sṛñjayān api kekayān ca mahā vīryān kṛtavarmā mahā rathaḥ te vadhyamānāḥ samare hārdikyena sma pāṇḍavāḥ jitvā pāṇḍu sutān yuddhe bhīmasena purogamān hārdikyaḥ samare atiṣṭhat vidhūmaḥ iva pāvakaḥ te drāvyamāṇāḥ samare hārdikyena mahā rathāḥ vimukhāḥ samapadyanta śara vṛṣṭibhiḥ arditāḥ uvāca śṛṇuṣva ekamanāḥ rājan yat mām tvam paripṛcchasi drāvyamāṇe bale tasmin hārdikyena mahātmanā lajjayā avanate ca api prahṛṣṭaiḥ ca eva tāvakaiḥ dvīpaḥ yaḥ āsīt pāṇḍūnām agādhe gādham icchatām śrutvā tu ninadam bhīmam tāvakānām mahā āhave uvāca sārathim tatra krodha amarṣa samanvitaḥ kurute kadanam paśya pāṇḍu sainye hi amarṣitaḥ enam jitvā punar sūta yāsyāmi vijayam prati nimeṣa antara mātreṇa kṛtavarmāṇam abhyayāt kṛtavarmā tu hārdikyaḥ śaineyam niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ tatas su niśitam bhallam śaineyaḥ kṛtavarmaṇe preṣayām āsa samare śarān ca caturaḥ aparān pṛṣṭharakṣam tathā sūtam avidhyat niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ tatas tam viratham kṛtvā sātyakiḥ satya vikramaḥ senām asya ardayām āsa śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ sā abhajyata atha pṛtanā śaineya śara pīḍitā tatas prāyāt vai tvaritaḥ sātyakiḥ satya vikramaḥ śṛṇu rājan yat akarot tava sainyeṣu vīryavān atītya sa mahā rāja droṇa anīka mahā arṇavam parājitya ca saṃhṛṣṭaḥ kṛtavarmāṇam āhave yantāram abravīt śūraḥ śanais yāhi iti asaṃbhramam dṛṣṭvā tu tava tat sainyam ratha aśva dvipa saṃkulam padāti jana saṃpūrṇam abravīt sārathim punar yat etat megha saṃkāśam droṇa anīkasya savyatas ete hi bahavaḥ sūta durnivāryāḥ ca saṃyuge duryodhana samādiṣṭāḥ mad arthe tyakta jīvitāḥ rāja putrāḥ mahā iṣvāsāḥ sarve vikrānta yodhinaḥ na ca a jitvā raṇe hi etān śakyaḥ prāptum jayadrathaḥ na api pārthaḥ mayā sūta śakyaḥ prāptum katham cana ete tiṣṭhanti sahitāḥ sarve vidyāsu niṣṭhitāḥ trigartānām ratha udārāḥ suvarṇa vikṛta dhvajāḥ mām eva abhimukhāḥ vīrāḥ yotsyamānāḥ vyavasthitāḥ atra mām prāpaya kṣipram aśvān codaya sārathe tatas prāyāt śanais sūtaḥ sātvatasya mate sthitaḥ rathena āditya varṇena bhāsvareṇa patākinā tam ūhuḥ sāratheḥ vaśyāḥ valgamānāḥ haya uttamāḥ mārutasya gatau tulyāḥ candra kunda nibhāḥ śubhāḥ āpatantam ratham tam tu śaṅkha varṇaiḥ haya uttamaiḥ parivavruḥ tatas śūrāḥ gaja anīkena sarvatas kirantaḥ vividhān tīkṣṇān sāyakān laghu vedhinaḥ sātvataḥ api śitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ gaja anīkam ayodhayat vajra aśani sama sparśaiḥ vadhyamānāḥ śaraiḥ gajāḥ prādravan raṇam utsṛjya śini vīrya samīritaiḥ śīrṇa dantāḥ virudhirāḥ bhinna mastaka piṇḍakāḥ viśīrṇa karṇa āsya karāḥ viniyantṛ patākinaḥ saṃbhinna varma ghaṇṭāḥ ca saṃnikṛtta mahā dhvajāḥ hata ārohāḥ diśaḥ rājan bhejire bhraṣṭa kambalāḥ ruvantaḥ vividhān rāvān jalada upama nisvanāḥ nārācaiḥ vatsadantaiḥ ca sātvatena vidāritāḥ kṣarantaḥ asṛj tathā mūtram purīṣam ca pradudruvuḥ evam tat kuñjara anīkam yuyudhānena pātitam śaraiḥ agni arka saṃkāśaiḥ pradudrāva samantataḥ yattaḥ saṃprāpayan nāgam rajata aśva ratham prati rukma varṇa karaḥ śūraḥ tapanīya aṅgadaḥ śuciḥ kuṇḍalī mukuṭī śaṅkhī raktacandana rūṣitaḥ raktacandana digdha aṅgaḥ sa aṅgadaḥ saha kuṇḍalaḥ śirasā dhārayan dīptām tapanīya mayīm srajam urasā dhārayan niṣkam kaṇṭha sūtram ca bhāsvaram sātyakiḥ vārayām āsa velā iva udvṛttam arṇavam nāgam nivāritam dṛṣṭvā śaineyasya śara uttamaiḥ akrudhyata raṇe rājñ jalasaṃdhaḥ mahā balaḥ saṃprāpayat raṇe rājñ nāga rājam mahā balam tatas kruddhaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ mārgaṇaiḥ bhāra sādhanaiḥ sa vāryamāṇaḥ bāṇa oghaiḥ śaineyena atha vīryavān asyataḥ vṛṣṇi vīrasya nicakarta śarāsanam avidhyat māgadhaḥ vīraḥ pañcabhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ a cintayan vai sa śarān na atyartham saṃbhramāt balī dhanuḥ anyat samādāya tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti uvāca ha vivyādha ṣaṣṭyā su bhṛśam śarāṇām prahasan iva kṣurapreṇa ca pītena muṣṭideśe mahat dhanuḥ tomaram vyasṛjat tūrṇam sātyakim prati māriṣa abhyagāt dharaṇīm ghoraḥ śvasan iva mahā uragaḥ triṃśadbhiḥ viśikhaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ jalasaṃdham atāḍayat pragṛhya tu tatas khaḍgam jalasaṃdhaḥ mahā balaḥ bhrājati sma tatas khaḍgaḥ saṃprāptaḥ pṛthivī talam atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya sarva kāya avadāraṇam śāla skandha pratīkāśam indra aśani sama svanam tatas sa ābharaṇau bāhū kṣurābhyām mādhava uttamaḥ vasuṃdharā dharāt bhraṣṭau pañca śīrṣau iva uragau tatas su daṃṣṭram su hanu cāru kuṇḍalam unnasam kṣureṇa asya tṛtīyena śiraḥ ciccheda sātyakiḥ tat pātita śiraḥ bāhu kabandham bhīma darśanam jalasaṃdham nihatya ājau tvaramāṇaḥ tu sātvataḥ naiṣādam pātayām āsa gaja skandhāt viśām pate rudhireṇa avasikta aṅgaḥ jalasaṃdhasya kuñjaraḥ vilambamānam avahat saṃśliṣṭam param āsanam śara arditaḥ sātvatena mardamānaḥ sva vāhinīm ghoram ārta svaram kṛtvā vidudrāva mahā gajaḥ hāhākāraḥ mahān āsīt te sainyasya māriṣa jalasaṃdham hatam dṛṣṭvā vṛṣṇīnām ṛṣabheṇa ha vimukhāḥ ca abhyadhāvanta tava yodhāḥ samantataḥ palāyane kṛta utsāhāḥ nirutsāhāḥ dviṣat jaye etasmin antare rājan droṇaḥ śastrabhṛtām varaḥ sa hi pārthān raṇe yattān dadhāra ekaḥ mahā balaḥ jalasaṃdham hatam dṛṣṭvā putraḥ te kuru puṃgavaḥ tam udīrṇam tathā dṛṣṭvā śaineyam kuru puṃgavāḥ tatas pravavṛte yuddham kurūṇām sātvatasya ca uvāca sātvatasya raṇe karma yoddhum dṛṣṭvā mahā rathāḥ amṛṣyamāṇāḥ saṃyattāḥ śaineyam samupādravan te kirantaḥ śara vrātān sarve yattāḥ prahāriṇaḥ tvaramāṇāḥ mahā rāja yuyudhānam ayodhayan tam droṇaḥ saptasaptatyā jaghāna niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ durmarṣaṇaḥ dvādaśabhiḥ duḥsahaḥ daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ vikarṇaḥ ca api niśitaiḥ triṃśadbhiḥ kaṅka pattribhiḥ durmukhaḥ daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ tathā duḥśāsanaḥ aṣṭabhiḥ citrasenaḥ ca śaineyam dvābhyām vivyādha māriṣa duryodhanaḥ ca mahatā śara varṣeṇa mādhavam apīḍayat raṇe rājñ śūrāḥ ca anye mahā rathāḥ sātyakiḥ puṇḍarīkākṣaḥ hi astreṣu pariniṣṭhitaḥ bhāradvājam tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ duḥsaham navabhiḥ tathā vikarṇam pañcaviṃśatyā citrasenam ca sapta daśabhiḥ citrasenam ca vikarṇam pañcaviṃśatyā durmarṣaṇam dvādaśabhiḥ caturbhiḥ ca viviṃśatim tatas rukma aṅgadam cāpam vidhunvānaḥ mahā rathaḥ abhyayāt sātyakiḥ tūrṇam putram te mahā ratham rājānam sarva lokasya sarva śastrabhṛtām varam śaraiḥ abhyāhanat gāḍham tatas yuddham abhūt tayoḥ tatas pravavṛte yuddham kuru mādhava vīrayoḥ vimuñcantau śarān tīkṣṇān saṃdadhānau ca sāyakān śātakumbha maya āpīḍaḥ babhau yūpaḥ iva ucchritaḥ nirbhinnaḥ ca śaraiḥ tena dviṣatā kṣiprakāriṇā na amṛṣyata raṇe rājā śatroḥ vijaya lakṣaṇam atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya hema pṛṣṭham durāsadam vivyādha sātyakim tūrṇam sāyakānām śatena ha pīḍitam nṛpatim dṛṣṭvā te putrāḥ mahā rathāḥ sātvatam śara varṣeṇa chādayām āsuḥ añjasā duryodhanam ca tvaritaḥ vivyādha aṣṭabhiḥ āśugaiḥ prahasan ca asya ciccheda kārmukam ripu bhīṣaṇam hatvā tu caturaḥ vāhān caturbhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ sārathim pātayām āsa kṣurapreṇa mahā yaśāḥ hāhā bhūtam jagat ca āsīt dṛṣṭvā rājānam āhave grasyamānam sātyakinā khe somam iva rāhuṇā tam tu śabdam mahat śrutvā kṛtavarmā mahā rathaḥ vidhunvānaḥ dhanuḥ śreṣṭham codayan ca eva vājinaḥ bhartsayan sārathim ca ugram yāhi yāhi iti sa tvaraḥ tam āpatantam saṃprekṣya vyādita āsyam iva antakam kṛtavarmā rathena eṣa drutam āpatate śarī nihaniṣyāmi tam saṃkhe vṛṣṇi vīram ariṃdamam āsasāda raṇe bhojam pratimānam dhanuṣmatām kṛtavarmā tu śaineyam ṣaḍviṃśatyā samārpayat niśitaiḥ sāyakaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ yantāram ca asya sapta caturaḥ ca haya udārān caturbhiḥ parama iṣubhiḥ rukma aṅgadī rukma varmā rukma puṅkhān avākirat tatas aśītim śineḥ pautraḥ sāyakān kṛtavarmaṇe prāhiṇot tvarayā yuktaḥ draṣṭu kāmaḥ dhanaṃjayam saḥ atividdhaḥ balavatā śatruṇā śatru tāpanaḥ acalaḥ sa purā bhūtvā samakampata māriṣa triṣaṣṭyā caturaḥ asya aśvān sapta sārathim śaraiḥ vivyādha niśitaiḥ tūrṇam sātyakiḥ kṛtavarmaṇaḥ hata aśva sūte tu rathe sthitāya śini puṃgavaḥ suvarṇa puṅkham viśikham samādhāya sa sātyakiḥ praiṣayat sātyakaḥ bāṇam hārdikyasya nara ṛṣabhaḥ saḥ aviśat kṛtavarmāṇam yama daṇḍa upamaḥ śaraḥ abhyagāt dharaṇīm ugraḥ rudhireṇa samukṣitaḥ saṃjāta rudhiraḥ ca ājau sātvata iṣubhiḥ arditaḥ sa siṃha daṃṣṭraḥ jānubhyām āpannaḥ amita vikramaḥ śara arditaḥ sātyakinā rathopasthe nara ṛṣabhaḥ sahasrabāhoḥ sadṛśam akṣobhyam iva sāgaram nivārya kṛtavarmāṇam sātyakiḥ prayayau tatas didṛkṣuḥ sa hi vegena prāyāt yatra dhanaṃjayaḥ yuyudhe sātvataḥ rājan didṛkṣuḥ pāṇḍu nandanam khaḍga śakti dhanuḥ kīrṇām gaja aśva ratha saṃkulām pravartitā ugra rudhirām śataśas kṣatriya ṛṣabhaiḥ prekṣatām sarva sainyānām madhyena śini puṃgavaḥ abhyagāt vāhinīm bhittvā vṛtrahā iva āsurīm camūm samāśvāsya ca hārdikyaḥ gṛhya ca anyat mahat dhanuḥ uvāca kālyamāneṣu sainyeṣu śaineyena tatas tatas bhāradvājaḥ śara vrātaiḥ mahadbhiḥ samavākirat paśyatām sarva sainyānām bali vāsavayoḥ iva prāvartata mahā raudraḥ saṃgrāmaḥ loma harṣaṇaḥ tatas droṇaḥ śineḥ pautram citraiḥ sarva āyasaiḥ śaraiḥ tribhiḥ āśīviṣa ākāraiḥ lalāṭe samavidhyata taiḥ lalāṭa arpitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ yuyudhānaḥ tu a jihma gaiḥ vyarocata mahā rāja triśṛṅgaḥ iva parvataḥ tatas asya bāṇān aparān indra aśani sama svanān bhāradvājaḥ antara prekṣī preṣayām āsa saṃyuge tān droṇa cāpa nirmuktān dāśārhaḥ patataḥ śarān dvābhyām dvābhyām su puṅkhābhyām ciccheda parama astra vid tām asya laghu tām droṇaḥ samavekṣya viśām pate punar pañcāśatā iṣūṇām śatena ca samārpayat laghu tām yuyudhānasya lāghavena viśeṣayan tathā eva yuyudhānena sṛṣṭāḥ śata sahasraśas avākiran droṇa ratham śarāḥ rudhira bhojanāḥ viśeṣam na adhyagacchāma samāvāstām nara ṛṣabhau ājaghāna bhṛśam kruddhaḥ dhvajam ca niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ sārathim ca śatena eva bhāradvājasya paśyataḥ lāghavam yuyudhānasya dṛṣṭvā droṇaḥ mahā rathaḥ saptatyā sātyakim viddhvā turagān ca tribhiḥ tribhiḥ gadām jagrāha mahatīm bhāradvājāya ca akṣipat tām āpatantīm sahasā paṭṭa baddhām ayasmayīm vivyādha bahubhiḥ vīram bhāradvājam śilā śitaiḥ sa viddhvā samare droṇam siṃhanādam amuñcata tam vai na mamṛṣe droṇaḥ sarva śastrabhṛtām varaḥ tathā śaktim gṛhītvā tu rukma daṇḍām ayasmayīm tarasā preṣayām āsa mādhavasya ratham prati an āsādya tu śaineyam sā śaktiḥ kāla saṃnibhā bhittvā ratham jagāma ugrā dharaṇīm dāruṇa svanā tatas droṇam śini pautraḥ rājan vivyādha pattriṇā dakṣiṇam bhujam āsādya pīḍayan bharata ṛṣabha mādhavaḥ api mahā rāja brāhmaṇam pīḍayan iva sa rathopastham āsādya muhūrtam saṃnyaṣīdata cakāra sātyakiḥ rājñ tatra karma ati mānuṣam tatas śara śatena eva yuyudhānaḥ mahā rathaḥ avidhyat brāhmaṇam saṃkhye hṛṣṭa rūpaḥ viśām pate tasya droṇaḥ śarān pañca preṣayām āsa bhārata te tasya kavacam bhittvā papuḥ śoṇitam āhave sāyakān vyasṛjat ca api vīraḥ rukmaratham prati tatas droṇasya yantāram nipātya eka iṣuṇā bhuvi aśvān vyadrāvayat bāṇaiḥ hata sūtān mahātmanaḥ sa rathaḥ pradrutaḥ saṃkhye maṇḍalāni sahasraśas cakāra rājataḥ rājñ bhrājamānaḥ iva aṃśumant tatas sārathinam hatvā droṇasya apātayat rathāt śoṇa aśvāḥ ca ratham gṛhya dudruvuḥ sarvatodiśam abhidravata gṛhṇīta hayān droṇasya dhāvata iti sma cukruśuḥ sarve rāja putrāḥ sa rājakāḥ te sātyakim apāsya āśu rājan yudhi mahā rathāḥ tān dṛṣṭvā pradrutān sarvān sātvatena śara arditān vātāyamānaiḥ taiḥ aśvaiḥ hṛtaḥ vṛṣṇi śara arditaiḥ pāṇḍu pāñcāla saṃbhagnam vyūham ālokya vīryavān śaineye na akarot yatnam vyūhasya eva abhirakṣaṇe nivārya pāṇḍu pāñcālān droṇa agniḥ pradahan iva tasthau krodha agni saṃdīptaḥ kālasūryaḥ iva uditaḥ uvāca droṇam sa jitvā puruṣa pravīraḥ tathā eva hārdikya mukhān tvadīyān prahasya sūtam vacanam babhāṣe hatān nihantāsmi kirīṭamālinā hi aham sa bhīmaḥ saha pārṣatena kiran samantāt sahasā śarān balī samāpatat śyenaḥ iva āmiṣam yathā tam yāntam aśvaiḥ śaśi śaṅkha varṇaiḥ vigāhya sainyam puruṣa pravīram na aśaknuvan vārayitum samantāt āditya raśmi pratimam nara agryam amarṣa pūrṇaḥ tu ati citra yodhī śarāsanī kāñcana varma dhārī tayoḥ abhūt bharata saṃprahāraḥ su dāruṇaḥ tam samabhipraśaṃsan yodhāḥ tvadīyāḥ ca hi somakāḥ ca vṛtra indrayoḥ yuddham iva amara oghāḥ śaraiḥ su tīkṣṇaiḥ śataśas abhyavidhyat sudarśanaḥ sātvata mukhyam ājau anāgatān eva tu tān pṛṣatkān ciccheda bāṇaiḥ śini puṃgavaḥ api saṃprekṣya bāṇān nihatān tadānīm sudarśanaḥ sātyaki bāṇa vegaiḥ krodhāt didhakṣan iva tigma tejāḥ śarān amuñcat tapanīya citrān punar sa bāṇaiḥ tribhiḥ agni kalpaiḥ ākarṇapūrṇaiḥ niśitaiḥ su puṅkhaiḥ vivyādha deha āvaraṇam vibhidya te sātyakeḥ āviviśuḥ śarīram ājaghnivān tān rajata prakāśān caturbhiḥ aśvān caturaḥ prasahya sudarśanasya iṣu gaṇaiḥ su tīkṣṇaiḥ hayān nihatya āśu nanāda nādam sudarśanasya api śini pravīraḥ kṣureṇa ciccheda śiraḥ prasahya sa kuṇḍalam pūrṇa śaśi prakāśam bhrājiṣṇu vaktram nicakarta dehāt nihatya tam pārthiva putra pautram raṇe yadūnām ṛṣabhaḥ tarasvī mudā sametaḥ parayā mahātmā rarāja rājan surarāja kalpaḥ mudā mahatyā abhiyutaḥ mahātmā mahā āhave śakraḥ iva amara īśaḥ uvāca nirjitya kṛtavarmāṇam bhāradvājam ca saṃyuge tatas sa sātyakiḥ dhīmān mahātmā vṛṣṇi puṃgavaḥ jalasaṃdham nihatya ājau śūrasenam ca pārthivam mlecchān ca bahudhā rājñ kāśyaputram ca saṃyuge niṣādān taṃkaṇān ca eva kaliṅgān magadhān api kekayān śūrasenān ca tathā parvata vāsinaḥ kāmbojān yavanān ca eva vasātīn ca śibīn api kosalān magadhān ca eva yātudhānān sa tittirān etān ca anyān raṇe hatvā agacchat yuddhe sa sātyakiḥ rudhira ogha nadīm ghorām keśa śaivala śādvalām śakti grāha samākīrṇām chattra haṃsa upaśobhitām dustarām bhīrubhiḥ nityam śūra loka pravāhinīm ratha aśva nāga kalilam śara śakti ūrmi mālinam khaḍga matsyam gadā grāham śūra āyudha mahā svanam prāṇa apahāriṇam raudram vāditra utkruṣṭa nāditam yodhānām asukha sparśam durdharṣam ajaya eṣiṇām tīrṇāḥ sma dustaram tāta droṇa anīka mahā arṇavam jalasaṃdha balena ājau puruṣādaiḥ iva āvṛtam śaurya sattva bala upetam śūra vāṇija sevitam atas anyam pṛtanā śeṣam manye kunadikām iva tartavyām alpa salilām codaya aśvān asaṃbhramam na hi me jāyate trāsaḥ dṛṣṭvā sainyāni anekaśas vahneḥ iva pradīptasya grīṣme śuṣkam tṛṇa ulapam paśya pāṇḍava mukhyena yātām bhūmim kirīṭinā patti aśva ratha nāga oghaiḥ patitaiḥ viṣamīkṛtām kauśeya aruṇa saṃkāśam etat uddhūyate rajaḥ abhyāśa stham aham manye śvetāśvam kṛṣṇasārathim saḥ eṣa śrūyate śabdaḥ gāṇḍīvasya amita ojasaḥ viṣphāryamāṇasya raṇe gāṇḍīvasya amita ojasaḥ tādṛśaḥ śrūyate śabdaḥ sainyānām sāgara upamaḥ yādṛśāni nimittāni mama prādurbhavanti vai śanais viśrambhayan aśvān yāhi yattaḥ ari vāhinīm yatra ete sa tanutrāṇāḥ suyodhana purogamāḥ daṃśitāḥ krūra karmāṇaḥ kāmbojāḥ yuddha durmadāḥ śara bāṇa āsana dharāḥ yavanāḥ ca prahāriṇaḥ śakāḥ kirātāḥ daradāḥ barbarāḥ tāmraliptakāḥ mām eva abhimukhāḥ sarve tiṣṭhanti samara arthinaḥ etān sa ratha nāga aśvān nihatya ājau sa pattinaḥ idam durgam mahā ghoram tīrṇam eva upadhāraya uvāca droṇaḥ vā rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ kṛpaḥ madra īśvaraḥ api vā tathā api saṃbhramaḥ na syāt tvām āśritya mahā bhuja na ca me saṃbhramaḥ kaḥ cit bhūta pūrvaḥ kadā cana āyuṣman katareṇa tvā prāpayāmi dhanaṃjayam keṣām kruddhaḥ asi vārṣṇeya keṣām mṛtyuḥ upasthitaḥ keṣām saṃyamanīm adya gantum utsahate manaḥ ke tvām yudhi parākrāntam kāla antaka yama upamam dṛṣṭvā vikrama saṃpannam vidraviṣyanti saṃyuge keṣām vaivasvataḥ rājā smarate adya mahā bhuja uvāca śineḥ pautraḥ tathā uvāca yantāram hṛṣṭa mānasaḥ uvāca muṇḍān etān haniṣyāmi dānavān iva vāsavaḥ pratijñām pārayiṣyāmi kāmbojān eva mā vaha adya eṣām kadanam kṛtvā kṣipram yāsyāmi pāṇḍavam adya drakṣyanti me vīryam kauravāḥ sa suyodhanāḥ makaradhvajāt mahā muṣṭim kṛṣṇāt dureṣu pātanam jagāda saṃbhramaḥ yuddhe mokṣaḥ śūra ātmaja ātmajaḥ muṇḍānīke hate sūta sarva sainyeṣu ca asakṛt śrutvā virāvam bahudhā saṃtapsyati suyodhanaḥ adya pāṇḍava mukhyasya śvetāśvasya mahātmanaḥ ācāryaka kṛtam mārgam darśayiṣyāmi saṃyuge patitān ratha nāgeṣu dṛṣṭvā śocanti śatravaḥ dṛṣṭvā duryodhanaḥ rājā paścāttāpam gamiṣyati mad sāyaka cita aṅgānām rudhiram sravatām bahu sainikānām vadham dṛṣṭvā saṃtapsyati suyodhana rudhira ukṣita sarva aṅgān mad bāṇa śakalīkṛtān dṛṣṭvā nāga varān saṃkhye adya rāja sahasrāṇi nihatāni mayā raṇe dṛṣṭvā duryodhanaḥ rājā saṃtapsyati mahā mṛdhe adya sneham ca bhaktim ca pāṇḍaveṣu mahātmasu balam vīryam kṛtajña tvam mama jñāsyanti kauravāḥ hatvā rāja sahasrāṇi darśayiṣyāmi rājsu uvāca evam uktaḥ tadā sūtaḥ śikṣitān sādhu vāhinaḥ śaśāṅka saṃnikāśān vai vājinaḥ acūcudat bhṛśam coditaḥ vṛṣṇi vīreṇa sa sūtaḥ sādhu śikṣitaḥ tatas śaśāṅka saṃkāśān vikurvāṇān haya uttamān saindhavān coditāḥ yantrāḥ ūhuḥ te satyakam raṇe te pibantaḥ iva ākāśam yuyudhānam haya uttamāḥ prāpayan yavanān śīghram manaḥ pavana raṃhasaḥ sātyakim te samāsādya pṛtanāsu anivartinam yavanāḥ su mahā balāḥ teṣām iṣūn atha astrāṇi vegavat nata parvabhiḥ acchinat sātyakiḥ rājan na enam te prāpnuvan śarāḥ uccakarta śirāṃsi ugraḥ yavanānām bhujān api śaikyāyasāni varmāṇi kāṃsyāni ca samantataḥ bhittvā dehān tathā teṣām śarāḥ jagmuḥ mahī talam te hanyamānāḥ vīreṇa mlecchāḥ sātyakinā raṇe su pūrṇa āyata muktaiḥ tān avyavacchinna piṇḍitaiḥ pañca ṣaṭ sapta ca aṣṭau ca bibheda yavanān śaraiḥ kāmbojānām sahasraiḥ tu śakānām ca viśām pate śabarāṇām kirātānām barbarāṇām tathā eva ca padātibhiḥ ca vīreṇa sātvatena hate raṇe patitaiḥ abhavan rājan saṃvṛtāḥ raṇa bhūmayaḥ evam tat yavana anīkam hatvā chittvā ca mādhavaḥ agamya rūpām pṛthivīm māṃsa śoṇita kardamām kṛtavan tatra śaineyaḥ kṣapayan tāvakam balam dasyūnām sa śirastrāṇaiḥ śirobhiḥ lūna mūrdhajaiḥ tatra tatra mahī kīrṇā vibarhaiḥ aṇḍajaiḥ iva kabandhaiḥ saṃvṛtam sarvam tāmra abhraiḥ kham iva āvṛtam te sa āśvayānāḥ nihatāḥ samāvavruḥ vasuṃdharām teṣām astrāṇi bāṇān ca śaineyaḥ nata parvabhiḥ nicakarta mahā rāja yavanānām śirodharān te śarāḥ nata parvāṇaḥ yuyudhānena preritāḥ bhittvā dehān tathā teṣām patanti sma mahī tale te hanyamānāḥ vīrāḥ tu vṛṣṇi vīreṇa saṃyuge śastra āhatāḥ patanti urvyām kāmbojāḥ sa padānugāḥ kāmbojānām bhujaiḥ chinnaiḥ yavanānām ca bhārata alpa avaśiṣṭāḥ saṃbhagnāḥ kṛcchra prāṇāḥ vicetasaḥ jitāḥ saṃkhye mahā rāja yuyudhānena daṃśitāḥ pārṣṇibhiḥ ca kaśābhiḥ ca tāḍayantaḥ turaṃgamān yavanānām ca tat sainyam śakānām ca mahat balam sa tatas puruṣa vyāghraḥ sātyakiḥ satya vikramaḥ prahṛṣṭaḥ tāvakān jitvā sūtam yāhi iti acodayat tat tasya samare karma dṛṣṭvā anyaiḥ a kṛtam purā cāraṇāḥ saha gandharvāḥ pūjayām cakrire bhṛśam tam yāntam pṛṣṭhagoptāram arjunasya viśām pate cāraṇāḥ prekṣya saṃhṛṣṭāḥ tvadīyāḥ ca api apūjayan uvāca mṛgān vyāghraḥ iva ājighran te sainyam abhīṣayat rukma pṛṣṭham mahā vegam rukma candraka saṃkulam rukma aṅgada śirastrāṇaḥ rukma varma samāvṛtaḥ rukma dhvaja varaḥ śūraḥ meru śṛṅge iva ābabhau sa dhanuḥ maṇḍalaḥ saṃkhye tejaḥ bhāsvara raśmivān śaradi iva uditaḥ sūryaḥ nṛ sūryaḥ virarāja ha vṛṣabha skandha vikrāntaḥ vṛṣabha akṣaḥ nara ṛṣabhaḥ tāvakānām babhau madhye gavām madhye yathā vṛṣaḥ vyāghrāḥ iva jighāṃsantaḥ tvadīyāḥ abhyadravan raṇe sātyakim samare rājan parivavruḥ te ātmajāḥ droṇa anīkam atikrāntam bhoja anīkam ca dustaram jalasaṃdha arṇavam tīrtvā kāmbojānām ca vāhinīm hārdikya makarāt muktam tīrṇam vai sainya sāgaram parivavruḥ su saṃkruddhāḥ tvadīyāḥ sātyakim rathāḥ duryodhanaḥ citrasenaḥ duḥśāsana viviṃśatī śakuniḥ duḥsahaḥ ca eva yuvā durmarṣaṇaḥ krathaḥ anye ca bahavaḥ śūrāḥ śastravantaḥ durāsadāḥ pṛṣṭhatas sātyakim yāntam anvadhāvan amarṣitāḥ atha śabdaḥ mahān āsīt tava sainyasya māriṣa tān abhidravataḥ sarvān samīkṣya śini puṃgavaḥ mām eva abhimukham tūrṇam gaja aśva ratha pattimat nādayan vai diśaḥ sarvāḥ ratha ghoṣeṇa sārathe pṛthivīm ca antarikṣam ca kampayan sāgarān api etat bala arṇavam tāta vārayiṣye mahā raṇe paurṇamāsyām iva uddhūtam velā iva salilāśayam tūṇī carma asimat ghoram gaja aśva ratha saṃkulam udvṛttaḥ sāgaraḥ yadvat velām āśrayate tathā mām āsādya hi tiṣṭhanti yaudhāḥ śata sahasraśas eṣa sainyāni śatrūṇām vidhamāmi śitaiḥ śaraiḥ nihatān āhave paśya padāti aśva ratha dvipān mad śaraiḥ agni saṃkāśaiḥ videha asūn sahasraśas samīpam sainikāḥ te tu śīghram īyuḥ yuyutsavaḥ jahi ādravasva tiṣṭha iti paśya paśya iti vādinaḥ tān evam bruvataḥ vīrān sātyakiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ jaghāna tri śatān aśvān kuñjarān ca catur śatān prāvartata mahā rāja deva asura raṇa upamaḥ pratyagṛhṇāt śineḥ pautraḥ śaraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ pracchādyamānaḥ samare śara jālaiḥ sa vīryavān asaṃbhramam mahā rāja tāvakān avadhīt bahūn āścaryam tatra rāja indra su mahat dṛṣṭavan aham na āsīt moghaḥ śaraḥ kaḥ cit āsan sarve tanu chidaḥ ratha nāga aśva kalilaḥ padāti ūrmi samākulaḥ śaineya velām āsādya sthitaḥ sainya mahā arṇavaḥ saṃbhrānta nara nāga aśvam āvartata muhur muhur rathinaḥ patti nāgāḥ ca sādinaḥ ca śarāḥ hatāḥ babhrāma tatra tatra eva gāvaḥ śīta arditāḥ iva padātinam ratham nāgam sādinam turagam tathā aviddham tatra na adrākṣam yuyudhānasya sāyakaiḥ na tādṛś kadanam rājan kṛtavān tatra phalgunaḥ yādṛś kṣayam anīkānām akarot sātyakiḥ nṛpa vīta bhīḥ lāghava upetaḥ kṛti tvam saṃpradarśayan vivyādha sūtam niśitaiḥ caturbhiḥ caturaḥ hayān duḥśāsanaḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ vivyādha śini puṃgavam śakuniḥ pañcaviṃśatyā citrasenaḥ ca pañcabhiḥ utsmayan vṛṣṇi śārdūlaḥ tathā bāṇaiḥ samāhataḥ gāḍha viddhān arīn kṛtvā mārgaṇaiḥ saḥ ati tejanaiḥ duḥśāsanam ca viṃśatyā vivyādha śini puṃgavaḥ atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya syālaḥ te viśām pate aṣṭabhiḥ sātyakim viddhvā punar vivyādha pañcabhiḥ duḥśāsanaḥ ca daśabhiḥ duḥsahaḥ ca tribhiḥ śaraiḥ durmukhaḥ ca dvādaśabhiḥ rājñ vivyādha sātyakim tān sarvān sahitān śūrān yatamānān mahā rathān pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ punar vivyādha sātyakiḥ tatas sa rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ tava putrasya sārathim vātāyamānaiḥ taiḥ aśvaiḥ apānīyata saṃgarāt tatas tava sutāḥ rājan sainikāḥ ca viśām pate rājñaḥ ratham abhiprekṣya vidrutāḥ śataśas abhavan vidrutam tatra tat sainyam dṛṣṭvā bhārata sātyakiḥ avākirat śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ rukma puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ prayayau sātyakiḥ rājñ śvetāśvasya ratham prati tam prayāntam mahā bāhum tāvakāḥ prekṣya māriṣaiḥ dṛṣṭam ca adṛṣṭa vat kṛtvā kriyām anyām prayojayan tam śarān ādadānam ca rakṣamāṇam ca sārathim ātmānam mocayantam ca tāvakāḥ samapūjayan uvāca katham ca eṣām tathā yuddhe dhṛtiḥ āsīt mumūrṣatām śaineya caritam dṛṣṭvā sadṛśam savyasācinaḥ kim nu vakṣyanti te kṣātram sainya madhye parājitāḥ katham ca sātyakiḥ yuddhe vyatikrāntaḥ mahā yaśāḥ katham ca mama putrāṇām jīvatām tatra saṃjaya ati adbhutam idam tāta tvad sakāśāt śṛṇomi aham kruddhasya yuyudhānasya sarve tiṣṭhantu pāṇḍavāḥ yathā paśu gaṇān siṃhaḥ tadvat hantā sutān mama yuyudhānaḥ na śakitaḥ hantum yaḥ puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ na etat īdṛśakam yuddham kṛtavān tatra phalgunaḥ yādṛśam kṛtavan yuddham śineḥ naptā mahā yaśāḥ uvāca śṛṇuṣva avahitaḥ bhūtvā yat te vakṣyāmi bhārata śṛṇuṣva rājan saṃgrāmam nara vāji gaja kṣayam te punar saṃnyavartanta kṛtvā saṃśaptakān mithas parām yuddhe matim kṛtvā putrasya te śāsanāt trīṇi sādi sahasrāṇi duryodhana purogamāḥ śakāḥ kāmboja vāhlīkāḥ yavanāḥ pāradāḥ tathā kuṇindāḥ taṅgaṇa ambaṣṭhāḥ paiśācāḥ ca sa mandarāḥ abhyadravanta śaineyam śalabhāḥ pāvakam yathā yuktāḥ ca pārvatīyānām rathāḥ pāṣāṇa yodhinām śūrāḥ pañcaśatāḥ rājan śaineyam samupādravan dviradānām sahasreṇa dvi sāhasraiḥ ca vājibhiḥ śara varṣāṇi muñcantaḥ vividhāni mahā rathāḥ duḥśāsanaḥ mahā rāja sātyaktim paryavārayat avadhīt ca ratha anīkam dviradānām ca tat balam sādinaḥ ca eva tān sarvān dasyūn api ca sarvaśas akṣaiḥ ca bahudhā bhagnaiḥ īṣā daṇḍaka bandhuraiḥ kūbaraiḥ mathitaiḥ ca api dhvajaiḥ ca api nipātitaiḥ varmabhiḥ cāmaraiḥ ca eva vyavakīrṇā vasuṃdharā giri rūpa dharāḥ ca api patitāḥ kuñjara uttamāḥ tatra tatra dharā ākīrṇā śayānaiḥ parvata upamaiḥ jātāḥ danti varāḥ rājan śerate bahavaḥ hatāḥ kumudasya tathā nāgāḥ airāvata kula udbhavāḥ nihatāḥ satyakena ājau nārācaiḥ agni saṃnibhaiḥ vanāyu jān pārvatīyān kāmboja āraṭṭa bāhlikān nānā deśa samutthān ca nānā jātyān ca pattinaḥ teṣu prakālyamāneṣu dasyūn duḥśāsanaḥ abravīt tān ca api sarvān saṃprekṣya putraḥ duḥśāsanaḥ te pāṣāṇa yodhinaḥ śūrān pārvatīyān acodayat aśma yuddheṣu kuśalāḥ na etat jānāti sātyakiḥ tathā eva kuravaḥ sarve na aśma yuddha viśāradāḥ abhidravata mā bhaiṣṭa na vaḥ prāpsyati sātyakiḥ te pārvatīyāḥ rājānaḥ sarve pāṣāṇa pāṇayaḥ udyataiḥ yuyudhānasya sthitāḥ maraṇa kāṅkṣiṇaḥ kṣepaṇīyaiḥ tathā api anye sātvatasya vadha eṣiṇaḥ mlecchāḥ pipāsavaḥ prājñāḥ rājānam iva mantriṇaḥ teṣām āpatatām eva śilā yuddham cikīrṣatām sātyakiḥ pratisaṃdhāya triṃśatam prāhiṇot śarān tām aśma vṛṣṭim tumulām pārvatīyaiḥ samīritām bibheda uraga saṃkāśaiḥ nārācaiḥ śini puṃgavaḥ tebhiḥ aśma cūrṇaiḥ dīpyadbhiḥ khadyotānām iva vrajaiḥ prāyas sainyāni avadhyanta hāhā bhūtāni māriṣa tatas pañcaśatāḥ śūrāḥ samudyata mahā śilāḥ punar daśa śatāḥ ca anye śata sāhasriṇaḥ tathā te hanyamānāḥ samare sātvatena mahātmanā aśma vṛṣṭim mahā ghorām pātayanti sma sātvate pāṣāṇa yodhinaḥ śūrān yatamānān avasthitān tatas punar basta mukhaiḥ aśma vṛṣṭim samantataḥ ayaḥ hastaiḥ śūla hastaiḥ daradaiḥ ambaṣṭhaiḥ ca kuṇindaiḥ ca kṣiptām kṣiptām sa sātyakiḥ nārācaiḥ prativivyādha prekṣamāṇaḥ mahā balaḥ adrīṇām bhidyamānānām antarikṣe śitaiḥ śaraiḥ aśma cūrṇaiḥ samākīrṇāḥ manuṣyāḥ ca vayāṃsi ca na aśaknuvan avasthātum bhramaraiḥ iva daṃśitāḥ hata śiṣṭāḥ virudhirāḥ bhinna mastaka piṇḍikāḥ nirdhūtaiḥ ca karaiḥ nāgāḥ vyaṅgāḥ ca śataśas kṛtāḥ hatvā pañcaśatān yodhān sa kṣaṇena eva māriṣa aśmanām bhidyamānānām sāyakaiḥ śrūyate dhvaniḥ padma pattreṣu dhārāṇām patatīnām iva dhvaniḥ mādhavena ardyamānasya sāgarasya iva dāruṇaḥ tam śabdam tumulam śrutvā droṇaḥ yantāram abravīt eṣa sūta raṇe kruddhaḥ sātvatānām mahā rathaḥ pāṣāṇa yodhibhiḥ nūnam yuyudhānaḥ samāgataḥ pratyuvāca tatas yantā droṇam śastrabhṛtām varam āyuṣman vidravati eva kurūṇām sainyam āturam paśya yodhān raṇe bhinnān dhāvamānān tatas tatas ete ca sahitāḥ śūrāḥ pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha sthāne vā gamane vā api dūram yātaḥ ca sātyakiḥ te vadhyamānāḥ samare yuyudhānena tāvakāḥ yuyudhāna ratham tyaktvā droṇa anīkāya dudruvuḥ yaiḥ tu duḥśāsanaḥ sārdham rathaiḥ pūrvam nyavartata uvāca duḥśāsana ratham dṛṣṭvā samīpe paryavasthitam bhāradvājaḥ tatas vākyam duḥśāsanam atha abravīt duḥśāsana rathāḥ sarve kasmāt ete pravidrutāḥ rāja putraḥ bhavān atra rāja bhrātā mahā rathaḥ dāsī jitā asi dyūte tvam yathākāma carā bhava vāsasām vāhikā rājñaḥ bhrātuḥ jyeṣṭhasya me bhava na santi patayaḥ sarve te adya ṣaṇḍhatilaiḥ samāḥ duḥśāsana evam uktvā tvam pūrvam kasmāt palāyase svayam vairam mahat kṛtvā pāñcālaiḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha ekam sātyakim āsādya katham bhītaḥ asi saṃyuge na jānīṣe purā tvam tu gṛhṇan akṣān durodare śarāḥ hi ete bhaviṣyanti dāruṇa āśīviṣa upamāḥ apriyāṇām ca vacanam pāṇḍaveṣu viśeṣataḥ āśīviṣa samān pārthān kopayitvā kva yāsyasi śocyā iyam bhāratī senā rājā ca eva suyodhanaḥ yasya tvam karkaśaḥ bhrātā palāyana parāyaṇaḥ nanu nāma tvayā vīra dīryamāṇā bhaya arditā sva bāhu balam āsthāya rakṣitavyā hi anīkinī kaḥ anyaḥ sthāsyati saṃgrāme bhītaḥ bhīte vyapāśraye yadā gāṇḍīvadhanvānam bhīmasenam ca kaurava yamau ca yudhi draṣṭāsi tadā tvam kim kariṣyasi yudhi phalguna bāṇānām sūrya agni sama tejasām na tulyāḥ sātyaki śarāḥ yeṣām bhītaḥ palāyase pṛthivyām dhāvamānasya na saṃpaśyāmi te śamam yadi tāvat kṛtā buddhiḥ palāyana parāyaṇā pṛthivī dharmarājasya śamena eva pradīyatām yāvat phalguna nārācāḥ nirmukta uraga saṃnibhāḥ na āviśanti śarīram te tāvat saṃśāmya pāṇḍavaiḥ yāvat te pṛthivīm pārthāḥ hatvā bhrātṛ śatam raṇe na ākṣipanti mahātmānaḥ tāvat saṃśāmya pāṇḍavaiḥ kṛṣṇaḥ ca samara ślāghī tāvat saṃśāmya pāṇḍavaiḥ yāvat bhīmaḥ mahā bāhuḥ vigāhya mahatīm camūm sodarān te na mṛdnāti tāvat saṃśāmya pāṇḍavaiḥ mayā śamavatā ca uktaḥ rakṣa śeṣam suyodhana saṃśāmya vīra pārthaiḥ tvam rakṣa sarvān mahīkṣitaḥ pūrvam uktaḥ ca te bhrātā bhīṣmeṇa sa suyodhanaḥ ajeyāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ saṃkhye saumya saṃśāmya pāṇḍavaiḥ tava api śoṇitam bhīmaḥ pāsyati iti mayā śrutam kim bhīmasya na jānāsi vikramam tvam su bāliśa sa yuddhe dhṛtim āsthāya yattaḥ yudhyasva pāṇḍavaiḥ gaccha tūrṇam rathena eva tatra tiṣṭhati sātyakiḥ śrutam ca aśruta vat kṛtvā prāyāt yena sa sātyakiḥ droṇaḥ api rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ pāñcālān pāṇḍavān tathā praviśya ca raṇe droṇaḥ pāñcālānām varūthinīm drāvayām āsa yodhān vai śataśas atha sahasraśas tatas droṇaḥ mahā rāja nāma viśrāvya saṃyuge pāṇḍu pāñcāla matsyānām pracakre kadanam mahat tam jayantam anīkāni bhāradvājam tatas tatas pāñcāla putraḥ dyutimān vīraketuḥ samabhyayāt sa droṇam pañcabhiḥ viddhvā śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ nanāda balavān nādam tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt tatra adbhutam mahā rāja dṛṣṭavan asmi saṃyuge yat droṇaḥ rabhasam yuddhe pāñcālyam na abhyavartata saṃniruddham raṇe droṇam pāñcālāḥ vīkṣya māriṣa te śaraiḥ agni saṃkāśaiḥ tomaraiḥ ca mahādhanaiḥ nihatya tān bāṇa gaṇān droṇaḥ rājan samantataḥ mahā jaladharān vyomni mātariśvā iva yathā vāyuḥ mahā abhrāṇi vivāt nityam viyanti uta tatas śaram mahā ghoram sūrya pāvaka saṃnibham sa bhittvā tu śaraḥ rājan pāñcālyam kula nandanam abhyagāt dharaṇīm tūrṇam lohita ārdraḥ jvalan iva tatas apatat rathāt tūrṇam pāñcālyaḥ kula nandanaḥ parvata agrāt iva mahān campakaḥ vāyu pīḍitaḥ pāñcālāḥ tvaritāḥ droṇam samantāt paryavārayan tathā citrarathaḥ ca eva bhrātṛ vyasana karṣitāḥ muñcantaḥ śara varṣāṇi tapānte jaladāḥ iva adṛśyam samare cakruḥ bhāradvājam su dhanvinaḥ krodham āhārayat teṣām abhāvāya dvijarṣabhaḥ tatas śara mayam jālam droṇaḥ teṣām avāsṛjat te hanyamānāḥ droṇasya śaraiḥ ākarṇa coditaiḥ tān vimūḍhān raṇe droṇaḥ prahasan iva bhārata vyaśva sūta rathān cakre kumārān kupitaḥ raṇe tathā aparaiḥ su niśitaiḥ bhallaiḥ teṣām mahā yaśāḥ puṣpāṇi iva vicinvan hi sa uttamāṅgāni apātayat nyakṛntat ca uttamāṅgāni yathā tāla vanāni ha devāsure purā yuddhe yathā daiteya dānavāḥ tān nihatya raṇe rājan bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān kārmukam bhrāmayām āsa hema pṛṣṭham durāsadam bhrāmayan bahudhā cāpam haṃsa pṛṣṭham durānanam pāñcālān nihatān dṛṣṭvā deva kalpān mahā rathān dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ bhṛśam kruddhaḥ netrābhyām pātayan jalam pāñcālyena raṇe dṛṣṭvā droṇam āvāritam śaraiḥ saṃchādyamānaḥ bahudhā pārṣatena mahātmanā tatas droṇam mahā rāja pāñcālyaḥ krodha mūrchitaḥ sa gāḍha viddhaḥ balinā bhāradvājaḥ mahā yaśāḥ tam vai tathāgatam dṛṣṭvā dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ parākramī samutsṛjya dhanuḥ tūrṇam asim jagrāha vīryavān āruroha ratham tūrṇam bhāradvājasya māriṣa āsannam āgatam dṛṣṭvā dhṛṣṭadyumnam jighāṃsayā yodhayām āsa samare dhṛṣṭadyumnam mahā ratham te hi vaitastikāḥ nāma śarāḥ āsanna yodhinaḥ droṇasya viditāḥ rājan dhṛṣṭadyumnam avākṣipan avaplutya rathāt tūrṇam bhagna vegaḥ parākramī kṛta saṃkalpa bhūyiṣṭhaḥ prādravat sva ratham prati vivyādha samare droṇam dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā rathaḥ droṇaḥ ca api mahā rāja śaraiḥ vivyādha pārṣatam tat adbhutam abhūt yuddham droṇa pāñcālayoḥ tadā trailokya kāṅkṣiṇoḥ āsīt śakra prahrādayoḥ iva maṇḍalāni vicitrāṇi yamakāni itarāṇi ca mohayantau manāṃsi ājau yodhānām droṇa pārṣatau sṛjantau śara varṣāṇi varṣāsu iva balāhakau kṣatriyāḥ ca mahā rāja ye ca anye tatra sainikāḥ avaśyam samare droṇaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnena saṃgataḥ vaśam eṣyati naḥ rājñaḥ pāñcālāḥ iti cukruśuḥ śiraḥ pracyāvayām āsa phalam pakvam taroḥ iva tatas te pradrutāḥ vāhāḥ rājan tasya mahātmanaḥ teṣu pradravamāṇeṣu pāñcālān sṛñjayān tathā vijitya pāṇḍu pāñcālān bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān svam vyūham punar āsthāya sthiraḥ abhavat ariṃdamaḥ uvāca tatas duḥśāsanaḥ rājñ śaineyam samupādravat sarvatas bharata śreṣṭha visṛjan sāyakān bahūn tam āpatantam ālokya sātyaki kauravam raṇa abhidrutya mahā bāhuḥ chādayām āsa sāyakaiḥ te chādyamānāḥ bāṇa oghaiḥ duḥśāsana purogamāḥ sātyakim ca śatena ājau viddhvā nādam mumoca saḥ ratham sūtam dhvajam tam ca cakre adṛśyam ajihmagaiḥ kiran śara sahasrāṇi parjanyaḥ iva vṛṣṭimān sa viddhvā sātyakim ṣaṣṭyā tathā ṣoḍaśabhiḥ śaraiḥ sa tu duḥśāsanam vīraḥ sāyakaiḥ āvṛṇot bhṛśam maśakam samanuprāptam ūrṇanābhiḥ iva ūrṇayā tvaran samāvṛṇot bāṇaiḥ duḥśāsanam amitra jit dṛṣṭvā duḥśāsanam rājā tathā śara śata ācitam trigartān codayām āsa yuyudhāna ratham prati te agacchan yuyudhānasya samīpam krūra kāriṇaḥ trigartānām tri sāhasrāḥ rathāḥ yuddha viśāradāḥ sthirām kṛtvā matim yuddhe bhūtvā saṃśaptakāḥ mithas teṣām prayatatām yuddhe śara varṣāṇi muñcatām yodhān pañcaśatān mukhyān agra anīke vyapothayat te apatanta hatāḥ tūrṇam śini pravara sāyakaiḥ mahā māruta vegena rugṇāḥ iva mahā drumāḥ hayaiḥ ca kanaka āpīḍaiḥ patitaiḥ tatra medinī śaineya śara saṃkṛttaiḥ śoṇita ogha pariplutaiḥ aśobhata mahā rāja kiṃśukaiḥ iva puṣpitaiḥ te vadhyamānāḥ samare yuyudhānena tāvakāḥ trātāram na adhyagacchanta paṅka magnāḥ iva dvipāḥ bhayāt pataga rājasya gartāni iva mahā uragāḥ hatvā pañcaśatān yodhān śaraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ tatas tān hata vidhvastān kṛtvā yodhān sahasraśas tam prayāntam nara śreṣṭham putraḥ duḥśāsanaḥ te vivyādha navabhiḥ tūrṇam śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ sa tu tam prativivyādha pañcabhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ śaineyaḥ te putram tu viddhvā pañcabhiḥ āśugaiḥ tatas duḥśāsanaḥ kruddhaḥ vṛṣṇi vīrāya gacchate sarva pāraśavīm śaktim visasarja jighāṃsayā tām tu śaktim tadā ghorām te putrasya sātyakiḥ ciccheda śatadhā rājan niśitaiḥ kaṅka pattribhiḥ sātyakim daśabhiḥ viddhvā siṃhanādam nanāda ha śaraiḥ agni śikhā ākāraiḥ ājaghāna stanāntare tribhiḥ eva mahābhāgaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ sarva āyasaiḥ tīkṣṇa vaktraiḥ aṣṭābhiḥ vivyadhe punar duḥśāsanaḥ tu viṃśatyā sātyakim pratyavidhyata preṣayām āsa vīrāya gṛddhra pakṣān śilā śitān sātvataḥ api mahā rāja tam vivyādha stanāntare tatas asya vāhān niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ jaghne mahā rathaḥ sārathim ca su saṃkruddhaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ ciccheda viśikhaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ tathā ubhau pārṣṇisārathī nimeṣa mātreṇa śaraiḥ ubhau ca prāṣṭhi sārathī tam prāptam api na iyeṣa hantum duḥśāsanam raṇe bhīmasenena hi vadhaḥ sutānām te bhārata pratijñātaḥ sabhā madhye sarveṣām eva saṃyuge tathā duḥśāsanam jitvā sātyakiḥ saṃyuge prabho uvāca kim tasyām mama senāyām na āsan ke cid mahā rathāḥ ye tathā sātyakim yāntam na eva aghnan na api avārayan yat kṛtam vṛṣṇi vīreṇa karma śaṃsasi me raṇe vṛṣṇi andhaka pravīrasya śrutvā mama vyathitam manaḥ atha vā śūnyam āsīt tat yena yātaḥ sa sātyakiḥ ekaḥ vai bahulāḥ senāḥ pramṛdnan puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ na santi tasmāt putrāḥ me yathā saṃjaya bhāṣase katham ca yudhyamānānām apakrāntaḥ mahātmanām ekaḥ bahūnām śaineyaḥ tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya uvāca rājan senā samudyogaḥ ratha nāga aśva pattimān tumulaḥ tava sainyānām yuga anta sadṛśaḥ abhavat āhṇikeṣu samūheṣu te sainyasya mānada tatra devāḥ sma bhāṣante cāraṇāḥ ca samāgatāḥ etat antāḥ samūhāḥ vai bhaviṣyanti mahī tale na ca eva tādṛśaḥ kaḥ cit vyūhaḥ āsīt viśām pate uddhṛtā pṛthivī nūnam yuddha hetoḥ samāgataiḥ iti tatra janāḥ sma āhuḥ dṛṣṭvā tām jana saṃsadam caṇḍa vāta abhipannānām samudrāṇām iva svanaḥ pārthivānām sametānām bahūni āsan narottama tvad bale pāṇḍavānām ca sahasrāṇi śatāni ca tāvakānām tadā hi āsan prayutāni arbudāni ca tathā eva rājan pāṇḍūnām sahasrāṇi sahasraśas saṃrabdhānām pravīrāṇām samare dṛḍha karmaṇām tatra āsīt su mahān śabdaḥ tumulaḥ loma harṣaṇaḥ pāṇḍavānām kurūṇām ca garjatām itaretaram kṣveḍāḥ kilakilā śabdāḥ tatra āsan vai sahasraśas bherī śabdāḥ ca tumulāḥ bāṇa śabdāḥ ca bhārata anyonyam nighnatām ca eva narāṇām śuśruve svanaḥ atha akrandat bhīmasenaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca māriṣa nakulaḥ sahadevaḥ ca dharmarājaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ praviṣṭau ari senām hi vīrau mādhava pāṇḍavau tayoḥ abhāve kuravaḥ kṛtārthāḥ syuḥ vayam ji yatra yātau mahātmanau tūrṇam parapuraṃjayau te yūyam sahitāḥ bhūtvā tūrṇam eva bala arṇavam kṣobhayadhvam mahā vegāḥ pavanāḥ sāgaram yathā bhīmasenena te rājan pāñcālyena ca coditāḥ ājaghnuḥ kauravān saṃkhye tyaktvā asūn ātmanaḥ priyān svarga artham mitra kārya artham na abhyarakṣanta jīvitam āryām yuddhe matim kṛtvā yuddhāya eva upatasthire hatvā sarvāṇi sainyāni prāyāt sātyakiḥ arjunam kavacānām prabhāḥ tatra sūrya raśmi vicitritāḥ dṛṣṭīḥ saṃkhye sainikānām pratijaghnuḥ samantataḥ tathā prayat pāṇḍaveyeṣu nirbhayaḥ sa saṃnipātaḥ tumulaḥ teṣām tasya ca bhārata uvāca kaccit duryodhanaḥ sūta na akārṣīt pṛṣṭhatas raṇam ekasya ca bahūnām ca saṃnipātaḥ mahā āhave viśeṣataḥ nṛpatinā viṣamaḥ pratibhāti me ekaḥ bahūn samāsādya kaccit na āsīt parāṅmukhaḥ uvāca rājan saṃgrāmam āścaryam te putrasya bhārata ekasya ca bahūnām ca śṛṇuṣva gadataḥ adbhutam duryodhanena sahasā pāṇḍavā pṛtanā raṇe tathā senām kṛ dṛṣṭvā tava putreṇa kaurava bhīmasena purogāḥ tam pāñcālāḥ samupādravan virāṭa drupadau ṣaḍbhiḥ śatena ca śikhaṇḍinam dhṛṣṭadyumnam ca viṃśatyā dharmaputram ca sapta śataśas ca aparān yodhān sa dvipān ca rathān raṇe na saṃdadhan vimuñcan vā maṇḍalīkṛta kārmukaḥ adṛśyata ripūn nighnan śikṣayā astra balena ca tasya tān nighnataḥ śatrūn hema pṛṣṭham mahat dhanuḥ bhallābhyām pāṇḍavaḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ tridhā ciccheda māriṣa ajastram maṇḍalībhūtam dadṛśuḥ samare janāḥ tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā bhallābhyām acchinat dhanuḥ vivyādha ca enam bahubhiḥ samyak astaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ varmāṇi āśu samāsādya te bhagnāḥ kṣitim āviśan tatas pramuditāḥ pārthāḥ parivavruḥ yudhiṣṭhiram yathā vṛtra vadhe devāḥ mudā śakram mahā ṛṣibhiḥ atha duryodhanaḥ rājā dṛḍham ādāya kārmukam tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti rājānam bruvan pāṇḍavam abhyayāt tam tathā vādinam rājan tava putram mahā ratham pratyudyayuḥ pramuditāḥ pāñcālāḥ jaya gṛddhinaḥ tān droṇaḥ pratijagrāha parīpsan yudhi pāṇḍavam caṇḍa vāta uddhutān meghān sa jalān acalaḥ yathā saṃprahṛṣṭaḥ tu sahasā tava sainya arṇavam prati tatra rājan mahān āsīt saṃgrāmaḥ bhūri vardhanaḥ pāṇḍavānām mahā bāho tāvakānām ca saṃyuge tatas śabdaḥ mahān āsīt punar yena dhanaṃjayaḥ arjunasya mahā bāho tāvakānām ca dhanvinām droṇasya api paraiḥ sārdham vyūha dvāre mahā raṇe evam eṣa kṣayaḥ vṛttaḥ pṛthivyām pṛthivīpate rudrasya ākrīḍa saṃkāśaḥ saṃhāraḥ sarva dehinām uvāca aparāhṇe mahā rāja saṃgrāmaḥ samapadyata śoṇa aśvam ratham āsthāya nara vīraḥ samāhitaḥ samare abhyadravat pāṇḍūn javam āsthāya madhyamam citra puṅkhaiḥ śitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ kalaśa uttama saṃbhavaḥ jaghāna somakān rājan sṛñjayān kekayān api varān varān hi yodhānām vicinvan iva bhārata akrīḍata raṇe rājan bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān tam abhyayāt bṛhatkṣatraḥ kekayānām mahā rathaḥ bhrātṝṇām pañcamaḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ spardhamānaḥ mahā rathaḥ bhrātṝṇām vīra pañcānām jyeṣṭhaḥ samara karkaśaḥ vimuñcan viśikhān tīkṣṇān ācāryam chādayan bhṛśam tasya droṇaḥ mahā rāja svarṇa puṅkhān śilā śitān preṣayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ sāyakān daśa sapta ca tān tu droṇa dhanuḥ muktān ghorān āśīviṣa upamān ekaikam daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ yudhi ciccheda hṛṣṭa vat tasya tat lāghavam dṛṣṭvā prahasan dvijasattamaḥ preṣayām āsa viśikhān aṣṭau saṃnata parvṇaḥ preṣayat sa śarān aṣṭau sahasram ca punar punar tān dṛṣṭvā patataḥ śīghram droṇa cāpa cyutān śarān bṛhatkṣatreṇa tat karma kṛtam dṛṣṭvā su duṣkaram tatas droṇaḥ mahā rāja kekayam vai viśeṣayan prāduścakre raṇe divyam brāhmam astram mahā tapāḥ brāhmeṇa eva mahā bāhuḥ āhave samudīritam brāhmena astreṇa tat muktam brāhmam astram viśām pate vivyādha brāhmaṇam ṣaṣṭyā svarṇa puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ tam droṇaḥ dvipadām śreṣṭhaḥ nārācena samarpayat kṛṣṇasarpaḥ yathā muc valmīkam nṛpa sattama tathā abhyagāt mahīm bāṇaḥ bhittvā kaikeyam āhave saḥ atividdhaḥ mahā rāja droṇena astra vidā bhṛśam krodhena mahatā āviṣṭaḥ vyāvṛtya nayane śubhe droṇam vivyādha saptatyā svarṇa puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ droṇaḥ tu bahudhā viddhaḥ bṛhatkṣatreṇa māriṣa asṛjat viśikhān tīkṣṇān kekayasya ratham prati vyākulīkṛtya tam droṇaḥ bṛhatkṣatram mahā ratham sārathim ca asya bāṇena rathanīḍāt apāharat dvābhyām dhvajam ca chattram ca chittvā bhūmau apātayat vyasṛjat sāyakam tīkṣṇam kekayam prati bhārata bhrātṝṇām pañcamaḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ mahā bala parākramaḥ sa gāḍha viddhaḥ tena āśu mahā rāja stanāntare rathāt puruṣa śārdūlaḥ saṃbhinna hṛdayaḥ apatat tatas sādhu visṛṣṭena nārācena dvijarṣabhaḥ hṛdi avidhyat bṛhatkṣatram bṛhatkṣatre hate rājan kekayānām mahā rathe śaiśupāliḥ su saṃkruddhaḥ yantāram idam abravīt sārathe yāhi yatra eṣa droṇaḥ tiṣṭhati daṃśitaḥ vinighnan kekayān sarvān pāñcālānām ca vāhinīm tasya tat vacanam śrutvā sārathiḥ rathinām varam droṇāya prāpayām āsa kāmbojaiḥ javanaiḥ hayaiḥ dhṛṣṭaketuḥ ca cedīnām ṛṣabhaḥ ati bala uditaḥ sahasā prāpatat droṇam pataṃgaḥ iva pāvakam saḥ abhyavidhyat tatas droṇam ṣaṣṭyā sa aśva ratha dhvajam punar ca anyaiḥ śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ suptam vyāghram tudan iva atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya śaiśupāliḥ mahā rathaḥ vivyādha sāyakaiḥ droṇam punar su niśitaiḥ dṛḍhaiḥ tasya droṇaḥ hayān hatvā sārathim ca mahā balaḥ sāratheḥ ca śiraḥ kāyāt cakarta prahasan iva atha enam pañcaviṃśatyā sāyakānām samārpayat gadām cikṣepa saṃkruddhaḥ bhāradvāja ratham prati bhāradvājāya cikṣepa ruṣitām iva pannagīm tām āpatantīm sahasā ghora rūpām bhaya āvahām aśmasāra mayīm gurum tapanīya vibhūṣitām sā papāta gadā bhūmau bhāradvājena sāditā gadām vinihatām dṛṣṭvā dhṛṣṭaketuḥ amarṣaṇaḥ tomaram vyasṛjat tūrṇam śaktim ca kanaka ujjvalām tomaram tu tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ droṇaḥ chittvā mahā mṛdhe śaktim ciccheda sahasā kṛtahastaḥ mahā balaḥ tatas asya viśikham tīkṣṇam vadha artham vadha kāṅkṣiṇaḥ preṣayām āsa samare bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān abhyagāt dharaṇīm bāṇaḥ haṃsaḥ padma saraḥ yathā sa gāḍha viddhaḥ tena āśu hṛdi rājñ mahā rathaḥ papāta ca rathāt tūrṇam dhṛṣṭaketuḥ mahā yaśāḥ pataṃgam hi graset cāṣaḥ yathā rājan bubhukṣitaḥ tathā droṇaḥ agrasat śūraḥ dhṛṣṭaketum mahā mṛdhe nihate cedi rāje tu tat khaṇḍam pitryam āviśat mahā vyāghraḥ mahā araṇye mṛga śāvam yathā balī teṣu prakṣīyamāṇeṣu pāṇḍaveyeṣu bhārata jarāsaṃdha sutaḥ vīraḥ svayam droṇam upādravat sa tu droṇam mahā rāja chādayan sāyakaiḥ śitaiḥ adṛśyam akarot tūrṇam jaladaḥ bhāskaram yathā tasya tat lāghavam dṛṣṭvā droṇaḥ kṣatriya mardanaḥ vyasṛjat sāyakān tūrṇam śataśas atha sahasraśas chādayitvā raṇe droṇaḥ ratha stham rathinām varam jārāsaṃdhim atho jaghne miṣatām sarva dhanvinām yaḥ yaḥ sma līyate droṇam tam tam droṇaḥ antaka upamaḥ ādatta sarva bhūtāni prāpte kāle yathā antakaḥ tatas droṇaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ nāma viśrāvya saṃyuge śaraiḥ aneka sāhasraiḥ pāṇḍaveyān vyamohayat tatas droṇa aṅkitāḥ bāṇāḥ svarṇa puṅkhāḥ śilā śitāḥ narān nāgān hayān ca eva nijaghnuḥ sarvatas raṇe te vadhyamānāḥ droṇena śakreṇa iva mahā asurāḥ samakampanta pāñcālāḥ gāvaḥ śīta arditāḥ iva tatas niṣṭānakaḥ ghoraḥ pāṇḍavānām ajāyata pratāpyamānāḥ sūryeṇa hanyamānāḥ ca sāyakaiḥ anvapadyanta pāñcālāḥ tadā saṃtrasta cetasaḥ mohitāḥ śara varṣeṇa bhāradvājasya saṃyuge ūru grāha gṛhītāḥ hi pāñcālānām mahā rathāḥ cedayaḥ ca mahā rāja sṛñjayāḥ somakāḥ tathā abhyadravanta saṃhṛṣṭāḥ bhāradvājam yuyutsayā bruvantaḥ ca raṇe anyonyam cedi pāñcāla sṛñjayāḥ yatantaḥ puruṣa vyāghrāḥ sarva śaktyā mahā dyutim ninīṣantaḥ raṇe droṇam yamasya sadanam prati yatamānān tu tān vīrān bhāradvājaḥ śilīmukhaiḥ yamāya preṣayām āsa cedi mukhyān viśeṣataḥ teṣu prakṣīyamāṇeṣu cedi mukhyeṣu bhārata pāñcālāḥ samakampanta droṇa sāyaka pīḍitāḥ prākrośan bhīmasenam te dhṛṣṭadyumna ratham prati dṛṣṭvā droṇasya karmāṇi tathārūpāṇi māriṣa brāhmaṇena tapaḥ nūnam caritam duścaram mahat droṇa astram agni saṃsparśam praviṣṭāḥ kṣatriya ṛṣabhāḥ yathābalam yathotsāham yathāsattvam mahā dyutiḥ teṣām tat vacanam śrutvā kṣatradharmā vyavasthitaḥ balaḥ sa saṃrabdhataraḥ bhūtvā droṇaḥ kṣatriya mardanaḥ tatra ādhāya śaram tīkṣṇam bhāra ghnam vimalam dṛḍham ākarṇapūrṇam ācāryaḥ balavān abhyavāsṛjat sa jīvitam upādāya dhārṣṭadyumneḥ śara uttamaḥ sa hatvā kṣatradharmāṇam jagāma dharaṇī talam atha droṇam samārohat cekitānaḥ mahā rathaḥ vyasṛjat samare bāṇān pratyamitra jighāṃsayā sa droṇam daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ pratyavidhyat stanāntare tasya ācāryaḥ ṣoḍaśabhiḥ avidhyat dakṣiṇam bhujam dhvajam ṣoḍaśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ yantāram ca asya sapta tasya sūte hate te aśvāḥ ratham ādāya vidrutāḥ samare śara saṃvītāḥ bhāradvājena māriṣa cekitāna ratham dṛṣṭvā vidrutam hata sārathim pāñcālān pāṇḍavān ca eva mahat bhayam atha āviśat tān sametān raṇe śūrān cedi pāñcāla sṛñjayān samantāt drāvayan droṇaḥ bahu aśobhata māriṣa ākarṇa palitaḥ śyāmaḥ vayasā aśītikāt paraḥ raṇe paryacarat droṇaḥ vṛddhaḥ ṣoḍaśa varṣa vat lubdhaḥ ayam kṣatriyān hanti vyāghraḥ kṣudra mṛgān iva kṛcchrān duryodhanaḥ lokān pāpaḥ prāpsyati durmatiḥ yasya lobhāt vinihatāḥ samare kṣatriya ṛṣabhāḥ śataśas śerate bhūmau nikṛttāḥ go vṛṣāḥ iva rudhireṇa parīta aṅgāḥ evam uktvā mahā rāja drupadaḥ akṣauhiṇī patiḥ uvāca vyūheṣu āloḍyamāneṣu pāṇḍavānām tatas tatas su dūram anvayuḥ pārthāḥ pāñcālāḥ saha somakaiḥ vartamāne tathā raudre saṃgrāme loma harṣaṇe pāñcāleṣu ca kṣīṇeṣu vadhyamāneṣu pāṇḍuṣu na apaśyat śaraṇam kim cit dharmarājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tatra avekṣya diśaḥ sarvāḥ savyasāci didṛkṣayā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ dadarśa atha na eva pārtham na mādhavam saḥ apaśyat nara śārdūlam vānara ṛṣabha lakṣaṇam gāṇḍīvasya ca nirghoṣam aśṛṇvān vyathita indriyaḥ apaśyan sātyakim ca api vṛṣṇīnām pravaram ratham cintayā abhiparīta aṅgaḥ dharmarājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ na adhyagacchat tadā śāntim tau apaśyān nara ṛṣabhau loka upakrośa bhīru tvāt dharmarājaḥ mahā yaśāḥ padavīm preṣitaḥ ca eva phalgunasya mayā raṇe śaineyaḥ sātyakiḥ satyaḥ mitrāṇām abhayaṃkaraḥ tat idam hi ekam eva āsīt dvidhā jātam mama adya vai sātyakiḥ ca hi mama jñeyaḥ pāṇḍavaḥ ca dhanaṃjayaḥ sātyakim preṣayitvā tu pāṇḍavasya padānugam kariṣyāmi prayatnena bhrātuḥ anveṣaṇam yadi bhrātuḥ anveṣaṇam kṛtvā dharmarājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ loka apavāda bhīru tvāt saḥ aham pārtham vṛkodaram padavīm preṣayiṣyāmi mādhavasya mahātmanaḥ praviṣṭaḥ bhāratīm senām makaraḥ sāgaram yathā asau hi śrūyate śabdaḥ śūrāṇām anivartinām mithas saṃyudhyamānānām vṛṣṇi vīreṇa dhīmatā śaktaḥ hi eṣa raṇe yattān pṛthivyām sarva dhanvinaḥ sva bāhu balam āsthāya prativyūhitum añjasā yasya bāhu balam sarve samāśritya mahātmanaḥ vana vāsāt nivṛttāḥ sma na ca yuddheṣu nirjitāḥ itas gate bhīmasene sātvatam prati pāṇḍave rakṣitau vāsudevena svayam ca astra viśāradau avaśyam tu mayā kāryam ātmanaḥ śoka nāśanam tasmāt bhīmam niyokṣyāmi sātvatasya padānugam tatas pratikṛtam manye vidhānam sātyakim prati ratham hema pariṣkāram bhīma antikam upānayat kaśmalam prāviśat rājā bahu tatra samādiśan sa kaśmala samāviṣṭaḥ bhīmam āhūya pārthivaḥ abravīt vacanam rājan kuntī putraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ na eva adrākṣam na ca aśrauṣam tava kaśmalam īdṛśam purā hi duḥkha dīrṇānām bhavān gatiḥ abhūt hi naḥ uttiṣṭha uttiṣṭha rāja indra śādhi kim karavāṇi te ājñāpaya kuru śreṣṭha mā ca śoke manaḥ kṛthāḥ tam abravīt aśru pūrṇaḥ kṛṣṇa sarpaḥ iva śvasan bhīmasenam idam vākyam pramlāna vadanaḥ nṛpaḥ yathā śaṅkhasya nirghoṣaḥ pāñcajanyasya śrūyate yathā hi pāñcajanyasya śrūyate ninadaḥ mahān nūnam adya hataḥ śete tava bhrātā dhanaṃjayaḥ yasya sattvavataḥ vīryam upajīvanti pāṇḍavāḥ yam bhayeṣu abhigacchanti sahasrākṣam iva amarāḥ sa śūraḥ saindhava prepsuḥ anvayāt bhāratīm camūm śyāmaḥ yuvā guḍākeśaḥ darśanīyaḥ mahā bhujaḥ mama priya hita artham ca śakra lokāt iha āgataḥ vṛddha upasevī dhṛtimān kṛtajñaḥ satya saṃgaraḥ praviṣṭaḥ mahatīm senām arpayantām dhanaṃjayaḥ praviṣṭe ca camūm ghorām arjune śatru nāśane preṣitaḥ sātvataḥ vīraḥ phalgunasya padānugaḥ tasya abhigamanam jāne bhīma na āvartanam punar arjuna artham mahā bāho sātvatasya ca kāraṇāt tam viddhi puruṣa vyāghram sātvatam ca mahā ratham sa tam mahā ratham paścāt anuyātaḥ te anujam tam apaśyān mahā bāhum aham vindāmi kaśmalam atha enam punar ācakṣva lohitākṣam sa keśavam dṛṣṭvā kuśalinaḥ kṛṣṇau sātvatam ca eva sātyakim saṃvidam mama kuryāḥ tvam siṃhanādena pāṇḍava asau hi pāñcajanyasya nadataḥ śrūyate svanaḥ kruddhena vāsudevena pūryamāṇasya pāṇḍava nūnam vinihataḥ śūraḥ savyasācī paraṃtapaḥ tasmāt kṛṣṇaḥ raṇe nūnam yudhyate yuddha kovidaḥ yasya vīryavataḥ vīryam upajīvanti pāṇḍavāḥ vacanam mama dharma jña jyeṣṭhaḥ bhrātā bhavāmi te na te arjunaḥ tathā jñeyaḥ jñātavyaḥ sātyakiḥ yathā cikīrṣuḥ mad priyam pārtha prayātaḥ savyasācinaḥ padavīm durgamām ghorām agamyām akṛtātmabhiḥ brahma īśāna indra varuṇān avahat yaḥ purā rathaḥ ājñām tu śirasā bibhrat eṣa gacchāmi mā śucaḥ sametya tān nara vyāghrān te dāsyāmi saṃvidam uvāca dhṛṣṭadyumnāya balavān suhṛdbhyaḥ ca punar punar dhṛṣṭadyumnam ca idam aha bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ viditam te mahā bāho yathā droṇaḥ mahā rathaḥ na ca me gamane kṛtyam tādṛś pārṣata vidyate yādṛśam rakṣaṇe rājñaḥ kāryam ātyayikam hi naḥ yāsyāmi padavīm bhrātuḥ sātvatasya ca dhīmataḥ etat hi sarva kāryāṇām paramam kṛtyam āhave tam abravīt mahā rāja dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ vṛkodaram īpsitena mahā bāho gaccha pārtha avicārayān na a hatvā samare droṇaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam katham cana tatas nikṣipya rājānam dhṛṣṭadyumnāya pāṇḍavaḥ rājñā mūrdhani ca āghrātaḥ pariṣvaktaḥ ca śatru hā āghrātaḥ ca tathā mūrdhni śrāvitaḥ ca āśiṣaḥ śubhāḥ kṛtvā pradakṣiṇān viprān arcitān tuṣṭa mānasān ālabhya maṅgalāni aṣṭau pītvā kairātakam madhu paśyan eva ātmanaḥ buddhim vijaya ānanda kāriṇīm anuloma anilaiḥ ca āśu pradarśita jaya udayaḥ bhīmasenaḥ mahā bāhuḥ kavacī śubha kuṇḍalī sa aṅgadaḥ sa tanutrāṇaḥ sa śarī rathinām varaḥ pīta rakta asita sitaiḥ vāsobhiḥ ca su veṣṭitaḥ kaṇṭha trāṇena ca babhau sa indrāyudhaḥ iva ambudaḥ pāñcajanya ravaḥ ghoraḥ punar āsīt viśām pate tam śrutvā ninadam ghoram trailokya trāsanam mahat eṣa vṛṣṇi pravīreṇa dhmātaḥ salilajaḥ bhṛśam pṛthivīm ca antarikṣam ca vinādayati śaṅkha rāj nūnam āryā mahat kuntī pāpam adya nidarśanam muhyanti iva hi me sarvāḥ dhanaṃjaya didṛkṣayā diśaḥ sa pradiśaḥ pārtha sātvatasya ca kāraṇāt bhīmasenaḥ mahā bāhuḥ kavacī daṃśitaḥ balī tatas pāṇḍu sutaḥ rājñ bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān baddha godhā aṅguli trāṇaḥ pragṛhīta śarāsanaḥ bhṛśam sa prahitaḥ bhrātrā bhrātā bhrātuḥ priyaṃkaraḥ āhatya dundubhim bhīmaḥ śaṅkham pradhmāya ca asakṛt vinadya siṃhanādam ca jyām vikarṣan punar punar tala śabdena vīrāṇām pātayitvā manāṃsi uta tam ūhuḥ javanāḥ dāntāḥ vikurvāṇāḥ haya uttamāḥ viśokena abhisaṃyattāḥ manaḥ māruta raṃhasaḥ ārujan virujan pārthaḥ jyām vikarṣan ca pāṇinā saḥ avakarṣan vikarṣan ca senā agram samaloḍayat tam prayāntam mahā bāhum pāñcālāḥ saha somakāḥ tam samāyāntam ālokya ghora rūpam sutāḥ te pṛṣṭhatas anuyayuḥ śūrāḥ maghavantam iva amarāḥ tam sa senāḥ mahā rāja sodaryāḥ paryavārayan duḥśalaḥ citrasenaḥ ca kuṇḍabhedī viviṃśatiḥ vṛndārakaḥ suhastaḥ ca suṣeṇaḥ dīrghalocanaḥ vividhaiḥ rathinām śreṣṭhāḥ saha sainyaiḥ saha anugaiḥ saṃyattāḥ samare śūrāḥ bhīmasenam upādravan taiḥ samantāt vṛtaḥ śūraiḥ samare sa mahā rathaḥ tān samīkṣya tu kaunteyaḥ bhīmasenaḥ parākramī te mahā astrāṇi divyāni tatra vīrāḥ adarśayan vārayantaḥ śaraiḥ bhīmam meghāḥ sūryam iva uditam sa tān atītya vegena droṇa anīkam upādravat agratas ca gaja anīkam śara varṣaiḥ avākirat saḥ acireṇa eva kālena tat gaja anīkam āśugaiḥ trāsitāḥ śarabhasya iva garjitena vane mṛgāḥ punar ca atītya vegena droṇa anīkam upādravat tasya droṇaḥ ratham rājñ chādayām āsa saṃyuge sa aśva sūta dhvajam tūrṇam tat adbhutam iva abhavat lalāṭe atāḍayat ca enam nārācena smayan iva ūrdhva raśmiḥ iva ādityaḥ vibabhau tatra pāṇḍavaḥ bhīmaḥ kariṣyate pūjām iti uvāca vṛkodaram bhīmam pūjām kariṣyantam guru vṛttam atha abravīt bhīmasena na te śakyam praveṣṭum ari vāhinīm yadi te saḥ anujaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ praviṣṭaḥ anumate mama anīkam na tu śakyam bhoḥ praveṣṭum iha vai tvayā kruddhaḥ provāca vai droṇam rakta tāmra īkṣaṇaḥ śvasan praviṣṭaḥ sa hi durdharṣaḥ śakrasya api viśet balam yena vai paramām pūjām kurvatā mānitaḥ hi asi na arjunaḥ aham ghṛṇī droṇa bhīmasenaḥ asmi te ripuḥ iti manyāmahe sarve bhavantam praṇatāḥ sthitāḥ eṣa te sadṛśam śatroḥ karma bhīmaḥ karomi aham atha udbhrāmya gadām bhīmaḥ kāla daṇḍam iva antakaḥ droṇāya avasṛjat rājan sa rathāt avapupluve sa aśva sūta dhvajam yānam droṇasya apothayat tadā droṇam tu viratham kṛtvā bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ prāmṛdnāt ca bahūn yodhān vāyuḥ vṛkṣān iva ojasā vicacāra raṇe rājan vāyu tulya parākramaḥ nirjitaḥ tu tadā anena pāṇḍavena mahātmanā anyam ca ratham āsthāya droṇaḥ praharatām varaḥ vyūha dvāram samāsādya yuddhāya samavasthitaḥ tatas kruddhaḥ mahā rāja bhīmasenaḥ parākramī agratas syandana anīkam śara varṣaiḥ avākirat te vadhyamānāḥ samare tava putrāḥ mahā rathāḥ bhīmam bhīma balam yuddhe ayodhayan tu jaya eṣiṇaḥ tatas duḥśāsanaḥ kruddhaḥ ratha śaktim samākṣipat sarva pāraśavām tīkṣṇām jighāṃsuḥ pāṇḍu nandanam āpatantīm mahā śaktim tava putra pracoditām atha anyaiḥ niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ saṃkruddhaḥ kuṇḍabhedinam suṣeṇam dīrghanetram ca tribhiḥ trīn avadhīt balī tatas vṛndārakam vīram kurūṇām kīrti vardhanam putrāṇām tava vīrāṇām yudhyatām avadhīt punar vadhyamānāḥ mahā rāja putrāḥ te balīyasā bhīmam praharatām śreṣṭham samantāt paryavārayan bāhyam mṛtyu bhayam kṛtvā samāvavruḥ vṛkodaram te śaraiḥ bhīma karmāṇam vavarṣuḥ pāṇḍavam yudh meghāḥ iva ātapa apāye dhārābhiḥ dharaṇīdharam sa tat bāṇa mayam varṣam aśma varṣam iva acalaḥ pratīcchan pāṇḍu dāyādaḥ na prāvyathata śatru hā tatas sudarśanam vīram putram te bharata ṛṣabha vivyādha samare tūrṇam sa papāta mamāra ca tomareṇa nihatya ājau preṣayām āsa mṛtyave saḥ acireṇa eva kālena tat ratha anīkam āśugaiḥ diśaḥ sarvāḥ samabhyasya vyadhamat pāṇḍu nandanaḥ diśaḥ vidrāvayām āsa nīhāram iva bhāskaraḥ vadhyamānāḥ ca samare putrāḥ te viśām pate prādravan sa rathāḥ sarve bhīmasena bhaya arditāḥ anuyāya tu kaunteyaḥ putrāṇām te mahat balam vadhyamānāḥ mahā rāja bhīmasenena tāvakāḥ siṃhanāda ravam cakre bāhu śabdam ca pāṇḍavaḥ tala śabdam ca su mahat kṛtvā bhīmaḥ mahā balaḥ kṛtvā śabdam ca bhīmam ca bhīmaḥ vai śvasana ātmajaḥ mahantam tala śabdam ca kṛtvā droṇa antikam yayau bhīṣayitvā ratha anīkam hatvā yodhān varān varān vyatītya rathinaḥ ca api droṇa anīkam upādravat uvāca tam uttīrṇam ratha anīkāt tamasaḥ bhāskaram yathā didhārayiṣuḥ ācāryaḥ śara varṣaiḥ avākirat piban iva śara oghān tān droṇa cāpa vara atigān sa tathā saṃvṛtaḥ bhīmaḥ prahasan iva bhārata udayacchat gadām tebhyaḥ ghorām tām siṃha vat nadan sa indra aśaniḥ iva indreṇa praviddhā saṃhata ātmanā prāmathnāt sā mahā rāja sainikān te saṃyuge ghoṣeṇa mahatā rājan pūrayitvā iva medinīm jvalatī tejasā bhīmā trāsayām āsa te sutān tām patatīm mahā vegām dṛṣṭvā tejobhiḥ saṃvṛtām prādravan tāvakāḥ sarve nadantaḥ bhairavān ravān tam ca śabdam asaṃsahyam tasyāḥ saṃlakṣya māriṣa siṃhanādam asahyam hi śrutvā bhīmasya saṃyuge te hanyamānāḥ bhīmena gadā hastena tāvakāḥ prādravanta raṇe bhītāḥ vyāghra ghrātāḥ mṛgāḥ iva sa tān vidrāvya kaunteyaḥ saṃkhye amitrān durāsadaḥ suparṇaḥ iva vegena pakṣirāj atyagāt camūm tathā tam viprakurvāṇam ratha yūthapa yūthapam bhāradvājaḥ mahā rāja bhīmasenam samabhyayāt droṇaḥ tu samare bhīmam vārayitvā śara ūrmibhiḥ akarot sahasā nādam pāṇḍūnām bhayam ādadhat droṇasya ca mahā rāja bhīmasya ca mahātmanaḥ yadā tu viśikhaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ droṇa cāpa viniḥsṛtaiḥ vadhyante samare vīrāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas tatas rathāt avaplutya vegam āsthāya pāṇḍavaḥ yathā hi go vṛṣaḥ varṣam pratigṛhṇāti līlayā tathā bhīmaḥ nara vyāghraḥ śara varṣam samagrahīt sa vadhyamānaḥ samare ratham droṇasya māriṣa īṣāyām pāṇinā gṛhya pracikṣepa mahā balaḥ parityajya ratham tūrṇam droṇaḥ bhagnam mahī tale parāṅmukham tathā yāntam bhagna utsāham gurum tadā tam api atiratham bhīmaḥ cikṣepa bhṛśa roṣitaḥ evam aṣṭau rathāḥ kṣiptāḥ guroḥ bhīmena līlayā droṇaḥ api tu nimeṣeṇa punar sva ratham āsthitaḥ tasmin kṣaṇe tasya yantā tūrṇam aśvān acodayat tatas sva ratham āsthāya bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ sa mṛdnan kṣatriyān ājau vātaḥ vṛkṣān iva uddhataḥ bhoja anīkam samāsādya hārdikyena abhirakṣitam saṃtrāsayan anīkāni tala śabdena māriṣa ajayat sarva sainyāni śārdūlaḥ iva go vṛṣān bhoja anīkam atikramya kāmbojānām ca vāhinīm tathā mleccha gaṇān ca anyān bahūn yuddha viśāradān sātyakim ca api saṃprekṣya yudhyamānam nara ṛṣabham bhīmasenaḥ mahā rāja draṣṭu kāmaḥ dhanaṃjayam atītya samare yodhān tāvakān pāṇḍu nandanaḥ saindhavasya vadha artham hi parākrāntam parākramī arjunam tatra dṛṣṭvā atha cukrośa mahataḥ ravān prāvṛṣ kāle mahā rāja nardan iva balāhakaḥ tam tu tasya mahā nādam pārthaḥ śuśrāva nardataḥ tatas pārthaḥ mahā nādam muñcan vai mādhavaḥ ca ha abhyayātām mahā rāja nardantau go vṛṣau iva vāsudeva arjunau śrutvā ninādam tasya śuṣmiṇaḥ punar punar praṇadatām didṛkṣantau vṛkodaram aprīyata mahā rāja dharmaputraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ viśokaḥ ca abhavat rājā śrutvā tam ninadam mahat dhanaṃjayasya ca raṇe jayam āśā stavān vibhuḥ smitam kṛtvā mahā bāhuḥ dharmaputraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ hṛdgatam manasā prāha dhyātvā dharma bhṛtām varaḥ dattā bhīma tvayā saṃvid kṛtam guru vacaḥ tathā na hi teṣām jayaḥ yuddhe yeṣām dveṣṭā asi pāṇḍava diṣṭyā jīvati saṃgrāme savyasācī dhanaṃjayaḥ diṣṭyā ca kuśalī vīraḥ sātyakiḥ satya vikramaḥ diṣṭyā śṛṇomi garjantau vāsudeva dhanaṃjayau yena śakram raṇe jitvā tarpitaḥ havyavāhanaḥ sa hantā dviṣatām saṃkhye diṣṭyā jīvati phalgunaḥ yasya bāhu balam sarve vayam āśritya jīvitāḥ sa hantā ripu sainyānām diṣṭyā jīvati phalgunaḥ nirjitāḥ rathinā ekena diṣṭyā pārthaḥ sa jīvati kālakeya sahasrāṇi caturdaśa mahā raṇe kālakeyān mahā iṣvāsān sahasrāṇi caturdaśa yaḥ avadhīt bhuja vīryeṇa diṣṭyā pārthaḥ sa jīvati jitavan yaḥ astra vīryeṇa diṣṭyā pārthaḥ sa jīvati kirīṭamālī balavān śveta aśvaḥ kṛṣṇa sārathiḥ mama priyaḥ ca satatam diṣṭyā jīvati phalgunaḥ putra śoka abhisaṃtaptaḥ cikīrṣuḥ karma duṣkaram jayadratha vadha anveṣī pratijñām kṛtavan hi yaḥ dṛṣṭvā saindhavakam saṃkhye śamam asmāsu dhāsyati dṛṣṭvā vinihatān bhrātṝn bhīmasenena saṃyuge dṛṣṭvā ca anyān bahūn yodhān pātitān dharaṇī tale śeṣasya rakṣaṇa artham ca saṃdhāsyati suyodhanaḥ uvāca tathā tu nardamānam tam bhīmasenam mahā balam na hi paśyāmi aham tam vai triṣu lokeṣu saṃjaya na hi paśyāmi aham tāta yaḥ tiṣṭheta raṇa ajire kaḥ tasya samare sthātā sākṣāt api śatakratuḥ pradhakṣyataḥ raṇa mukhe ke vīrāḥ pramukhe sthitāḥ kālyamānān hi mama putrān bhīmena avekṣya saṃyuge kālena iva prajāḥ sarvāḥ ke bhīmam paryavārayan na mama arjunāt bhayam tādṛś kṛṣṇāt na api ca sātvatāt ke śūrāḥ paryavartanta tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya uvāca tathā tu nardamānam tam bhīmasenam mahā ratham vyākṣipan balavat cāpam atimātram amarṣaṇaḥ karṇaḥ tu yuddham ākāṅkṣan darśayiṣyan balam balī rurodha mārgam bhīmasya vātasya iva mahīruhaḥ bhīmaḥ api dṛṣṭvā sa āvegam puras vaikartanam sthitam cukopa balavat vīraḥ cikṣepa asya śilā śitān tān pratyagṛhṇāt karṇaḥ api pratīpam preṣayat śarān tatas tu sarva yodhānām yatatām prekṣatām tadā prāvepan iva gātrāṇi karṇa bhīma samāgame rathinām sādinām ca eva tayoḥ śrutvā tala svanam bhīmasenasya ninadam ghoram śrutvā raṇa ajire kham ca bhūmim ca saṃbaddhām menire kṣatriya ṛṣabhāḥ punar ghoreṇa nādena pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥ samare sarva yodhānām dhanūṃṣi abhyapatan kṣitau keṣām cit alpa sattvānām tam śrutvā ninadam yudhi śastrāṇi nyapatan dorbhyaḥ keṣām cit ca asavaḥ adravan vitrastāni ca sarvāṇi śakṛt mūtram prasusruvuḥ vāhanāni mahā rāja babhūvuḥ vimanāṃsi ca tam śrutvā ninadam ghoram śakṛt mūtram sa śoṇitam prādurāsan nimittāni ghorāṇi ca bahūni ca gṛdhra kaṅka vaḍaiḥ ca āsīt antarikṣam samāvṛtam tatas karṇaḥ tu viṃśatyā śarāṇām bhīmam ārdayat vivyādha ca asya tvaritaḥ sūtam pañcabhiḥ āśugaiḥ sāyakānām
