catuḥṣaṣṭyā kṣiprakārī mahā balaḥ tasya karṇaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ sāyakān caturaḥ akṣipat asaṃprāptān tu tān bhīmaḥ sāyakaiḥ nata parvabhiḥ tam karṇaḥ chādayām āsa śara vrātaiḥ anekaśas saṃchādyamānaḥ karṇena bahudhā pāṇḍu nandanaḥ ciccheda cāpam karṇasya muṣṭideśe mahā rathaḥ atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya sajyam kṛtvā ca sūtajaḥ vivyādha samare bhīmam bhīma karmā mahā rathaḥ tasya bhīmaḥ bhṛśam kruddhaḥ trīn śarān nata parvṇaḥ dhātu prasyandinaḥ śailāt yathā gairika rājayaḥ kim cit vicalitaḥ karṇaḥ su prahāra abhipīḍitaḥ sa sāyakam dhanuḥ kṛtvā bhīmam vivyādha māriṣa cikṣepa ca punar bāṇān śataśas atha sahasraśas sa chādyamānaḥ sahasā karṇena dṛḍha dhanvinā dhanuḥ jyām acchinat tūrṇam utsmayan pāṇḍu nandanaḥ vāhān ca caturaḥ saṃkhye vyasūn cakre mahā rathaḥ hata aśvāt tu rathāt karṇaḥ samāplutya viśām pate syandanam vṛṣasenasya samārohat mahā rathaḥ nirjitya tu raṇe karṇam bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān tasya tam ninadam śrutvā prahṛṣṭaḥ abhūt yudhiṣṭhiraḥ karṇam ca nirjitam matvā bhīmasenena bhārata samantāt śaṅkha ninadam pāṇḍu senā akarot tadā cakre yudhiṣṭhiraḥ saṃkhye harṣa nādaiḥ ca saṃkulām śatru senā dhvanim śrutvā tāvakāḥ hi api nānadan gāṇḍīvam prākṣipat pārthaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ api abjam avādayat aśrūyata mahā rāja sarva sainyeṣu bhārata mṛdu pūrvam ca rādheyaḥ dṛḍha pūrvam ca pāṇḍavaḥ tat sainyam kaluṣībhūtam na prājñāyata kim cana āsure tu mahā sainye tārakam pāvakiḥ yathā tam bhīmasenaḥ mahatā śara varṣeṇa vārayan vivyādha sārathim ca asya hayān ca caturaḥ śaraiḥ dhvajam ca asya patākām ca bhallaiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ karṇaḥ api rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ bhīmasenena kampitaḥ bhīmaḥ ciccheda khaḍgam ca carmaṇā saha māriṣa dṛṣṭvā karṇam ca pārthena bādhitam bahubhiḥ śaraiḥ duryodhanaḥ mahā rāja duḥśalam pratyabhāṣata karṇam kṛcchra gatam paśya śīghram yānam prayaccha ha evam uktaḥ tatas rājā duḥśalaḥ samupādravat duḥśalasya ratham karṇaḥ ca āruroha mahā rathaḥ tau pārthaḥ sahasā gatvā vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ punar ca karṇam viddhvā api duḥśalasya śiraḥ aharat duḥśalam nihatam dṛṣṭvā bhīmasenena māriṣa tasya eva dhanuḥ ādāya karṇaḥ vivyādha pāṇḍavam bhīmaḥ viddhvā hayān ca eva sārathim ca punar punar karṇam abhyadravat pārthaḥ prahasan ca mahā balaḥ tat sainyam śakalībhūtam na prājñāyata kim cana uvāca tūrṇam abhyapatat droṇam manaḥ māruta vegavān iha dṛṣṭaḥ itas naṣṭaḥ sa rathaḥ prādravat nṛpaḥ muhūrtāt iva putraḥ te droṇam āsādya māriṣa arjunaḥ bhīmasenaḥ ca sātyakiḥ ca aparājitaḥ saṃprāptāḥ sindhurājasya samīpam ari karśanāḥ vyāyacchanti ca tatra api sarve eva aparājitāḥ katham sātyaki bhīmābhyām vyatikrāntaḥ asi mānada āścarya bhūtam loke asmin samudrasya iva śoṣaṇam nāśaḥ eva tu me nūnam mandabhāgyasya saṃyuge yatra tvām puruṣa vyāghram atikrāntāḥ trayaḥ rathāḥ tat bravītu bhavān kṣipram sādhu tat saṃvidhīyatām uvāca cintyam bahu mahā rāja kṛtyam yat tatra mama śṛṇu trayaḥ hi samatikrāntāḥ pāṇḍavānām mahā rathāḥ yāvat eva bhayam paścāt tāvat eṣām puraḥsaram sā purastāt ca paścāt ca gṛhītā bhāratī camūḥ na sabhāyām jayaḥ vṛttaḥ na api tatra parājayaḥ yān sma tān glahate ghorān śakuniḥ kuru saṃsadi akṣān saṃmanyamānaḥ sa pra kśarāḥ te durāsadāḥ na te akṣāḥ niśitāḥ ghorāḥ śarāḥ tvad tanucchadaḥ senām durodaram viddhi śarān akṣān viśām pate atra sarve mahā rāja tyaktvā jīvitam ātmanaḥ tatra naḥ glahamānānām dhruvau tāta jaya ajayau tatra yāhi svayam śīghram tān ca rakṣasva rakṣiṇaḥ iha eva tu aham āsiṣye preṣayiṣyāmi ca aparān nirotsyāmi ca pāñcālān sahitān pāṇḍu sṛñjayaiḥ tatas duryodhanaḥ prāyāt tūrṇam ācārya śāsanāt udyamya ātmānam ugrāya karmaṇe sa padānugaḥ tau hi pūrvam mahā rāja vāritau kṛtavarmaṇā pārśvena senām āyāntau kuru rājaḥ dadarśa ha pārśve bhittvā camūm vīrau praviṣṭau te vāhinīm tvaritaḥ tvaramāṇābhyām bhrātṛbhyām bhārataḥ balī viṃśatyā sārathim ca asya caturbhiḥ caturaḥ hayān iṣudhī kārmukam ca asya samakṛntat ratha uttame sārathim ca asya bhallena rathanīḍāt apāharat tau samāsādayat vīraḥ śaraiḥ kāya asthi bhedibhiḥ tau tam su niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ avidhyetām mahā rathau atha anyat su mahā tejāḥ dhanuḥ gṛhya mahā balaḥ chādayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ pāñcālau kuru nandanaḥ yudhāmanyuḥ tu saṃkruddhaḥ śarān triṃśatam āyasān tathā uttamaujāḥ saṃkruddhaḥ śaraiḥ hema vibhūṣitaiḥ jaghāna caturaḥ ca aśvān ubhau ca pārṣṇisārathī uttamaujāḥ hata aśvaḥ tu hata sūtaḥ ca saṃyuge yudhāmanyu ratham śīghram āruroha paraṃtapaḥ sa ratham prāpya tam bhrātuḥ duryodhana hayān śaraiḥ bahubhiḥ tāḍayām āsa te hatāḥ prāpatan bhuvi yudhāmanyuḥ dhanuḥ śīghram śarāvāpam ca saṃyuge hata aśva sūtāt sa rathāt avaplutya mahā rathaḥ gadām ādāya te putraḥ pāñcālyau abhyadhāvata gadayā pothayām āsa sa aśva sūta dhvajam raṇe etat īdṛśakam kārṣīt putraḥ te janādhipa gadayā gadinām śreṣṭhaḥ sarva loka mahā rathaḥ madra rāja ratham tūrṇam āruroha paraṃtapaḥ pāñcālānām tu mukhyau tau rāja putrau mahā balau uvāca vartamāne mahā rāja saṃgrāme loma harṣaṇe vyākuleṣu ca sainyeṣu pīḍyamāneṣu sarvaśas uvāca arjunasya ratha upānte kīdṛśaḥ saḥ abhavat raṇaḥ pūrvam hi nirjitaḥ karṇaḥ bhīmasenena saṃyuge katham bhūyas tu rādheyaḥ bhīmam āgāt mahā rathaḥ bhīmaḥ vā sūtatanayam pratyudyātaḥ katham raṇe mahā ratha samākhyātam pṛthivyām pravaram ratham bhīṣma droṇau atikramya dharmaputraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ bhayāt yasya mahā bāhoḥ na śete bahulāḥ samāḥ katham karṇam yudhām śreṣṭham bhīmaḥ ayudhyata saṃyuge katham nu tau ayudhyetām sūtaputra vṛkodarau bhrātṛ tvam darśitam pūrvam ghṛṇī ca api sa sūtajaḥ bhīmaḥ vā sūtaputreṇa smaran vairam purā kṛtam karṇaḥ jeṣyati saṃgrāme sahitān pāṇḍavān iti yam samāśritya putraiḥ mama kṛtam vairam mahā rathaiḥ anekān viprakārān ca sūtaputra samudbhavān smaramāṇaḥ katham bhīmaḥ yuyudhe sūtasūnunā yaḥ ajayat pṛthivīm sarvām rathena ekena vīryavān yaḥ jātaḥ kuṇḍalābhyām ca kavacena saha eva ca astra hetoḥ purā tāta bhārgavam samapūjayat tasya prasādāt brahmāstram labdhavan ca bhṛgūttamāt yathā tayoḥ yuddham abhūt yaḥ ca āsīt vijayī tayoḥ uvāca iyeṣa gantum yatra āstām vīrau kṛṣṇa dhanaṃjayau ājuhāva raṇe yāntam bhīmam ādhirathiḥ tadā uvāca tat darśayasi kasmāt me pṛṣṭham pārtha didṛkṣayā kuntyāḥ putrasya sadṛśam na idam pāṇḍava nandana tena mām abhitas sthitvā śara varṣaiḥ avākira bhīmasenaḥ tad āhvānam karṇān na amarṣayat yudhi dvairathe daṃśitam yattam sarva śastrabhṛtām varam vidhitsuḥ kalahasya antam jighāṃsuḥ karṇam akṣiṇot tam ca hatvā itarān sarvān hantu kāmaḥ mahā balaḥ tasmai prāsṛjat ugrāṇi vividhāni paraṃtapaḥ amarṣī pāṇḍavaḥ kruddhaḥ śara varṣāṇi māriṣa tasya tāni iṣu varṣāṇi matta dvirada gāminaḥ sūtaputraḥ astra māyābhiḥ agrasat su mahā yaśāḥ sa yathāvat mahā rāja vidyayā vai su pūjitaḥ ācārya vat mahā iṣvāsaḥ karṇaḥ paryacarat raṇe yudhyamāneṣu vīreṣu paśyatsu ca samantataḥ tam bhīmasenaḥ saṃprāptam vatsadantaiḥ stanāntare sūtam tu sūtaputrasya su puṅkhaiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ karṇaḥ jāmbūnadaiḥ jālaiḥ saṃchannān vāta raṃhasaḥ vivyādha turagān vīraḥ pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥ tatas bāṇa mayam jālam bhīmasena ratham prati karṇena vihitam rājan nimeṣa ardhāt adṛśyata sa rathaḥ sa dhvajaḥ tatra sa sūtaḥ pāṇḍavaḥ tadā prācchādyata mahā rāja karṇa cāpa cyutaiḥ śaraiḥ tasya karṇaḥ catuḥṣaṣṭyā vyadhamat kavacam dṛḍham tatas a cintya mahā vegān karṇa kārmuka niḥsṛtān samāśliṣyat asambhrāntaḥ sūtaputram vṛkodaraḥ sa karṇa cāpa prabhavān iṣūn āśīviṣa upamān bibhrat bhīmaḥ mahā rāja na jagāma vyathām raṇe sa karṇa cāpam ciccheda bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ trāsayitvā mahā rāja gām amita vikramaḥ vivyādha samare karṇam bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān bhīmasenam mahā bāhum saindhavasya vadha eṣiṇam mṛdu pūrvam ca rādheyaḥ bhīmam ājau ayodhayat tam bhīmasenaḥ na amṛṣyat avamānam amarṣaṇaḥ te śarāḥ preṣitāḥ rājan bhīmasenena saṃyuge nipetuḥ sarvatas bhīmāḥ kūjantaḥ iva pakṣiṇaḥ hema puṅkhāḥ mahā rāja bhīmasena dhanuḥ cyutāḥ abhyadravan te rādheyam vṛkāḥ kṣudra mṛgam yathā karṇaḥ tu rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ chādyamānaḥ samantataḥ rājan vyasṛjat ugrāṇi śara varṣāṇi saṃyuge tasya tān aśani prakhyān iṣūn samara śobhinaḥ punar ca śara varṣeṇa chādayām āsa bhārata punar bāṇa mayam varṣam vyasṛjat pāṇḍavam prati tathā karṇena samare pīḍyamānaḥ samantataḥ tatra bhārata bhīmam tu dṛṣṭavantaḥ sma sāyakaiḥ samācita tanum saṃkhye śvāvidham śalalaiḥ iva hema puṅkhān śilā dhautān karṇa cāpa cyutān śarān dadhāra samare vīraḥ sva raśmīn iva bhāskaraḥ tapanīya nibhaiḥ puṣpaiḥ palāśaḥ iva kānane samṛddha kusuma āpīḍaḥ vasante aśoka vat taruḥ tat tu bhīmaḥ mahā rāja karṇasya caritam raṇe na amṛṣyata mahā iṣvāsaḥ krodhāt udvṛtya cakṣuṣī sa karṇam pañcaviṃśatyā nārācānām samārpayat mahīdharam iva śvetam gūḍha pādaiḥ viṣa ulbaṇaiḥ viviśuḥ ca yathā eva ugrāḥ valmīkam bhujaga uttamāḥ sapta niśitaiḥ tūrṇam śaraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ tam vivyādha punar bhīmaḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ aṣṭa eva ca marmasu amara vikrāntaḥ sūtaputram mahā raṇe marmaṇi anaparādhī saṃdidhitsuḥ kalaham tadā tatas karṇasya saṃkruddhaḥ bhīmasenaḥ pratāpavān ciccheda kārmukam tūrṇam sarva upakaraṇāni ca tathā api samare tūrṇam vivyādha urasi pāṇḍavaḥ pāṇḍavaḥ tu punar viddhvā sapta sāyaka uttamaiḥ anyaiḥ ca bahu sam rājan śaraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ jaghāna caturaḥ ca aśvān sūtam ca tvaritaḥ śaraiḥ nārācaiḥ arka raśmi ābhaiḥ karṇam vivyādha ca urasi te jagmuḥ dharaṇīm sarve karṇam nirbhidya māriṣa yathā hi jaladam bhittvā rājan sūryasya raśmayaḥ bhīmasenaḥ dṛḍham kopāt punar vivyādha pattriṇā tathā puruṣa mānī sa pratyapāyāt ratha antaram bhīmasena bhayāt karṇaḥ uvāca yasmin jaya āśā satatam putrāṇām mama saṃjaya tam dṛṣṭvā vimukham saṃkhye kim nu duryodhanaḥ abravīt katham ca yuyudhe bhīmaḥ vīrya ślāghī mahā balaḥ karṇaḥ vā samare tāta kim akārṣīt atas param uvāca bhīmasenam raṇe dṛṣṭvā jvalantam iva pāvakam tasya tulyaḥ astra māyābhiḥ tat viśiṣṭaḥ atha vā vṛṣaḥ śiṣyaḥ śiṣya guṇaiḥ yuktaḥ kāla antaka yama upamaḥ sa bhīmasenena jitaḥ pāṇḍu putreṇa bhārata śiṣya tvam prāptavān karṇaḥ tasya tulyaḥ astra māyayā tat viśiṣṭaḥ api vā karṇaḥ śiṣyaḥ śiṣya guṇaiḥ yutaḥ kuntī putreṇa bhīmena nirjitaḥ sa tu līlayā abhyayāt pāṇḍavam karṇaḥ vāta uddhūtaḥ iva arṇavaḥ kruddham ādhirathim dṛṣṭvā putrāḥ te viśām pate cāpa śabdam mahat kṛtvā tala śabdam ca bhairavam punar eva tatas rājan mahān āsīt su dāruṇaḥ vimardaḥ sūtaputrasya bhīmasya ca viśām pate anyonyam īkṣām cakrāte dahantau iva locanaiḥ vyāghrau iva su saṃrabdhau śyenau iva ca śīghra gau tatas bhīmaḥ smaran kleśān akṣa dyūte vane api ca virāṭa nagare ca eva prāptam duḥkham ariṃdamaḥ rāṣṭrāṇām sphīta ratnānām haraṇam ca te ātmajaiḥ satatam ca parikleśān sa putreṇa tvayā kṛtān kṛṣṇāyāḥ ca parikleśam sabhā madhye durātmabhiḥ keśa pakṣa graham ca eva duḥśāsana kṛtam tathā paruṣāṇi ca vākyāni karṇena uktāni bhārata narakam patitāḥ pārthāḥ sarve ṣaṇḍhatila upamāḥ dāsī bhogena kṛṣṇām ca bhoktu kāmāḥ sutāḥ te yat ca api tān pravrajataḥ kṛṣṇājina nivāsinaḥ paruṣāṇi uktavan karṇaḥ sabhāyām saṃnidhau te putraḥ te viśeṣeṇa kāla dyūtena noditaḥ tṛṇīkṛtya ca yat pārthān te putraḥ vavalga ha bālyāt prabhṛti ca ari ghnaḥ tāni duḥkhāni cintayan evam bahuvidhān ghorān smaran dīpta agni saṃnibhaḥ cāpam bharata śārdūlaḥ tyakta ātmā karṇam abhyayāt bhānumadbhiḥ śilā dhautaiḥ bhānoḥ pracchādayat prabhām tatas prahasya ādhirathiḥ tūrṇam asyan śitān śarān mahā rathaḥ mahā bāhuḥ mahā vegaiḥ mahā balaḥ vivyādha ādhirathiḥ bhīmam navabhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ sa tottraiḥ iva mātaṅgaḥ vāryamāṇaḥ patatribhiḥ abhyadhāvat asambhrāntaḥ sūtaputram vṛkodaraḥ tam āpatantam vegena rabhasam pāṇḍava ṛṣabham akṣubhyata balam harṣāt uddhūtaḥ iva sāgaraḥ tat uddhūtam balam dṛṣṭvā ratha nāga aśva pattimat bhīmaḥ karṇam samāsādya chādayām āsa sāyakaiḥ aśvān ṛśya savarṇān tu haṃsa varṇaiḥ haya uttamaiḥ vyāmiśrayat raṇe karṇaḥ pāṇḍavam chādayan śaraiḥ ṛśya varṇān hayān karkaiḥ miśrān māruta raṃhasaḥ nirīkṣya te putrāṇām hāhākṛtam abhūt balam te hayāḥ bahu aśobhanta miśritāḥ vāta raṃhasaḥ sita asitāḥ mahā rāja yathā vyomni balāhakāḥ saṃtrastāḥ samakampanta tvadīyānām mahā rathāḥ yama rāṣṭra upamam ghoram āsīt āyodhanam tayoḥ durdarśam bharata śreṣṭha pretarāja puram yathā samājam iva tat citram prekṣamāṇāḥ mahā rathāḥ na alakṣayan jayam vyaktam ekaikasya nivāraṇe tayoḥ praikṣanta saṃmardam saṃnikṛṣṭa mahā astrayoḥ chādayantau hi śatrughnau anyonyam sāyakaiḥ śitaiḥ śara jāla āvṛtam vyoma cakrāte śara vṛṣṭibhiḥ tau anyonyam jighāṃsantau śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ mahā rathau prekṣaṇīyatarau āstām vṛṣṭimantau iva ambudau suvarṇa vikṛtān bāṇān pramuñcantau ariṃdamau tābhyām muktāḥ vyakāśanta kaṅka barhiṇa vāsasaḥ paṅktayaḥ śaradi mattānām sārasāṇām iva ambare tatas bhīmaḥ mahā rāja karṇam viddhvā tribhiḥ śaraiḥ sārathim ca asya bhallena rathanīḍāt apāharat aśvān ca caturaḥ śvetān nijaghāna śitaiḥ śaraiḥ mahā gajau yathā dṛptau viṣāṇa agraiḥ parasparam saṃsaktam sūtaputreṇa dṛṣṭvā bhīmam ariṃdamam atibhāram amanyetām bhīme kṛṣṇa dhanaṃjayau tatra ādhirathi bhīmābhyām śaraiḥ muktaiḥ dṛḍha āhatāḥ kṛtaḥ mahān mahā rāja putrāṇām te jana kṣayaḥ manuṣya aśva gajānām ca śarīraiḥ gata jīvitaiḥ kṣaṇena bhūmiḥ saṃjajñe saṃvṛtā bharata ṛṣabha ākrīḍam iva rudrasya dakṣa yajña nibarhaṇe uvāca vārayet yaḥ raṇe karṇaḥ sa yakṣa asura mānavān sa katham pāṇḍavam yuddhe bhrājamānam iva śriyā na atarat saṃyuge tāta tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya katham ca yuddham bhūyaḥ abhūt tayoḥ prāṇa durodare karṇam prāpya raṇe sūta mama putraḥ suyodhanaḥ śrutvā tu nirjitam karṇam asakṛt bhīma karmaṇā na hi karṇaḥ mahā iṣvāsān pārthān saṃjaya kṛtavān yāni yuddhāni karṇaḥ pāṇḍu sutaiḥ saha sarvatra pāṇḍavāḥ karṇam ajayanta raṇa ajire ajayyāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ tāta devaiḥ api sa vāsavaiḥ nikṛtyā nikṛti prajñaḥ rājyam hṛtvā mahātmanām jitān iti eva manvānaḥ pāṇḍavān avamanyate putra sneha abhibhūtena mayā ca api akṛtātmanā dharme sthitāḥ mahātmānaḥ nikṛtāḥ pāṇḍu nandanāḥ śama kāmaḥ sadā pārthaḥ dīrghaprekṣī yudhiṣṭhiraḥ aśaktaḥ iti manvānaiḥ putraiḥ mama nirākṛtaḥ tāni duḥkhāni anekāni viprakārān ca sarvaśas hṛdi kṛtvā mahā bāhuḥ bhīmaḥ ayudhyata sūtajam tasmāt me saṃjaya brūhi karṇa bhīmau yathā raṇe ayudhyetām yudhi śreṣṭhau paraspara vadha eṣiṇaḥ uvāca paśyatām sarva sainyānām keśava arjunayoḥ api śṛṇu rājan yathā vṛttaḥ saṃgrāmaḥ karṇa bhīmayoḥ parākrāntam parākramya vivyādha triṃśatā śaraiḥ mahā vegaiḥ prasanna agraiḥ śātakumbha pariṣkṛtaiḥ āhanat bharata śreṣṭha bhīmam vaikartanaḥ śaraiḥ rathanīḍāt ca yantāram bhallena apātayat kṣitau sa kāṅkṣan bhīmasenasya vadham vaikartanaḥ vṛṣaḥ śaktim kanaka vaiḍūrya citra daṇḍām parāmṛśat pragṛhya ca mahā śaktim kāla śaktim iva aparām samutkṣipya ca rādheyaḥ saṃdhāya ca mahā balaḥ cikṣepa bhīmasenāya jīvitānta karīm iva śaktim visṛjya rādheyaḥ puraṃdaraḥ iva aśanim śaktim viyat gatām drṣṭvā śakra aśani sama dyutim nanāda su mahā nādam balavān sūtanandanaḥ tam ca nādam tatas śrutvā putrāḥ te hṛṣitāḥ abhavan tām karṇa bhuja nirmuktām arka vaiśvānara prabhām śaktim viyanti ciccheda bhīmaḥ sapta āśugaiḥ mārgamāṇaḥ iva prāṇān sūtaputrasya māriṣa prāhiṇot nava saṃrabdhaḥ śarān barhiṇa vāsasaḥ svarṇa puṅkhān śilā dhautān yama daṇḍa upamān mṛdhe karṇaḥ api anyat dhanuḥ gṛhya hema pṛṣṭham durāsadam vikṛṣya ca mahā tejāḥ vyasṛjat sāyakān nava suvarṇa vikṛtaiḥ bāṇaiḥ suvarṇa vikṛtān śarān vasuṣeṇena nirmuktān nava rājan mahā śarān chittvā bhīmaḥ mahā rāja nādam siṃhaḥ iva anadat tau vṛṣau iva nardantau balinau vāśitā antare śārdūlau iva ca anyonyam atyartham ca hi agarjatām anyonyam prajihīrṣantau anyonyasya antara eṣiṇaḥ mahā gajau iva āsādya viṣāṇa agraiḥ parasparam śaraiḥ pūrṇa āyata utsṛṣṭaiḥ anyonyam abhijaghnatuḥ nirdahantau mahā rāja śara vṛṣṭyā parasparam śaṅkha śabdam ca kurvāṇau yuyudhāte parasparam tasya bhīmaḥ punar cāpam muṣṭau ciccheda māriṣa śaṅkha varṇāḥ ca tān aśvān bāṇaiḥ ninye yama kṣayam sārathim ca tathā api asya rathanīḍāt apātayat tatas vaikartanaḥ karṇaḥ cintām prāpa duratyayām sa chādyamānaḥ samare hata aśvaḥ hata sārathiḥ tathā kṛcchra gatam dṛṣṭvā karṇam duryodhanaḥ nṛpaḥ gaccha durjaya rādheyam purā grasati pāṇḍavaḥ abhyadravat bhīmasenam vyāsaktam vikiran śarān sa bhīmam navabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ aśvān aṣṭabhiḥ ardayat ṣaḍbhiḥ sūtam tribhiḥ ketum punar tam ca api saptabhiḥ bhīmasenaḥ api saṃkruddhaḥ sa aśva yantāram āśugaiḥ su alaṃkṛtam kṣitau kṣuṇṇam ceṣṭamānam yathā uragam samācinot bāṇa gaṇaiḥ śataghnīm iva śaṅkubhiḥ tathā api atirathaḥ karṇaḥ bhidyamānaḥ sma sāyakaiḥ uvāca ratham anyam samāsthāya sadyas vivyādha pāṇḍavam mahā gajau iva āsādya viṣāṇa agraiḥ parasparam śaraiḥ pūrṇa āyata utsṛṣṭaiḥ anyonyam abhijaghnatuḥ tam bhīmaḥ daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ pratyavidhyat ajihmagaiḥ punar vivyādha viṃśatyā śarāṇām nata parvaṇām sāyakānām tatas pārthaḥ triṣaṣṭyā pratyavidhyata tottraiḥ iva mahā nāgam kaśābhiḥ iva vājinam saḥ atividdhaḥ mahā rāja pāṇḍavena yaśasvinā sṛkviṇī lelihan vīraḥ krodha saṃrakta locanaḥ ciccheda kārmukam tūrṇam pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥ tatas śaram mahā rāja sarva kāya avadāraṇam prāhiṇot bhīmasenāya balāya indraḥ iva aśanim agacchat dārayan bhūmim citrapuṅkhaḥ śilīmukhaḥ tatas bhīmaḥ mahā bāhuḥ krodha saṃrakta locanaḥ sarva śaikyām catur kiṣkum gurvīm rukma aṅgadām gadām prāhiṇot sūtaputrāya a vicārayan tayā jaghāna ādhiratheḥ sat aśvān sādhu vāhinaḥ tatas bhīmaḥ mahā bāhuḥ kṣurābhyām bharata ṛṣabha mahā balān mahā vegān sat aśvān gadayā hatān sūtam ca nihatam dṛṣṭvā ketum ca vinipātitam virathaḥ rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ vārayām āsa yat ripum viratham tam ratha śreṣṭham dṛṣṭvā ādhirathim āhave eṣa durmukha rādheyaḥ bhīmena virathīkṛtaḥ tam rathena nara śreṣṭham saṃpādaya mahā ratham tvaramāṇaḥ abyayāt karṇam bhīmam ca avārayat śaraiḥ vāyuputraḥ prahṛṣṭaḥ abhūt parilelihan tatas karṇam mahā rāja vārayitvā śilīmukhaiḥ durmukhāya ratham śīghram preṣayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ āsthitaḥ prababhau rājan dīpyamānaḥ iva aṃśumant śayānam bhinna marmāṇam durmukham śoṇita ukṣitam dṛṣṭvā karṇaḥ aśru pūrṇa akṣaḥ muhūrtam na abhyavartata tam gatāsum atikramya kṛtvā karṇaḥ pradakṣiṇam dīrgham uṣṇam śvasan vīraḥ na kim cit pratyapadyata tasmin tu vivare rājan nārācān gārdhra vāsasaḥ prāhiṇot sūtaputrāya bhīmasenaḥ caturdaśa apiban sūtaputrasya śoṇitam rakta bhojanāḥ kruddhāḥ iva manuṣya indra bhujagāḥ kāla coditāḥ prasarpamāṇāḥ medinyām te vyarocanta mārgaṇāḥ te medinīm prasarpantaḥ śobhante rudhira ukṣitāḥ ardha praviṣṭāḥ saṃrabdhāḥ bilāni iva mahā uragāḥ tam pratyavidhyat rādheyaḥ jāmbūnada vibhūṣitaiḥ prāviśan medinīm bhīmāḥ krauñcam pattrarathāḥ iva te vyarocanta nārācāḥ praviśantaḥ vasuṃdharām gacchati astam dinakare dīpyamānāḥ iva aṃśavaḥ sa vihvalaḥ mahā rāja karṇaḥ bhīma bala arditaḥ prādravat javanaiḥ aśvaiḥ raṇam hitvā mahā yaśāḥ tathā puruṣa mānī san pratyapāyāt raṇa ajirāt āhave atirathaḥ atiṣṭhat jvalan iva hutāśanaḥ uvāca yatra ādhirathiḥ āyastaḥ na atarat pāṇḍavam raṇe karṇaḥ pārthān sa govindān jetum utsahate raṇe na ca karṇa samam yodham loke paśyāmi kam cana karṇaḥ hi balavān śūraḥ dṛḍha dhanvā jita klamaḥ vasuṣeṇa sahāyam mām na alam deva api saṃyuge kim u pāṇḍu sutāḥ rājan gata sattvāḥ vicetasaḥ tatra tam nirjitam dṛṣṭvā bhujaṃgam iva nirviṣam pataṃgam iva saṃdīptam bhīma agnim samaveśayat aśvatthāmā madra rājaḥ kṛpaḥ karṇaḥ ca saṃgatāḥ na śaktāḥ pramukhe sthātum nūnam bhīmasya saṃjaya te api ca asya mahā ghoram balam nāga ayuta upamam jānantaḥ vyavasāyam ca krūram māruta tejasaḥ kimartham krūra karmāṇam yama kāla antaka upamam bala saṃrambha vīrya jñāḥ kopayiṣyanti saṃyuge karṇaḥ tu ekaḥ mahā bāhuḥ sva bāhu balam āśritaḥ bhīmasenam an ādṛtya raṇe ayudhyata sūtajaḥ na sa pāṇḍu sutaḥ jetum śakyaḥ kena cit āhave droṇam yaḥ saṃpramathya ekaḥ praviṣṭaḥ mama vāhinīm bhīmaḥ dhanaṃjaya anveṣī kaḥ tam archet jijīviṣuḥ pretarāja puram prāpya nivarteta api mānavaḥ pataṃgāḥ iva vahnim te prāviśan alpa cetasaḥ śaptam saṃrambhinā ugra kurūṇām śṛṇvatām tadā tat nūnam abhisaṃcintya dṛṣṭvā karṇam ca nirjitam duḥśāsanaḥ saha bhrātrā bhayāt bhīmāt upāramat karṇaḥ duḥśāsanaḥ aham ca jeṣyāmaḥ yudhi pāṇḍavān sa nūnam viratham dṛṣṭvā karṇam bhīmena nirjitam sa nūnam nirjitam karṇam dṛṣṭvā bhīmena saṃyuge pratyākhyānāt ca kṛṣṇasya bhṛśam tapyati saṃjaya dṛṣṭvā bhrātṝn hatān yuddhe bhīmasenena daṃśitān ātma aparādhāt su mahat nūnam tapyati putrakaḥ kaḥ hi jīvitam anvicchan pratīpam pāṇḍavam vrajet bhīmam bhīma āyudham kruddham sākṣāt kālam iva sthitam na pāṇḍavāḥ na pāñcālāḥ na ca keśava sātyakī aho mama sutānām hi vipannam sūta jīvitam uvāca tvam asya jagataḥ mūlam vināśasya na saṃśayaḥ svayam vairam mahat kṛtvā putrāṇām vacane sthitaḥ ucyamānaḥ na gṛhṇīṣe martyaḥ pathyam iva auṣadham svayam pītvā mahā rāja kālakūṭam su durjaram prāpya idānīm phalam tasya yathā pītvā viṣam tathā su kṛtasya su pṛṣṭasya sujātasya mahā mṛdhe dṛṣṭvā karṇam tu putrāḥ te bhīmasena parājitam na amṛṣyanta mahā iṣvāsāḥ sodaryāḥ pañca māriṣa pāṇḍavam citra saṃnāhāḥ tam pratīpam upādravan te samantāt mahā bāhum parivārya vṛkodaram diśaḥ śaraiḥ samāvṛṇvan śalabhānām iva vrajaiḥ āgacchataḥ tān sahasā kumārān deva rūpiṇaḥ tava dṛṣṭvā tu tanayān bhīmasena samīpa gān visṛjan viśikhān rājan svarṇa puṅkhān śilā śitān tam tu bhīmaḥ abhyayāt tūrṇam vāryamāṇaḥ sutaiḥ te avākiran bhīmasenam śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ tān bāṇaiḥ pañcaviṃśatyā sa aśvān rājan nara ṛṣabhān bhīmasenaḥ tatas bāṇaiḥ pañca rājan sutān te sa sūtān bhīma dhanuṣaḥ bhīmaḥ ninye yama kṣayam citra puṣpa dharāḥ bhagnāḥ vātena iva mahā drumāḥ saṃvārya ādhirathim bāṇaiḥ yat jaghāna te ātmajān sa vāryamāṇaḥ bhīmena śitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ samantataḥ tam bhīmasenaḥ saṃrambhāt krodha saṃrakta locanaḥ uvāca tava ātmajān tu patitān dṛṣṭvā karṇaḥ pratāpavān krodhena mahatā āviṣṭaḥ nirviṇṇaḥ abhūt sa jīvitāt āgaskṛtam iva ātmānam mene ca ādhirathiḥ tadā yat pratyakṣam tava sutāḥ bhīmena nihatāḥ raṇe bhīmasenam tatas kruddhaḥ samādravata sambhramāt punar vivyādha saptatyā svarṇa puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ avahāsam tu tam pārthaḥ na amṛṣyata vṛkodaraḥ tatas vivyādha rādheyam śatena nata parvaṇām punar ca viśikhaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ viddhvā pañcabhiḥ āśugaiḥ raṇe bhūyas api rādheyam viddhvā pañcabhiḥ āyasaiḥ atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya karṇaḥ bhārata durmanāḥ iṣubhiḥ chādayām āsa bhīmasenam samantataḥ prajahāsa mahā hāsam kṛte pratikṛtam punar iṣubhiḥ kārmukam ca asya cakarta puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ tat papāta mahā rāja svarṇa pṛṣṭham mahā svanam papāta atha mahat cāpam hema pṛṣṭham durāsadam avārohat rathāt tasmāt atha karṇaḥ mahā rathaḥ gadām gṛhītvā samare bhīmasenāya ca akṣipat tām āpatantīm sahasā gadām dṛṣṭvā vṛkodaraḥ tatas bāṇa sahasrāṇi preṣayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ sūtaputra vadha ākāṅkṣī tvaramāṇaḥ parākramī tān iṣūn iṣubhiḥ karṇaḥ vārayitvā mahā mṛdhe kavacam bhīmasenasya pātayām āsa sāyakaiḥ atha enam pañcaviṃśatyā kṣudrakāṇām samārpayat paśyatām sarva bhūtānām tat adbhutam iva abhavat raṇe apreṣayata kruddhaḥ sūtaputrasya māriṣa te tasya kavacam bhittvā tathā bāhum ca dakṣiṇam abhyaguḥ dharaṇīm tīkṣṇāḥ valmīkam iva pannagāḥ sa chādyamānaḥ bāṇa oghaiḥ bhīmasena dhanuḥ cyutaiḥ punar eva abhavat karṇaḥ bhīmasenāt parāṅmukhaḥ rādheyam tu raṇe dṛṣṭvā padātinam avasthitam abhyayus pāṇḍavam yuddhe visṛjantaḥ śitān śarān citropacitraḥ citrākṣaḥ cārucitraḥ śarāsanaḥ āgacchataḥ tān sahasā bhīmaḥ rājan mahā rathaḥ tān āpatataḥ eva āśu bhīmasenaḥ mahā rathaḥ sa aśva sūta dhvajān yattān pātayām āsa saṃyuge te hatāḥ nyapatan bhūmau vāta nunnāḥ iva drumāḥ dṛṣṭvā vinihatān putrān te rājan mahā rathān aśru pūrṇa mukhaḥ karṇaḥ kaśmalam samapadyata abhyayāt pāṇḍavam yuddhe tvaramāṇaḥ parākramī tau anyonyam śaraiḥ viddhvā svarṇa puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ vyabhrājetām mahā rāja puṣpitau iva kiṃśukau vyadhamat kavacam kruddhaḥ sūtaputrasya pāṇḍavaḥ pañcāśatā mahā bāhuḥ vivyādha bharata ṛṣabha raktacandana digdha aṅgau śaraiḥ kṛta mahā vraṇau śoṇita aktau vyarājetām kāla sūryau iva uditau vyabhrājetām mahā rāja vidhūmau iva pāvakau vyāghrau iva nara vyāghrau daṃṣṭrābhiḥ itaretaram śara daṃṣṭrāḥ vidhunvānau tatakṣatuḥ ariṃdamau śara dhārā sṛjau vīrau meghau iva vavarṣatuḥ vāraṇau iva saṃsaktau raṅga madhye virejatuḥ rathābhyām nādayantau ca diśaḥ sarvāḥ viceratuḥ tau rathābhyām mahā rāja maṇḍala āvartana ādiṣu vyarocetām mahātmanau vṛtra vajradharau iva vāraṇau iva ca anyonyam viṣāṇābhyām ariṃdamau nirbhindantau sva gātrāṇi sāyakaiḥ cāru rejatuḥ maṇḍalāni vikurvāṇau rathābhyām ratha sattamau siṃhau iva parākrāntau nara siṃhau mahā balau yuyudhāte mahā vīryau śakra vairocanī yathā sa hasta ābharaṇābhyām tu bhujābhyām vikṣipan dhanuḥ sa cāpa ghoṣa stanitaḥ śara dhārā ambudaḥ mahān pāṇḍavaḥ vyakirat karṇam ghanaḥ adrim iva vṛṣṭibhiḥ bhīmam ācchādayat tūrṇam yathā adrim toyadaḥ ambunā su puṅkhaiḥ kaṅka vāsobhiḥ yat karṇam chādayat śaraiḥ putrāḥ te mahā rāja dadṛśuḥ pāṇḍavasya ha uvāca tava ca ādhirathiḥ dṛṣṭvā syandanebhyaḥ cyutān sutān putrān tava dadarśa atha bhīmasenena pātitān niḥśvasan dīrgham uṣṇam ca punar pāṇḍavam abhyayāt babhau karṇaḥ śarān asyan raśmivān iva bhāskaraḥ karṇa cāpa cyutaiḥ bāṇaiḥ prācchādyata vṛkodaraḥ karṇa cāpa cyutāḥ citrāḥ śarāḥ barhiṇa vāsasaḥ viviśuḥ sarvatas pārtham vāsāya iva aṇḍajāḥ drumam karṇa cāpa cyutāḥ bāṇāḥ saṃpatantaḥ tatas tatas rukma puṅkhāḥ vyarājanta haṃsāḥ śreṇīkṛtāḥ iva cāpa dhvaja upaskarebhyaḥ chatrāt īṣā mukhāt yugāt prabhavantaḥ vyadṛśyanta rājan ādhiratheḥ śarāḥ kham pūrayan mahā vegān khagamān khaga vāsasaḥ suvarṇa vikṛtān citrān mumoca ādhirathiḥ śarān tyaktvā prāṇān abhikrudhya vivyādha navabhiḥ śaraiḥ tasya vegam asaṃsahyam dṛṣṭvā karṇasya pāṇḍavaḥ mahataḥ ca śara oghān tān na eva avyathata vīryavān tatas vidhamya ādhiratheḥ śara jālāni pāṇḍavaḥ vivyādha karṇam viṃśatyā punar anyaiḥ śi śaraiḥ yathā eva hi śaraiḥ pārthaḥ sūtaputreṇa chāditaḥ tathā eva karṇam samare chādayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ dṛṣṭvā tu bhīmasenasya vikramam yudhi bhārata abhyanandan tvadīyāḥ ca saṃprahṛṣṭāḥ ca cāraṇāḥ bhūriśravāḥ kṛpaḥ drauṇiḥ madra rājaḥ jayadrathaḥ uttamaujāḥ yudhāmanyuḥ sātyakiḥ keśava arjunau kuru pāṇḍavānām pravarāḥ daśa rājan mahā rathāḥ rājñaḥ ca rāja putrān ca sodaryān ca viśeṣataḥ karṇam gacchata bhadram vaḥ parīpsantaḥ vṛkodarāt purā nighnanti rādheyam bhīma cāpa cyutāḥ śarāḥ te yatadhvam mahā iṣvāsāḥ sūtaputrasya rakṣaṇe duryodhana samādis sodaryāḥ sapta māriṣa te samāsādya kaunteyam āvṛṇvan śara vṛṣṭibhiḥ parvatam vāri dhārābhiḥ prāvṛṣi iva balāhakāḥ te apīḍayan bhīmasenam kruddhāḥ sapta mahā rathāḥ prajā saṃharaṇe rājan somam sapta grahāḥ iva tatas vāmena kaunteyaḥ pīḍayitvā śarāsanam muṣṭinā pāṇḍavaḥ rājan dṛḍhena su pariṣkṛtam manuṣya sama tām jñātvā sapta saṃdhāya sāyakān tebhyaḥ vyasṛjat āyastaḥ sūrya raśmi nibhān prabhuḥ nirāsata sa dehebhyaḥ putrāṇām atha taiḥ asūn te kṣiptāḥ bhīmasenena śarāḥ bhārata bhāratān vidārya kham samutpetuḥ svarṇa puṅkhāḥ śilā śitāḥ teṣām vidārya cetāṃsi śarāḥ hema vibhūṣitāḥ hitvā hitvā kṣitim jagmuḥ teṣām eva asubhiḥ saha vyarājanta mahā rāja suparṇāḥ iva khecarāḥ śoṇita ādih vāja agra sapta heman pariṣkṛ putrāṇām tava rāja indra pītvā śoṇitam udgatāḥ giri sānu ruhāḥ bhagnāḥ dvipena iva mahā drumāḥ śatruṃjayaḥ śatru sahaḥ citraḥ citra āyudhaḥ dṛḍhaḥ putrāṇām te sarveṣām nihatānām vṛkodaraḥ śocati ati bhṛśam duḥkhāt vikarṇam pāṇḍavaḥ priyam vikarṇa tena asi hataḥ pratijñā rakṣitā mayā tvam agāḥ saṃgaram vīra kṣātra dharmam anusmaran viśeṣataḥ asi nṛpateḥ tathā naḥ hite rataḥ nyāyatas anyāyatas na evam ekaḥ śokaḥ mahā dyutiḥ uvāca agādha buddhiḥ gāṅgeyaḥ kṣitau suraguroḥ samaḥ tyājitaḥ samare prāṇān ajeyaḥ tridaśaiḥ api tān nihatya mahā bāhuḥ rādheyasya eva paśyataḥ siṃhanāda ravam ghoram asṛjat pāṇḍu nandanaḥ ācaṣṭa iva ca tat yuddham bhīmasya vijayam tathā tam śrutvā su mahā nādam bhīmasenasya dhanvinaḥ tatas hṛṣṭaḥ mahā rāja vāditrāṇām mahā svanaiḥ bhīmasena ravam pārthaḥ pratijagrāha sarvaśas harṣeṇa mahatā yuktaḥ kṛta saṃjñe vṛkodare ekatriṃśat mahā rāja putrān tava mahā rathān hatān duryodhanaḥ dṛṣṭvā kṣattuḥ sasmāra tat vacaḥ sabhām ānāyya pāñcālīm karṇena sahitaḥ alpa dhīḥ yat ca karṇaḥ abravīt kṛṣṇām sabhāyām paruṣam vacaḥ pramukhe pāṇḍu putrāṇām tava ca eva viśām pate kauravāṇām ca sarveṣām ācāryasya ca saṃnidhau śṛṇvataḥ tava rāja indra kauravāṇām ca sarvaśas vinaś pāṇḍavāḥ kṛṣṇe śāśvatam narakam gam patim anyam vṛṇīṣva iti tasya idam phalam āgatam yat sma tām paruṣāṇi āhuḥ sabhām ānāyya draupadīm pāṇḍavān ugra dhanuṣaḥ krodhayantaḥ te ātmajāḥ yat ca ṣaṇḍhatila ādīni paruṣāṇi te ātmajaiḥ śrāvitāḥ te mahātmānaḥ pāṇḍavāḥ kopayiṣṇubhiḥ tam bhīmasenaḥ krodha agnim trayodaśa samāḥ sthitam vilapan ca bahu kṣattā śamam na alabhata tvayi tvayā vṛddhena dhīreṇa kārya tattva artha darśiṇā na kṛtam suhṛdām vākyam daivam atra parāyaṇam vināśa hetuḥ putrāṇām bhavān eva mataḥ mama pravarān ātmajānām te sutān ca anyān mahā rathān yān yān ca dadṛśe bhīmaḥ cakṣuḥ viṣayam āgatān putrān te mahā bāho tvarayā tān jaghāna ha tvad kṛte hi aham adrākṣam dahyamānām varūthinīm sahasraśas śaraiḥ muktaiḥ pāṇḍavena vṛṣeṇa ca uvāca mahān apanayaḥ sūta mama eva atra viśeṣataḥ saḥ idānīm anuprāptaḥ manye saṃjaya śocataḥ idānīm atra kim kāryam prakariṣyāmi saṃjaya yathā tu eṣa kṣayaḥ vṛttaḥ mama apanaya saṃbhavaḥ vīrāṇām tat mama ācakṣva sthirībhūtaḥ asmi saṃjaya uvāca karṇa bhīmau mahā rāja parākrāntau mahā āhave bāṇa varṣāṇi avarṣetām vṛṣṭimantau iva ambudau bhīma nāma aṅkitāḥ bāṇāḥ svarṇa puṅkhāḥ śilā śitāḥ viviśuḥ karṇam āsādya bhindantaḥ iva jīvitam ākīryata raṇe bhīmaḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas tayoḥ śaraiḥ mahā rāja saṃpatadbhiḥ samantataḥ babhūva tava sainyānām saṃkṣobhaḥ sāgara upamaḥ avadhyata camū madhye ghoraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ vāraṇaiḥ patitaiḥ rājan vājibhiḥ ca naraiḥ saha adṛśyata mahī kīrṇā vāta nunnaiḥ drumaiḥ iva te vadhyamānāḥ samare bhīma cāpa cyu śaraiḥ prādravan tāvakāḥ yodhāḥ kim etat iti ca abruvan protsāritam mahā vegaiḥ karṇa pāṇḍavayoḥ śaraiḥ te śara ātura bhūyiṣṭhāḥ hata aśva nara vāhanāḥ utsṛjya karṇam bhīmam ca prādravan sarvatodiśam nūnam pārtha artham eva asmān mohayanti divaukasaḥ evam bruvantaḥ yodhāḥ te tāvakāḥ bhaya pīḍitāḥ śarapātam samutsṛjya sthitāḥ yuddha didṛkṣavaḥ tatas prāvartata nadī ghora rūpā mahā āhave babhūva ca viśeṣeṇa bhīrūṇām bhaya vardhinī vāraṇa aśva manuṣyāṇām rudhira ogha samudbhavā saṃvṛtāḥ gata sattvaiḥ ca manuṣya gaja vājibhiḥ sa anukarṣa patākaiḥ ca dvipa aśva ratha bhūṣaṇaiḥ jātarūpa pariṣkāraiḥ dhanurbhiḥ su mahādhanaiḥ suvarṇa puṅkhaiḥ iṣubhiḥ nārācaiḥ ca sahasraśas prāsa tomara saṃghātaiḥ khaḍgaiḥ ca sa paraśvadhaiḥ suvarṇa vikṛtaiḥ ca api gadā musala paṭṭiśaiḥ kanaka aṅgada keyūraiḥ kuṇḍalaiḥ maṇibhiḥ śubhaiḥ cūḍāmaṇibhiḥ uṣṇīṣaiḥ svarṇa sūtraiḥ ca māriṣa gaja aśva manujaiḥ bhinnaiḥ śastraiḥ syandana bhūṣaṇaiḥ dṛṣṭvā cāraṇa siddhānām vismayaḥ samapadyata gajābhyām saṃprayuktābhyām āsīt naḍa vanam yathā tathābhūtam mahat sainyam āsīt bhārata saṃyuge vimardaḥ karṇa bhīmābhyām āsīt ca paramaḥ raṇe uvāca tatas karṇaḥ mahā rāja bhīmam viddhvā tribhiḥ śaraiḥ mumoca śara varṣāṇi citrāṇi ca bahūni ca vadhyamānaḥ mahā rāja sūtaputreṇa pāṇḍavaḥ sa karṇam karṇinā karṇe pītena niśitena ca vivyādha su bhṛśam saṃkhye taila dhautena māriṣa sa kuṇḍalam mahat karṇāt karṇasya apātayat bhuvi tapanīyam mahā rāja dīptam jyotiḥ iva ambarāt nigalat amṛtāt ekāt tāmarasam sura śilpinā kṛtam ājaghāna bhṛśam bhīmaḥ smayan iva mahā balaḥ punar asya tvaran bhīmaḥ nārācān daśa bhārata raṇe praiṣīt mahā vegān yama daṇḍa upamān tathā te lalāṭam samāsādya sūtaputrasya māriṣa viviśuḥ coditāḥ tena valmīkam iva pannagāḥ nīlotpala mayīm mālām dhārayan sa purā yathā saḥ atividdhaḥ bhṛśam karṇaḥ pāṇḍavena tarasviṇā sa muhūrtāt punar saṃjñām labdhvā karṇaḥ paraṃtapaḥ tatas kruddhaḥ raṇe karṇaḥ pīḍitaḥ dṛḍhadhanvanā tasmai karṇaḥ śatam rājan iṣūṇām gārdhra vāsasām amarṣī balavān kruddhaḥ preṣayām āsa bhārata tatas prāsṛjat ugrāṇi śara varṣāṇi pāṇḍavaḥ tān a cintya mahā bāhuḥ bhīmaḥ bhīma parākramaḥ tatas karṇaḥ mahā rāja pāṇḍavam niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ ājaghāna urasi kruddhaḥ kruddha rūpam paraṃtapaḥ tau ubhau nara śārdūlau śārdūlau iva daṃṣṭriṇaḥ śara daṃṣṭrau samāsādya tatakṣatuḥ anantaram jīmūtau iva ca anyonyam tau vavarṣatuḥ āhave śara jālaiḥ ca vividhaiḥ chādayām āsatuḥ mṛdhe tatas bhīmaḥ mahā bāhuḥ rādheyasya mahātmanaḥ kṣurapreṇa dhanuḥ chittvā karṇam vivyādha pattriṇā tat apāsya dhanuḥ chinnam sūtaputraḥ mahā manāḥ tṛtīyam ca caturtham ca pañcamam ṣaṣṭham eva ca saptamam ca aṣṭamam ca eva navamam daśamam tathā ekādaśam dvādaśam ca trayodaśam atha api vā caturdaśam pañcadaśam ṣoḍaśam ca vṛkodaraḥ tathā saptadaśam ca evam aṣṭādaśam atha api vā bahūni bhīmaḥ ciccheda karṇasya evam dhanūṃṣi ca nimeṣa ardhāt tatas karṇaḥ dhanuḥ hastaḥ vyatiṣṭhata dṛṣṭvā ca kuru sauvīra saindhavānām bala kṣayam sa varma dhvaja śastraiḥ ca patitaiḥ saṃvṛtām mahīm bhraṣṭa śrīkaiḥ nara varaiḥ pāṃsu kuṇṭhita mūrdhajaiḥ hasti aśva nara dehān ca gatāsūn prekṣya sarvatas bhīmam praikṣata rādheyaḥ rājan ghoreṇa cakṣuṣā madhyaṃdina gataḥ arciṣmān śaradi iva divākaraḥ āsīt ādhiratheḥ ghoram vapuḥ śara śata arciṣaḥ karābhyām ādadānasya saṃdadhānasya ca āśugān vikarṣataḥ muñcataḥ vā na antaram dadṛśuḥ raṇe agni cakra upamam ghoram maṇḍalīkṛtam āyudham karṇasya āsīt mahā rāja savya dakṣiṇam asyataḥ svarṇa puṅkhāḥ su niśā karṇa cāpa cyu śarāḥ prācchādayat mahā rāja diśaḥ sūryasya ca prabhām tatas kanaka puṅkhānām śarāṇām nata parvaṇām dhanuḥ cyutānām viyanti dadṛśe bahudhā vrajaḥ śarāsanāt ādhiratheḥ prabhavantaḥ sma sāyakāḥ śreṇīkṛtāḥ vyarājanta rājan krauñcāḥ iva ambare gārdhra patrān śilā dhautān kārtasvara vibhūṣitān mahā vegān pradīpta agrān mumoca ādhirathiḥ śarān te tu cāpa bala uddhūtāḥ śātakumbha vibhūṣitāḥ te vyomni ratna vikṛtāḥ vyakāśanta sahasraśas śalabhānām iva vrātāḥ śarāḥ karṇa samīritāḥ cāpāt ādhiratheḥ muktāḥ prapatantaḥ sma sāyakāḥ ekaḥ dīrghaḥ iva prāṃśuḥ prabhavan dṛśyate śaraḥ parvatam vāri dhārābhiḥ chādayan iva toyadaḥ karṇaḥ prācchādayat kruddhaḥ bhīmam sāyaka vṛṣṭibhiḥ tām samudram iva uddhūtām śara vṛṣṭim samutthitām rukma pṛṣṭham mahat cāpam bhīmasya āsīt viśām pate ākarṣāt maṇḍalībhūtam śakra cāpam iva aparam tasmāt śarāḥ prādurāsan pūrayantaḥ iva ambaram gagane racitā mālā kāñcanī iva vyarājata tatas vyomni viṣaktāni śara jālāni bhāgaśas āhatāni vyaśīryanta bhīmasenasya pattribhiḥ taiḥ taiḥ kanaka puṅkhānām dyauḥ āsīt saṃvṛtā vrajaiḥ na sma sūryaḥ tadā ābhāti na sma vāti samīraṇaḥ śara jāla āvṛte vyomni na ca ajñāyata kim cana sa bhīmam chādayan bāṇaiḥ sūtaputraḥ pṛthagvidhaiḥ upārohat an ādṛtya tasya vīryam mahātmanaḥ tayoḥ visṛjatoḥ tatra śara jālāni māriṣa vāyu bhūtāni adṛśyanta saṃsaktāni itaretaram ākāśe bharata śreṣṭha pāvakaḥ samajāyata tasmai karṇaḥ śitān bāṇān karmāra parimārjitān suvarṇa vikṛtān kruddhaḥ prāhiṇot vadha kāṅkṣayā viśeṣayan sūtaputram bhīmaḥ tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt punar ca asṛjat ugra śara varṣāṇi pāṇḍavaḥ tatas caṭacaṭā śabdaḥ godhā ghātāt abhūt tayoḥ tala śabdaḥ ca su mahān siṃhanādaḥ ca bhairavaḥ ratha nemi ninādaḥ ca jyā śabdaḥ ca eva dāruṇaḥ yodhāḥ vyupāraman yuddhāt didṛkṣantaḥ parākramam karṇa pāṇḍavayoḥ rājan paraspara vadha eṣiṇoḥ mumucuḥ puṣpa varṣam ca vidyādhara gaṇāḥ tathā tatas bhīmaḥ mahā bāhuḥ saṃrambhī dṛḍha vikramaḥ astraiḥ astrāṇi saṃvārya śaraiḥ vivyādha sūtajam karṇaḥ api bhīmasenasya nivārya iṣūn mahā balaḥ prāhiṇot nava nārācān āśīviṣa samān raṇe nārācān sūtaputrasya tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt tatas bhīmaḥ mahā bāhuḥ śaram kruddha antaka upamam tribhiḥ śaraiḥ śaram rājan pāṇḍavasya pratāpavān punar ca asṛjat ugrāṇi śara varṣāṇi pāṇḍavaḥ tasya tāni ādade karṇaḥ sarvāṇi astrāṇi abhīta vat yudhyataḥ pāṇḍu putrasya sūtaputraḥ astra māyayā tasya iṣudhī dhanuḥ jyām ca bāṇaiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ raśmīn yoktrāṇi ca aśvānām karṇaḥ vaikartanaḥ acchinat atha asya aśvān punar hatvā tribhiḥ vivyādha sārathim dhvajam ciccheda rādheyaḥ patākāḥ ca nyapātayat sa vidhanvā mahā rāja ratha śaktim parāmṛśat tām avāsṛjat āvidhya kruddhaḥ karṇa ratham prati tām ādhirathiḥ āyastaḥ śaktim hema pariṣkṛtām āpatatīm mahā ulkā ābhām ciccheda daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ sā apatat daśadhā rājan nikṛttā karṇa sāyakaiḥ sa dhanuḥ sūtaputrasya chittvā jyām ca su saṃśitaḥ vyāyacchat sa śarān karṇaḥ kuntī putra jighāṃsayā sahasraśas mahā rāja rukma puṅkhān su tejanān sa vadhyamānaḥ balavān karṇa cāpa cyutaiḥ śaraiḥ tasya tat caritam dṛṣṭvā saṃgrāme vijaya eṣiṇaḥ tat asya kuravaḥ sarve cāraṇāḥ ca abhyapūjayan yat iyeṣa rathāt karṇam hantum tārkṣyaḥ iva uragam sva ratham pṛṣṭhatas kṛtvā yuddhāya eva vyavasthitaḥ saṃrabdhaḥ pāṇḍavam saṃkhye yuddhāya samupasthitam tayoḥ āsīt saṃprahāraḥ kruddhayoḥ nara siṃhayoḥ amṛṣyamāṇayoḥ saṃkhye deva dānavayoḥ iva kṣīṇa śastraḥ tu kaunteyaḥ karṇena samabhidrutaḥ śaraiḥ bhīmam atikramya karṇaḥ bhṛśam apīḍayat amṛṣyamāṇaḥ ca bhṛśam śāntaḥ karṇa astra pīḍitaḥ dṛṣṭvā arjuna hatān nāgān patitān parvata upamān ratha mārga vighāta artham vyāyudhaḥ praviveśa ha pāṇḍavaḥ jīvita ākāṅkṣī rādheyam na abhyahārayat vyavasthānam atha ākāṅkṣan dhanaṃjaya śaraiḥ hatam ratha ayutāni cikṣepa hayānām ayutāni ca nara ayutāni ca tathā karṇāya amita tejase śakti ṛṣṭi prāsa parigha kampana ākuṭa mudgarān cikṣepa karṇāya balī gṛhītvā medinī talāt tān kṣiptān bhīma bala vat vāyunā samudīrayan raṇa aṅgaṇa abhyāsa gataḥ ciccheda āśu vṛṣaḥ tadā mahā grahaḥ iva āviṣṭaḥ nirviṣaṇṇaḥ vṛkodaraḥ hasti aṅgāni atha karṇāya prāhiṇot pāṇḍavaḥ nadan cakrāṇi aśvān tathā vāhān yat yat paśyati bhū tale tat tat ādāya cikṣepa kruddhaḥ karṇāya pāṇḍavaḥ tat asya sarvam ciccheda kṣiptam kṣiptam śitaiḥ śaraiḥ śaktaḥ api na avadhīt karṇam samarthaḥ pāṇḍu nandanaḥ rakṣamāṇaḥ pratijñām tām yā kṛtā savyasācinā tam evam vyākulam bhīmam bhūyas bhūyas śitaiḥ śaraiḥ mūrcchayā abhiparīta aṅgam akarot sūtanandanaḥ vyāyudham na avadhīt ca enam karṇaḥ kuntyāḥ vacaḥ smaran dhanuṣaḥ agreṇa tam karṇaḥ tu abhidrutya parāmṛśat dhanuṣā spṛṣṭa mātreṇa kruddhaḥ sarpaḥ iva śvasan tāḍitaḥ bhīmasenena krodhāt ārakta locanaḥ a kṛtāstraka mā yotsīḥ bāla saṃgrāma kātara yatra bhojyam bahuvidham bhakṣyam peyam ca pāṇḍava sūdam tvām aham ājāne mātsya preṣyaka kārakam puṣpa mūla phala āhāraḥ vrateṣu niyameṣu ca sūdān bhṛtyajanān dāsān tvam gṛhe tvarayan bhṛśam yogyaḥ tāḍayitum krodhāt bhojana artham vṛkodara saṃjayaḥ evam tam viratham dṛṣṭvā smṛtvā karṇaḥ abravīt vacaḥ kaumāre yāni ca api āsan apriyāṇi viśām pate pūrva vṛttāni ca api enam rūkṣāṇi aśrāvayat bhṛśam rādheya śṛṇu mama vākyam sūryaputra bala adhika yuṣmābhiḥ yadi aham mārgyaḥ tadā kim bahu jalpitaiḥ atha tvayā na mārgyaḥ aham tadā gacchāmi muñca mām evam tam virathīkṛtya uccais saṃtarjya pāṇḍavam mudā paramayā yuktaḥ darśayan kṛṣṇa pāṇḍavau atha enam tatra saṃlīnam aspṛśat dhanuṣā punar prahasan ca punar vākyam bhīmam āha vṛṣaḥ tadā yoddhavyam āviśān yatra na yoddhavyam tu mādṛśaiḥ mādṛśaiḥ yudhyamānānām etat ca anyat ca vidyate gaccha vā yatra tau kṛṣṇau tau tvā rakṣiṣyataḥ raṇe bhīma śabda artha sadbhāvī purāṇaḥ tvam hi mama mataḥ mārutiḥ māruta sutaḥ śastreṣu astreṣu ca uttamaḥ nipuṇaḥ asi sadā bhīma na tvam yuddha viśārada tam utsmayan kaṇṭha deśe pāṇinā saṃspṛśan vṛṣaḥ chattra vajra aṅkuśa aṅkena mātuḥ vākyam anusmaran karṇasya vacanam śrutvā bhīmasenaḥ ati dāruṇam vaca karṇam prahasan sarveṣām śṛṇvatām vacaḥ jitaḥ tvam asakṛt duṣṭa katthase tvam vṛthak ātmanā tathā tvām ghātayiṣyāmi paśyatsu sarva rājasu bhīmasya matam ājñāya karṇaḥ buddhimatām varaḥ virarāma raṇāt tasmāt paśyatām sarva dhanvinām bhīmaḥ api rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ dhanadāt śāpam āptavan gataḥ padma apahāreṇa praṇāmam na akarot purā anena kāraṇena eva karṇāt bhayam avāptavān karṇena api tadā utsṛṣṭaḥ mātuḥ vacana kāriṇā evam tam viratham kṛtvā karṇaḥ rājan vyakatthata pramukhe vṛṣṇi siṃhasya pārthasya ca mahātmanaḥ tam bruvāṇam tu bhīmaḥ tu kāṅkṣan bhīma parākramaḥ na ca akārṣīt drutam smṛtvā hi arjunasya mahā balam tasya kārmukam ārujya babhañja āśu parākramī tatas dṛṣṭvā mahā rāja vāsudevaḥ mahā dyutiḥ saṃjayaḥ arjuna arjuna paśya imam bhīmam karṇena bādhitam evam uktaḥ tadā pārthaḥ keśavena mahātmanā bhīmasenam tathābhūtam krodha saṃrakta locanaḥ amarṣa vaśam āpannaḥ nirdahan iva cakṣuṣā karṇena virathīkṛtya tarjyamānam vṛkodaram dṛṣṭvā arjunaḥ bhṛśam kruddhaḥ krodha saṃrakta locanaḥ tatas rājan śilā dhautān śarān śākhāmṛga dhvajaḥ prāhiṇot sūtaputrāya keśavena pracoditaḥ tatas pārtha bhuja utsṛṣṭāḥ śarāḥ kāñcana bhūṣaṇāḥ gāṇḍīva prabhavāḥ karṇam haṃsāḥ krauñcam iva āviśan sa bhujaṃgaiḥ iva āyastaiḥ gāṇḍīva preṣitaiḥ śaraiḥ bhīmasenāt apāsedhat sūtaputram dhanaṃjayaḥ karṇaḥ bhīmāt apāyāsīt rathena mahatā drutam bhīmaḥ api sātyakeḥ vāham samāruhya nara ṛṣabhaḥ anvayāt bhrātaram saṃkhye pāṇḍavam savyasācinam tatas karṇam samuddiś tvaramāṇaḥ dhanaṃjaya nārācam krodha tāmra akṣaḥ praiṣīt mṛtyum iva antakaḥ nārācaḥ abhyapatat karṇam tūrṇam gāṇḍīva coditaḥ tam antarikṣe nārācam drauṇiḥ ciccheda pattriṇā dhanaṃjaya bhayāt karṇam ujjihīrṣuḥ mahā rathaḥ tatas drauṇim catuḥṣaṣṭyā vivyādha kupitaḥ arjuna śareṇa ekena vivyātha tam rājānam mahā balaḥ karṇe pārthena vikṣiptam nārācam drauṇiḥ acchinat śilīmukhaiḥ mahā rāja mā gāḥ tiṣṭha iti ca bravīt sa tu matta gaja ākīrṇam anīkam ratha saṃkulam tūrṇam abhyāviśat drauṇiḥ dhanaṃjaya śara arditaḥ tatas suvarṇa pṛṣṭha dhanuṣām kūj raṇa śabdam gāṇḍīva ghoṣeṇa kaunteyaḥ abhyabhavat balī dhanaṃjayaḥ tathā yāntam pṛṣṭhatas drauṇim abhyayāt na ati dīrgham iva adhvānam śaraiḥ saṃtrāsayan balam vidārya dehān nārācaiḥ nara vāraṇa vājinām pākaśāsanaḥ āyastaḥ pārthaḥ saṃnijaghāna ha uvāca dātavyam adya manye aham pāṇḍavānām svakam punar pādayoḥ praṇatena api bhuktvā api ucchiṣṭam api areḥ a jīvataḥ tathā eva āsīt na sukham na parā gatiḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ tu saṃkruddhaḥ praviṣṭaḥ māmakam balam rakṣitam droṇa karṇābhyām apraveśyam suraiḥ api tābhyām ūrjita vīryābhyām āpyāyita parākramaḥ sahitaḥ kṛṣṇa bhīmābhyām śinīnām ṛṣabhena ca tadā prabhṛti mā śokaḥ dahati agniḥ iva āśayam grastān hi pratipaśyāmi bhūmipālān sa saindhavān apriyam su mahat kṛtvā sindhurājaḥ kirīṭinaḥ cakṣuḥ viṣayam āpannaḥ katham mucyeta jīvitaḥ anumānāt ca paśyāmi na asti saṃjaya saindhavaḥ yuddham tu tat yathā vṛttam tat mama ācakṣva pṛcchataḥ yat ca vikṣobhya mahatīm senām saṃloḍya ca asakṛt ekaḥ praviṣṭaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ nalinīm iva kuñjaraḥ tasya vṛṣṇi pravīrasya brūhi yuddham yathātatham uvāca tathā tu vaikartana pīḍitam tam bhīmam prayāntam puruṣa pravīram na aśaknuvan vārayitum tvadīyāḥ sarve rathāḥ bhārata mādhava agryam amarṣa pūrṇaḥ tu anivṛtta yodhī śarāsanī kāñcana varma dhārī anāgatān eva tu tān pṛṣatkān ciccheda bāṇaiḥ śini puṃgavaḥ api punar sa bāṇaiḥ tribhiḥ agni kalpaiḥ ākarṇapūrṇaiḥ niśitaiḥ su puṅkhaiḥ vivyādha deha āvaraṇam vidārya te sātyakeḥ āviviśuḥ śarīram ājaghnivān tān rajata prakāśān aśvān caturbhiḥ caturaḥ prasahya sa kuṇḍalam pūrṇa śaśi prakāśam bhrājiṣṇu vaktram nicakarta dehāt nihatya tam pārthiva putra pautram saṃkhye madhūnām ṛṣabhaḥ pramāthī anvāgatam vṛṣṇi varam samīkṣya tathā ari madhye parivartamānam ghnantam kurūṇām iṣubhiḥ balāni punar punar vāyuḥ iva abhra pūgān tatas avahan saindhavāḥ sādhu dāntāḥ go kṣīra kunda indu hima prakāśāḥ suvarṇa jāla avatatāḥ sat aśvāḥ yatas yatas kāmayate nṛ siṃhaḥ kṛtvā mukham bhārata yodha mukhyam duḥśāsanam tvad sutam ājamīḍha te sarvatas saṃparivārya saṃkhye śaineyam ājaghnuḥ anīka sāhāḥ sa ca api tān pravaraḥ sātvatānām nyavārayat bāṇa jālena vīraḥ nivārya tān tūrṇam amitra ghātī naptā śineḥ pattribhiḥ agni kalpaiḥ duḥśāsanasya api jaghāna vāhān udyamya bāṇāsanam ājamīḍha kṛṣṇaḥ ca dṛṣṭvā puruṣa pravīram uvāca tam udyatam mahā bāhum duḥśāsana ratham prati tvaritam tvaraṇīyeṣu dhanaṃjaya hita eṣiṇam trigartānām mahā iṣvāsāḥ suvarṇa vikṛta dhvajāḥ senā samudram āviṣṭam ānartam paryavārayan avākiran śara vrātaiḥ kruddhāḥ parama dhanvinaḥ ajayat rāja putrān tān yatamānān mahā raṇe ekaḥ pañcāśatam śatrūn sātyakiḥ satya vikramaḥ saṃprāpya bhāratī madhyam tala ghoṣa samākulam asi śakti gadā pūrṇam aplavam salilam yathā atha enam anuvṛttāḥ tu trigartāḥ sahitāḥ punar tīvreṇa ratha vaṃśena mahatā paryavārayan vikarṣantaḥ atimātrāṇi cāpāni bharata ṛṣabha tatra adbhutam apaśyāma śaineya caritam raṇe pratyañci diśi tam dṛṣṭvā prācyām paśyāma lāghavāt udīcīm dakṣiṇām prācīm pratīcīm prasṛtaḥ tathā nṛtyan iva acarat śūraḥ yathā ratha śatam tathā tat dṛṣṭvā caritam tasya siṃha vikrānta gāminaḥ trigartāḥ saṃnyavartanta saṃtaptāḥ sva janam prati tām ca senām atikramya trigartānām nara ṛṣabhaḥ ajayat śūrasenān ca yatamānān mahā raṇe ekaḥ tatas mahā bāhuḥ sahasrān śatru tāpanaḥ saṃnaddhānām padātīnām avadhīt puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ tam anye śūrasenānām śūrāḥ saṃkhye nyavārayan niyacchantaḥ śara vrātaiḥ mattam dvipam iva aṅkuśaiḥ tān nyavārayat āyastān muhūrtam iva sātyakiḥ tām ca senām atikramya kaliṅgānām duratyayām atha pārtham mahā bāhuḥ dhanaṃjayam upāsadat jaghāna su bahūn yaudhān śataśas atha sahasraśas te hatāḥ nipatanti sma pramṛṣṭāḥ dīrgha bāhunā tatas prāyāt asambhrāntaḥ dadarśa ca dhanaṃjayam tam dṛṣṭvā puruṣa vyāghram yuyudhānaḥ samāśvasat asau āyāti śaineyaḥ te pārtha padānugaḥ eṣa śiṣyaḥ sakhā ca eva tava satya parākramaḥ sarvān yodhān tṛṇīkṛtya vijigye puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ eṣa kaurava yodhānām kṛtvā ghoram upadravam tava prāṇaiḥ priyataraḥ kirīṭin eti sātyakiḥ eṣa droṇam tathā bhojam kṛtavarmāṇam eva ca kadarthīkṛtya viśikhaiḥ phalguna abhyeti sātyakiḥ dharmarāja priya anveṣī hatvā yodhān varān varān śūraḥ ca eva kṛtāstraḥ ca phalguna abhyeti sātyakiḥ tava darśanam anvicchan pāṇḍava abhyeti sātyakiḥ ācārya pramukhān pārtha āyāti eṣa hi sātyakiḥ sva bāhu balam āśritya vidārya ca varūthinīm priya śiṣyaḥ ca te pārtha tvayā tulya parākramaḥ vidārya kauravām senām eṣaḥ āyāti satyakaḥ nihatya bahulāḥ senāḥ pārtha eṣaḥ abhyeti sātyakiḥ eṣa rāja sahasrāṇām vaktraiḥ paṅkaja saṃnibhaiḥ āstīrya vasudhām pārtha kṣipram āyāti sātyakiḥ eṣa duryodhanam jitvā bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitam raṇe nihatya jalasaṃdham ca kṣipram āyāti sātyakiḥ rudhira oghavatīm kṛtvā nadīm śoṇita kardamām rudhirasya nadīm kṛtvā rathebha nara vājinām tṛṇa vat nyasya kauravyān eṣaḥ āyāti sātyakiḥ iti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā keśavasya arjunaḥ tadā tatas aprahṛṣṭaḥ kaunteyaḥ keśavam vākyam abravīt na me priyam mahā bāho yat mām abhyeti sātyakiḥ na hi jānāmi vṛttāntam dharmarājasya keśava sātvatena vihīnaḥ sa yadi jīvati vā na vā etena hi mahā bāho rakṣitavyaḥ sa pārthivaḥ tam eṣa katham utsṛjya mama kṛṣṇa padānugaḥ rājā droṇāya ca utsṛṣṭaḥ saindhavaḥ ca a nipātitaḥ pratyudyātaḥ ca śaineyam eṣa bhūriśravāḥ raṇe jñātavyaḥ ca hi mama rājā rakṣitavyaḥ ca sātyakiḥ śrāntaḥ ca eṣa mahā bāhuḥ alpa prāṇaḥ ca sāṃpratam pariśrāntāḥ hayāḥ ca asya haya yantā ca mādhava na ca bhūriśravāḥ śrāntaḥ sa sahāyaḥ ca keśava bhūriśravāḥ kṛtāstraḥ ca rakṣyaḥ mādhava satyakaḥ api idānīm bhavet asya kṣemam asmin samāgame kaccit na sāgaram tīrtvā sātyakiḥ satya vikramaḥ goṣpadam prāpya sīdeta mahā ojāḥ śini puṃgavaḥ ācāryāt bhayam utsṛjya yaḥ preṣayati sātyakim grahaṇam dharmarājasya khagaḥ śyenaḥ iva āmiṣam nityam āśaṃsate droṇaḥ kaccit syāt kuśalī nṛpaḥ āmiṣa arthī yathā śyenaḥ nityam tiṣṭhati brāhmaṇaḥ uvāca krodhāt bhūriśravāḥ rājan sahasā samupādravat tam abravīt mahā bāhuḥ kauravyaḥ śini puṃgavam adya prāptaḥ asi diṣṭyā me cakṣuḥ viṣayam iti uta cira abhilaṣitam kāmam adya prāpsyāmi saṃyuge adya tvām samare hatvā nityam śūra abhimāninam nandayiṣyāmi dāśārha kuru rājam suyodhanam adya mad bāṇa nirdagdham patitam dharaṇī tale drakṣyataḥ tvām raṇe vīrau sahitau keśava arjunau adya dharmasutaḥ rājā śrutvā tvām nihatam mayā sa vrīḍaḥ bhavitā sadyas yena asi iha praveśitaḥ adya yuddham mahā ghoram tava dāsyāmi sātvata adya saṃyamanīm yātā mayā tvam nihataḥ raṇe yathā rāma anujena ājau rāvaṇiḥ lakṣmaṇena vai adya kṛṣṇaḥ ca pārthaḥ ca dharmarājaḥ ca mādhava hate tvayi nirutsāhāḥ raṇam tyakṣyanti asaṃśayam adya te apacitim kṛtvā śitaiḥ mādhava sāyakaiḥ cakṣuḥ viṣaya saṃprāptaḥ na tvam mādhava mokṣyase siṃhasya viṣayam prāptaḥ yathā kṣudra mṛgaḥ tathā na aham bhīṣayitum śakyaḥ vāc mātreṇa tu kevalam sa mām nihanyāt saṃgrāme yaḥ mām kuryāt nirāyudham samāḥ tu śāśvatīḥ hanyāt yaḥ mām hanyāt hi saṃyuge kim mṛṣā uktena bahunā karmaṇā tu samācara na a hatvā saṃnivartiṣye tvām adya puruṣa adhama bhūriśravāḥ sātyakiḥ ca vavarṣatuḥ ariṃdamau śara varṣāṇi bhīmāni meghau iva parasparam tau ubhau śara varṣābhyām anyonyam abhivarṣatām bhūriśravāḥ sātyakiḥ ca saumadattiḥ tu śaineyam pracchādya iṣubhiḥ āśugaiḥ jighāṃsuḥ bharata śreṣṭha vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ daśabhiḥ sātyakim viddhvā saumadattiḥ atha aparān mumoca niśitān bāṇān jighāṃsuḥ śini puṃgavam saumadattiḥ śarān asyan tān asya viśikhān tīkṣṇān antarikṣe viśām pate tau pṛthak śara varṣābhyām avarṣetām parasparam uttama abhijanau vīrau kuru vṛṣṇi yaśaskarau ratha śaktibhiḥ anyonyam viśikhaiḥ ca api akṛntatām vyaṣṭambhayetām anyonyam prāṇa dyūta abhidevinaḥ evam uttama karmāṇau kuru vṛṣṇi yaśaskarau parasparam ayudhyetām vāraṇau iva yūthapau sātyakiḥ saumadattiḥ ca śara vṛṣṭyā parasparam hṛṣṭa vat dhārtarāṣṭrāṇām paśyatām abhyavarṣatām vṛṣṭim tām abhivarṣantau śarāṇām mahatīm tadā saṃpraikṣanta janāḥ tatra yudhyamānau yudhām patī yūthapau vāśitā hetoḥ prayuddhau iva kuñjarau bhūyas bhūyas śaraiḥ rājñ takṣantau krodha mūrchitau ayudhyatām mahā raṅge vane kesariṇaḥ iva atha anyonyam patākāḥ ca ratha upakaraṇāni ca saṃcicchedatuḥ āyastau bāṇaiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ punar ca śara varṣābhyām anyonyam abhivarṣatām virathau asi yuddhāya sameyātām mahā raṇe ārṣabhe carmaṇī citre pragṛhya vipule śubhe vikośau ca api asī kṛtvā samare tau viceratuḥ carantau vividhān mārgān maṇḍalāni ca bhāgaśas sa khaḍgau citra varmāṇau sa niṣka aṅgada bhūṣaṇau saṃpātam samudīrṇam ca darśayantau yaśasvinaḥ darśayantau ubhau śikṣām lāghavam sauṣṭhavam tathā raṇe raṇa utkaṭau rājan anyonyam paryakarṣatām paśyatām sarva sainyānām vīrau āśvasatām punar asibhyām carmaṇī śubhre vipule ca śarāvare śikṣā bala samudbhūtāḥ sarva yodha praharṣaṇāḥ dvipau iva viṣāṇa agraiḥ śṛṅgaiḥ iva mahā ṛṣabhau bhuja yoktra avabandhaiḥ ca śirobhyām ca avaghātanaiḥ pāda avakarṣa saṃdānaiḥ tomara aṃkuśa lāsanaiḥ gata pratyāgata ākṣepaiḥ pātana utthāna saṃplutaiḥ dvātriṃśat karaṇāni syuḥ yāni yuddhāni bhārata kṣīṇa āyudhe sātvate yudhyamāne tatas abravīt arjunam vāsudevaḥ paśyasva enam viratham yudhyamānam raṇe ketum sarva dhanurdharāṇām uvāca sindhurāja vadhe saktam pārtham kṛṣṇaḥ abravīt punar sīdantam sātyakim paśya pārtha enam parirakṣa ca praviṣṭaḥ bhāratīm senām te pāṇḍava pṛṣṭhatas yodhitaḥ ca mahā vīryaiḥ sarvaiḥ bhārata bhārataiḥ dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ ca ye mukhyāḥ ye ca mukhyāḥ mahā rathāḥ nihatāḥ vṛṣṇi vīreṇa śataśas atha sahasraśas pariśrāntaḥ yudhām śreṣṭhaḥ saṃprāptaḥ bhūri dakṣiṇam yuddha kāṅkṣiṇam āyāntam na etat samam iva arjuna tatas bhūriśravāḥ kruddhaḥ sātyakim yuddha durmadam keśava arjunayoḥ rājan samare prekṣamāṇayoḥ atha kṛṣṇaḥ mahā bāhuḥ arjunam pratyabhāṣata paśya vṛṣṇi andhaka vyāghram saumadatti vaśam gatam pariśrāntam gatam bhūmau kṛtvā karma su duṣkaram tava antevāsinam śūram pālaya arjuna sātyakim na vaśam yajñaśīlasya gacchet eṣa vara ari han tvad kṛte puruṣa vyāghra tat āśu kriyatām vibho atha abravīt dhṛṣṭa manāḥ vāsudevam dhanaṃjayaḥ paśya vṛṣṇi pravīreṇa krīḍantam kuru puṃgavam uvāca iti evam bhāṣamāṇe tu pāṇḍave vai dhanaṃjaye hāhākāraḥ mahān asīt sainyānām bharata ṛṣabha pātite tu atha śaineye kṛṣṇaḥ arjunam abhāṣata sa siṃhaḥ iva mātaṅgam vikarṣan bhūri dakṣiṇaḥ mām eva ca mahā bāho pariyānti mahā rathāḥ dhruvam ca yodhayāmi etān chidra anveṣaṇa tatparān rakṣāmi sātyakim ca eva saumadattim vaśam gatam aprāptaḥ na mayā kṛṣṇa hantum bhūriśravāḥ raṇe avaśyam ca mayā kṛṣṇa vṛṣṇi vīrasya rakṣaṇam uvāca pareṇa nihataḥ mā sma prāṇān hāsīt mahā rathaḥ evam uktvā arjunaḥ kṛṣṇam parān āśu śitaiḥ śaraiḥ chādayām āsa saṃkruddhaḥ pare ca api dhanaṃjayam atha kośāt viniṣkṛṣya khaḍgam bhūriśravāḥ raṇe mūrdhajeṣu nijagrāha padā ca urasi atāḍayat śuśubhe sa bhujaḥ tasya tapanīya vibhūṣitaḥ tatas asya chettum ārabdhaḥ śiraḥ kāyāt sa kuṇḍalam tāvat kṣaṇāt sātvataḥ api śiraḥ saṃbhramayan tvaran yathā rathāṃgam kaulālaḥ daṇḍa viddham tu bhārata saha eva bhūriśravasaḥ bāhunā keśa dhāriṇā hāhākṛtam abhūt sarvam pāṇḍavānām mahat balam tāvakāḥ ca mudā yuktāḥ siṃhanādam vicukruśuḥ nimīlita akṣāḥ tu abhavan janāḥ saṃgrāma bhīravaḥ tathā tu parikṛṣyantam dṛṣṭvā sātvatam āhave paśya vṛṣṇi andhaka vyāghram saumadatti vaśam gatam tava śiṣyam mahā bāho dhanuṣi an avaram tvayā asatyaḥ vikramaḥ pārtha yatra bhūriśravāḥ raṇe viśeṣayati vārṣṇeyam sātyakim satya vikramam yuddhvā bhṛśam pariśrāntaḥ kṣīṇa āyudha paricchadaḥ evam uktaḥ mahā bāhuḥ vāsudevena pāṇḍavaḥ manasā pūjayām āsa bhūriśravasam āhave vikarṣan sātvata śreṣṭham krīḍamānaḥ iva āhave saṃharṣayati mām bhūyas kurūṇām kīrti vardhanaḥ pravaram vṛṣṇi vīrāṇām yat na hanyāt hi sātyakim evam tu manasā rājan pārthaḥ saṃpūjya kauravam vāsudevam mahā bāhuḥ arjunaḥ pratyabhāṣata saindhava āsakta dṛṣṭi tvāt na enam paśyāmi mādhava tam kṛṣṇa mokṣayiṣyāmi dāvāt siṃha śiśum yathā iti uktvā vacanam kurvan vāsudevasya pāṇḍavaḥ tatas kṣurapram niśitam gāṇḍīve samayojayat pārtha bāhu visṛṣṭaḥ sa mahā ulkā iva nabhas cyutā sa khaḍgam yajñaśīlasya patriṇā bāhum acchinat uvāca sa bāhuḥ apatat bhūmau sa khaḍgaḥ sa śubha aṅgadaḥ prahariṣyan hṛtaḥ bāhuḥ adṛśyena kirīṭinā sa mogham kṛtam ātmānam dṛṣṭvā pārthena kauravaḥ utsṛjya sātyakim krodhāt garhayām āsa pāṇḍavam sa vibāhuḥ mahā rājaḥ eka pakṣaḥ iva aṇḍajaḥ uvāca pāṇḍavam ca eva sarva kṣatrasya paśyataḥ nṛśaṃsam bata kaunteya karma idam kṛtavan asi kim nu vakṣyasi rājānam dharmaputram yudhiṣṭhiram kim kurvāṇaḥ mayā saṃkhye hataḥ bhūriśravāḥ iti idam indreṇa te sākṣāt upadiṣṭam mahātmanā astram rudreṇa vā pārtha droṇena atha kṛpeṇa vā āryeṇa sukaram hi āhuḥ ārya karma dhanaṃjaya āśu tad śīla tām eti tat idam tvayi dṛśyate katham hi rāja vaṃśyaḥ tvam kauraveya viśeṣataḥ kṣatra dharmāt apakrāntaḥ su vṛttaḥ carita vrataḥ vārṣṇeya apasadam prāpya kṣudram kṛtam idam tvayā idam tu yat ati kṣudram vārṣṇeya arthe kṛtam tvayā īdṛśam vyasanam dadyāt yaḥ na kṛṣṇasakhaḥ bhavet vrātyāḥ saṃśliṣ karmāṇaḥ prakṛtyā eva vigarhitāḥ vṛṣṇi andhakāḥ katham pārtha pramāṇam bhavatā kṛtāḥ uvāca hṛṣīkeśena saṃbandham garhase mām ca mūḍha vat raṇānām asi dharma jñaḥ sarva śāstra artha pāragaḥ na ca adharmam aham kuryām jānan ca eva hi muhyase yudhyante kṣatriyāḥ śatrūn svaiḥ svaiḥ parivṛtāḥ nṛpa bhrātṛbhiḥ pitṛbhiḥ putraiḥ tathā saṃbandhi bāndhavaiḥ aham hi sātyakim śiṣyam sukha saṃbandhim eva ca mad arthe yudhyamānam ca tyaktvā prāṇān su dustyajān mama bāhum raṇe rājan dakṣiṇam yuddha durmadam nikṛtyamānam tam dṛṣṭvā katham śatru vaśam gatam tvayā nikṛṣyamāṇam ca dṛṣṭavān asmi niṣkriyam taiḥ rakṣyamāṇaḥ sa nṛpaḥ rakṣitavyaḥ mahā mṛdhe yadi aham sātyakim dṛṣṭvā tūṣṇīm āsiṣye āhave yaśaḥ ca eva sva pakṣebhyaḥ phalam mitrasya rakṣaṇāt dhanuḥ jyām karṣataḥ ca eva yudhyataḥ saha śatrubhiḥ śrāntaḥ ca śrānta vāhaḥ ca kṣīṇa sarva āyudhaḥ tvayā īdṛśam sātyakim saṃkhye nirjitya ca mahā ratham adhikam tvam vijānīṣe tathā api anya manāḥ bhavān tathā kṛcchra gatam dṛṣṭvā sātyakim kaḥ kṣamiṣyati tvam tu garhaya ca ātmānam ātmānam yaḥ na rakṣasi katham kariṣyase vīra yaḥ vā tvām saṃśrayet janaḥ ātta śastrasya hi raṇe vṛṣṇī putram jighāṃsataḥ evam uktvā mahā bāhuḥ yūpaketuḥ mahā yaśāḥ dhanaṃjayena vīreṇa viniḥśvasya muhur muhur yuyudhānam parityajya raṇe prāyam upāviśat śarān āstīrya savyena pāṇinā puṇya lakṣaṇaḥ yiyāsuḥ brahma lokāya prāṇān prāṇeṣu atha ajuhot sūrye cakṣuḥ samādhāya prasannam salile manaḥ tatas sa sarva senāyām janaḥ kṛṣṇa dhanaṃjayau garhayām āsa tam ca api śaśaṃsa puruṣa ṛṣabham garhayām āsuḥ api etau śaśaṃsuḥ bhūri dakṣiṇam nindyamānau tathā kṛṣṇau na ūcatuḥ kim cit apriyam praśasyamānaḥ ca tathā na ahṛṣyat yūpaketanaḥ tān tathā vādinaḥ rājan putrān te dhanaṃjayaḥ amṛṣyamāṇaḥ manasā teṣām tasya ca bhāṣitam asaṃkruddha manāḥ vācā smārayan iva bhārata uvāca pāṇḍu tanayaḥ sa ākṣepam iva phalgunaḥ na śakyaḥ māmakaḥ hantum yaḥ me syāt bāṇa gocare yūpaketo samīkṣya tvam na mām garhitum arhasi ātta śastrasya hi raṇe vṛṣṇi vīram jighāṃsataḥ saumadatteḥ ayam sādhu sarva sāhāyya kāriṇaḥ asmadīyāḥ mayā rakṣyāḥ prāṇa bādhe upasthite satyakaḥ ca vaśam nītaḥ kauraveṇa mahātmanā uvāca uvāca ca enam kauravyam arjunaḥ śoka pīḍitaḥ avasthām īdṛśīm prāptaḥ śaraṇyaḥ śaraṇa pradaḥ yatra tvam puruṣa vyāghraḥ prāptaḥ pāpām imām daśām yatra tvam kuru śārdūla prāptaḥ pāpām imām daśām yad kṛte nara śārdūlaḥ prāptaḥ pāpām imām daśām kaḥ hi nāma pumān loke mādṛśaḥ puruṣottama evam uktaḥ tu pārthena śirasā bhūmim aspṛśat pāṇinā ca eva savyena prāhiṇot asya dakṣiṇam yūpaketuḥ mahā rāja tūṣṇīm āsīt avāṅmukhaḥ yā prītiḥ dharmarāje me bhīme ca vadatām vare mayā tu samanujñātaḥ kṛṣṇena ca mahātmanā gaccha puṇya kṛtām lokān śibiḥ auśīnaraḥ yathā ye lokāḥ mama vimalāḥ brahma ādyaiḥ sura vṛṣabhaiḥ api iṣyamāṇāḥ mad tulyaḥ bhava garuḍa uttama aṅga yānaḥ uvāca avāṅmukhāḥ babhūvuḥ ca sainikāḥ sarve eva te muhūrtāt iva viśramya sātyakiḥ krodha mūrcchitaḥ amarṣa vaśam āpannaḥ saumadatti nirākṛtaḥ uvāca khaḍgam ādāya cicchitsuḥ śiraḥ tasya mahātmanaḥ nihatam pāṇḍu putreṇa pramattam bhūri dakṣiṇam iyeṣa sātyakiḥ hantum śala agrajam akalmaṣam nivāryamāṇaḥ kṛṣṇena phalgunena ca māriṣa nṛśaṃsam kṛtavan pāpaḥ yuyudhānaḥ narādhipa krośatām sarva sainyānām nindyamānaḥ su durmanāḥ vāryamāṇaḥ sa kṛṣṇena pārthena ca mahātmanā bhīmena cakrarakṣābhyām aśvatthāmnā kṛpeṇa ca vikrośatām ca sainyānām avadhīt tam yata vratam prāya upaviṣṭāya raṇe pārthena chinna bāhave sātyakiḥ kaurava indrāya khaḍgena apāharat śiraḥ na abhyanandanta tat sainyāḥ sātyakim tena karmaṇā sahasrākṣa samam tatra siddha cāraṇa mānavāḥ pakṣa vādān ca bahuśas prāvadan tasya sainikāḥ na vārṣṇeyasya aparādhaḥ bhavitavyam hi tat tathā tasmāt manyuḥ na vaḥ kāryaḥ krodhaḥ duḥkha karaḥ nṛṇām hantavyaḥ ca eṣa vīreṇa na atra kāryā vicāraṇā dhik enam iti ca akrandan kṣatriyāḥ krodha mūrchitāḥ uvāca dharma vādaiḥ adharmiṣṭhāḥ dharma kañcukam āsthitāḥ yadā bālaḥ subhadrāyāḥ sutaḥ śastra vinākṛtaḥ mayā tu etat pratijñātam kṣepe kasmin cit eva hi śṛṇudhvam sarvam eva iha śrutvā garhatha mānavāḥ yaḥ mām niṣpiṣya saṃgrāme jīvan hanyāt padā ruṣā ceṣṭamānam pratīghāte sa bhujam mām sa cakṣuṣaḥ yuktaḥ hi asya pratīghātaḥ kṛtaḥ me kuru puṃgavāḥ yat tu pārthena mad snehāt svām pratijñām ca rakṣatā sa khaḍgaḥ asya hṛtaḥ bāhuḥ etena eva asmi vañcitaḥ api ca ayam purā gītaḥ ślokaḥ vālmīkinā bhuvi sarvakālam manuṣyeṇa vyavasāyavatā sadā pīḍā karam amitrāṇām yat syāt kartavyam eva tat anuṣṭhitam mayā tat ca tasmāt garhatha mūḍha vat uvāca evam ukte mahā rāja sarve kaurava pāṇḍavāḥ su nīla keśam vara dasya tasya śūrasya pārāvata lohita akṣam dṛṣṭvā su nāsam su kapola yuktam ākrāmat ūrdhvam vara daḥ vara arhaḥ vyāvṛtya dharmeṇa pareṇa rodasī uvāca ajitaḥ droṇa bhīṣmābhyām karṇena ca kṛpeṇa ca tīrṇaḥ sainya arṇavam vīraḥ pratiśrutya yudhiṣṭhire nigṛhya bhūriśravasā balāt bhuvi nipātitaḥ uvāca śṛṇu rājan iha utpattim śaineyasya yathā purā yathā ca bhūriśravasaḥ yatra te saṃśayaḥ nṛpa yaduḥ nāma mahā rāja sarva śāstra viśāradaḥ budhasya āsīt mahā indra ābhaḥ putraḥ ekaḥ purūravāḥ purūravasaḥ āyūḥ tu āyuṣaḥ nahuṣaḥ smṛtaḥ nahuṣasya yayātiḥ tu rājarṣiḥ deva saṃmitaḥ yayāteḥ devayānyām tu yaduḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ abhavat sutaḥ yadoḥ abhūt anvavāye devamīḍhaḥ iti śrutaḥ śūrasya śauriḥ nṛvaraḥ vasudevaḥ mahā yaśāḥ dhanuṣi an avaraḥ śūraḥ kārtavīrya samaḥ yudhi tad vīryaḥ ca api tatra eva kule śiniḥ abhūt nṛpaḥ tatra vai devakīm devīm vasudeva artham āptavān tām dṛṣṭvā devakīm śaure ratha sthām puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ tām dṛṣṭvā nīyamānām tu vasudevāya devakīm na amṛṣyata mahā tejāḥ somadattaḥ śineḥ nṛpa madhye rāja sahasrāṇām prekṣakāṇām samantataḥ prasādayan mahādevam amarṣa vaśam āsthitaḥ tasya tuṣ mahādevaḥ varāṇām vara daḥ prabhuḥ vareṇa chandayām āsa sa tu vavre varam nṛpaḥ madhye rāja sahasrāṇām padā hanyāt ca saṃyuge sa śiraḥ kampam āha idam na etat evam bhavet nṛpa na tu mārayitum śakyaḥ kṛṣṇa saṃrakṣitaḥ hi asau na ati hṛṣṭa manāḥ saḥ api puram āgāt mahīpatiḥ paśyatām sarva sainyānām padā ca enam atāḍayat na hi śakyāḥ raṇe jetum sātvatāḥ manuja ṛṣabha labdha lakṣyāḥ ca saṃgrāme bahavaḥ citra yodhinaḥ na tulyam vṛṣṇibhiḥ iha dṛśyate kim cana prabho na jñātim avamanyante vṛddhānām śāsane ratāḥ na deva asura gandharvāḥ na yakṣa uraga rākṣasāḥ jetāraḥ vṛṣṇi vīrāṇām na punar mānuṣāḥ raṇe eteṣām rakṣitāraḥ ca ye syuḥ kasyām cit āpadi nityam deva pare dāntāḥ dātāraḥ ca a vikatthanāḥ tena vṛṣṇi pravīrāṇām cakram na pratihanyate na tu vṛṣṇi pravīrāṇām sametya antam vrajet nṛpa śineḥ duhitṛ saṃbhūtaḥ eṣa vīraḥ sa sātyakiḥ uvāca uvāca bhūriśravasi saṃkrānte para lokāya bhārata vāsudevam mahā bāhuḥ arjunaḥ samacūcudat codaya aśvān bhṛśam kṛṣṇa yatas rājā jayadrathaḥ śrūyate puṇḍarīkākṣa triṣu dharmeṣu vartate astam eti mahā bāho tvaramāṇaḥ divākaraḥ kāryam saṃrakṣyate ca eṣa kuru senā mahā rathaiḥ codaya aśvān tathā kṛṣṇa yathā hanyām jayadratham uvāca sa smitau samudekṣetām prauḍhā bālā vadhūḥ iva tatas kṛṣṇaḥ mahā bāhuḥ rajata pratimān hayān tvaramāṇāḥ mahā rāja senā mukhyāḥ samāvrajan duryodhanaḥ ca karṇaḥ ca vṛṣasenaḥ atha madra rāj netrābhyām krodha dīptābhyām saṃpraikṣat nirdahan iva amānuṣāṇi karmāṇi kurvantau puruṣa ṛṣabhau arjunam vīkṣya saṃyāntam jayadratha ratham prati uvāca rājñ putraḥ te karṇam rājā suyodhanaḥ alpa avaśiṣṭam divasam nṛ vīra vighātayasva adya ripum śara oghaiḥ mithyāpratijñaḥ kaunteyaḥ pravekṣyati hutāśanam vinaṣṭaiḥ pāṇḍaveyaiḥ ca sa śaila vana kānanām vasuṃdharām imām karṇa bhokṣyāmaḥ hata kaṇṭakām kārya akāryam a jānan vai pratijñām kṛtavan raṇe nūnam ātma vināśāya pāṇḍavena kirīṭinā rakṣitam madra rājena kṛpeṇa ca mahātmanā drauṇinā rakṣyamāṇam ca mayā duḥśāsanena ca katham prāpsyati bībhatsuḥ saindhavam kāla coday yudhyante bahavaḥ śūrāḥ lambate ca divākaraḥ sa tvam karṇa mayā sārdham śūraiḥ ca anyaiḥ mahā rathaiḥ drauṇinā tvam hi sahitaḥ madra īśena kṛpeṇa ca dṛḍha lakṣyeṇa śūreṇa bhīmasenena dhanvinā bhṛśam udvejitaḥ saṃkhye śara jālaiḥ anekaśas sthātavyam iti tiṣṭhāmi raṇe saṃprati mānada na eva aṅgam iṅgati kim cit me saṃtaptasya raṇa iṣubhiḥ yotsyāmi tu tathā rājan śaktyā mama parayā raṇe na hi me yudhyamānasya sāyakān ca asyataḥ śitān saindhavam prāpsyate vīraḥ savyasācī dhanaṃjayaḥ yat tu śaktimatā kāryam satatam hita kāriṇā tvad priya artham mahā rāja jayaḥ daive pratiṣṭhitaḥ adya yotsye arjunam aham pauruṣam svam vyapāśritaḥ paśyantu sarva bhūtāni dāruṇam loma harṣaṇam karṇa kauravayoḥ evam raṇe saṃbhāṣamāṇayoḥ arjunaḥ niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ jaghāna te vāhinīm ciccheda tīkṣṇa agra mukhaiḥ śūrāṇām anivartinām bhujān parigha saṃkāśān hasti hasta upamān raṇe śirāṃsi ca mahā bāhuḥ ciccheda niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ hasti hastān haya grīvāḥ ratha akṣān ca samantataḥ śoṇita aktān haya ārohān gṛhīta prāsa tomarān haya vāraṇa mukhyāḥ ca prāpatanta sahasraśas dhvajāḥ chatrāṇi cāpāni cāmarāṇi śirāṃsi ca acireṇa mahīm pārthaḥ cakāra rudhira uttarām hata bhūyiṣṭha yodham tat kṛtvā tava balam balī āsasāda durādharṣaḥ saindhavam satya vikramaḥ tam tathā avasthitam dṛṣṭvā tvadīyāḥ vīrya saṃmatāḥ na amṛṣyanta mahā iṣvāsāḥ phalgunam puruṣa ṛṣabhāḥ duryodhanaḥ ca karṇaḥ ca vṛṣasenaḥ atha madra rāj saṃrabdhāḥ saindhavasya arthe samāvṛṇvan kirīṭinam saṃgrāma kovidam pārtham sarve yuddha viśāradāḥ saindhavam pṛṣṭhatas kṛtvā jighāṃsantaḥ arjuna acyutau te bhujaiḥ bhogi bhoga ābhaiḥ dhanūṃṣi āyamya sāyakān mumucuḥ sūrya raśmi ābhān śataśas phalgunam prati tān astān asyamānān ca kirīṭī yuddha durmadaḥ dvidhā tridhā aṣṭadhā ekaikam chittvā vivyādha tān raṇe siṃha lāṅgūla ketuḥ tu darśayan śaktim ātmanaḥ śāradvatī sutaḥ rājan arjunam pratyavārayat sa viddhvā daśabhiḥ pārtham vāsudevam ca sapta atha enam kaurava śreṣṭhāḥ sarve eva mahā rathāḥ visphārayantaḥ cāpāni visṛjantaḥ ca sāyakān iṣūṇām akṣaya tvam ca dhanuṣaḥ gāṇḍivasya ca astraiḥ astrāṇi saṃvārya drauṇeḥ śāradvatasya ca tam drauṇiḥ pañcaviṃśatyā vṛṣasenaḥ ca sapta śliṣṭam tu sarvatas cakruḥ ratha maṇḍalam āśu te sūrya astamayam icchantaḥ tvaramāṇāḥ mahā rathāḥ siṣicuḥ mārgaṇaiḥ ghoraiḥ girim meghāḥ iva ambuṣu dhanaṃjayasya gātreṣu śūrāḥ parigha bāhavaḥ nivārya tān śara vrātaiḥ divyāni astrāṇi darśayan hata bhūyiṣṭha yodham tat kṛtvā tava balam balī āsasāda durādharṣaḥ saindhavam satya vikramaḥ tam karṇaḥ saṃyuge rājan pratyavārayat āśugaiḥ tam pārthaḥ daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ pratyavidhyat raṇa ajire sūtaputram mahā bāhuḥ sarva sainyasya paśyataḥ sātvataḥ ca tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ karṇam vivyādha māriṣa tān karṇaḥ prativivyādha ṣaṣṭyā ṣaṣṭyā mahā rathaḥ tatra adbhutam apaśyāma sūtaputrasya māriṣa phalgunaḥ tu mahā bāhuḥ karṇam vaikartanam raṇe sāyakānām śatena eva sarva marmasu atāḍayat rudhira ukṣ sarva aṅgaḥ sūtaputraḥ pratāpavān śaraiḥ pañcāśatā vīraḥ phalgunam pratyavidhyata tasya tat lāghavam dṛṣṭvā na amṛṣyata raṇe arjunaḥ atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya sūtaputraḥ pratāpavān sāyakaiḥ bahu sāhasraiḥ chādayām āsa pāṇḍavam tām śastra vṛṣṭim atulām karṇa cāpa samutthitām vyadhamat sāyakaiḥ pārthaḥ śalabhān iva mārutaḥ chādayām āsa ca tadā sāyakaiḥ arjunaḥ raṇe paśyatām sarva yodhānām darśayan pāṇi lāghavam nara siṃhaḥ mahā rathaḥ vavarṣa sāyakaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ karṇaḥ api dviṣatām hantā chādayām āsa phalgunam sāyakaiḥ bahu sāhasraiḥ kṛta pratikṛta īpsayā pārthaḥ aham asmi tiṣṭha tvam karṇaḥ aham tiṣṭha phalguna prekṣaṇīyau ca abhavatām sarva yodha samāgame praśasyamānau samare siddha cāraṇa vātikaiḥ ayudhyetām mahā rāja paraspara vadha eṣiṇaḥ tatas duryodhanaḥ rājan tāvakān abhyabhāṣata yattāḥ rakṣata rādheyam na a hatvā samare arjunam nivartiṣyati rādheyaḥ iti mām uktavan vṛṣaḥ ākarṇa muktaiḥ iṣubhiḥ karṇasya caturaḥ hayān sārathim ca asya bhallena rathanīḍāt apāharat chādayām āsa ca śaraiḥ te putrasya paśyataḥ sa chādyamānaḥ samare hata aśvaḥ hata sārathiḥ tam tathā viratham dṛṣṭvā ratham āropya svam tadā aśvatthāmā mahā rāja bhūyas arjunam ayodhayat āvavre arjuna mārgam ca śara jālena bhārata śāradvataḥ tu viṃśatyā vāsudevam samārpayat dhanaṃjayam dvādaśabhiḥ ājaghāna śilīmukhaiḥ caturbhiḥ sindhurājaḥ ca vṛṣasenaḥ ca saptabhiḥ pṛthak pṛthak mahā rāja kṛṣṇa pārthau avidhyatām droṇaputram catuḥṣaṣṭyā madra rājam śatena ca saindhavam daśabhiḥ bhallaiḥ vṛṣasenam tribhiḥ śaraiḥ śāradvatam ca viṃśatyā viddhvā pārthaḥ samunnadat te pratijñā apratīghātam icchantaḥ savyasācinaḥ atha arjunaḥ sarvatodhāram astram prāduścakre trāsayan dhārtarāṣṭrān tam pratyudīyuḥ kuravaḥ pāṇḍu sūnum rathaiḥ mahārhaiḥ śara varṣāṇi avarṣan na amuhyata prāpya sa rāja putraḥ kirīṭamālī visṛjan pṛṣatkān rājya prepsuḥ savyasācī kurūṇām smaran kleśān dvādaśa varṣa vṛttān gāṇḍīva muktaiḥ iṣubhiḥ mahātmā sarvāḥ diśaḥ vyāvṛṇot aprameyaiḥ pradīpta ulkam abhavat ca antarikṣam deheṣu bhūrīṇi apatan vayāṃsi kirīṭamālī mahatā mahā yaśāḥ śarāsanena asya śarān anīka jit gadāḥ ca gurūḥ parighān ayasmayān asīn ca śaktīḥ ca raṇe narādhipāḥ mahanti śastrāṇi ca bhīma darśanāḥ pragṛhya pārtham sahasā abhidudruvuḥ mahā indra cāpa pratimam sa gāṇḍivam cakarṣa dorbhyām vihasan bhṛśam yayau dahan tvadīyān yama rāṣṭra vardhanaḥ sa tān udīrṇān sa ratha aśva vāraṇān padāti saṃghān ca mahā dhanuḥ dharaḥ vipanna sarva āyudha jīvitān raṇe cakāra vīraḥ yama rāṣṭra vardhanān uvāca śrutvā ninādam dhanuṣaḥ ca tasya vispaṣṭam utkṛṣṭam iva antakasya śakra aśani sphoṭa samam su ghoram dhanaṃjayena trāsa udvignam bhaya udbhrāntam tvadīyam tat balam nṛpa yugānta vāta saṃkṣubdham calat vīci taraṃgitam pralīna mīna makaram sāgara ambhaḥ iva abhavat sa raṇe vyacarat pārthaḥ prekṣaṇīyaḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ yugapad dikṣu sarvāsu citrāṇi astrāṇi darśayan ādadānam mahā rāja saṃdadhānam ca pāṇḍavam utkarṣantam vikarṣantam na abhyapaśyāma lāghavāt prāduś cakre mahā rāja trāsayan sarva bhāratān tatas śarāḥ prādur āsan divya astra pratimantritāḥ pradīptāḥ ca śikhi mukhāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas ākarṇapūrṇa nirmuktaiḥ agni arka aṃśu nibhaiḥ śaraiḥ tatas śastra andhakāram tat kauravaiḥ samudīritam aśakyam manasā api anyaiḥ pāṇḍavaḥ saṃbhraman iva nāśayām āsa vikramya śaraiḥ divya astra mantritaiḥ naiśam tamaḥ aṃśubhiḥ kṣipram dina ādau iva bhāskaraḥ tatas tu tāvakam sainyam dīptaiḥ śara gabhastibhiḥ ākṣipat palvala ambūni nidāgha arkaḥ iva prabhuḥ tatas divya astra vidvasā prahitāḥ sāyaka aṃśavaḥ samāplavan dviṣat sainyam lokam bhānoḥ iva aṃśavaḥ tathā apare samutsṛṣṭāḥ viśikhāḥ tigma tejasaḥ hṛdayāni āśu vīrāṇām viviśuḥ priya bandhu vat ye enam īyuḥ samare tvad yodhāḥ śūra māninaḥ śalabhāḥ iva te dīptāḥ agnim prāpya yayuḥ kṣayam evam sa mṛdnan śatrūṇām jīvitāni yaśāṃsi ca pārthaḥ cacāra saṃgrāme mṛtyuḥ vigrahavān iva sa kirīṭāni vastrāṇi sa aṅgadān vipulān bhujān sa kuṇḍala yugān karṇān keṣām cit aharat śaraiḥ sa tomarān gaja sthānām sa prāsān haya sādinām sa carmaṇaḥ padātīnām rathinām ca sa dhanvanaḥ sa pratodān niyantṝṇām bāhūn ciccheda pāṇḍavaḥ pradīpta ugra śara arciṣmān babhau tatra dhanaṃjayaḥ tam devarāja pratimam sarva śastrabhṛtām varam darśayantam mahā astrāṇi prekṣaṇīyam dhanaṃjayam nirīkṣitum na śekuḥ te yatnavantaḥ api pārthivāḥ dīpta ugra saṃbhṛta śaraḥ kirīṭī virarāja ha varṣāsu iva udīrṇa jalaḥ sa indradhanva ambudaḥ mahān mahā astra saṃplave tasmin jiṣṇunā saṃpravartite utkṛtta vadanaiḥ dehaiḥ śarīraiḥ kṛtta bāhubhiḥ bhujaiḥ ca pāṇi nirmuktaiḥ pāṇibhiḥ vyaṅgulīkṛtaiḥ hayaiḥ chinna khura grīvaiḥ rathaiḥ ca śakalīkṛtaiḥ nikṛtta antraiḥ kṛtta pādaiḥ tathā anyaiḥ kṛtta saṃdhibhiḥ niśceṣṭaiḥ visphuradbhiḥ ca kūjadbhiḥ ca sahasraśas mṛtyoḥ āghāta lalitam tat pārtha āyodhanam mahat apaśyāma mahīpāla bhīrūṇām bhaya vardhanam ākrīḍam iva rudrasya purā abhyardayataḥ paśūn gajānām kṣura nirmuktaiḥ karaiḥ sa bhujagā iva bhūḥ vicitra uṣṇīṣa mukuṭaiḥ keyūra aṅgada kuṇḍalaiḥ svarṇa citra tanutraiḥ ca bhāṇḍaiḥ ca gaja vājinām kirīṭa śata saṃkīrṇā tatra tatra samācitā virarāja bhṛśam citrā mahī nava vadhūḥ iva majjā medaḥ kardaminīm śoṇita ogha taraṃgiṇīm marma asthibhiḥ agādhām ca keśa śaivala śādvalām śiraḥ bāhu upala taṭām rugṇa kroḍa asthi saṃkaṭām citra dhvaja patākā āḍhyām chattra cāpa ūrmi mālinīm vigata asu mahā kāyām gaja deha abhisaṃkulām ratha uḍupa śata ākīrṇām haya saṃghāta rodhasam prāsa asi śakti paraśu viśikha ahi durāsadām bala kaṅka mahā nakrām gomāyu makara utkaṭām gṛdhra udagra mahā grāhām śivā viruta bhairavām nṛtyat preta piśāca ādyaiḥ bhūtaiḥ kīrṇām sahasraśas gatāsu yodha niśceṣṭa śarīra śata vāhinīm mahā pratibhayām raudrām ghorām vaitaraṇīm iva nadīm pravartayām āsa bhīrūṇām bhaya vardhinīm tam dṛṣṭvā tasya vikrāntam antakasya iva rūpiṇaḥ abhūta pūrvam kuruṣu bhayam āgāt raṇa ajire tatas ādāya vīrāṇām astraiḥ astrāṇi pāṇḍavaḥ ātmānam raudram ācaṣṭa raudra karmaṇi niṣṭhitaḥ na śekuḥ sarva bhūtāni pāṇḍavam prativīkṣitum prasṛtān tasya gāṇḍīvāt śara vrātān mahātmanaḥ saṃgrāme samapaśyāma haṃsa paṅktīḥ iva ambare ākāśe samadṛśyanta haṃsānām iva paṅktayaḥ vinivārya sa vīrāṇām astraiḥ astrāṇi sarvaśas darśayan raudram ātmānam ugre karmaṇi dhiṣṭhitaḥ visṛjan dikṣu sarvāsu śarān asita sārathiḥ sa raṇe vyacarat tūrṇam prekṣaṇīyaḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ bhramantaḥ iva śūrasya śara vrātāḥ mahātmanaḥ adṛśyanta antarikṣa sthāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas ādadānam mahā iṣvāsam saṃdadhānam ca pāṇḍavam visṛjantam ca kaunteyam na anupaśyāmahe tadā tathā sarvāḥ diśaḥ rājan sarvān ca rathinaḥ raṇe vivyādha ca catuḥṣaṣṭyā śarāṇām nata parvaṇām saindhava abhimukham yāntam yodhāḥ saṃprekṣya pāṇḍavam nyavartanta raṇāt vīrāḥ nirāśāḥ tasya jīvite yaḥ yaḥ abhyadhāvat ākrande tāvakaḥ pāṇḍavam raṇe tasya tasya anta gāḥ bāṇāḥ śarīre nyapatan prabho arjunaḥ jayatām śreṣṭhaḥ śaraiḥ arka aṃśu saṃnibhaiḥ drauṇim pañcāśatā avidhyat vṛṣasenam tribhiḥ śaraiḥ kṛpāyamāṇaḥ kaunteyaḥ kṛpam navabhiḥ ārdayat śalyam ṣoḍaśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ karṇam dvātriṃśatā śaraiḥ saindhavam tu catuḥṣaṣṭyā viddhvā siṃhaḥ iva anadat saindhavaḥ tu tathā viddhaḥ śaraiḥ gāṇḍīvadhanvanā sa varāha dhvajaḥ tūrṇam gārdhra patrān a jihma gān āśīviṣa sama prakhyān karmāra parimārjitān mumoca niśitān saṃkhye sāyakān savyasācini tribhiḥ tu viddhvā gāṇḍīvam nārācaiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ arjunam aṣṭau vājinaḥ avidhyat dhvajam ca ekena pattriṇā punar pārtham dhvajam pārtham kirīṭam vājinaḥ dhanuḥ bhūyas ca eva arjunam saṃkhye śara varṣaiḥ avākirat sa vikṣipya arjunaḥ tīkṣṇān saindhava preṣitān śarān sāratheḥ ca śiraḥ kāyāt dhvajam ca samalaṃkṛtam sa chid yaṣṭiḥ su mahat śīryamāṇaḥ śara āhataḥ varāhaḥ sindhurājasya papāta agni śikhā upamaḥ ādityam prekṣamāṇaḥ tu bībhatsuḥ lihan apaśyat na antaram tasya rakṣibhiḥ saṃvṛtasya vai atha abravīt vāsudevaḥ kuntī putram dhanaṃjayam śrī bhagavant uvāca srakṣyāmi aham upāyam tam ādityasya apavāraṇe ātma jīvita lābhāt ca pratijñāyāḥ ca nāśanāt iva ādityam dṛṣṭvā mohena bāliśaḥ na hi śakṣyati atha ātmānam rakṣitum harṣa saṃbhavāt vac iti vaktvā tu tatas pārtham kṣipram eva aharat prabhām pārthaḥ tu balavān jñātvā tamaḥ dṛṣṭvā ati duḥkhitaḥ janārdanena sṛṣṭam vai tamaḥ āditya nāśanam abhavan tāvakāḥ dṛṣṭvā harṣa saṃkula cetasaḥ atha arjunam hṛṣīkeśaḥ śoka pūrṇam atha abravīt paśya kaunteya sindhūnām pārthivam pāpa kāriṇam unnamayya śiraḥ grīvam vīkṣate sūrya maṇḍalam vac tasya śīghram pṛṣatkena kāyāt śīrṣam apāhara śaram tīkṣṇam amaraiḥ api duḥsaham tat tathā uktam bhagavatā tamaḥ bhūtvā viśām pate andham tamaḥ iva ajñānam ādityasya aharat prabhām abravīt pāṇḍavam tatra tvaramāṇaḥ janārdanaḥ eṣa madhye kṛtaḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ pārtha vīraiḥ mahā rathaiḥ jīvita īpsuḥ mahā bāho bhītaḥ tiṣṭhati saindhavaḥ etān a nirjitya raṇe ṣaṭ rathān puruṣa ṛṣabha yogam atra vidhāsyāmi sūryasya āvaraṇam prati harṣeṇa jīvita ākāṅkṣī vināśa artham te prabho na gopsyati durācāraḥ saḥ ātmānam katham cana tatas asṛjat tamaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ sūryasya āvaraṇam prati yogī yogena saṃyuktaḥ yoginām īśvaraḥ hariḥ sṛṣṭe tamasi kṛṣṇena gataḥ astam iti bhāskaraḥ tvadīyāḥ jahṛṣuḥ yodhāḥ pārtha nāśāt narādhipa te prahṛṣṭāḥ raṇe rājan na apaśyan sainikāḥ ravim unnāmya vaktrāṇi tadā sa ca rājā jayadrathaḥ vīkṣamāṇe tatas tasmin sindhurāje divākaram punar eva abravīt kṛṣṇaḥ dhanaṃjayam idam vacaḥ paśya sindhupatim vīram prekṣamāṇam divākaram ayam kālaḥ mahā bāho vadhāya asya durātmanaḥ chinddhi mūrdhānam asya āśu kuru sāphalyam ātmanaḥ iti evam keśavena uktaḥ pāṇḍu putraḥ pratāpavān nyavadhīt tāvakam sainyam śaraiḥ arka agni saṃnibhaiḥ kṛpam vivyādha viṃśatyā karṇam pañcāśatā śaraiḥ śalyam duryodhanam ca eva ṣaḍbhiḥ ṣaḍbhiḥ atāḍayat vṛṣasenam tathā aṣṭābhiḥ ṣaṣṭyā saindhavam eva ca tathā eva anyān mahā bāhuḥ tvadīyān pāṇḍu nandanaḥ gāḍham viddhvā śaraiḥ rājan jayadratham upādravat tam samīpa sthitam dṛṣṭvā lelihānam iva analam jayadrathasya goptāraḥ saṃśayam paramam gatāḥ tatas sarve mahā rāja tava yodhāḥ jaya eṣiṇaḥ siṣicuḥ śara dhārābhiḥ pākaśāsanim āhave saṃchādyamānaḥ kaunteyaḥ śara jālaiḥ anekaśas tatas śara mayam jālam tumulam pākaśāsanaḥ te hanyamānāḥ vīreṇa yodhāḥ rājan raṇe tava prajahuḥ saindhavam bhītāḥ dvau samam na api adhāvatām tādṛś na bhāvī bhūtaḥ vā yat cakāra mahā yaśāḥ dvipān dvipa gatān ca eva hayān haya gatān api na tatra samare kaḥ cit mayā dṛṣṭaḥ narādhipa gajaḥ vājī naraḥ vā api yaḥ na pārtha śara āhataḥ rajasā tamasā ca eva yodhāḥ saṃchanna cakṣuṣaḥ kaśmalam prāviśan ghoram na anvajānan parasparam te śaraiḥ bhinna marmāṇaḥ sainikāḥ pārtha coditaiḥ tasmin mahā bhīṣaṇake prajānām iva saṃkṣaye raṇe mahati duṣpāre vartamāne su dāruṇe ānābhi niramajjan ca ratha cakrāṇi śoṇite mattāḥ vegavataḥ rājan tāvakānām raṇa aṅgaṇe hastinaḥ ca hata ārohāḥ dārita aṅgāḥ sahasraśas svāni anīkāni mṛdnantaḥ ārta nādāḥ pradudruvuḥ hayāḥ ca patita ārohāḥ pattayaḥ ca narādhipa pradudruvuḥ bhayāt rājan dhanaṃjaya śara āhatāḥ muktakeśāḥ vikavacāḥ kṣarantaḥ kṣatajam kṣitau prapalāyanta saṃtrastāḥ tyaktvā raṇa śiraḥ janāḥ ūru grāha gṛhītāḥ ca ke cid tatra abhavan bhuvi hatānām ca apare madhye dviradānām nililyire evam tava balam rājan drāvayitvā dhanaṃjayaḥ nyavadhīt sāyakaiḥ ghoraiḥ sindhurājasya rakṣiṇaḥ karṇam drauṇim kṛpam śalyam vṛṣasenam suyodhanam chādayām āsa tīvreṇa śara jālena pāṇḍavaḥ na gṛhṇan akṣipan rājan amuñcan na api saṃdadhan adṛśyata arjunaḥ saṃkhye śīghra astra tvāt katham cana dhanuḥ maṇḍalam eva asya dṛśyate sma āsyataḥ sadā sāyakāḥ ca vyadṛśyanta niścarantaḥ samantataḥ śalyasya sūtam bhallena rathanīḍāt apātayat gāḍha viddhau ubhau kṛtvā śaraiḥ svasrīya mātulau arjunaḥ jayatām śreṣṭhaḥ drauṇi śāradvatau raṇe evam tān vyākulīkṛtya tvadīyānām mahā rathān ujjahāra śaram ghoram pāṇḍavaḥ anala saṃnibham sarva bhāra saham śaśvat gandha mālya arcitam mahat samādadhan mahā bāhuḥ gāṇḍive kṣipram arjunaḥ antarikṣe mahā nādaḥ bhūtānām abhavat nṛpa astam mahīdhara śreṣṭham yiyāsati divākaraḥ śṛṇuṣva eva ca mama vākyam jayadratha vadham prati śrūyatām tat yathāvṛttam karaṇam saindhavam prati antarhitā tadā vāṇī megha dundubhi nisvanā tava ātmajaḥ ayam martyeṣu kula śīla dama ādibhiḥ guṇaiḥ bhaviṣyati vibho sadṛśaḥ vaṃśayoḥ dvayoḥ kṣatriya pravaraḥ loke nityam śūra abhisatkṛtaḥ śiraḥ chetsyati saṃkruddhaḥ śatruḥ na ālakṣitaḥ bhuvi jñātīn sarvān uvāca idam putra sneha abhipīḍitaḥ dharaṇyām mama putrasya pātayiṣyati yaḥ śiraḥ tasya api śatadhā mūrdhā phaliṣyati na saṃśayaḥ vṛddhakṣatraḥ vanam yātaḥ tapaḥ ca iṣṭam samāsthitaḥ tasmāt jayadrathasya tvam śiraḥ chittvā mahā mṛdhe utsaṅge pātayasva āśu vṛddhakṣatrasya bhārata atha tvam asya mūrdhānam pātayiṣyasi bhū tale tava api śatadhā mūrdhā phaliṣyati na saṃśayaḥ yathā ca etat na jānīyāt sa rājā pṛthivīpatiḥ tathā kuru kuru śreṣṭha divyam astram upāśritaḥ etat śrutvā tu vacanam parisaṃlihan vṛddhakṣatra āśrama dvāram aharat tat areḥ śiraḥ sarva bhāra saham śaśvat gandha mālya arcitam śaram ekam tūṇī śayam ghoram indra aśani sama prabham samādhatta mahā bāhuḥ gāṇḍīve kṣipram arjunaḥ tatas dhanaṃjayaḥ śīghram śaram tam bhāskara tviṣam ujjihīrṣuḥ śiraḥ kāyāt saindhavasya mahātmanaḥ sa tu gāṇḍīva nirmuktaḥ śaraḥ śyenaḥ iva āśu gaḥ prapatiṣyati śīrṣe tu kṛṣṇaḥ arjunam atha abravīt uvāca tathā kuru kuru śreṣṭha vakṣye tasya api kāraṇam śrutvā tu vacanam tasya tvaramāṇaḥ astra māyayā durhṛdām a praharṣāya suhṛdām harṣaṇāya ca dīrgha kālam avāk ca eva saṃprakrīḍan iva arjunaḥ śaraiḥ kadambakīkṛtya kāle tasmin ca pāṇḍavaḥ yodhayām āsa tān ca eva pāṇḍavaḥ ṣaṭ mahā rathān tatas su mahat āścaryam tatra apaśyāma bhārata jayadrathasya arjuna bāṇa nālam dṛṣṭam naraiḥ ca upari vartamānam sa deva śatrūn iva devarājaḥ kirīṭamālī vyadhamat sapatnān pūrṇām pratijñām samavāpya dhīraḥ atha abravīt keśavam pāṇḍaveyaḥ tam bhūmi deśam ca śiraḥ vinetum saṃdhyām upāste tejasvī saṃbandhī te māriṣa upāsīnasya tasya atha kṛṣṇa keśam sa kuṇḍalam gate tasya api śatadhā mūrdhā agacchat ariṃdama tat śiraḥ śatadhā rājan papāta pṛthivī tale vāsudevaḥ ca bībhatsum praśaśaṃsa mahā ratham tatas dṛṣṭvā vinihatam sindhurājam jayadratham paścāt jñātam mahīpāla te putraiḥ saha anugaiḥ akṣauhiṇīḥ aṣṭa hatvā jāmātā tava saindhavaḥ hatam jayadratham dṛṣṭvā te putrāḥ narādhipa karmaṇā tena pārthasya vismitāḥ sarva devatāḥ etad artham śiraḥ tasya cyāvayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ astram pāśupatam pārthaḥ saṃhartum upacakrame saṃhāram ca pramokṣam ca dṛṣṭvā tatra divaukasaḥ vismayam paramam jagmuḥ praśaśaṃsuḥ ca pāṇḍavam evam astreṇa tān vīraḥ yodhayitvā dhanaṃjayaḥ jayadratha śiraḥ paścāt cyāvayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ tat śiraḥ cyāvamānam tu dadṛśuḥ tāvakāḥ yudhi śalya karṇa kṛpāḥ rājan mohitāḥ savyasācinā śirasi cyāvite tasya śaraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ paścāt kāyaḥ apatat bhūmim śocayan sarva pārthivān dṛṣṭvā tu nihatam saṃkhe sindhurājam mahā ratham duḥkhāt aśrūṇi mumucuḥ nirāśāḥ ca abhavan jaye dadhmau śaṅkham mahā bāhuḥ arjunaḥ ca paraṃtapaḥ praharṣam atulam lebhe kṛṣṇaḥ pārthaḥ ca bhārata bhīmasenaḥ api saṃgrāme bodhayan iva pāṇḍavam siṃhanādena mahatā pūrayām āsa rodasī bhīmaḥ ca vṛṣṇi siṃhaḥ ca yudhāmanyuḥ ca bhārata uttamaujāḥ ca vikrāntaḥ śaṅkhān dadhmuḥ pṛthak pṛthak tam śrutvā tu mahā nādam dharmaputraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ udapadyata sainyasya pāṇḍūnām hṛṣṭa cetasām droṇasya somakaiḥ sārdham saṃgrāmaḥ loma harṣaṇaḥ pāṇḍavāḥ tu jayam labdhvā saindhavam vinihatya ca arjunaḥ api raṇe yodhān tāvakān ratha sattamān sa deva śatrūn iva devarājaḥ kirīṭamālī vyadhamat samantāt yathā tamāṃsi abhyuditaḥ tamoghnaḥ pūrvām pratijñām samavāpya vīraḥ uvāca etat su caritam rājan yaḥ śṛṇoti iha bhakti apamṛtyum jayati āśu labhate sarva saṃpadaḥ uvāca paśyatām sarva yodhānām māmakānām mahā raṇe katham drauṇi kṛpaiḥ guptaḥ karṇena ca mahā raṇe phalguna agni mukham ghoram praviṣṭaḥ sādhu saindhavaḥ bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitaḥ sūta kim akārṣīt anantaram uvāca saindhavam nihatam dṛṣṭvā raṇe pārthena māriṣa amarṣa vaśam āpannaḥ kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ tadā mahatā śara varṣeṇa pāṇḍavam samavākirat tau enam rathinām śreṣṭhau rathābhyām ratha sattamam ubhau ubhayatas tīkṣṇaiḥ viśikhaiḥ abhyavarṣatām sa tathā śara varṣābhyām su mahadbhyām mahā bhujaḥ pīḍyamānaḥ parām ārtim agamat rathinām varaḥ cakāra ācāryakam tatra kuntī putraḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ astraiḥ astrāṇi saṃvārya drauṇeḥ śāradvatasya ca manda vegān iṣūn tābhyām ajighāṃsuḥ avāsṛjat te na ati bhṛśam abhyaghnan viśikhāḥ jaya coditāḥ bahu tvāt tu parām ārtim śarāṇām tau agacchatām atha śāradvataḥ rājan kaunteya śara pīḍitaḥ vihvalam tam abhijñāya bhartāram śara pīḍitam aśvatthāmā api apāyāsīt pāṇḍaveyāt ratha antaram dṛṣṭvā śāradvatam pārthaḥ mūrchitam śara pīḍitam rathaḥ eva mahā iṣvāsaḥ kṛpaṇam paryadevayat aśru pūrṇa mukhaḥ dīnaḥ vacanam ca idam abravīt paśyan idam mahā prājñaḥ kṣattā rājānam uktavān nīyatām para lokāya sādhu ayam kula pāṃsana tat idam samanuprāptam vacanam satya vādinaḥ tad kṛte hi adya paśyāmi śara talpa gatam kṛpam kaḥ hi brāhmaṇam ācāryam abhidruhyeta mādṛśaḥ ṛṣi putraḥ mama ācāryaḥ droṇasya dayitaḥ sakhā eṣa śete rathopasthe mad bāṇaiḥ abhipīḍitaḥ akāmayānena mayā viśikhaiḥ arditaḥ bhṛśam avāsīdat rathopasthe prāṇān pīḍayati iva me śara arditena hi mayā prekṣaṇīyaḥ mahā dyutiḥ kṛpaṇam sva rathe sannam paśya kṛṣṇa yathā
