gatam upākṛtya tu vai vidyām ācāryebhyaḥ nara ṛṣabhāḥ ye tu vidyām upādāya gurubhyaḥ puruṣa adhamāḥ tat idam narakāya adya kṛtam karma mayā dhruvam ācāryam śara varṣeṇa rathe sādayatā kṛpam yat tat pūrvam upākurvan astram mām abravīt kṛpaḥ tat idam vacanam sādhoḥ ācāryasya mahātmanaḥ na anuṣṭhitam tam eva ājau viśikhaiḥ abhivarṣatā tatas kirīṭinā rājan vihvale gautame kṛte saindhavam nihatam dṛṣṭvā rādheyaḥ samupādravat pāñcālyau sātyakiḥ ca eva sahasā samupādravan upāyāntam tu rādheyam dṛṣṭvā pārthaḥ mahā rathaḥ eṣa prayāti ādhirathiḥ sātyakeḥ syandanam prati na mṛṣyati hatam nūnam bhūriśravasam āhave yatra yāti eṣa tatra tvam codaya aśvān janārdana mā somadatteḥ padavīm gamayet sātyakim vṛṣaḥ evam uktaḥ mahā bāhuḥ keśavaḥ savyasācinā pratyuvāca mahā tejāḥ kāla yuktam idam vacaḥ alam eṣa mahā bāhuḥ karṇāya ekaḥ hi pāṇḍava kim punar draupadeyābhyām sahitaḥ sātvata ṛṣabhaḥ na ca tāvat kṣamaḥ pārtha karṇena tava saṃgaraḥ tvad artham pūjyamānā eṣā rakṣyate para vīra han karṇaḥ hi balavān ekaḥ śaktaḥ asmān jetum ojasā na karṇam hi vayam śaktāḥ jetum sa bala vāhanāḥ pramādāt ca ghṛṇi tvāt ca tena śakyatamaḥ mataḥ atas karṇaḥ prayātu atra sātvatasya yathā tathā aham jñāsyāmi kauravya kālam asya durātmanaḥ yatra enam viśikhaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ pātayiṣyati bhū tale tadā gantāsi pārtha tvam tena yoddhum durātmanā uvāca yaḥ asau karṇena vīreṇa vārṣṇeyasya samāgamaḥ akāṅkṣitaḥ ca karṇena sa bhavatu ati tejasaḥ sātyakiḥ ca api virathaḥ kam samārūḍhavān ratham cakrarakṣau ca pāñcālyau tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya uvāca hanta te varṇayiṣyāmi yathāvṛttam mahā raṇe śuśrūṣasva sthiraḥ bhūtvā durācaritam ātmanaḥ paśyatām sarva sainyānām keśava arjunayoḥ api vijetavyaḥ yathā vīraḥ sātyakiḥ yūpaketunā atīta anāgatam rājan sa hi vetti janārdanaḥ atas sūtam samāhūya dārukam saṃdideśa ha rathaḥ me yujyatām kālyam iti rājan mahā balaḥ dārukaḥ kṛṣṇa saṃdiṣṭam rātrau uktam hṛdā vahan na hi devāḥ na gandharvāḥ na yakṣa uraga rākṣasāḥ mānavāḥ vā vijetāraḥ kṛṣṇayoḥ santi ke cana pitāmaha purogāḥ ca devāḥ siddhāḥ ca tam viduḥ tayoḥ prabhāvam atulam śṛṇu yuddham ca tat yathā sātyakim viratham dṛṣṭvā karṇam ca abhyudyata āyudham dadhmau śaṅkham mahā vegam ārṣabheṇa atha mādhavaḥ dārukaḥ avetya saṃdeśam śrutvā śaṅkhasya ca svanam haya udagraiḥ mahā vegaiḥ hema bhāṇḍa vibhūṣitaiḥ dhanaṃjaya ratham hitvā rādheyam pratyudīyayuḥ rādheyaḥ api mahā rāja śara varṣam samutsṛjan tādṛśam bhuvi vā yuddham divi vā śrutam iti uta tayoḥ dṛṣṭvā mahā rāja karma saṃmūḍha cetanam gata pratyāgata āvṛttaiḥ maṇḍalaiḥ saṃnivartanaiḥ atīva avahitāḥ draṣṭum karṇa śaineyayoḥ raṇam mitra arthe tau parākrāntau spardhinau śuṣmiṇau raṇe karṇaḥ ca amara saṃkāśaḥ yuyudhānaḥ ca sātyakiḥ anyonyam tau mahā rāja śara varṣaiḥ avarṣatām pramamātha śineḥ pautram karṇaḥ sāyaka vṛṣṭibhiḥ amṛṣyamāṇaḥ nidhanam kauravya jalasaṃdhayoḥ jalasaṃdham hatam dṛṣṭvā bhūriśravasam eva ca karṇaḥ śoka samāviṣṭaḥ mahā uragaḥ iva śvasan sa śaineyam raṇe kruddhaḥ pradahan iva cakṣuṣā śaraiḥ eva prajagrāha satyakaḥ vṛṣṇi puṃgavaḥ karṇam ca prativivyādha śarān tad prahitān śitān atakṣatām atha anyonyam ubhau vijaya kāṅkṣiṇaḥ mahatā śara varṣeṇa gajaḥ pratigajam yathā tatas karṇam śini pautraḥ sarva pāraśavaiḥ śaraiḥ sārathim ca asya bhallena rathanīḍāt apāharat aśvān ca caturaḥ śvetān nijaghne niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ chittvā dhvajam śatena eva śatadhā puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ tatas vimanasaḥ rājan tāvakāḥ puruṣa ṛṣabhāḥ vṛṣasenaḥ karṇa sutaḥ śalyaḥ madra adhipaḥ tathā kṛpaḥ ca madra rājaḥ ca vṛṣasenaḥ ca saṃyuge tatas paryākulam sarvam na prājñāyata kim cana tathā sātyakinā vīre virathe sūtaje kṛte tadā puruṣa vīreṇa satyakena tathākṛte hāhākāraḥ tatas rājan sarva sainyeṣu ca abhavat karṇaḥ api vihvalaḥ rājan sātvatena arditaḥ śaraiḥ kṛtām rājya pradānena pratijñām paripālayan duḥśāsana mukhān śūrān na avadhīt sātyakiḥ vaśī rakṣan pratijñām ca punar bhīmasena kṛ purā bhīmasenena tu vadhaḥ putrāṇām te pratiśru punar dyūte ca pārthena vadhaḥ karṇasya śaṃśrutaḥ na aśaknuvan ca tam hantum sātyakim pravarāḥ rathāḥ drauṇiḥ ca kṛtavarmā ca tathā eva anye mahā rathāḥ nirjitāḥ dhanuṣā ekena śataśas kṣatriya ṛṣabhāḥ kṛṣṇayoḥ sadṛśaḥ vīrye sātyakiḥ śatru karśanaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ vā api bhavet loke pārthaḥ vā api dhanurdharaḥ uvāca ajayyam ratham āsthāya vāsudevasya sātyakiḥ viratham kṛtavān karṇam vāsudeva samaḥ yuvā sarva kṣatriya vīrāṇām eka vīraḥ tu sūtajam dārukeṇa samāyuktam sva bāhu bala darpitaḥ kaccit anyam samārūḍhaḥ sa ratham sātyakiḥ punar etat icchāmi aham śrotum kuśalaḥ hi asi bhāṣitum uvāca śṛṇu rājan yathā tasya ratham anyam mahāmatiḥ āyasaiḥ kāñcanaiḥ ca api paṭṭaiḥ naddham sa kūbaram aśvaiḥ vāta javaiḥ yuktam hema bhāṇḍa paricchadaiḥ pāṇḍuraiḥ indu saṃkāśaiḥ sarva śabda atigaiḥ dṛḍhaiḥ citra kāñcana saṃnāhaiḥ vāji mukhyaiḥ viśām pate ghaṇṭā jāla ākula ravam śakti tomara vidyutam dārukaḥ api yathākāmam prayayau keśava antikam karṇasya api mahā rāja śaṅkha go kṣīra pāṇḍuraiḥ citra kāñcana saṃnāhaiḥ sat aśvaiḥ vegavattaraiḥ etat te sarvam ākhyātam yat mām tvam paripṛcchasi bhūyas ca api nibodha tvam tava apanaya jam kṣayam ekatriṃśat tava sutāḥ bhīmasenena pātitāḥ śataśas nihatāḥ śūrāḥ sātvatena arjunena ca bhīṣmam pramukhatas kṛtvā bhagadattam ca māriṣa uvāca tathā gateṣu śūreṣu teṣām mama ca saṃjaya kim vai bhīmaḥ tadā akārṣīt tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya kim vai bhīma arjunau tatra sātyakiḥ ca akarot tadā uvāca virathaḥ bhīmasenaḥ vai karṇa vāc śalya pīḍitaḥ amarṣa vaśam āpannaḥ phalgunam vākyam abravīt akṛtāstraka mā yodhīḥ bāla saṃgrāma kātara iti mām abravīt karṇaḥ paśyataḥ te dhanaṃjaya etat vratam mahā bāho tvayā saha kṛtam mayā karṇa karṇa vṛthak dṛṣṭe sūtaputra ātma saṃstuta adharmabuddhe śṛṇu me yat tvā vakṣyāmi sāṃpratam dvividham karma śūrāṇām yuddhe jaya parājayau māhātmyam paśya bhīmasya karṇa janma kule tathā na uktavān paruṣam yat tvā palāyana parāyaṇam viratham hatavan vīram pāṇḍavam sūtadāyada kulasya sadṛśam ca api rādheya kṛtavan asi tvam idānīm nara śreṣṭha prastutam na avabudhyase pitryam karma asya saṃgrāmaḥ tava astu anyaḥ kula ucitaḥ aham tvām api rādheya bravīmi raṇa mūrdhani sarva śastrabhṛtām madhye kuru kāryāṇi sarvaśas yadṛcchayā bhīmasenam viratham kṛtavān asi katham cit viratham kṛtvā yat tvam rūkṣam abhāṣathāḥ na ca kam cana nindanti santaḥ śūrāḥ nara ṛṣabhāḥ tvam tu prākṛta vijñānaḥ tat tat vadasi sūtaja pūrayantam yathāśakti śūra karma āhave tathā yudhyamānam parākrāntam śūram ārya vrate ratam paśyatām sarva sainyānām keśavasya mama eva ca na ca tvām paruṣam kim cit uktavān paṇḍu nandanaḥ yasmāt tu bahu rūkṣam ca śrāvitaḥ te vṛkodaraḥ hantāsmi vṛṣasenam te prekṣamāṇasya saṃyuge ye ca anye api upayāsyanti buddhi mohena mām nṛpāḥ tān ca sarvān haniṣyāmi satyena āyudham ālabhe tvām ca mūḍha a kṛta prajñam atimāninam āhave muṇḍinam tu haniṣyāmi tvām ca karṇa ati māninam dṛṣṭvā duryodhanaḥ mandaḥ bhṛśam tapsyati pātitam mahān su tumulaḥ śabdaḥ babhūva rathinām tadā manda raśmiḥ sahasrāṃśuḥ astam girim upāgamat tatas saṃdhyām upāsīnāḥ sarve eva nṛpa uttamāḥ lohitāyati ca āditye tvaramāṇaḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ sahitaḥ cakrarakṣābhyām śinīnām ṛṣabhena ca tatas rājan hṛṣīkeśaḥ saṃgrāma śirasi sthitam tīrṇa pratijñam bībhatsum pariṣvajya idam abravīt diṣṭyā saṃpāditā jiṣṇo pratijñā mahatī tvayā diṣṭyā ca nihataḥ pāpaḥ vṛddhakṣatraḥ saha ātmajaḥ dhārtarāṣṭra balam prāpya deva senā api bhārata sīdeta samare jiṣṇo na atra kāryā vicāraṇā na tam paśyāmi lokeṣu cintayan puruṣam kva cit mahā prabhāvāḥ bahavaḥ tvayā tulya adhikā api vā sametāḥ pṛthivīpālāḥ dhārtarāṣṭrasya kāraṇāt te tvām prāpya raṇe kruddham na abhyavartanta daṃśitāḥ na īdṛśam śaknuyāt kaḥ cit raṇe kartum parākramam yādṛśam kṛtavan adya tvam ekaḥ śatru tāpanaḥ vardhayiṣyāmi bhūyas tvām vijita arim hata dviṣam anāścaryaḥ jayaḥ teṣām yeṣām nāthaḥ asi mādhava tvad prasādāt mahīm kṛtsnām saṃprāpsyati yudhiṣṭhiraḥ vardhanīyāḥ tava vayam preṣyāḥ ca madhusūdana evam uktaḥ smayan kṛṣṇaḥ śanakais vāhayan hayān darśayām āsa pārthāya krūram āyodhanam mahat śrī kṛṣṇaḥ uvāca pṛthivyām śerate śūrāḥ pārthivāḥ tvad śaraiḥ hatāḥ vikīrṇa śastra ābharaṇāḥ vipanna aśva ratha dvipāḥ saṃchinna bhinna varmāṇaḥ vaiklavyam paramam gatāḥ sa sattvāḥ gatasattvāḥ ca prabhayā parayā yutāḥ sa jīvāḥ iva lakṣyante gatasattvāḥ narādhipāḥ teṣām śaraiḥ svarṇa puṅkhaiḥ śastraiḥ ca vividhaiḥ śitaiḥ vāhanaiḥ āyudhaiḥ ca eva saṃpūrṇām paśya medinīm varmabhiḥ carmabhiḥ hāraiḥ śirobhiḥ ca sa kuṇḍalaiḥ uṣṇīṣaiḥ mukuṭaiḥ sragbhiḥ cūḍāmaṇibhiḥ ambaraiḥ kaṇṭha sūtraiḥ aṅgadaiḥ ca niṣkaiḥ api ca su prabhaiḥ anyaiḥ ca ābharaṇaiḥ citraiḥ bhāti bhārata medinī anukarṣaiḥ upāsaṅgaiḥ patākābhiḥ dhvajaiḥ tathā upaskaraiḥ adhiṣṭhānaiḥ īṣā daṇḍaka bandhuraiḥ śaktibhiḥ bhindipālaiḥ ca tūṇaiḥ śūlaiḥ paraśvadhaiḥ śataghnībhiḥ bhuśuṇḍībhiḥ khaḍgaiḥ paraśubhiḥ tathā suvarṇa vikṛtābhiḥ ca kaśābhiḥ bharata ṛṣabha ghaṇṭābhiḥ ca gaja indrāṇām bhāṇḍaiḥ ca vividhaiḥ api pṛthivyām pṛthivī hetoḥ pṛthivīpatayaḥ hatāḥ pṛthivīm upaguhya aṅgaiḥ suptāḥ kāntām iva priyām imān ca giri kūṭa ābhān nāgān airāvata upamān kṣarataḥ śoṇitam bhūri śastra cheda darīmukhaiḥ tava bāṇa hatān vīra paśya niṣṭanataḥ kṣitau hayān ca patitān paśya svarṇa bhāṇḍa vibhūṣitān gandharvanagara ākārān rathān ca nihata īśvarān chinna dhvaja patākā akṣān vicakrān hata sārathīn paśya pārtha hayān bhūmau vimāna upama darśanān pattīn ca nihatān vīra śataśas atha sahasraśas dhanuḥ bhṛtaḥ carma bhṛtaḥ śayānān rudhira ukṣitān mahīm āliṅgya sarva aṅgaiḥ pāṃsu dhvasta śiroruhān niśācara śva vṛka piśāca modanam mahī talam nara vara paśya durdṛśam janārdanaḥ tām ari bhūmim añjasā ajātaśatrum samupetya pāṇḍavam vividhaiḥ ca paristomaiḥ aśvānām ca prakīrṇakaiḥ kuthābhiḥ ca vicitrābhiḥ varūthaiḥ ca mahādhanaiḥ saṃstīrṇām vasudhām paśya citra paṭṭaiḥ iva āvṛtām saṃsyūtān vājibhiḥ sārdham dharaṇyām paśya ca aparān padāti sādi saṃghān ca kṣataja ogha pariplutān uvāca evam saṃdarśayan kṛṣṇaḥ raṇa bhūmim kirīṭinaḥ svaiḥ sametaḥ sa muditaḥ pāñcajanyam vyanādayat sa darśayan eva kirīṭīne ari hā janārdanaḥ tām ari bhūmim añjasā ajātaśatrum samupetya pāṇḍavam sātyakiḥ pārtham abhyāyāt bhīmasenaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ yudhāmanyu uttamaujau ca pāñcālasya ātmajau ubhau te nivārya śaraiḥ drauṇim karṇam ca saha bhūmipaiḥ uvāca cacakṣe saṃprahṛṣṭa ātmā hatam pārthena saindhavam diṣṭyā nistīrṇavan ca eva pratijñām anujaḥ te sa tu evam uktaḥ kṛṣṇena hṛṣṭaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā rathāt āplutya bhārata paryaṣvajat tadā kṛṣṇau ānanda aśru pariplutaḥ avatīrya rathāt rājā paryaṣvajata keśavam saṃprahṛṣṭa manāḥ rājan dharmarājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ pramṛjya vadanam śubhram puṇḍarīka sama prabham abravīt vāsudevam ca pāṇḍavam ca dhanaṃjayam diṣṭyā paśyāmi saṃgrāme tīrṇa bhārau mahā rathau diṣṭyā ca nihataḥ pāpaḥ saindhavaḥ puruṣa adhamaḥ kṛṣṇa diṣṭyā mama prītiḥ mahatī pratipāditā diṣṭyā śatru gaṇāḥ ca eva nimagnāḥ śoka sāgare na teṣām duṣkaram kim cit triṣu lokeṣu vidyate sarva loka guruḥ yeṣām tvam nāthaḥ madhusūdana tava prasādāt govinda vayam jeṣyāmahe ripūn yathā pūrvam prasādāt te dānavān pākaśāsanaḥ dhruvaḥ hi teṣām vārṣṇeya yeṣām tuṣṭaḥ asi mādhava tvad prasādāt dhṛṣīkeśa rājyam prāpsyāmi ca uttamam na teṣām vidyate pāpam saṃgrāme vā parājayaḥ tridaśa īśvara nāthaḥ tvam yeṣām tuṣṭaḥ asi mādhava tvad prasādāt dhṛṣīkeśa śakraḥ sura gaṇa īśvaraḥ trailokya vijayam śrīmān prāptavān raṇa mūrdhani amara tvam gatāḥ kṛṣṇa lokān ca aśnuvate akṣayān sura īśa tvam gataḥ śakraḥ hatvā daityān sahasraśas tvad prasādāt dhṛṣīkeśa jagat sthāvara jaṅgamam ekārṇavam idam pūrvam sarvam āsīt tamaḥ mayam tvad prasādāt prakāśa tvam jagant prāptam narottama sraṣṭāram sarva lokānām paramātmānam acyutam ye prapannāḥ hṛṣīkeśam na te muhyanti karhi cit purāṇam paramam devam devadevam sanātanam tvām bhaktāḥ ye hṛṣīkeśa durgāṇi atitaranti te param purāṇam puruṣam purāṇānām param ca yat lokādim viśvakarmāṇam akṣaya kṣaram akṣaram manasaḥ paramām yonim kham vāyuḥ jyotiṣām nidhim tam prapadya mahātmānam bhūtim āpnoti anuttamām sraṣṭāram sarva varṇānām bhuvaḥ ca prakṛtim parām yogānām ca param brahma dīptam brahma vidām nidhim carācarasya sraṣṭāram pratihartāram eva ca tvām ajam kāraṇa ātmānam prapadye pāṇḍava priyam parameśa pareśa īśa tiryañcam īśa nareśvara tvam īśa īśa īśvara īśāna prabho vardhasva mādhava saṃhṛṣṭa indriya citta ātmā na aśakat vaktum ojasā muhūrtam iva harṣeṇa tūṣṇīm bhūtvā mahāmatiḥ tatas harṣa anvitaḥ rājā harṣa aśru pluta locanaḥ ati adbhutam idam kṛṣṇa kṛtam pārthena dhīmatā kim tu na ati adbhutam teṣām yeṣām naḥ tvam samāśrayaḥ tvam ca eva asmābhiḥ āśritya kṛtaḥ śastra samudyamaḥ suraiḥ iva asura vadhe śakram śakrānuja āhave bālyāt prabhṛti te kṛṣṇa karmāṇi śrutavān aham amānuṣāṇi divyāni mahānti ca bahūni ca yadā eva anugṛhītāḥ sma tvayā sneha anurāgataḥ śatrūn hatān prāptām ca medinīm mārkaṇḍeyaḥ purāṇa ṛṣiḥ carita jñaḥ tava anagha māhātmyam anubhāvam ca purā kīrtitavān muniḥ asitaḥ devalaḥ ca eva nāradaḥ ca mahā tapāḥ tvam śreyaḥ tvam yaśaḥ ca agryam kāraṇam jagataḥ tathā tvayā sṛṣṭam idam sarvam jagat sthāvara jaṅgamam an ādi nidhanam devam viśvam īśam prajāpatim bhūtātmānam mahātmānam anantam viśvatomukham nārāyaṇam param devam paramātmānam aīśvaram jñāna yonim harim viṣṇum mumukṣūṇām parāyaṇam param purāṇam puruṣam purāṇānām param ca yat evamādi guṇānām te karmaṇām divi ca iha ca atīta bhūta bhavyānām saṃkhyātā atra na vidyate sarvatas rakṣaṇīyāḥ sma sa śakrāṇām divaukasām yaiḥ tvam sarva guṇa upetaḥ suhṛd naḥ upapāditaḥ iti evam dharmarājena hariḥ uktaḥ mahā yaśāḥ anurūpam idam vākyam pratyuvāca janārdanaḥ sādhu tvāt ārjavāt ca eva hataḥ pāpaḥ jayadrathaḥ ayam ca puruṣa vyāghra tvad anudhyāna bṛṃhitaḥ tat ayam bharata śreṣṭha bhrātā te pāṇḍava arjunaḥ sainya kṣayam raṇe kṛtvā sindhurāja śiraḥ aharat tatas dharmasutaḥ jiṣṇum pariṣvajya viśām pate pramṛjya vadanam ca asya paryāśvāsayata prabhuḥ asahyam ca aviṣahyam ca devaiḥ api sa vāsavaiḥ diṣṭyā nistīrṇa bhāraḥ asi hata ariḥ ca asi śatru han diṣṭyā satyā pratijñā iyam kṛtā hatvā jayadratham evam uktvā guḍākeśam dharmarājaḥ mahā yaśāḥ pasparśa puṇya gandhena pṛṣṭhe hastena pārthivaḥ iti uktau tau mahātmanau ubhau keśava pāṇḍavau tau abrūtām tadā hṛṣṭau rājānam pṛthivīpatim tava kopa agninā dagdhaḥ pāpaḥ rājā jayadrathaḥ udīrṇam ca api su mahat dhārtarāṣṭra balam raṇe tvām hi cakṣuḥ haṇam vīram kopayitvā suyodhanaḥ sa mitra bandhuḥ samare prāṇān tyakṣyati durmatiḥ śara talpa gataḥ śete bhīṣmaḥ kuru pitāmahaḥ durlabhaḥ hi jayaḥ teṣām saṃgrāme ripu sūdana yātāḥ mṛtyu vaśam te vai yeṣām kruddhaḥ asi pāṇḍava rājyam prāṇāḥ priyāḥ putrāḥ saukhyāni vividhāni ca acirāt tasya naśyanti yeṣām kruddhaḥ asi mānada vinaṣṭān kauravān manye sa putra paśu bāndhavān śrī bhagavān uvāca evam etat mahā bāho vinaṣṭāḥ kauravāḥ mṛdhe tatas bhīmaḥ mahā bāhuḥ sātyakiḥ ca mahā rathaḥ abhivādya gurum jyeṣṭham mārgaṇaiḥ kṣata vikṣatau sthitau āstām mahā iṣvāsau pāñcālyaiḥ parivāritau tau dṛṣṭvā muditau vīrau prāñjalī ca agratas sthitau diṣṭyā paśyāmi vām vīrau vimuktau sainya sāgarāt droṇa grāhāt durādharṣāt dhārdikya makara ālayāt diṣṭyā ca nirjitāḥ saṃkhye pṛthivyām sarva pārthivāḥ yuvām vijayinau ca api diṣṭyā paśyāmi saṃyuge diṣṭyā droṇaḥ jitaḥ saṃkhye hārdikyaḥ ca mahā balaḥ diṣṭyā vikarṇibhiḥ karṇaḥ raṇe nītaḥ parābhavam vimukhaḥ ca kṛtaḥ śalyaḥ yuvābhyām puruṣa ṛṣabhau diṣṭyā yuvam kuśalinaḥ saṃgrāmāt punar āgatau paśyāmi rathinām śreṣṭhau ubhau yuddha viśāradau sainya arṇavam samuttīrṇau diṣṭyā paśyāmi ca anaghau mama prāṇa samau ca eva diṣṭyā paśyāmi vām aham iti uktvā pāṇḍavaḥ rājā yuyudhāna vṛkodarau sasvaje puruṣa vyāghrau harṣāt bāṣpam mumoca ha tatas pramuditam sarvam balam āsīt viśām pate pāṇḍavānām jayam dṛṣṭvā yuddhāya ca manaḥ dadhe uvāca durmanāḥ niḥśvasan uṣṇaḥ bhagna daṃṣṭraḥ iva uragaḥ dṛṣṭvā tat kadanam ghoram sva balasya kṛtam mahat jiṣṇunā bhīmasenena sātvatena ca saṃyuge sa vivarṇaḥ kṛśaḥ dīnaḥ bāṣpa vipluta locanaḥ na droṇaḥ na ca rādheyaḥ na aśvatthāmā kṛpaḥ na ca na hi asya vidyate trātā sākṣāt api puraṃdaraḥ yam upāśritya saṃgrāme kṛtaḥ śastra samudyamaḥ paruṣāṇi sabhā madhye proktavān yaḥ sma pāṇḍavān vadhaḥ yena pratijñātaḥ saṃyuge savyasācinaḥ yasya vīryam samāśritya śamam yācantam acyutam evam klānta manāḥ rājan upāyāt droṇam īkṣitum tatas tat sarvam ācakhyau kurūṇām vaiśasam mahat parān vijayataḥ ca api dhārtarāṣṭrān nimajjataḥ paśya mūrdhāvasiktānām ācārya kadanam kṛtam kṛtvā pramukhatas śūram bhīṣmam mama pitāmaham tam nihatya pralubdhaḥ ayam śikhaṇḍī pūrṇamānasaḥ pāñcālaiḥ sahitaḥ sarvaiḥ senā agram abhikarṣati aparaḥ ca api durdharṣaḥ śiṣyaḥ te savyasācinā akṣauhiṇīḥ sapta hatvā hataḥ rājā jayadrathaḥ mad vijaya kāmānām suhṛdām upakāriṇām gantāsmi katham ānṛṇyam gatānām yama sādanam ye mad artham parīpsanti vasudhām vasudhādhipāḥ saḥ aham kāpuruṣaḥ kṛtvā mitrāṇām kṣayam īdṛśam na aśvamedha sahasreṇa pātum ātmānam utsahe vyāyacchantaḥ jigīṣantaḥ prāptāḥ vaivasvata kṣayam katham patita vṛttasya pṛthivī suhṛdām druhaḥ vivaram na aśakat dātum mama pārthiva saṃsadi saḥ aham rudhira sikta aṅgam rājñām madhye pitāmaham śayānam na aśakam trātum bhīṣmam āyodhane hatam jalasaṃdham mahā iṣvāsam paśya sātyakinā hatam mad artham udyatam śūram prāṇān tyaktvā mahā ratham kāmbojam nihatam dṛṣṭvā tathā alambuṣam eva ca anyān bahūn ca suhṛdaḥ jīvita arthaḥ adya kaḥ mama vyāyacchantaḥ hatāḥ śūrāḥ mad arthe ye a parāṅmukhāḥ yatamānāḥ param śaktyā vijetum ahitān mama teṣām gatvā aham ānṛṇyam adya śaktyā paraṃtapa satyam te pratijānāmi sarva śastrabhṛtām vara iṣṭāpūrtena ca śape vīryeṇa ca sutaiḥ api nihatya tān raṇe sarvān pāñcālān pāṇḍavaiḥ saha śāntim labdhāsmi teṣām vā raṇe gantā salokatām na hi idānīm sahāyāḥ me parīpsanti anupaskṛtāḥ śreyaḥ hi pāṇḍūn manyante na tathā asmān mahā bhuja bhavān upekṣām kurute su śiṣya tvāt dhanaṃjaye tādṛś rūpam idam kāryam kṛtam mama suhṛd bruvaiḥ abhīṣāhāḥ śūrasenāḥ śibayaḥ atha vasātayaḥ saḥ aham adya gamiṣyāmi yatra te puruṣa ṛṣabhāḥ hatāḥ mad artham saṃgrāme yudhyamānāḥ kirīṭinā na hi me jīvitena arthaḥ tān ṛte puruṣa ṛṣabhān ācāryaḥ pāṇḍu putrāṇām anujānātu naḥ bhavān uvāca uvāca niṣṭānakaḥ mahān āsīt sainyānām te bhārata saindhavam nihatam dṛṣṭvā bhūriśravasam eva ca yena mantreṇa nihatāḥ śataśas kṣatriya ṛṣabhāḥ muhūrtam iva tu dhyātvā bhṛśam ārtaḥ abhyabhāṣata ajayyam samare nityam bruvāṇam savyasācinam etena eva arjunam jñātum alam kaurava saṃyuge yat śikhaṇḍī avadhīt bhīṣmam pālyamānaḥ kirīṭinā avadhyam nihatam dṛṣṭvā saṃyuge deva mānuṣaiḥ aham na iyam asti iti bhāratī yam puṃsām triṣu lokeṣu sarva śūram amaṃsmahi tasmin vinihate śūre kim śeṣam paryupāsmahe yān sma tān glahate tātaḥ śakuniḥ kuru saṃsadi akṣān na te akṣāḥ niśitāḥ bāṇāḥ te śatru tāpanāḥ akṣān tu manyase bāṇān śobhamānān śitān śarān yān tadā khyāpyamānān tvam vidureṇa na budhyase tāḥ tāḥ vilapataḥ ca api vidurasya mahātmanaḥ dhīrasya vācaḥ na aśrauṣīḥ kṣemāya vadataḥ śivāḥ yaḥ avamanya vacaḥ pathyam suhṛdām āpta kāriṇām sva matam kurute mūḍhaḥ sa śocyaḥ nacirāt iva yat ca naḥ prekṣamāṇānām kṛṣṇām ānāyayaḥ sabhām an arhatīm kule jātām sarva dharma anucāriṇīm tasya adharmasya gāndhāre phalam prāptam idam tvayā yat ca tān pāṇḍavān dyūte viṣameṇa vijitya ha prāvrājayaḥ tadā araṇye raurava ajina vāsasaḥ putrāṇām iva ca eteṣām dharmam ācaratām sadā na karma kṛtavan na adhīte sa bhavet brāhmaṇabruvaḥ pāṇḍavānām ayam kopaḥ tvayā śakuninā saha āhṛtaḥ dhṛtarāṣṭrasya saṃmate kuru saṃsadi duḥśāsanena saṃyuktaḥ karṇena parivardhitaḥ kṣattuḥ vākyam an ādṛtya tvayā abhyastaḥ punar punar tat hi naḥ krodha vṛkṣaḥ ca kṛta mūlaḥ mahātmanām āśaṃsata paritrāṇam arjunāt sa mahīpatiḥ na kim cit anupaśyāmi jīvita trāṇam ātmanaḥ majjantam iva ca ātmānam dhṛṣṭadyumnasya kilbiṣe paśyāmi a hatvā pāñcālān saha tena śikhaṇḍinā aśaktaḥ sindhurājasya bhūtvā trāṇāya bhārata sauvarṇam satya saṃdhasya dhvajam akliṣṭa karmaṇaḥ hataḥ bhūriśravāḥ ca eva kim śeṣam tatra manyase yat ca apaśyam hatam bhīṣmam paśyataḥ te anujasya vai duḥśāsanasya kauravya kurvāṇam karma duṣkaram imāni pāṇḍavānām ca sṛñjayānām ca bhārata anīkāni ādravante mām sahitāni adya māriṣa na a hatvā sarva pāñcālān kavacasya vimokṣaṇam rājan brūyāḥ sutam me tvam aśvatthāmānam āhave na somakāḥ pramoktavyāḥ jīvitam parirakṣatā yat ca pitrā anuśiṣṭaḥ asi tat vacaḥ paripālaya dharma artha kāma kuśalaḥ dharma arthau api a pīḍayan dharma pradhānaḥ kāryāṇi kuryāḥ ca iti punar punar cakṣuḥ manobhyām saṃtoṣyāḥ viprāḥ sevyāḥ ca śaktitas na ca eṣām vipriyam kāryam te hi vahni śikhā upamāḥ eṣa tu aham anīkāni praviśāmi ari sūdana raṇāya mahate rājan tvayā vāc śalya pīḍitaḥ rātrau api hi yotsyante saṃrabdhāḥ kuru sṛñjayāḥ evam uktvā tatas prāyāt droṇaḥ pāṇḍava sṛñjayān muṣṇan kṣatriya tejāṃsi nakṣatrāṇām iva aṃśumant dīrgham uṣṇam viniḥśvasya kṣatriya anta karaḥ balī uvāca paśya kṛṣṇa sahāyena pāṇḍavena kirīṭinā ācārya vihitam vyūham bhinnam devaiḥ su durbhidam miṣatām yodha mukhyānām saindhavaḥ vinipātitaḥ paśya rādheya rājānaḥ pṛthivyām pravarāḥ yudhi pārthena ekena nihatāḥ siṃhena iva itare mṛgāḥ alpa avaśeṣam sainyam me kṛtam śakrātmajena ha pratijñāyāḥ gataḥ pāram hṛtvā saindhavam arjunaḥ paśya rādheya pṛthvīśān pṛthivyām pātitān bahūn an icchataḥ katham vīra droṇasya yudhi pāṇḍavaḥ abhayam saindhavasya ājau dattvā droṇaḥ paraṃtapaḥ prādāt kirīṭine dvāram paśya nirguṇa tām mama yadi adāsyam anujñām vai pūrvam eva gṛhān prati mayā anāryeṇa saṃruddhaḥ droṇāt prāpya abhayam raṇe paśya yodha varān karṇa śataśas atha sahasraśas pārtha nāma aṅkitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ sarve nītāḥ yama kṣayam katham eka rathena ājau bahūnām naḥ prapaśyatām vipannaḥ saindhavaḥ rājā yodhāḥ ca eva sahasraśas adya me bhrātaraḥ kṣīṇāḥ citrasena ādayaḥ yudhi bhīmasenam samāsādya paśyatām naḥ durātmanām uvāca ācāryam mā vigarhasva śaktyā yudhyati asau dvijaḥ yathābalam yathotsāham tyaktvā jīvitam ātmanaḥ yadi enam samatikramya praviṣṭaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ na atra sūkṣmaḥ api doṣaḥ syāt ācāryasya katham cana kṛtī dakṣaḥ yuvā śūraḥ kṛtāstraḥ laghu vikramaḥ divya astra yuktam āsthāya ratham vānara lakṣaṇam kṛṣṇena ca gṛhīta aśvam abhedya kavaca āvṛtaḥ gāṇḍīvam ajaram divyam dhanuḥ ādāya vīryavān pravarṣan niśitān bāṇān bāhu draviṇa darpitaḥ ācāryaḥ sthaviraḥ rājan śīghra yāne tathā akṣamaḥ bāhu vyāyāma ceṣṭāyām aśaktaḥ tu narādhipa tena enam abhyatikrāntaḥ śvetāśvaḥ kṛṣṇa sārathiḥ tasmāt doṣam na paśyāmi droṇasya anena hetunā ajayyān pāṇḍavān manye droṇena astra vidā mṛdhe tathā hi enam atikramya praviṣṭaḥ śvetavāhanaḥ tatas naḥ yudhyamānānām param śaktyā suyodhana param yatnam kurvatām ca tvayā sārdham raṇa ajire hatvā mākam pauruṣam hi daivam paścāt karoti naḥ satatam ceṣṭamānānām nikṛtyā vikrameṇa ca nihatya yatnam ca mama daivam yāti sva kārya tām nūnam etena mārgeṇa gantavyaḥ jana saṃkṣayaḥ tatas vyāyacchamānānām daivam paścāt karoti naḥ yat kartavyam manuṣyeṇa vyavasāyavatā satā nikṛtyā nikṛtāḥ pārthāḥ viṣa yogaiḥ ca bhārata dagdhāḥ jatu gṛhe ca api dyūtena ca parājitāḥ rāja nītim vyapāśritya prahitāḥ ca eva kānanam yatataḥ tava teṣām ca daivam mārgeṇa yāsyati na teṣām mati pūrvam hi su kṛtam dṛśyate kva cit duṣkṛtam te vā vīra buddhyā hīnam kuru udvaha tena yuktaḥ hi puruṣaḥ kārya akāryam niyujyate na tathā pāṇḍu putrāṇām evam yuddham avartata taiḥ alpaiḥ bahavaḥ yūyam kṣayam nītāḥ prahāriṇaḥ uvāca evam saṃbhāṣamāṇānām bahu tat tat janādhipa pāṇḍavānām anīkāni samadṛśyanta saṃyuge tāvakānām paraiḥ sārdham rājan durmantrite te uvāca tat udīrṇa gaja aśva ogham balam te janādhipa pāṇḍu senām abhidrutya yodhayām āsa sarvatas pāñcālāḥ kuravaḥ ca eva yodhayantaḥ parasparam yama rāṣṭrāya mahate para lokāya dīkṣitāḥ śūrāḥ śūraiḥ samāgamya śara tomara śaktibhiḥ rathinām rathibhiḥ sārdham rudhira srāvi dāruṇam vāraṇāḥ ca mahā rāja samāsādya parasparam viṣāṇaiḥ dārayām āsuḥ saṃkruddhāḥ ca mada utkaṭāḥ haya ārohān haya ārohāḥ prāsa śakti paraśvadhaiḥ pattayaḥ ca mahā bāho śataśas śastra pāṇayaḥ gotrāṇām nāmadheyānām kulānām ca eva māriṣa śravaṇāt hi vijānīmaḥ pāñcālān kurubhiḥ saha anyonyam samare yodhāḥ śara śakti paraśvadhaiḥ śaraiḥ daśa diśaḥ rājan teṣām muktaiḥ sahasraśas tathā prayudh pāṇḍaveyeṣu nirbhayaḥ abhyavartata putraḥ te pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm sa saṃnipātaḥ tumulaḥ tasya teṣām ca bhārata uvāca kaccit duryodhanaḥ sūta na akārṣīt pṛṣṭhatas raṇam ekasya ca bahūnām ca saṃnipātaḥ mahān abhūt viśeṣataḥ hi nṛpateḥ viṣamam pratibhāti me ekaḥ bahūn samāsādya kaccit na āsīt parāṅmukhaḥ droṇaḥ karṇaḥ kṛpaḥ ca eva kṛtavarmā ca sātvataḥ na avārayan katham yuddhe rājānam rāja kāṅkṣiṇaḥ eṣā nītiḥ parā yuddhe dṛṣṭā tatra mahā ṛṣibhiḥ uvāca māmakāḥ rathinām śreṣṭhāḥ kim akurvata saṃjaya rājan saṃgrāmam āścaryam putrasya te bhārata ekasya ca bahūnām ca śṛṇu me bruvataḥ adbhutam droṇena vāryamāṇaḥ asau karṇena ca kṛpeṇa ca prāviśat pāṇḍavām senām makaraḥ sāgaram yathā pāñcālān pāṇḍavān ca eva vivyādha niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ tathā putraḥ tava balam nāśayat tat mahā balaḥ na śekuḥ bhāratam yuddhe pāṇḍavāḥ samavekṣitum palāyane kṛta utsāhāḥ nirutsāhāḥ dviṣat jaye paryadhāvanta pāñcālāḥ vadhyamānāḥ mahātmanā ardyamānāḥ śaraiḥ tūrṇam nyapatan pāṇḍu sainikāḥ vyadravan ca bhayāt yodhāḥ dṛṣṭvā tam parama āhave vyātta ānanam iva prāptam antakam prāṇa hāriṇam na tādṛśam raṇe karma kṛtavantaḥ tu tāvakāḥ yādṛśam kṛtavān rājā putraḥ te viśām pate putreṇa tava sā senā pāṇḍavī mathitā raṇe kṣīṇa toya anila arkābhyām hata tviṣ iva padminī babhūva pāṇḍavī senā tava putrasya tejasā pāṇḍu senām hata dṛṣṭvā te putreṇa bhārata bhīmasena purogāḥ tu pāñcālāḥ samupādravan virāṭa drupadau ṣaḍbhiḥ śatena ca śikhaṇḍinam kekayān ca eva cedīn ca bahubhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ śataśas ca aparān yodhān sa dvipa aśva rathān raṇe sā tena pāṇḍavā senā vadhyamānā śilīmukhaiḥ tam tapantam iva ādityam kuru rājam mahā āhave na aśakan vīkṣitum rājan pāṇḍu putrasya sainikāḥ abhyadhāvat kuru patim te putram jigīṣayā vivyādha daśabhiḥ tūrṇam dhvajam ciccheda ca iṣuṇā sārathim dayitam rājñaḥ pāṇḍavasya mahātmanaḥ caturbhiḥ caturaḥ ca eva bāṇaiḥ vivyādha vājinaḥ tasya tān nighnataḥ śatrūn rukma pṛṣṭham mahat dhanuḥ bhallābhyām pāṇḍavaḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ tridhā ciccheda māriṣa vivyādha ca enam daśabhiḥ samyak astaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ marmāṇi bhittvā te sarve saṃbhagnāḥ kṣitim āviśan tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā tava putrasya māriṣa śaram parama durvāram preṣayām āsa saṃyuge sa śaram sūrya raśmi ābham ati ugram anivāraṇam hā hataḥ asi iti rājānam uktvā amuñcat yudhiṣṭhiraḥ niṣasāda rathopasthe bhṛśam saṃmūḍha cetanaḥ tatas pāñcāla sainyānām bhṛśam āsīt ravaḥ mahān hataḥ rājā iti rāja indra muditānām samantataḥ bāṇa śabda ravaḥ ca ugraḥ śuśruve tatra māriṣa hṛṣṭaḥ duryodhanaḥ ca api dṛḍham ādāya kārmukam tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti rājānam bruvan pāṇḍavam abhyayāt tam evaṃvādinam vīram dhārtarāṣṭram mahā ratham pratyudyayuḥ tam tvaritāḥ pāñcālāḥ rāja gṛddhinaḥ caṇḍa vāta uddhatān meghān nighnan raśmi mucaḥ yathā tatas rājan mahān āsīt saṃgrāmaḥ bhūri vardhanaḥ tāvakānām pareṣām ca sametānām yuyutsayā uvāca yat tadā prāviśat pāṇḍūn ācāryaḥ kupitaḥ vaśī uktvā duryodhanam samyak mama śāstra atigam sutam katham droṇam mahā iṣvāsam pāṇḍavāḥ paryavārayan ke arakṣan dakṣiṇam cakram ācāryasya mahātmanaḥ ke ca asya pṛṣṭhatas anvāsan vīrāḥ vīrasya yodhinaḥ yat prāviśat mahā iṣvāsaḥ pāñcālān aparājitaḥ nṛtyan sa ratha mārgeṣu sarva śastrabhṛtām varaḥ nirdahan sarva sainyāni pāñcālānām ratha ṛṣabhaḥ uvāca sāyāhne saindhavam hatvā rājñā pārthaḥ sametya ca sātyakiḥ ca mahā iṣvāsaḥ droṇam eva abhyadhāvatām tathā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tūrṇam bhīmasenaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ pṛthak camūbhyām saṃsaktau droṇam eva abhyadhāvatām dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śatānīkaḥ virāṭaḥ ca sa kekayaḥ matsyāḥ śālveya senāḥ ca droṇam eva yayuḥ yudhi drupadaḥ ca tathā rājā pāñcālaiḥ abhirakṣitaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumna pitā rājan droṇam eva abhyavartata draupadeyāḥ mahā iṣvāsāḥ rākṣasaḥ ca ghaṭotkacaḥ prabhadrakāḥ ca pāñcālāḥ ṣaṣ sahasrāḥ prahāriṇaḥ tathā itare nara vyāghrāḥ pāṇḍavānām mahā rathāḥ teṣu śūreṣu yuddhāya gateṣu bharata ṛṣabha babhūva rajanī ghorā bhīrūṇām bhaya vardhinī yodhānām aśivā raudrā rājan antaka gāminī kuñjara aśva manuṣyāṇām prāṇānta karaṇā tadā tasyām rajanyām ghorāyām nadantyaḥ sarvatas śivāḥ ulūkāḥ ca api adṛśyanta śaṃsantaḥ vipulam bhayam viśeṣataḥ kauravāṇām dhvajinyām ati dāruṇam bherī śabdena mahatā mṛdaṅgānām svanena ca gajānām garjitaiḥ ca api turaṅgāṇām ca heṣitaiḥ tatas samabhavat yuddham saṃdhyāyām ati dāruṇam droṇasya ca mahā rāja sṛñjayānām ca sarvaśas tamasā ca āvṛte loke na prājñāyata kim cana na apaśyāma rajaḥ bhaumam kaśmalena abhisaṃvṛtāḥ mṛdaṅga ānaka nirhrādaiḥ jharjharaiḥ paṭahaiḥ tathā ghoraḥ caṭacaṭā śabdaḥ śastrāṇām patatām abhūt śātakaumbhaiḥ ca kavacaiḥ bhūṣaṇaiḥ ca tamaḥ abhyagāt tatas sā bhāratī senā maṇi hema vibhūṣitā dyauḥ iva āsīt sa nakṣatrā rajanyām bharata ṛṣabha śakti dhvaja samākulā dāruṇa abhirutā ghorā kṣveḍita utkruṣṭa nāditā samāvṛṇvan diśaḥ sarvāḥ mahā indra aśani nisvanaḥ sā niśīthe mahā rāja senā adṛśyata bhāratī aṅgadaiḥ kuṇḍalaiḥ niṣkaiḥ śastraiḥ ca eva avabhāsitā tatra nāgāḥ rathāḥ ca eva jāmbūnada vibhūṣitāḥ niśāyām pratyadṛśyanta meghāḥ iva sa vidyutaḥ ṛṣṭi śakti gadā bāṇa musala prāsa paṭṭiśāḥ saṃpatantaḥ vyadṛśyanta bhrājamānāḥ iva agnayaḥ duryodhana purovātām ratha nāga balāhakām vāditra ghoṣa stanitām cāpa vidyut dhvajaiḥ vṛtām droṇa pāṇḍava parjanyām khaḍga śakti gadā aśanim śara dhārā astra pavanām bhṛśam śīta uṣṇa saṃkulām ghorām vismāpanīm ugrām jīvita chidam aplavām tām prāviśan ati bhayām senām yuddha cikīrṣavaḥ bhīrūṇām trāsa janane śūrāṇām harṣa vardhane droṇam abhyadravan kruddhāḥ sahitāḥ pāṇḍu sṛñjayāḥ tān sarvān vimukhān cakre kān cit ninye yama kṣayam tāni nāga sahasrāṇi rathānām ayutāni ca padāti haya saṃghānām prayutāni arbudāni ca uvāca amṛṣyamāṇe saṃrabdhe kā vaḥ abhūt vai matiḥ tadā duryodhanam tathā putram uktvā śāstra atigam mama yat prāviśat ameya ātmā kim pārthaḥ pratyapadyata yat abhyagāt mahā tejāḥ pāñcālān aparājitaḥ ke ca asya pṛṣṭhatas agacchan vīrāḥ śūrasya yudhyataḥ manye aham pāṇḍavān sarvān bhāradvāja śara arditān śiśire kampamānāḥ vai kṛśāḥ gāvaḥ iva abhibho praviśya sa mahā iṣvāsaḥ pāñcālān ari mardanaḥ sarveṣu sainyeṣu ca saṃgateṣu rātrau sameteṣu mahā ratheṣu saṃloḍyamāneṣu pṛthagvidheṣu ke vaḥ tadānīm matimantaḥ āsan hatān ca eva viṣaktān ca parābhūtān ca śaṃsasi rathinaḥ virathān ca eva kṛtān yuddheṣu māmakān teṣām saṃloḍyamānānām pāṇḍavaiḥ hata cetasām prahṛṣṭān ca api udagrān ca nityam śaṃsasi pāṇḍavān aprahṛṣṭān vimanasaḥ vitrastān ca eva māmakān katham eṣām tadā tatra pārthānām apalāyinām uvāca rātri yuddhe tadā rājan vartamāne su dāruṇe droṇam abhyadravan rātrau pāṇḍavāḥ saha sainikāḥ tatas droṇaḥ kekayān ca dhṛṣṭadyumnasya ca ātmajān preṣayat mṛtyu lokāya sarvān iṣubhiḥ āśugaiḥ tān sarvān preṣayām āsa para lokāya bhārata pramathnantam tadā vīram bhāradvājam mahā ratham abhyavartata saṃkruddhaḥ śibiḥ rājan pratāpavān tam āpatantam saṃprekṣya pāṇḍavānām mahā ratham vivyādha daśabhiḥ droṇaḥ sarva pāraśavaiḥ śaraiḥ tam śibi prativivyādha triṃśat niśi śaraiḥ tasya droṇaḥ hayān hatvā sārathim ca mahātmanaḥ atha asya sa śirastrāṇam śiraḥ kāyāt apāharat sa tena saṃgṛhīta aśvaḥ punar abhyadravat ripūn kaliṅgānām ca sainyena kaliṅgasya sutaḥ raṇe kaliṅgānām tu tam śūra krudh krudh vṛkodara tasya muṣṭi hatasya ājau pāṇḍavena balīyasā sarvāṇi asthīni sahasā prāpatan vai pṛthak pṛthak tasmin tathā hate tena siṃhanādaḥ mahān abhūt pāñcālānām mahā rāja sādhu sādhu iti pāṇḍavam tam karṇaḥ bhrātaraḥ ca asya na amṛṣyanta mahā rathāḥ te bhīmasenam nārācaiḥ jaghnuḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ tatas śatru ratham tyaktvā bhīmaḥ dhruva ratham gataḥ dhruvam ca asyantam aniśam muṣṭinā samapothayat bhīmaḥ svam ratham āgamat yathā kācamaṇiḥ nyastaḥ muṣṭinā ekena līlayā tathā cūrṇam abhūt tatra karṇa bhrātā drumaḥ tathā sa tathā pāṇḍu putreṇa balinā nihataḥ apatat tam nihatya mahā rāja bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ jayarāta ratham prāpya muhur siṃhaḥ iva anadat jayarātam atha ākṣipya nadan savyena pāṇinā sūtam ca asya mahā bāhuḥ gṛhya rājñ tathā eva ca talena nāśayām āsa karṇasya eva agratas sthitam pādayoḥ gṛhya tau vīrau bhīmaḥ karṇasya paśyataḥ karṇaḥ tu pāṇḍave śaktim kāñcanīm samavāsṛjat tatas tām eva jagrāha prahasan pāṇḍu nandanaḥ karṇāya eva ca durdharṣaḥ cikṣepa ājau vṛkodaraḥ punar sva ratham āsthāya dudrāva te vāhinīm tam āyāntam jighāṃsantam bhīmam kruddham iva antakam nyavārayan mahā bāhum te putrāḥ viśām pate mahatā śara varṣeṇa chādayantaḥ vṛkodaram sārathim ca hayān ca eva śaraiḥ ninye yama kṣayam tau eka ratham ārūḍhau bhrātarau para tāpanau saṃgrāma śirasaḥ madhye bhīmam dvau abhyadhāvatām ratham ekam samāruhya bhīmam bāṇaiḥ avidhyatām kṛpasya somadattasya vāhlīkasya ca pāṇḍavaḥ āruroha mahā bāhuḥ miṣatām sarva dhanvinām pāda prahāreṇa dharām prāveśayat ariṃdamaḥ tatas hāhākṛte sainye dṛṣṭvā bhīmam nṛpa bruvan rudraḥ ayam bhīma rūpeṇa dhārtarāṣṭreṣu gṛdhyati evam uktvā apalāyanta sarve bhārata pārthivāḥ visaṃjñāḥ avāhayan vāhān na ca dvau saha dhāvataḥ tatas bale bhṛśa lulite niśā mukhe su pūjitaḥ nṛpa vṛṣabhaiḥ vṛkodaraḥ tatas yamau drupada virāṭa kekayāḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ca api parām mudam yayuḥ vṛkodaram bhṛśam abhipūjayan ca te yathā andhake pratinihate haram surāḥ tatas sutāḥ tava varuṇa ātmaja upamāḥ ruṣā anvitāḥ saha guruṇā mahātmanā yudhiṣṭhira drupada virāṭa sātvatāḥ sasṛṃjayāḥ tava tanayān avārayan niśā mukhe mahātmanām nṛpa vara yuddham adbhutam uvāca prāya upaviṣṭe tu hate putre sātyakinā tatas somadattaḥ bhṛśam kruddhaḥ sātyakim vākyam abravīt kṣatra dharmaḥ purā dṛṣṭaḥ yaḥ tu devaiḥ mahātmabhiḥ parāṅmukhāya dīnāya nyasta śastrāya yācate kṣatra dharma rataḥ prājñaḥ katham nu praharet raṇe dvau eva kila vṛṣṇīnām tatra khyātau mahā rathau katham prāya upaviṣṭāya pārthena chinna bāhave nṛśaṃsam patanīyam ca tādṛśam kṛtavān asi adya chetsyāmi te mūḍha śiraḥ vikramya pattriṇā śape sātvata putrābhyām iṣṭena sukṛtena ca an atītām imām rātrim yadi tvām vīra māninam arakṣyamāṇam pārthena jiṣṇunā sa suta anujam na hanyām niraye ghore pateyam vṛṣṇi pāṃsana dadhmau śaṅkham ca tāreṇa siṃhanādam nanāda ca tatas kamala pattra akṣaḥ siṃha daṃṣṭraḥ mahā balaḥ sātvataḥ bhṛśa saṃkruddhaḥ somadattam atha abravīt na aham bhīṣayitum śakyaḥ kṣatra vṛtte sthitaḥ tvayā hataḥ bhūriśravāḥ vīraḥ tava putraḥ mahā rathaḥ śalaḥ ca eva tathā rājan bhrātṛ vyasana karśitaḥ tvām ca api adya vadhiṣyāmi sa putra paśu bāndhavam tiṣṭha idānīm raṇe yattaḥ kauravaḥ asi viśeṣataḥ yasmin dānam damaḥ śaucam ahiṃsā hrīḥ dhṛtiḥ kṣamā anapāyīni sarvāṇi nityam rājñi yudhiṣṭhire mṛdaṅga ketoḥ tasya tvam tejasā nihataḥ purā sa karṇa saubalaḥ saṃkhye vināśam samupeṣyasi śape aham kṛṣṇa caraṇaiḥ iṣṭāpūrtena ca eva ha yadi tvām sa sutam pāpam na hanyām yudhi roṣitaḥ pravṛttau śara saṃpātam kartum puruṣa sattamau śakuniḥ ca su saṃkruddhaḥ sarva śastrabhṛtām varaḥ sāgram śata sahasram tu hayānām tasya dhīmataḥ rakṣyamāṇa ca balibhiḥ chādayām āsa sātyaki tam chādyamānam viśikhaiḥ dṛṣṭvā saṃnata parvabhiḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ abhyayāt kruddhaḥ pragṛhya mahatīm camūm caṇḍa vāta abhisṛṣṭānām udadhīnām iva svanaḥ tam vimūḍham samālakṣya sārathiḥ tvarayā anvitaḥ apovāha raṇāt vīram somadattam mahā ratham tam visaṃjñam samālokya yuyudhāna śara arditam abhyadhāvat tatas droṇaḥ yadu vīra jighāṃsayā tam āyāntam abhiprekṣya yudhiṣṭhira purogamāḥ tatas pravavṛte yuddham droṇasya saha pāṇḍavaiḥ baleḥ iva suraiḥ pūrvam trailokya jaya kāṅkṣayā tatas sāyaka jālena pāṇḍava anīkam āvṛṇot bhāradvājaḥ mahā tejāḥ vivyādha ca yudhiṣṭhiram sātyakim daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ viṃśatyā pārṣatam śaraiḥ sahadevam tathā aṣṭābhiḥ śatena ca śikhaṇḍinam draupadeyān mahā bāhuḥ pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥ virāṭam matsyam aṣṭabhiḥ drupadam daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ anyān ca sainikān viddhvā yudhiṣṭhiram upādravat te vadhyamānāḥ droṇena pāṇḍu putrasya sainikāḥ prādravan vai bhayāt rājan sārta nādāḥ diśaḥ daśa kālyamānam tu tat sainyam dṛṣṭvā droṇena phalgunaḥ dṛṣṭvā droṇaḥ tu bībhatsum abhidhāvantam āhave tatas yuddham abhūt bhūyas bhāradvājasya pāṇḍavaiḥ vyadhamat pāṇḍu sainyāni tūla rāśim iva analaḥ rājan aniśam atyantam dṛṣṭvā droṇam śara arciṣam maṇḍalīkṛta dhanvānam tapantam iva bhāskaram tasya tasya śiraḥ chittvā yayau droṇa śaraḥ kṣitim evam sā pāṇḍavā senā vadhyamānā mahātmanā pradudrāva punar bhī paśyataḥ savyasācinaḥ saṃprabhagnam balam dṛṣṭvā droṇena niśi bhārata codayām āsa dāśārhaḥ hayān droṇa ratham prati bhīmasenaḥ api tam dṛṣṭvā yāntam droṇāya phalgunam sva sārathim uvāca idam droṇa anīkāya mām vaha saḥ api tasya vacaḥ śrutvā viśokaḥ vāhayat dhayān tau dṛṣṭvā bhrātarau yattau droṇa anīkam abhidrutau pāñcālāḥ sṛñjayāḥ matsyāḥ cedi kārūṣa kośalāḥ anvagacchan mahā rāja kekayāḥ ca mahā rathāḥ tatas rājan abhūt ghoraḥ saṃgrāmaḥ loma harṣaṇaḥ bībhatsuḥ dakṣiṇam pārśvam uttaram ca vṛkodaraḥ mahadbhyām ratha vṛndābhyām balam jagṛhatuḥ tava tau dṛṣṭvā puruṣa vyāghrau bhīmasena dhanaṃjayau dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ abhyayāt rājñ sātyakiḥ ca mahā balaḥ caṇḍa vāta abhipannānām udadhīnām iva svanaḥ āsīt rājan bala oghānām tadā anyonyam abhighnatām saumadatti vadhāt kruddhaḥ dṛṣṭvā sātyakim āhave kārṣṇāyasa mayam ghoram ṛkṣa carma āvṛtam mahat mahantam ratham āsthāya triṃśat natvā antara antaram vikṣiptam aṣṭa cakreṇa vivṛta akṣeṇa kūjatā lohita ārdra patākam tam antra mālā vibhūṣitam aṣṭa cakra samāyuktam āsthāya vipulam ratham śūla mudgara dhāriṇyā śaila pādapa hastayā rakṣasām ghora rūpāṇām akṣauhiṇyā samāvṛtaḥ tam udyata mahā cāpam niśāmya vyathitāḥ nṛpāḥ tatas tam giri śṛṅga ābham bhīma rūpam bhaya āvaham daṃṣṭra karāla ugra mukham śaṅku karṇam mahā hanum ūrdhva keśam virūpa akṣam dīpta āsyam nimnita udaram mahā abhra ābha gala dvāram kirīṭa channa mūrdhajam trāsanam sarva bhūtānām vyātta ānanam iva antakam vīkṣya dīptam iva āyāntam ripu vikṣobha kāriṇam tam udyata mahā cāpam rākṣasa indram ghaṭotkacam vāyunā kṣobhita āvartā gaṅgā iva ūrdhva taraṅgiṇī ghaṭotkaca prayuktena siṃhanādena bhīṣitāḥ prasusruvuḥ gajāḥ mūtram vivyathuḥ ca narāḥ bhṛśam tatas aśma vṛṣṭiḥ atyartham āsīt tatra samantataḥ saṃdhyā kāla adhika balaiḥ pramuktā rākṣasaiḥ kṣitau āyasāni ca cakrāṇi bhuśuṇḍyaḥ prāsa tomarāḥ patanti aviralāḥ śūlāḥ śataghnyaḥ paṭṭiśāḥ tathā tat ugram ati raudram ca dṛṣṭvā yuddham narādhipāḥ tanayāḥ tava karṇaḥ ca vyathitāḥ prādravan diśaḥ nihatāyām tu māyāyām amarṣī sa ghaṭotkacaḥ visasarja śarān ghorān te aśvatthāmānam āviśan bhujagāḥ iva vegena valmīkam krodha mūrchitāḥ te śarāḥ rudhira abhyaktāḥ bhittvā śāradvatī sutam viviśuḥ dharaṇīm śīghrāḥ rukma puṅkhāḥ śilā śitāḥ aśvatthāmā tu saṃkruddhaḥ laghu hastaḥ pratāpavān cakram śata sahasra aram agṛhṇāt vyathitaḥ bhṛśam kṣura antam bāla sūrya ābham maṇi vajra vibhūṣitam vegena mahatā gacchat vikṣiptam drauṇinā śaraiḥ ghaṭotkacaḥ tatas tūrṇam dṛṣṭvā cakram nipātitam drauṇim prācchādayat bāṇaiḥ svarbhānuḥ iva bhāskaram ghaṭotkaca sutaḥ śrīmān bhinnāñjana caya upamaḥ rurodha drauṇim āyāntam prabhañjanam iva adrirāj pautreṇa bhīmasenasya śaraiḥ saḥ añjanaparvaṇā dhvajam ekena bāṇena ciccheda añjanaparvaṇaḥ dvābhyām tu ratha yantāram tribhiḥ ca asya triveṇukam gadā hema aṅgadā rājan tūrṇam haiḍimba sūnunā bhrāmya utkṣiptā śaraiḥ sā api drauṇinā abhyāhatā apatat vavarṣa añjanaparvā sa druma varṣam nabhastalāt mārgaṇaiḥ abhivivyādha ghanam sūryaḥ iva aṃśubhiḥ mahīdharaḥ iva ati uccaḥ śrīmān añjanaparvataḥ tam ayasmaya varmāṇam drauṇiḥ bhīma ātmaja ātmajam jaghāna añjanaparvāṇam maheśvaraḥ iva andhakam atha dṛṣṭvā hatam putram aśvatthāmnā mahā balam drauṇeḥ sakāśam abhyetya roṣāt pracalita aṅgadaḥ prāha vākyam asambhrāntaḥ vīram śāradvatī sutam dahantam pāṇḍava anīkam vanam agnim iva uddhatam tiṣṭha tiṣṭha na me jīvan droṇaputra gamiṣyasi uvāca kim tu roṣa anvitaḥ jantuḥ hanyāt ātmānam api uta uvāca śrutvā etat krodha tāmra akṣaḥ putra śoka samanvitaḥ aśvatthāmānam āyastaḥ bhaimaseniḥ abhāṣata bhīmāt khalu aham utpannaḥ kurūṇām vipule kule pāṇḍavānām aham putraḥ samareṣu anivartinām rakṣasām adhirājaḥ aham daśagrīva samaḥ bale tiṣṭha tiṣṭha na me jīvan droṇaputra gamiṣyasi yuddha śraddhām aham te adya vineṣyāmi raṇa ajire iti uktvā roṣa tāmra akṣaḥ rākṣasaḥ su mahā balaḥ ratha akṣa mātraiḥ iṣubhiḥ abhyavarṣat ghaṭotkacaḥ rathinām ṛṣabham drauṇim dhārābhiḥ iva toyadaḥ śara vṛṣṭim śaraiḥ drauṇiḥ aprāptām tām vyaśātayat tatas antarikṣe bāṇānām saṃgrāmaḥ anyaḥ iva abhavat niśāmya nihatām māyām drauṇinā raṇa māninā ghaṭotkacaḥ tatas māyām sasarja antarhitaḥ punar śūla prāsa asi musala jala prasravaṇaḥ mahān tam añjana caya prakhyam drauṇiḥ dṛṣṭvā mahīdharam sa tena astreṇa śaila indraḥ kṣiptaḥ kṣipram anaśyata tatas sa toyadaḥ bhūtvā nīlaḥ sa indrāyudhaḥ divi aśma vṛṣṭibhiḥ ati ugraḥ drauṇim ācchādayat raṇe sa mārgaṇa gaṇaiḥ drauṇiḥ diśaḥ pracchādya sarvatas śatam ratha sahasrāṇām jaghāna dvipadām varaḥ sa dṛṣṭvā punar āyāntam rathena āyata kārmukam ghaṭotkacam asambhrāntam rākṣasaiḥ bahubhiḥ vṛtam siṃha śārdūla sadṛśaiḥ matta dvirada vikramaiḥ vivṛta āsya śiraḥ grīvaiḥ haiḍimba anucaraiḥ saha nānā śastra dharaiḥ vīraiḥ nānā kavaca bhūṣaṇaiḥ viṣaṇṇam abhisaṃprekṣya putram te drauṇiḥ abravīt tiṣṭha duryodhana adya tvam na kāryaḥ saṃbhramaḥ tvayā nihaniṣyāmi amitrān te na tava asti parājayaḥ satyam te pratijānāmi paryāśvāsaya vāhinīm uvāca vṛtaḥ śata sahasreṇa rathānām raṇa śobhinām ṣaṣṭyā gaja sahasraiḥ ca prayāhi tvam dhanaṃjayam karṇaḥ ca vṛṣasenaḥ ca kṛpaḥ nīlaḥ tathā eva ca udīcyāḥ kṛtavarmā ca purumitraḥ śrutārpaṇaḥ duḥśāsanaḥ nikumbhaḥ ca kuṇḍabhedī urukramaḥ puraṃjayaḥ dṛḍharathaḥ patākī hemapaṅkajaḥ śalya aruṇi indrasenāḥ ca saṃjayaḥ vijayaḥ jayaḥ kamalākṣaḥ puruḥ krāthī jayavarmā sudarśanaḥ ete tvām anuyāsyanti pattīnām ayutāni ṣaḍ dāritān drauṇinā bāṇaiḥ bhṛśam vikṣata vigrahān piprīṣuḥ te sutān rājan didhakṣuḥ ca eva pāṇḍavān vibhāvaryām su tumulam śakra prahrādayoḥ iva jaghāna urasi saṃkruddhaḥ viṣa agni pratimaiḥ dṛḍhaiḥ sa taiḥ abhyāhataḥ gāḍham śaraiḥ bhīma suta īritaiḥ bhūyas ca añjalikena asya mārgaṇena mahā prabham drauṇi hasta sthitam cāpam ciccheda āśu ghaṭotkacaḥ vavarṣa viśikhān tīkṣṇān vāri dhārāḥ iva ambudaḥ tatas śāradvatī putraḥ preṣayām āsa bhārata suvarṇa puṅkhān śatru ghnān kha carān kha carān prati tad bāṇaiḥ arditam yūtham rakṣasām pīna vakṣasām vidhamya rākṣasān bāṇaiḥ sa aśva sūta rathān vibhuḥ dadāha bhagavān vahniḥ bhūtāni iva yuga kṣaye sa dagdhvā akṣauhiṇīm bāṇaiḥ nairṛtān ruruce bhṛśam rarāja jayatām śreṣṭhaḥ droṇaputraḥ te ahitān tatas ghaṭotkacaḥ kruddhaḥ rakṣasām bhīma karmaṇām drauṇim hata iti mahatīm codayām āsa tām camūm ghaṭotkacasya tām ājñām pratigṛhya atha rākṣasāḥ daṃṣṭra daṃṣṭra ujjvalāḥ mahā vaktrāḥ ghora rūpāḥ bhayānakāḥ vyatta ānanāḥ dīrgha jihvāḥ krodha tāmra īkṣaṇāḥ bhṛśam siṃhanādena mahatā nādayantaḥ vasuṃdharān hantum abhyadravan drauṇim nānā praharaṇa āyudhāḥ śaktīḥ śataghnīḥ parighān aśanīḥ śūla paṭṭiśān khaḍgān gadāḥ bhindipālān musalāni paraśvadhān tomarān ca kaṇapān kampanān śitān hulān bhuśuṇḍi aśma guḍān sthūṇāḥ kārṣṇāyasīḥ tathā mudgarān ca mahā ghorān samare śatru dāraṇān drauṇi mūrdhani asajjanta rākṣasāḥ bhīma vikramāḥ cikṣipuḥ krodha tāmra akṣāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas patamānam samīkṣya atha yodhāḥ te vyathitāḥ abhavan śaraiḥ vidhvaṃsayām āsa vajra kalpaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ tatas anyaiḥ viśikhaiḥ tūrṇam svarṇa puṅkhaiḥ mahāmanāḥ tat bāṇaiḥ arditam yūtham rakṣasām pīna vakṣasām te rākṣasāḥ su saṃkruddhāḥ droṇaputreṇa tāḍitāḥ kruddhāḥ sma prādravan drauṇim jighāṃsantaḥ mahā balāḥ yat ekaḥ rākṣasīm senām kṣaṇāt drauṇiḥ mahā astra vid dadāha jvalitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ rākṣasa indrasya paśyataḥ sa dahan rākṣasa anīkam rarāja drauṇiḥ āhave yuga ante anta sarva bhūtāni saṃvartakaḥ iva analaḥ tam dahantam anīkāni śaraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ teṣu rāja sahasreṣu pāṇḍaveyeṣu bhārata na enam nirīkṣitum kaḥ cit śaknoti drauṇim āhave ṛte ghaṭotkacāt vīrāt rākṣasa indrāt mahā balāt tat vinadya mahā nādam siṃha vat bhīma vikramaḥ sa cikṣepa tatas krudh droṇaputrāya rākṣasa aṣṭa cakrām mahā raudrām aśanīm rudra nirmitām sa aśva sūta dhvajam vāham bhasma kṛtvā mahā prabhā viveśa vasudhām bhittvā sa aśaniḥ bhṛśa dāruṇā drauṇeḥ tat karma dṛṣṭvā tu sarva bhūtāni apūjayan mumoca niśitān bāṇān punar drauṇeḥ mahā urasi dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ api asambhrāntaḥ mumoca āśīviṣa upamān suvarṇa puṅkhān viśikhān droṇaputrasya vakṣasi tatas mumoca nārācān drauṇiḥ tābhyām sahasraśas ati tīvram abhūt yuddham tayoḥ puruṣa siṃhayoḥ yodhānām prīti jananam drauṇeḥ ca bharata ṛṣabha ṣaḍbhiḥ vāji sahasraiḥ ca bhīmaḥ tam deśam āvrajat tatas bhīma ātmajam rakṣaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam ca sa anugam nimeṣa antara mātreṇa sa aśva sūta ratha dvipām akṣauhiṇīm rākṣasānām śā bāṇaiḥ aśātayat miṣataḥ bhīmasenasya haiḍimbeḥ pārṣatasya ca pragāḍham añjaḥ gatibhiḥ nārācaiḥ abhitāḍitāḥ nipetuḥ dviradāḥ bhūmau dvi śṛṅgāḥ iva parvatāḥ rarāja vasudhā kīrṇā visarpadbhiḥ iva uragaiḥ kṣiptaiḥ kāñcana daṇḍaiḥ ca nṛpa chatraiḥ kṣitiḥ babhau dyauḥ iva udita candra arkā graha ākīrṇā yuga kṣaye pravṛddha dhvaja maṇḍūkām bherī vistīrṇa kacchapām chatra haṃsa āvali juṣṭām phena cāmara mālinīm kaṅka gṛdhra mahā grāhām na eka āyudha jhaṣa ākulām vistīrṇa gaja pāṣāṇām hata aśva makara ākulām ratha kṣipta mahā vaprām patākā rucira drumām śara mīnām mahā raudrām prāsa śakti ugra ḍuṇḍubhām majjā māṃsa mahā paṅkām kabandha āvarjita uḍupām keśa śaivala kalmāṣām bhīrūṇām kaśmala āvahām nāga indra haya yodhānām śarīra vyaya sambhavām śoṇita ogha mahā vegām drauṇiḥ prāvartayat nadīm yodha ārta rava nirghoṣām kṣataja ūrmi samākulām nihatya rākṣasān bāṇaiḥ drauṇiḥ haiḍimbam ārdayat sa nārāca gaṇaiḥ pārthān drauṇiḥ viddhvā mahā balaḥ punar śrutaṃjayam nāma surathasya anujam raṇa balānīkam jayānīkam jayāśvam ca abhijaghnivān punar śareṇa tīkṣṇena drauṇiḥ siṃhaḥ iva unnadan tribhiḥ ca anyaiḥ śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ su puṅkhaiḥ rukmamālinam śatruṃjayam ca balinam śakra lokam nināya ha kuntibhoja sutān ca ājau daśabhiḥ daśa jaghnivāḥ aśvatthāmā su saṃkruddhaḥ saṃdhāya ugram ajihmagam mumoca ākarṇa pūrṇena dhanuṣā śaram uttamam yama daṇḍa upamam ghoram uddiśya āśu ghaṭotkacam sa bhittvā hṛdayam tasya rākṣasasya mahat śaraḥ viveśa vasudhām śīghram sa puṅkhaḥ pṛthivīpate tad han pat jñā dhṛṣṭadyumna mahat ratha drauṇeḥ sakāśāt rāja indra apaninye ratha antaram tathā parāṅmukha ratham sainyam yaudhiṣṭhiram nṛpa tam siddha gandharva piśāca saṃghāḥ nāgāḥ suparṇāḥ pitaraḥ vayāṃsi rakṣaḥ gaṇāḥ bhūta gaṇāḥ ca drauṇim apūjayan apsarasaḥ surāḥ ca uvāca drupadasya ātmajān dṛṣṭvā kuntibhoja sutān tathā droṇaputreṇa nihatān rākṣasān ca sahasraśas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ bhīmasenaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca pārṣataḥ somadattaḥ punar dṛṣṭvā sātyakim āhave mahatā śara varṣeṇa chādayām āsa sarvatas tvadīyānām pareṣām ca ghoram vijaya kāṅkṣiṇām tam dṛṣṭvā samupāyāntam rukma puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ vṛddham ṛddham guṇaiḥ sarvaiḥ yayātim iva nāhuṣam vivyādha daśabhiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ śaraiḥ vajra nipātibhiḥ sātyakiḥ ca agni saṃkāśam mumoca śaram uttamam visṛjan śara varṣāṇi kāla varṣī iva toyadaḥ bhīmaḥ atha sātvatasya arthe vāhlīkam navabhiḥ śaraiḥ pīḍayan vai mahātmānam vivyādha raṇa mūrdhani prātipīyaḥ tu saṃkruddhaḥ śaktim bhīmasya vakṣasi nicakhāna mahā bāhuḥ puraṃdaraḥ iva aśanim sā pāṇḍavena prahitā vāhlīkasya śiraḥ aharat sa papāta hataḥ pṛthvyām vajra āhataḥ iva adrirāj putrāḥ te abhyardayan bhīmam daśa dāśaratheḥ samāḥ nāgadattaḥ dṛḍharathaḥ vīrabāhuḥ ayobhujaḥ dṛḍhaḥ suhastaḥ virajāḥ pramāthī ca ugrayāyī api tān dṛṣṭvā cukrudhe bhīmaḥ jagṛhe bhāra sādhanān caṇḍa vāta prabhagnāḥ vā parvata agrāt mahīruhāḥ nārācaiḥ daśabhiḥ bhīmaḥ tān nihatya te ātmajān karṇasya dayitam putram vṛṣasenam avākirat tatas vṛṣarathaḥ nāma bhrātā karṇasya viśrutaḥ jaghāna bhīmam nārācaiḥ tam api abhi avadhīt balī tatas sapta rathān vīraḥ syālānām te bhārata śakuneḥ bhrātaraḥ vīrāḥ gajākṣaḥ śarabhaḥ vibhuḥ subhagaḥ bhānudattaḥ ca śūrāḥ pañca mahā rathāḥ abhidrutya śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ bhīmasenam atāḍayan sa tudyamānaḥ nārācaiḥ vṛṣṭi vegaiḥ iva ṛṣabhaḥ jaghāna pañcabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ pañca eva ati balaḥ rathān tān dṛṣṭvā nihatān vīrān viceluḥ nṛpa sattamāḥ tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ kruddhaḥ tava anīkam aśātayat miṣataḥ kumbhayoneḥ ca putrāṇām ca te anagha ambaṣṭhān mālavān śūrān trigartān sa śibīn api prāhiṇot mṛtyu lokāya gaṇān yuddhe yudhiṣṭhiraḥ abhīṣāhān śūrasenān vāhlīkān sa vasātikān nikṛtya pṛthivīm rājā cakre śoṇita kardamām yaudheya āraṭṭa rājanya madrakāṇām gaṇān yudhi prāhiṇot mṛtyu lokāya śūrān bāṇaiḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ iti āsīt tumulaḥ śabdaḥ yudhiṣṭhira ratham prati sainyāni drāvayantam tam droṇaḥ dṛṣṭvā yudhiṣṭhiram vāruṇam yāmyam āgneyam tvāṣṭram sāvitram eva ca cikṣepa parama krudh jighāṃsuḥ pāṇḍu nandanam kṣiptāni kṣipyamāṇāni tāni ca astrāṇi dharmajaḥ satyām cikīrṣamāṇaḥ tu pratijñām kumbhasaṃbhavaḥ patiḥ kurūṇām gaja siṃha gāmī tatas kim cit ghoreṇa tamasā āvṛte sarva bhūtāni ca param trāsam jagmuḥ mahīpate brahmāstram udyatam dṛṣṭvā kuntī putraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ vyadhamat roṣa tāmra akṣaḥ vāyavya astreṇa bhārata vāyavya astreṇa vyadhamat roṣa paryākula īkṣaṇaḥ te hanyamānāḥ droṇena pāñcālāḥ prādravan bhayāt tatas kirīṭī bhīmaḥ ca sahasā saṃnyavartatām mahadbhyām ratha vaṃśābhyām parigṛhya balam tava bībhatsuḥ dakṣiṇam pārśvam uttaram tu vṛkodaraḥ bhāradvājam śara oghābhyām mahadbhyām abhyavarṣatām tau tadā sṛñjayāḥ ca eva pāñcālāḥ ca mahā ojasaḥ tatas sā bhāratī senā vadhyamānā kirīṭinā droṇena vāryamāṇāḥ te svayam te sutena ca na aśakyanta mahā rāja yodhāḥ vārayitum tadā uvāca udīryamāṇam tat dṛṣṭvā pāṇḍavānām mahat balam aviṣahyam ca manvānaḥ karṇam duryodhanaḥ abravīt ayam sa kālaḥ saṃprāptaḥ mitrāṇām mitra vatsala pāñcālaiḥ matsya kaikeyaiḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ ca mahā rathaiḥ ete nadanti saṃhṛṣṭāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ jita kāśinaḥ śakra upamāḥ ca bahavaḥ pāñcālānām ratha vrajāḥ uvāca tam api āśu parājitya tatas hantāsmi pāṇḍavam satyam te pratijānāmi samāśvasihi bhārata hantāsmi pāṇḍu tanayān pāñcālān ca samāgatān jayam te pratijānāmi vāsavasya iva pāvakiḥ priyam tava mayā kāryam iti jīvāmi pārthiva sarveṣām eva pārthānām phalgunaḥ balavattaraḥ tasya amoghām vimokṣyāmi śaktim śakra vinirmitām tava vaśyāḥ bhaviṣyanti vanam yāsyanti vā punar mayi jīvati kauravya viṣādam mā kṛthāḥ kva cit aham jeṣyāmi samare sahitān sarva pāṇḍavān pāñcālān kekayān ca eva vṛṣṇīn ca api samāgatān bāṇa oghaiḥ śakalīkṛtya tava dāsyāmi medinīm uvāca evam bruvāṇam karṇam tu kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ abravīt smayan iva mahā bāhuḥ sūtaputram idam vacaḥ śobhanam śobhanam karṇa sa nāthaḥ kuru puṃgavaḥ samāgamaḥ pāṇḍu sutaiḥ dṛṣṭaḥ te bahuśas yudhi sarvatra nirjitaḥ ca asi pāṇḍavaiḥ sūtanandana hriyamāṇe tadā karṇa gandharvaiḥ dhṛtarāṣṭra je virāṭa nagare ca api sametāḥ sarva kauravāḥ katham utsahase jetum sa kṛṣṇān sarva pāṇḍavān garjitvā sūtaputra tvam śārada abhram iva ajalam niṣphalaḥ dṛśyase karṇa tat ca rājā na budhyate purā pārtham hi te dṛṣṭvā durlabham garjitam bhavet bāhubhiḥ kṣatriyāḥ śūrāḥ vāgbhiḥ śūrāḥ dvijātayaḥ dhanuṣā phalgunaḥ śūraḥ karṇaḥ śūraḥ manorathaiḥ evam paruṣitaḥ tena tadā śāradvatena saḥ karṇaḥ praharatām śreṣṭhaḥ kṛpam vākyam atha abravīt śūrāḥ garjanti satatam prāvṛṣi iva balāhakāḥ phalam ca āśu prayacchanti bījam uptam ṛtau iva doṣam atra na paśyāmi śūrāṇām raṇa mūrdhani tat tat vikatthamānānām bhāram ca udvahatām mṛdhe yam bhāram puruṣaḥ voḍhum manasā hi vyavasyati vṛthā śūrāḥ na garjanti sa jalāḥ iva toyadāḥ sāmarthyam ātmanaḥ jñātvā tatas garjanti paṇḍitāḥ saḥ aham adya raṇe yattaḥ sahitau kṛṣṇa pāṇḍavau hatvā pāṇḍu sutān ājau saha kṛṣṇān sa sātvatān duryodhanāya dāsyāmi pṛthivīm hata kaṇṭakām uvāca yadā kṣipasi vai kṛṣṇau dharmarājam ca pāṇḍavam deva gandharva yakṣāṇām manuṣya uraga rakṣasām daṃśitānām api raṇe ajeyau kṛṣṇa pāṇḍavau nityam dharma rataḥ ca eva kṛtāstraḥ ca viśeṣataḥ dhṛtimān ca kṛtajñaḥ ca dharmaputraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ bhrātaraḥ ca asya balinaḥ sarva astreṣu kṛta śramāḥ guru vṛtti ratāḥ prājñāḥ dharma nityāḥ yaśasvinaḥ saṃbandhinaḥ ca indra vīryāḥ su anuraktāḥ prahāriṇaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca daurmukhiḥ janamejayaḥ yeṣām arthāya saṃyattaḥ matsya rājaḥ saha anugaḥ śatānīkaḥ sudaśanaḥ śrutānīkaḥ śrutadhvajaḥ balānīkaḥ jayānīkaḥ jayāśvaḥ rathavāhanaḥ jayapriyaḥ candrodayaḥ kāmarathaḥ virāṭa bhrātaraḥ śubhāḥ yamau ca draupadeyāḥ ca rākṣasaḥ ca ghaṭotkacaḥ yeṣām arthāya yudhyante na teṣām vidyate kṣayaḥ sa yakṣa rākṣasa gaṇam sa bhūta bhujaga dvipam niḥśeṣam astra vīryeṇa kuryātām bhīma phalgunau yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ca pṛthivīm nirdahet ghora cakṣuṣā aprameya balaḥ śauriḥ yeṣām arthe ca daṃśitaḥ uvāca abravīt ca tadā karṇaḥ gurum śāradvatam kṛpam satyam uktam tvayā brahman pāṇḍavān prati yat vacaḥ ete ca anye ca bahavaḥ guṇāḥ pāṇḍu suteṣu vai ajayyāḥ ca raṇe pārthāḥ devaiḥ api sa vāsavaiḥ tathā api pārthān jeṣyāmi śaktyā vāsava dattayā mama api amoghā dattā iyam śaktiḥ śakreṇa vai dvija hate tu pāṇḍave kṛṣṇaḥ bhrātaraḥ ca asya sodarāḥ anarjunāḥ na śakṣyanti mahīm bhoktum katham cana anarjunāyām ca bhuvi vinaśyeyuḥ na saṃśayaḥ teṣu naṣṭeṣu sarveṣu pṛthivī iyam sa sāgarā su nītaiḥ iha sarva arthāḥ sidhyante na atra saṃśayaḥ tvam tu vṛddhaḥ ca vipraḥ ca aśaktaḥ ca api saṃyuge kṛta snehaḥ ca pārtheṣu mohāt mām avamanyase atra api śṛṇu me vākyam yathāvat gadataḥ dvija duḥśāsanaḥ vṛṣasenaḥ madra rājaḥ tvam eva ca somadattaḥ ca bhūriḥ ca tathā drauṇiḥ viviṃśatiḥ tiṣṭheyuḥ daṃśitāḥ yatra sarve yuddha viśāradāḥ śūrāḥ ca hi kṛtāstrāḥ ca balinaḥ svarga lipsavaḥ ete sthāsyanti saṃgrāme pāṇḍavānām vadha arthinaḥ jayam ākāṅkṣamāṇāḥ hi kauraveyasya daṃśitāḥ yatra bhīṣmaḥ mahā bāhuḥ śete śara śata ācitaḥ bhūriśravāḥ jayaḥ ca eva jalasaṃdhaḥ sudakṣiṇaḥ śalaḥ ca rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ bhagadattaḥ ca vīryavān nihatāḥ samare śūrāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ balavattarāḥ yān ca tān stauṣi satatam duryodhana ripūn dvija teṣām api hatāḥ śūrāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas kṣīyante sarva sainyāni kurūṇām pāṇḍavaiḥ saha prabhāvam na atra paśyāmi pāṇḍavānām katham cana yatiṣye aham yathāśakti yoddhum taiḥ saha saṃyuge uvāca tathā paruṣitam dṛṣṭvā sūtaputreṇa mātulam uvāca yat arjuna guṇān tathyān kīrtayānam nara adhama kva te vīryam kva ca astrāṇi yat tvām nirjitya saṃyuge gāṇḍīvadhanvā hatavān prekṣataḥ te jayadratham yena sākṣāt mahādevaḥ yodhitaḥ samare purā tam icchasi vṛthak jetum sūta adhama manorathaiḥ yam hi kṛṣṇena sahitam sarva śastrabhṛtām varam jetum na śaktāḥ sahitāḥ sa indrāḥ api sura asurāḥ karṇa paśya su durbuddhe tiṣṭha idānīm nara adhama eṣa te adya śiraḥ kāyāt uddharāmi su durmate uvāca nyavārayat mahā rāja kṛpaḥ ca dvipadām varaḥ uvāca śūraḥ ayam samara ślāghī durmatiḥ ca dvija adhamaḥ āsādayatu mad vīryam muñca imam kuru sattama uvāca āyānti pāṇḍavāḥ brahman āhvayantaḥ samantataḥ uvāca prasādyamānaḥ tu tatas rājñā drauṇiḥ mahā manāḥ tatas kṛpaḥ uvāca idam ācāryaḥ su mahāmanāḥ saumya svabhāvāt rāja indra kṣipram āgata mārdavaḥ tatas te pāṇḍavāḥ rājan pāñcālāḥ ca yaśasvinaḥ ājagmuḥ sahitāḥ tatra tarjayantaḥ punar punar duryodhana vacaḥ śrutvā aśvatthāmā mahā balaḥ karṇaḥ api rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ cāpam udyamya vīryavān paryatiṣṭhata tejasvī sva bāhu balam āśritaḥ tatas pravavṛte yuddham karṇasya saha pāṇḍavaiḥ saṃrabdhasya mahā rāja siṃhanāda vināditam tatas te pāṇḍavāḥ rājan pāñcālāḥ ca yaśasvinaḥ dṛṣṭvā karṇam mahā bāhum uccais śabdam atha anadan ayam karṇaḥ kutas karṇaḥ tiṣṭha karṇa mahā raṇe anye tu dṛṣṭvā rādheyam krodha rakta īkṣaṇāḥ bruvan sarvaiḥ pārthiva śārdūlaiḥ na anena arthaḥ asti jīvatā atyanta vairī pārthānām satatam pāpa pūruṣaḥ eṣa mūlam hi anarthānām duryodhana mate sthitaḥ mahatā śara varṣeṇa chādayantaḥ mahā rathāḥ vadha artham sūtaputrasya pāṇḍaveyena coditāḥ tān tu sarvān tathā dṛṣṭvā dhāvamānān mahā rathān dṛṣṭvā nagara kalpam tam uddhūtam sainya sāgaram piprīṣuḥ tava putrāṇām saṃgrāmeṣu aparājitaḥ sāyaka oghena balavān kṣiprakārī mahā balaḥ tatas tu śara varṣeṇa pārthivāḥ tam avārayan dhanūṃṣi te vidhunvānāḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas ayodhayanta rādheyam śakram daitya gaṇāḥ iva śara varṣam tu tat karṇaḥ pārthivaiḥ samudīritam tat yuddham abhavat teṣām kṛta pratikṛta eṣiṇām nivārya ca śara oghān tān pārthivānām mahā rathaḥ yugeṣu īṣāsu chatreṣu dhvajeṣu ca hayeṣu ca ātma nāma aṅkitān bāṇān rādheyaḥ prāhiṇot śitān tatas te vyākulībhūtāḥ rājānaḥ karṇa pīḍitāḥ babhramuḥ tatra tatra eva gāvaḥ śīta arditāḥ iva hayānām vadh gajānām rathin tathā tatra tatra abhyavekṣāmaḥ saṃghān karṇena pātitān āstīrṇā vasudhā sarvā śūrāṇām anivartinām hataiḥ ca hanyamānaiḥ ca niṣṭanadbhiḥ ca sarvaśas tatas duryodhanaḥ rājā dṛṣṭvā karṇasya vikramam aśvatthāmānam āsādya tadā vākyam uvāca ha yudhyate asau raṇe karṇaḥ daṃśitaḥ sarva pārthivaiḥ paśya etām dravatīm senām karṇa sāyaka pīḍitām kārttikeyena vidhvastām āsurīm pṛtanām iva dṛṣṭvā etām nirjitām senām raṇe karṇena dhīmatā abhiyāti eṣa bībhatsuḥ sūtaputra jighāṃsayā tat yathā paśyamānānām sūtaputram mahā ratham na hanyāt pāṇḍavaḥ saṃkhye tathā nītiḥ vidhīyatām tatas drauṇiḥ kṛpaḥ śalyaḥ hārdikyaḥ ca mahā rathaḥ bībhatsuḥ api rāja indra pāñcālaiḥ abhisaṃvṛtaḥ āyāntam dṛśya kaunteyam vṛtram deva camūm iva pratyudyayau tadā karṇaḥ yathā śakraḥ pratāpavān uvāca saṃrabdham phalgunam dṛṣṭvā kāla antaka yama upamam āśaṃsate ca bībhatsum yuddhe jetum su dāruṇe uvāca āyāntam pāṇḍavam dṛṣṭvā gajaḥ pratigajam yathā asaṃbhrāntataraḥ karṇaḥ partyudīyāt dhanaṃjayam vārayām āsa tejasvī pāṇḍavaḥ śatru tāpanaḥ tam karṇaḥ śara jālena chādayām āsa māriṣa gāṇḍīvadhanuṣaḥ maurvīm chittvā acyutam atāḍayat tasya tat lāghavam pārthaḥ na amṛṣyata mahā balaḥ tūrṇam jyām ca samāropya gāṇḍīve ca navām dṛḍhām tasmai bāṇān śilā dhautān prasanna agrān a jihma gān prāhiṇot sūtaputrāya triṃśatam śatru tāpanaḥ vivyādha ca enam saṃrabdhaḥ bāṇena ekena vīryavān punar ādāya tat cāpam nimeṣa ardhāt mahā balaḥ chādayām āsa bāṇa oghaiḥ phalgunam kṛtahasta vat śara vṛṣṭim tu tām muktām sūtaputreṇa bhārata tau parasparam āsādya śara varṣeṇa pārthiva chādayetām mahā iṣvāsau kṛta pratikṛta eṣiṇau tat adbhutam abhūt yuddham karṇa pāṇḍavayoḥ mṛdhe tatas pārthaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ dṛṣṭvā karṇasya vikramam sāratheḥ ca śiraḥ kāyāt aharat śatru tāpanaḥ atha enam chinna dhanvānam hata aśvam hata sārathim vivyādha sāyakaiḥ pārthaḥ caturbhiḥ pāṇḍu nandanaḥ hata aśvāt tu rathāt tūrṇam avaplutya nara ṛṣabhaḥ āruroha ratham tūrṇam kṛpasya śara pīḍitaḥ rādheyam nirjitam dṛṣṭvā tāvakāḥ bharata ṛṣabha dhanaṃjaya śaraiḥ nunnāḥ prādravanta diśaḥ daśa nivartayām āsa tadā vākyam ca idam uvāca ha alam drutena vaḥ śūrāḥ tiṣṭhadhvam kṣatriya ṛṣabhāḥ eṣa pārtha vadhāya aham svayam gacchāmi saṃyuge aham pārthān haniṣyāmi sa pāñcālān sa somakān adya me yudhyamānasya saha gāṇḍīvadhanvanā drakṣyanti vikramam pārthāḥ kālasya iva yuga kṣaye adya mad bāṇa jālāni vimuktāni sahasraśas drakṣyanti samare yodhāḥ śalabhānām iva āyatīḥ adya bāṇa mayam varṣam sṛjataḥ mama dhanvinaḥ jeṣyāmi adya raṇe pārtham sāyakaiḥ nata parvabhiḥ tiṣṭhadhvam samare śūrāḥ bhayam tyajata phalgunāt yathā velām samāsādya sāgaraḥ makara ālayaḥ iti uktvā prayayau rājā sainyena mahatā vṛtaḥ tam prayāntam mahā bāhum dṛṣṭvā śāradvataḥ tadā aśvatthāmānam āsādya vākyam etat uvāca ha eṣa rājā mahā bāhuḥ amarṣī krodha mūrchitaḥ yāvat naḥ paśyamānānām prāṇān pārthena saṃgataḥ yāvat phalguna bāṇānām gocaram na adhigacchati na bhasmīkriyate rājā tāvat yuddhāt nivāryatām ayuktam iva paśyāmi tiṣṭhatsu asmāsu mānada svayam yuddhāya yat rājā pārtham yāti asahāyavān mātulena evam uktaḥ tu drauṇiḥ śastrabhṛtām varaḥ mām an ādṛtya kauravya te nityam hita eṣiṇam aham āvārayiṣyāmi pārtham tiṣṭha suyodhana ācāryaḥ pāṇḍu putrān vai putra vat parirakṣati sukha arhāḥ paramam duḥkham prāpnuvanti aparājitāḥ aśvatthāman prasīdasva nāśaya etān mama ahitān tava astra gocare śaktāḥ sthātum devāḥ api na anagha pāñcālān somakān ca eva jahi drauṇe saha anugān vayam śeṣān haniṣyāmaḥ tvayā eva parirakṣitāḥ ete hi somakāḥ vipra pāñcālāḥ ca yaśasvinaḥ tān vāraya mahā bāho kekayān ca narottama purā kurvanti niḥśeṣam rakṣyamāṇāḥ kirīṭinā aśvatthāman tvarā yuktaḥ yāhi śīghram ariṃdama ādau vā yadi vā paścāt tava idam karma māriṣa tvam utpannaḥ mahā bāho pāñcālānām vadham prati kariṣyasi jagat sarvam apāñcālam kila acyuta tasmāt tvam puruṣa vyāghra pāñcālān jahi sa anugān na te astra gocare śaktāḥ sthātum devāḥ sa vāsavāḥ kim u pārthāḥ sa pāñcālāḥ satyam etat vacaḥ mama na tvām samarthāḥ saṃgrāme pāṇḍavāḥ saha somakaiḥ iyam hi dravate senā pārtha sāyaka pīḍitā nigrahe pāṇḍu putrāṇām pāñcālānām ca mānada uvāca priyāḥ hi pāṇḍavāḥ nityam mama ca api pituḥ ca me tathā eva āvām priyau teṣām na tu yuddhe kuru udvaha śaktitas tāta yudhyāmaḥ tyaktvā prāṇān abhīta vat aham karṇaḥ ca śalyaḥ ca kṛpaḥ hārdikyaḥ eva ca nimeṣāt pāṇḍavām senām kṣapayema nṛpa uttama te ca api kauravīm senām nimeṣa ardhāt kuru udvaha yudhyatām pāṇḍavān śaktyā teṣām ca asmān yuyutsatām tejaḥ tu tejaḥ āsādya praśamam yāti bhārata aśakyā tarasā jetum pāṇḍavānām anīkinī jīvatsu pāṇḍu putreṣu tat hi satyam bravīmi te ātma artham yudhyamānāḥ te samarthāḥ pāṇḍu nandanāḥ sarva atiśaṅkī mānī ca tatas asmān atiśaṅkase manye tvam kutsitaḥ rājan pāpa ātmā pāpa pūruṣaḥ anyān api sa naḥ kṣudra śaṅkase pāpa bhāvitaḥ eṣa gacchāmi saṃgrāmam tvad kṛte kuru nandana yotsye aham śatrubhiḥ sārdham jeṣyāmi ca varān varān pāñcālaiḥ saha yotsyāmi somakaiḥ kekayaiḥ tathā pāṇḍaveyaiḥ ca saṃgrāme tvad priya artham ariṃdama adya mad bāṇa nirdagdhāḥ pāñcālāḥ somakāḥ tathā siṃhena iva arditāḥ gāvaḥ vidraviṣyanti sarvatas adya dharmasutaḥ rājā dṛṣṭvā mama parākramam dṛṣṭvā vinihatān saṃkhye pāñcālān somakaiḥ saha evam uktvā mahā bāhuḥ putram duryodhanam te cikīrṣuḥ tava putrāṇām priyam prāṇabhṛtām varaḥ tatas abravīt sa kaikeyān pāñcālān gautamīsutaḥ evam uktāḥ tu te sarve śastra vṛṣṭim apātayan drauṇim prati mahā rāja jalam jaladharāḥ iva tān nihatya śarān drauṇiḥ daśa vīrān apothayat pramukhe pāṇḍu putrāṇām dhṛṣṭadyumnasya ca abhibho te hanyamānāḥ samare pāñcālāḥ sṛñjayāḥ tathā tān dṛṣṭvā dravataḥ śūrān pāñcālān saha somakān tatas kāñcana citrāṇām sa jala ambuda nādinām vṛtaḥ śatena śūrāṇām rathānām anivartinām putraḥ pāñcāla rājasya dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā rathaḥ drauṇim iti abravīt vākyam dṛṣṭvā yodhān nipātitān samāgaccha mayā sārdham yadi śūraḥ asi saṃyuge aham tvām nihaniṣyāmi tiṣṭha idānīm mama agratas tatas tam ācārya sutam dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ pratāpavān te tu paṅktīkṛtāḥ drauṇim śarāḥ viviśuḥ āśugāḥ rukma puṅkhāḥ prasanna agrāḥ sarva kāya avadāraṇāḥ saḥ atividdhaḥ bhṛśam kruddhaḥ pada ākrāntaḥ iva uragaḥ mānī drauṇiḥ asambhrāntaḥ bāṇa pāṇiḥ abhāṣata dhṛṣṭadyumna sthiraḥ bhūtvā muhūrtam pratipālaya yāvat tvām niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ preṣayāmi yama kṣayam drauṇiḥ evam atha ābhāṣya pārṣatam para vīra hā chādayām āsa bāṇa oghaiḥ samantāt laghu hasta vat drauṇim pāñcāla tanayaḥ vāgbhiḥ ātarjayat tadā na jānīṣe pratijñām me vipra utpattim tathā eva ca imām tu rajanīm prāptām aprabhātām su durmate tām darśaya sthiraḥ bhūtvā na me jīvan vimokṣyase iti uktaḥ paruṣam vākyam pārṣatena dvijottamaḥ krodham āhārayat tīvram tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt nirdahan iva cakṣurbhyām pārṣatam saḥ abhyavaikṣata chādayām āsa ca śaraiḥ niḥśvasan pannagaḥ yathā sa chādyamānaḥ samare drauṇinā rāja sattama sarva pāñcāla senābhiḥ saṃvṛtaḥ ratha sattamaḥ na akampata mahā bāhuḥ sva dhairyam samupāśritaḥ sāyakān ca eva vividhān aśvatthāmni mumoca ha tau punar saṃnyavartetām prāṇa dyūta pare raṇe utsṛjantau mahā iṣvāsau śara vṛṣṭīḥ samantataḥ drauṇi pārṣatayoḥ yuddham ghora rūpam bhayānakam dṛṣṭvā saṃpūjayām āsuḥ siddha cāraṇa vātikāḥ śara oghaiḥ pūrayantau tau ākāśam pradiśaḥ tathā alakṣyau samayudhyetām mahat kṛtvā śaraiḥ tamaḥ nṛtyamānau iva raṇe maṇḍalīkṛta kārmukau ayudhyetām mahā bāhū citram laghu ca suṣṭhu ca siṃhanāda ravāḥ ca āsan dadhmuḥ śaṅkhān ca māriṣa vāditrāṇi abhyavādyanta śataśas atha sahasraśas tatas drauṇiḥ mahā rāja pārṣatasya mahātmanaḥ dhvajam dhanuḥ tathā chatram ubhau ca pārṣṇisārathī sūtam aśvān ca caturaḥ nihatya abhyadravat raṇe pāñcālān ca eva tān sarvān bāṇaiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ vyadrāvayat ameya ātmā śataśas atha sahasraśas tatas pravivyathe senā pāṇḍavā bharata ṛṣabha dṛṣṭvā drauṇeḥ mahat karma vāsavasya iva saṃyuge śatena ca śatam hatvā pāñcālānām mahā rathaḥ tribhiḥ ca niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ hatvā trīn vai mahā rathān nāśayām āsa pāñcālān bhūyiṣṭham ye vyavasthitāḥ te vadhyamānāḥ pāñcālāḥ samare saha sṛñjayaiḥ sa jitvā samare śatrūn droṇaputraḥ mahā rathaḥ nanāda su mahā nādam tapānte jaladaḥ yathā sa nihatya bahūn śūrān aśvatthāmā vyarocata yuga ante sarva bhūtāni bhasma kṛtvā iva pāvakaḥ uvāca tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ca eva bhīmasenaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ droṇaputram mahā rāja samantāt paryavārayan tatas duryodhanaḥ rājā bhāradvājena saṃvṛtaḥ ghora rūpam mahā rāja bhīrūṇām bhaya vardhanam ambaṣṭhān mālavān vaṅgān śibīn traigartakān api prāhiṇot mṛtyu lokāya gaṇān kruddhaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ abhīṣāhān śūrasenān kṣatriyān yuddha durmadān nikṛtya pṛthivīm cakre bhīmaḥ śoṇita kardamām yaudheya āraṭṭa rājanyān madrakān ca gaṇān yudhi prāhiṇot mṛtyu lokāya kirīṭī niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ pragāḍham añjaḥ gatibhiḥ nārācaiḥ abhipīḍitāḥ nipetuḥ dviradāḥ bhūmau dvi śṛṅgāḥ iva parvatāḥ rarāja vasudhā kīrṇā visarpadbhiḥ iva uragaiḥ dyauḥ iva āditya candra ādyaiḥ grahaiḥ kīrṇā yuga kṣaye iti āsīt tumulaḥ śabdaḥ śoṇāśvasya ratham prati te hanyamānāḥ droṇena pāñcālāḥ prādravan bhayāt tatas kirīṭī bhīmaḥ ca sahasā saṃnyavartatām bībhatsuḥ dakṣiṇam pārśvam uttaram tu vṛkodaraḥ bhāradvājam śara oghābhyām mahadbhyām abhyavarṣatām tau tadā sṛñjayāḥ ca eva pāñcālāḥ ca mahā rathāḥ tatas sā senā vadhyamānā kirīṭinā droṇena vāryamāṇāḥ te svayam te sutena ca na śakyante mahā rāja yodhāḥ vārayitum tadā sā pāṇḍu putrasya śaraiḥ dāryamāṇā mahā camūḥ utsṛjya śataśas vāhān tatra ke cit narādhipāḥ prādravanta mahā rāja bhaya āviṣṭāḥ samantataḥ uvāca sātyakiḥ prāha yantāram somadattāya mām vaha na hi a hatvā raṇe śatrum vāhlīkam kaurava adhamam tatas saṃpreṣayat yantā saindhavān tān mahā javān turaṃgamān śaṅkha varṇān sarva śabda atigān raṇe tam āpatantam saṃprekṣya sātvatam rabhasam raṇe vimuñcan śara varṣāṇi parjanyaḥ iva vṛṣṭimān chādayām āsa śaineyam jaladaḥ bhāskaram yathā chādayām āsa bāṇa oghaiḥ samantāt bharata ṛṣabha somadattaḥ tu tam ṣaṣṭyā vivyādha urasi mādhavam sātyakiḥ ca api tam rājñ avidhyat sāyakaiḥ śitaiḥ sātyakiḥ prativivyādha somadattam śitaiḥ śaraiḥ tau anyonyam śaraiḥ kṛttau vyarājetām nara ṛṣabhau su puṣpau puṣpa samaye puṣpitau iva kiṃśukau rudhira ukṣita sarva aṅgau kuru vṛṣṇi yaśaskarau ghora rūpau hi tau āstām vṛṣṭimantau iva ambudau śara saṃbhinna gātrau tau sarvatas śakalīkṛtau śvāvidhau iva rāja indra vyadṛṣyetām śara kṣatau khadyotaiḥ āvṛtau rājan prāvṛṣi iva vanaspatī adṛśyetām raṇe kruddhau ulkābhiḥ iva kuñjarau atha enam pañcaviṃśatyā sāyakānām samārpayat tvaramāṇaḥ tvarā kāle punar ca daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ vāhlīkasya raṇe rājan sātyakiḥ prahasan iva somadattaḥ tu asambhrāntaḥ dṛṣṭvā ketum nipātitam śaineyam pañcaviṃśatyā sāyakānām samācinot atha enam rukma puṅkhānām śatena nata parvaṇām sātyakim chādayām āsa śara vṛṣṭyā mahā balaḥ sātyakim ca iṣu jālena somadattaḥ apīḍayat daśabhiḥ sātvatasya arthe bhīmaḥ ahan bāhlika ātmajam samīpam preṣayām āsa pretarājasya bhārata sāratheḥ ca śiraḥ kāyāt bhallena nata parvaṇā jahāra ratha śārdūlaḥ prahasan śini puṃgavaḥ tatas śaram mahā ghoram jvalantam iva pāvakam mumoca sātvataḥ rājan svarṇa puṅkham śilā śitam tam dṛṣṭvā nihatam tatra somadattam mahā rathāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ ca mahā rāja saha madraiḥ prabhadrakaiḥ mahatā śara varṣeṇa yuyudhānam upādravan chādyamānam śaraiḥ dṛṣṭvā yuyudhānam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ mahatyā senayā sārdham droṇa anīkam upādravat tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ kruddhaḥ tāvakānām mahā balam śaraiḥ vidrāvayām āsa bhāradvājasya paśyataḥ sainyāni drāvayantam tu droṇaḥ dṛṣṭvā yudhiṣṭhiram tatas su niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ pārtham vivyādha sapta saḥ atividdhaḥ mahā bāhuḥ parisaṃlihan tatas śara sahasreṇa droṇam vivyādha pārthivaḥ tatas muhūrtam vyathitaḥ śara ghāta prapīḍitaḥ pratilabh tatas saṃjñām muhūrta dvijasattama krodhena mahatā āviṣṭaḥ vāyavya astram avāsṛjat asambhrāntaḥ tatas pārthaḥ dhanuḥ ākṛṣya vīryavān ciccheda ca dhanuḥ dīrgham brāhmaṇasya ca pāṇḍavaḥ atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya droṇaḥ kṣatriya mardanaḥ tatas abravīt vāsudevaḥ kuntī putram yudhiṣṭhiram yudhiṣṭhira mahā bāho yat tvā vakṣyāmi tat śṛṇu yaḥ asya sṛṣṭaḥ vināśāya saḥ enam śvas haniṣyati rājā rājñā hi yoddhavyaḥ na a rājñā yuddham iṣyate yāvat mātreṇa ca mayā sahāyena dhanaṃjayaḥ vāsudeva vacaḥ śrutvā dharmarājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ muhūrtam cintayitvā tu tatas dāruṇam āhavam vinighnan tāvakān yodhān vyādita āsyaḥ iva antakaḥ bhīmasya nighnataḥ śatrūn pārṣṇim jagrāha pāṇḍavaḥ bhīma antikam upāyāte rājarāje yudhiṣṭhire nivṛtte kauravān hantum viṣṇu vākya praṇodite droṇaḥ api pāṇḍu pāñcālān vyadhamat rajanī mukhe nādayan tala ghoṣeṇa tava sainyāni māriṣa uvāca na apaśyanta raṇe yodhāḥ parasparam avasthitāḥ nara nāga aśva mathanam paramam loma harṣaṇam droṇa karṇa kṛpāḥ vīrāḥ bhīma pārṣata sātyakāḥ anyonyam kṣobhayām āsuḥ sainyāni nṛpa sattama ahanyanta mahā rāja dhāvamānāḥ ca saṃyuge tatas sarvāṇi sainyāni senā gopāḥ ca bhārata uvāca teṣām saṃloḍyamānānām pāṇḍavaiḥ nihata ojasām andhe tamasi magnānām āsīt kā vaḥ matiḥ tadā katham prakāśaḥ teṣām vā mama sainyeṣu vā punar babhūva loke tamasā tathā saṃjaya saṃvṛte uvāca tatas sarvāṇi sainyāni hata śiṣṭāni yāni vai droṇaḥ purastāt jaghane tu śalyaḥ tathā drauṇiḥ pārśvatas saubalaḥ ca svayam tu sarvāṇi balāni rājan rājā abhyayāt gopayan vai niśāyām uvāca sarvān ca padāti saṃghān duryodhanaḥ pārthiva sāntva pūrvam utsṛjya sarve parama āyudhāni gṛhṇīta hastaiḥ jvalitān pradīpān te coditāḥ pārthiva sattamena tatas prahṛṣṭāḥ jagṛhuḥ pradīpān vidyādharāḥ ca apsarasām gaṇāḥ ca nāgāḥ sa yakṣa uraga kinnarāḥ ca hṛṣṭāḥ divisthāḥ jagṛhuḥ pradīpān adṛśyanta dīpāḥ sa sugandhi tailāḥ viśeṣataḥ nārada parvatābhyām saṃbodhyamānāḥ kuru pāṇḍava artham sā bhūyas eva dhvajinī vibhaktā vyarocata agni prabhayā niśāyām mahādhanaiḥ ābharaṇaiḥ ca divyaiḥ śastraiḥ pradīptaiḥ abhisaṃpatadbhiḥ pratyaśvam ekaḥ ca mahā pradīpaḥ kṛtāḥ tu taiḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ kauraveyaiḥ kṣaṇena sarve vihitāḥ pradīpāḥ vyadīpayan ca dhvajinīm tadā āśu sarvāḥ tu senāḥ vyatisevyamānāḥ padātibhiḥ pāvaka taila hastaiḥ prakāśyamānāḥ dadṛśuḥ niśāyām yathā antarikṣe jaladāḥ taḍidbhiḥ prakāśitāyām tu tathā dhvajinyām droṇaḥ agni kalpaḥ pratapan samantāt rarāja rāja indra suvarṇa varmā madhyam gataḥ sūryaḥ iva aṃśumālī jāmbūnadeṣu ābharaṇeṣu ca eva niṣkeṣu śuddheṣu śarāvareṣu gadāḥ ca śaikyāḥ parighāḥ ca śubhrāḥ ratheṣu śaktyaḥ ca vivartamānāḥ pratiprabhāḥ raśmibhiḥ ājamīḍha punar punar saṃjanayanti dīptāḥ chatrāṇi bāla vyajana anuṣaṅgāḥ dīptāḥ mahā ulkāḥ ca tathā eva rājan vyāghūrṇamānāḥ ca suvarṇa mālā vyāyacchatām tatra tadā virejuḥ śastra prabhābhiḥ ca virājamānam dīpa prabhābhiḥ ca tadā balam tat prakāśitam ca ābharaṇa prabhābhiḥ bhṛśam prakāśam nṛpate babhūva pītāni śastrāṇi asṛj ukṣitāni vīra avadhūtāni tanu druhāṇi dīptām prabhām prājanayanta tatra tapātyaye vidyut iva antarikṣe vaktrāṇi aśobhanta tadā narāṇām vāyu īritāni iva mahā ambujāni tathā tava āsīt dhvajinī pradīptā mahā bhaye bhārata bhīma rūpā tat saṃpradīptam balam asmadīyam niśāmya pārthāḥ tvaritāḥ tathā eva sarveṣu sainyeṣu padāti saṃghān acodayan te atha cakruḥ pradīpān gaje gaje sapta kṛtāḥ pradīpāḥ rathe rathe ca eva daśa pradīpāḥ dvau aśva pṛṣṭhe paripārśvatas anye sarveṣu sainyeṣu padāti saṃghāḥ vyāmiśritāḥ hasti ratha aśva vṛndaiḥ vyadīpayan te dhvajinīm pradīptām tathā balam pāṇḍaveya abhiguptam bhās kurvatā bhānumatā graheṇa divākareṇa agniḥ iva abhitaptaḥ tayoḥ prabhāḥ pṛthivīm antarikṣam sarvāḥ vyatikramya diśaḥ ca vṛddhāḥ tena prakāśena bhṛśam prakāśam babhūva teṣām tava ca eva sainyam tena prakāśena divaṃgamena saṃbodhitāḥ deva gaṇāḥ ca rājan gandharva yakṣa asura siddha saṃghāḥ samāgaman apsarasaḥ ca sarvāḥ tat deva gandharva samākulam ca yakṣa asura indra apsarasām gaṇaiḥ ca ratha aśva nāga ākula dīpa dīptam saṃrabdha yodha āhata vidruta aśvam mahat balam vyūḍha ratha aśva nāgam sura asura vyūha samam babhūva tat śakti saṃgha ākula caṇḍa vātam mahā ratha abhram ratha vāji ghoṣam tasmin mahā agni pratimaḥ mahātmā saṃtāpayan pāṇḍavān vipra mukhyaḥ uvāca samājagmuḥ atho vīrāḥ paraspara vadha eṣiṇaḥ te sametya raṇe rājan śastra prāsa asi dhāriṇaḥ pradīpānām sahasraiḥ ca dīpyamānaiḥ samantataḥ ratna ācitaiḥ svarṇa daṇḍaiḥ gandha taila avasecitaiḥ dahyamānā iva lokānām abhāve vai vasuṃdharā prādīpyanta diśaḥ sarvāḥ pradīpaiḥ taiḥ samantataḥ varṣā pradoṣe khadyotaiḥ vṛtāḥ vṛkṣāḥ iva ābabhuḥ asajjanta tatas vīrāḥ vīreṣu eva pṛthak pṛthak nāgāḥ nāgaiḥ samājagmuḥ turagāḥ saha vājibhiḥ tatas arjunaḥ mahā rāja kauravāṇām anīkinīm uvāca amṛṣyamāṇe durdharṣe kim vaḥ āsīt manaḥ tadā droṇam ca ke vyarakṣanta praviṣṭe śvetavāhane ke arakṣan dakṣiṇam cakram ke ca droṇasya savyatas ke pṛṣṭhatas asya hi abhavan vīrāḥ vīrasya yudhyataḥ yat prāviśat mahā iṣvāsaḥ pāñcālān aparājitaḥ dadāha ca śaraiḥ droṇaḥ pāñcālānām ratha vrajān hṛṣṭān udīrṇān saṃgrāme na tu saṃjaya māmakān hatān ca eva viṣaṇṇān ca viprakīrṇān ca śaṃsasi rathinaḥ virathān ca eva kṛtān yuddheṣu māmakān uvāca droṇasya matam ājñāya yoddhu kāmasya tām niśām duryodhanaḥ mahā rāja vaśyān bhrātṝn abhāṣata vikarṇam citrasenam ca mahābāhum ca kauravam durdharṣam dīrghabāhum ca ye ca teṣām padānugāḥ droṇam yattāḥ parākrāntāḥ sarve rakṣata pṛṣṭhatas hārdikyaḥ dakṣiṇam cakram śalyaḥ ca eva uttaram tathā trigartānām ca ye śūrāḥ hata śiṣṭāḥ mahā rathāḥ ācāryaḥ hi su saṃyattaḥ bhṛśam yattāḥ ca pāṇḍavāḥ tam rakṣata su saṃyattāḥ nighnantam śātravān raṇe te yūyam sahitāḥ sarve bhṛśam yattāḥ mahā rathāḥ droṇam rakṣata pāñcālyāt dhṛṣṭadyumnāt mahā rathāt pāṇḍaveyeṣu sainyeṣu yodham paśyāmi aham na tam yaḥ jayeta raṇe droṇam dhṛṣṭadyumnāt ṛte nṛpāḥ sa guptaḥ somakān hanyāt sṛñjayān ca sa rājakān sṛñjayeṣu atha sarveṣu nihateṣu camū mukhe dhṛṣṭadyumnam raṇe drauṇiḥ nāśayiṣyati asaṃśayam tathā arjunam raṇe karṇaḥ vijeṣyati mahā rathaḥ bhīmasenam aham ca api yuddhe jeṣyāmi daṃśitaḥ śeṣān ca pāṇḍavān yodhāḥ prasabham hīna tejasaḥ tasmāt rakṣata saṃgrāme droṇam eva mahā rathāḥ vyādideśa tatas sainyam tasmin tamasi dāruṇe ubhayoḥ senayoḥ ghoram vijayam prati kāṅkṣiṇoḥ nānā śastra samāvāpaiḥ anyonyam paryapīḍayan drauṇiḥ pāñcāla rājānam bhāradvājaḥ ca sṛñjayān chādayām āsatuḥ saṃkhye śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ pāṇḍu pāñcāla senānām kauravāṇām ca māriṣa āsīt niṣṭānakaḥ ghoraḥ nighnatām itaretaram na eva asmābhiḥ na pūrvaiḥ naḥ dṛṣṭam pūrvam tathāvidham yuddham yādṛśam eva āsīt tām rātrim su mahā bhayam uvāca manuṣya nara nāgānām abhāvāya narādhipa yudhiṣṭhiraḥ abravīt rājā svān yodhān manuja adhipa abravīt pāṇḍavān ca eva pāñcālān ca sa somakān rājñaḥ te vacanāt rājan pāñcālāḥ somakāḥ tathā tān vayam pratigarjantaḥ pratyudyātāḥ tu amarṣitāḥ yathāśakti yathotsāham yathāsattvam ca saṃyuge dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā rāja droṇam eva anvapadyata śaineyam śara varṣāṇi vikirantam samantataḥ abhyayāt kauravaḥ rājan bhūriḥ saṃgrāma mūrdhani karṇaḥ vaikartanaḥ rājan vārayām āsa pāṇḍavam bhīmasenam atha āyāntam vyādita āsyam iva antakam nakulam ca yudhām śreṣṭham sarva yuddha viśāradam śakuniḥ saubalaḥ rājan vārayām āsa sa tvaraḥ śikhaṇḍinam atha āyāntam rathena rathinām varam kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ rājan vārayām āsa saṃyuge prativindhyam atha āyāntam mayūra sadṛśaiḥ hayaiḥ duḥśāsanaḥ mahā rāja yattaḥ yattam avārayat bhaimasenim atha āyāntam māyā śata viśāradam aśvatthāmā pituḥ mānam kurvāṇaḥ pratyaṣedhayat vārayām āsa samare droṇa prepsum mahā ratham virāṭam drutam āyāntam droṇasya nidhanam prati madra rājaḥ su saṃkruddhaḥ vārayām āsa bhārata śatānīkam atha āyāntam nākulim rabhasam raṇe arjunam ca yudhām śreṣṭham prādravantam mahā ratham tathā droṇam mahā iṣvāsam nighnantam śātravān raṇe dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ atha pāñcālyaḥ hṛṣṭa rūpam avārayat tathā anyān pāṇḍu putrāṇām samāyātān mahā rathān tāvakāḥ rathinaḥ rājan vārayām āsuḥ ojasā gaja ārohāḥ gajaiḥ tūrṇam saṃnipatya mahā mṛdhe yodhayantaḥ sma dṛśyante śataśas atha sahasraśas niśīthe turagāḥ rājan ādravantaḥ parasparam sādinaḥ sādibhiḥ sārdham prāsa śakti ṛṣṭi pāṇayaḥ gadābhiḥ musalaiḥ ca eva nānā śastraiḥ ca saṃghaśas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tu hārdikyam viddhvā pañcabhiḥ āśugaiḥ punar vivyādha viṃśatyā tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt hārdikyam daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ bāhuvoḥ urasi ca arpayat tasya pārthaḥ dhanuḥ chittvā hasta āvāpam nikṛtya ca prāhiṇot niśitān bāṇān pañca rājan śilā śitān prāviśan dharaṇīm ugrāḥ valmīkam iva pannagāḥ akṣṇoḥ nimeṣa mātreṇa saḥ anyat ādāya kārmukam vivyādha pāṇḍavam ṣaṣṭyā sūtam ca navabhiḥ śaraiḥ tasya śaktim ameya ātmā pāṇḍavaḥ bhujaga upamām sā hema citrā mahatī pāṇḍavena praveritā nirbhidya dakṣiṇam bāhum prāviśat dharaṇī talam hārdikyam chādayām āsa śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ tatas tu samare śūraḥ vṛṣṇīnām pravaraḥ rathī vyaśva sūta ratham cakre nimeṣa ardhāt yudhiṣṭhiram tatas tu pāṇḍavaḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ khaḍga carma samādade tomaram tu tatas gṛhya svarṇa daṇḍam durāsadam preṣayat samare tūrṇam hārdikyasya yudhiṣṭhiraḥ kavacam ca asya saṃkruddhaḥ śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ adārayat hārdikya śara saṃchinnam kavacam tat mahātmanaḥ vyaśīryata raṇe rājñ tārā jālam iva ambarāt sa chinna dhanvā virathaḥ śīrṇa varmā śara arditaḥ apāyāsīt raṇāt tūrṇam dharmaputraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ uvāca bhūriḥ tu samare rājan śaineyam rathinām varam atha enam sātyakiḥ kruddhaḥ pañcabhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ vivyādha hṛdaye tūrṇam prāsravat tasya śoṇitam tau anyonyam mahā rāja tatakṣāte śaraiḥ bhṛśam tayoḥ āsīt mahā rāja śastra vṛṣṭiḥ su dāruṇā kruddhayoḥ sāyaka mucoḥ yama antaka nikāśayoḥ atha enam chinna dhanvānam navabhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ vivyādha hṛdaye tūrṇam tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt saḥ atividdhaḥ balavatā śatruṇā śatru tāpanaḥ sa viddhvā sātvatam bāṇaiḥ tribhiḥ eva viśām pate chinna dhanvā mahā rāja sātyakiḥ krodha mūrchitaḥ prajahāra mahā vegām śaktim tasya mahā urasi lohitāṅgaḥ iva ākāśāt dīpta raśmiḥ yadṛcchayā tam tu dṛṣṭvā hatam śūram aśvatthāmā mahā rathaḥ tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca ābhāṣya śaineyam sa narādhipa abhyavarṣat śara ogheṇa merum vṛṣṭyā yathā ambudaḥ ghaṭotkacaḥ abravīt rājñ nādam muktvā mahā rathaḥ tiṣṭha tiṣṭha na me jīvan droṇaputra gamiṣyasi eṣa tvā adya haniṣyāmi mahiṣam skanda rāj iva yuddha śraddhām aham te adya vineṣyāmi raṇa ajire iti uktvā roṣa tāmra akṣaḥ rākṣasaḥ para vīra hā ratha akṣa mātraiḥ iṣubhiḥ abhyavarṣat ghaṭotkacaḥ rathinām ṛṣabham drauṇim dhārābhiḥ iva toyadaḥ śara vṛṣṭim tu tām prāptām śaraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ śātayām āsa samare tarasā drauṇiḥ utsmayan tatas śara śataiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ marma bhedibhiḥ āśugaiḥ sa śaraiḥ ācitaḥ tena rākṣasaḥ raṇa mūrdhani vyakāśata mahā rāja śvāvidh śalalitaḥ yathā tatas krodha samāviṣṭaḥ bhaimaseniḥ pratāpavān kṣurapraiḥ ardhacandraiḥ ca nārācaiḥ sa śilīmukhaiḥ varāhakarṇaiḥ nālīkaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ ca api vikarṇibhiḥ tām śastra vṛṣṭim atulām vajra aśani sama svanām vyadhamat sa mahā tejāḥ mahā abhrāṇi iva mārutaḥ tatas antarikṣe bāṇānām saṃgrāmaḥ anyaḥ iva abhavat ghora rūpaḥ mahā rāja yodhānām harṣa vardhanaḥ sa mārgaṇa gaṇaiḥ drauṇiḥ diśaḥ pracchādya sarvatas priya artham te putrāṇām rākṣasam samavākirat tatas pravavṛte yuddham drauṇi rākṣasayoḥ mṛdhe sa moham anusaṃprāptaḥ dhvaja yaṣṭim samāśritaḥ tatas hāhākṛtam sainyam te sarvam janādhipa hatam sma menire sarve tāvakāḥ tam viśām pate tam tu dṛṣṭvā tathā avastham aśvatthāmānam āhave pāñcālāḥ sṛñjayāḥ ca eva siṃhanādam pracakrire pratilabhya tatas saṃjñām aśvatthāmā mahā balaḥ dhanuḥ prapīḍya vāmena kareṇa amitra karśanaḥ mumoca ākarṇa pūrṇena dhanuṣā śaram uttamam yama daṇḍa upamam ghoram uddiśya āśu ghaṭotkacam sa bhittvā hṛdayam tasya rākṣasasya śara uttamaḥ viveśa vasudhām ugraḥ su puṅkhaḥ pṛthivīpate rākṣasa indraḥ su balavān drauṇinā raṇa māninā dṛṣṭvā vimūḍham haiḍimbam sārathiḥ tam raṇa ajirāt drauṇeḥ sakāśāt saṃbhrāntaḥ tu apaninye tvarā anvitaḥ nanāda su mahā nādam droṇaputraḥ mahā balaḥ vapuṣā pratijajvāla madhyāhne iva bhāskaraḥ tam bhīmasenaḥ navabhiḥ śaraiḥ vivyādha māriṣa duryodhanaḥ api viṃśatyā śarāṇām pratyavidhyata tau sāyakaiḥ avacchannau adṛśyetām raṇa ajire pañcabhiḥ bharata śreṣṭha tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt vivyādha kaurava śreṣṭham navatyā nata parvaṇām gṛhītvā cikṣepa sa śarān rājan paśyatām sarva dhanvinām kauravam pañcaviṃśatyā kṣudrakāṇām samārpayat atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ vivyādha nṛpatim tūrṇam sapta niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ dvitīyam ca tṛtīyam ca caturtham pañcamam tathā āttam āttam mahā rāja bhīmasya dhanuḥ ācchinat tava putraḥ mahā rāja jita kāśī mada utkaṭaḥ sa tadā chidyamāneṣu kārmukeṣu punar punar śaktim cikṣepa samare sarva pāraśavām śubhām mṛtyoḥ iva svasāram hi dīptām ketuśikhām iva aprāptām eva tām śaktim tridhā ciccheda kauravaḥ tatas bhīmaḥ mahā rāja gadām gurum mahā prabhām tatas sā sahasā vāhān tava putrasya saṃyuge āplutaḥ sahasā yānam nandakasya mahātmanaḥ tāvakāḥ sainikāḥ ca api menire nihatam nṛpam tad tu ninadam śru tras sarva yodhin bhīmasenasya nādam ca śrutvā rājan mahātmanaḥ tatas yudhiṣṭhiraḥ rājā hatam matvā suyodhanam pāñcālāḥ kekayāḥ matsyāḥ sṛñjayāḥ ca viśām pate uvāca sahadevam atha āyāntam droṇa prepsum viśām pate tam karṇaḥ prativivyādha śatena nata parvaṇām tatas anyat dhanuḥ ādāya mādrī putraḥ pratāpavān karṇam vivyādha viṃśatyā tat adbhutam iva abhavat tasya karṇaḥ hayān hatvā śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ tatas gurum mahā ghorām hema citrām mahā gadām tām āpatantīm sahasā sahadeva praveritām vyaṣṭambhayat śaraiḥ karṇaḥ bhūmau ca enām apātayat gadām vinihatām dṛṣṭvā sahadevaḥ tvarā anvitaḥ śaktim cikṣepa karṇāya tām api asya ācchinat śaraiḥ sahadevaḥ mahā rāja dṛṣṭvā karṇam vyavasthitam īṣā daṇḍaka yoktrān ca yugāni vividhāni ca hasti aṅgāni tathā aśvān ca mṛtān ca puruṣān bahūn sa nirāyudham ātmānam jñātvā mādravatī sutaḥ vāryamāṇaḥ ca viśikhaiḥ
