sahadevaḥ raṇam jahau abravīt prahasan vākyam sahadevam viśām pate mā yudhyasva raṇe vīra viśiṣṭaiḥ rathibhiḥ saha sadṛśaiḥ yudhya mādreya vacaḥ me mā viśaṅkithāḥ evam uktvā tu tam karṇaḥ rathena rathinām varaḥ prāyāt pāñcāla pāṇḍūnām sainyāni prahasan iva vadha prāptam tu mādreyam na avadhīt samare ari hā kuntyāḥ smṛtvā vacaḥ rājan satya saṃdhaḥ mahā rathaḥ sahadevaḥ tatas rājan vimanāḥ śara pīḍitaḥ karṇa vāc śalya taptaḥ ca jīvitāt niravidyata āruroha ratham ca api pāñcālyasya mahātmanaḥ virāṭam saha senam tu droṇa arthe drutam āgatam madra rājaḥ śara ogheṇa chādayām āsa dhanvinam yādṛśam hi abhavat rājan jambha vāsavayoḥ purā madra rājaḥ mahā rāja virāṭam vāhinīpatim ājaghne tvaritam tīkṣṇaiḥ śatena nata parvaṇām prativivyādha tam rājā navabhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ hata aśvāt tu rathāt tūrṇam avaplutya mahā rathaḥ tasthau visphārayan cāpam vimuñcan ca śitān śarān śatānīkaḥ tatas dṛṣṭvā bhrātaram hata vāhanam śatānīkam atha āyāntam madra rājaḥ mahā mṛdhe āruroha ratham tūrṇam tam eva dhvaja mālinam madra rāja ratham tūrṇam chādayām āsa pattribhiḥ ājaghāna urasi dṛḍham virāṭam vāhinīpatim kaśmalam ca āviśat tīvram virāṭaḥ bharata ṛṣabha tatas sā mahatī senā prādravat niśi bhārata vadhyamānā śara śataiḥ śalyena āhava śobhinā tām dṛṣṭvā vidrutām senām vāsudeva dhanaṃjayau prāyātām tatra rāja indra yatra śalyaḥ vyavasthitaḥ lohita ārdra patākam tam rakta mālya vibhūṣitam kārṣṇāyasa mayam ghoram ṛkṣa carma āvṛtam mahat raudreṇa citra pakṣeṇa vivṛta akṣeṇa kūjatā rurodha arjunam āyāntam prabhañjanam iva kiran bāṇa gaṇān rājan śataśas arjuna mūrdhani gṛdhra kāka bala ulūka kaṅka gomāyu harṣaṇam draṣṭṝṇām prīti jananam sarveṣām bharata ṛṣabha tatra āsīt su ciram kālam yuddham samam iva abhavat tatas pārthaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ divyam viṣphārayan dhanuḥ āpūrayan diśaḥ bāṇaiḥ jyā kṣepeṇa vinādayan tam arjunaḥ śatena eva pattriṇām abhyatāḍayat virathasya udyam khaḍgam śareṇa asya dvidhā ācchid tam vijitya arjunaḥ tūrṇam droṇa antikam upāyayau kiran śara gaṇān rājan nara vāraṇa vājiṣu vadhyamānāḥ mahā rāja pāṇḍavena yaśasvinā sainikāḥ nyapatan urvyām vāta nunnāḥ iva drumāḥ teṣu tu utsādyamāneṣu phalgunena mahātmanā saṃprādravat balam sarvam putrāṇām te viśām pate uvāca śatānīkam śaraiḥ tūrṇam nirdahantam camūm te nākuliḥ citrasenam tu nārācena ardayat bhṛśam sa ca tam prativivyādha daśabhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ citrasenaḥ mahā rāja śatānīkam punar yudhi gātrāt saṃcyāvayām āsa tat adbhutam iva abhavat saḥ apeta varmā putraḥ te virarāja bhṛśam nṛpa dhanuḥ anyat mahā rāja jagrāha ari vidāraṇam tatas tūrṇam citrasenaḥ nākulim navabhiḥ śaraiḥ śatānīkaḥ atha saṃkruddhaḥ citrasenasya māriṣa jaghāna caturaḥ vāhān sārathim ca nara uttamaḥ nākulim pañcaviṃśatyā śarāṇām ārdayat balī āruroha ratham tūrṇam hārdikyasya mahātmanaḥ drupadam tu saha anīkam droṇa prepsum mahā ratham vṛṣasenaḥ abhyayāt tūrṇam kiran śara śataiḥ tadā ṣaṣṭyā śarāṇām vivyādha bāhuvoḥ urasi ca anagha bahubhiḥ sāyakaiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ ājaghāna stanāntare tau ubhau śara nunna aṅgau śara kaṇṭakinaḥ raṇe vyabhrājetām mahā rāja śvāvidhau śalalaiḥ iva kiṃśukau iva ca utphullau vyakāśetām raṇa ajire viddhvā vivyādha saptatyā punar ca anyaiḥ tribhiḥ śaraiḥ vṛṣasena śaraiḥ nunnaḥ vyapayāsīt mahīpatiḥ tatas śara sahasrāṇi vimuñcan vibabhau tadā karṇa putraḥ mahā rāja varṣamāṇaḥ iva ambudaḥ saḥ anyat kārmukam ādāya rukma baddham navam dṛḍham tūṇāt ākṛṣya vimalam bhallam pītam śitam dṛḍham kārmuke yojayitvā tam drupadam saṃnirīkṣya ca ākarṇapūrṇam mumuce trāsayan sarva somakān kaśmalam prāviśat rājā vṛṣasena śara āhataḥ tasmin prabhagne rāja indra pāñcālānām mahā rathe vyarājata mahī rājan vīta abhrā dyauḥ iva grahaiḥ prāvṛṣ kāle mahā rāja vidyudbhiḥ iva toyadaḥ tena ardyamānāḥ samare dravamāṇāḥ ca somakāḥ vyarājanta mahā rāja pradīpaiḥ avabhāsitāḥ teṣu rāja sahasreṣu tāvakeṣu pareṣu ca ekaḥ eva jvalan tasthau vṛṣasenaḥ pratāpavān sa vijitya raṇe śūrān somakānām mahā rathān tayoḥ samāgamaḥ rājan citra rūpaḥ babhūva ha apūjayan mahā rāja te sainye mahā rathāḥ duḥśāsanaḥ tribhiḥ bāṇaiḥ lalāṭe samavidhyata virarāja mahā bāhuḥ sa śṛṅgaḥ iva parvataḥ patākāḥ ca sa tūṇīrān raśmīn yoktrāṇi ca abhibho ciccheda tilaśas kruddhaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ virathaḥ sa tu dharma ātmā dhanuṣpāṇiḥ avasthitaḥ ayodhayat tava sutam kiran śara śatān bahūn tam dṛṣṭvā viratham tatra bhrātaraḥ asya mahā rathāḥ abhyavartanta saṃgrāme mahatyā senayā vṛtāḥ tatas pravavṛte yuddham tava teṣām ca bhārata niśīthe dāruṇe kāle yama rāṣṭra vivardhanam uvāca abhyayāt saubalaḥ kruddhaḥ tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt kṛta vairau tu tau vīrau anyonya vadha kāṅkṣiṇau śaraiḥ pūrṇa āyata utsṛṣṭaiḥ anyonyam abhijaghnatuḥ yathā eva saubalaḥ kṣipram śara varṣāṇi muñcati tathā eva nakulaḥ rājan śikṣām saṃdarśayan yudhi tau ubhau samare śūrau śara kaṇṭakinau tadā vyarājetām mahā rāja kaṇṭakaiḥ iva śālmalī su jihmam prekṣamāṇau ca rājan vivṛta locanau niṣasāda rathopasthe kaśmalam ca enam āviśat atyanta vairiṇam dṛptam dṛṣṭvā śatrum tathāgatam nanāda śakuniḥ rājan tapānte jaladaḥ yathā pratilabhya tatas saṃjñām nakulaḥ pāṇḍu nandanaḥ abhyayāt saubalam bhūyas vyātta ānanaḥ iva antakaḥ saṃkruddhaḥ śakunim ṣaṣṭyā vivyādha bharata ṛṣabha punar ca eva śatena eva nārācānām stanāntare tatas asya sa śaram cāpam muṣṭideśe sa cicchide dhvajam ca tvaritam chittvā rathāt bhūmau apātayat viśikhena ca tīkṣṇena pītena niśitena ca ūrū nirbhidya ca ekena nakulaḥ pāṇḍu nandanaḥ śyenam sa pakṣam vyādhena pātayām āsa tam tadā dhvaja yaṣṭim pariṣvajya kāminīm kāmukaḥ yathā tam visaṃjñam nipatitam dṛṣṭvā syālam te anagha apovāha rathena āśu sārathiḥ dhvajinī mukhāt tatas saṃcukruśuḥ pārthāḥ ye ca teṣām padānugāḥ nirjitya ca raṇe śatrūn nakulaḥ śatru tāpanaḥ abravīt sārathim kruddhaḥ droṇa anīkāya mām vaha tasya tat vacanam śrutvā mādrī putrasya dhīmataḥ śikhaṇḍinam tu samare droṇa prepsum viśām pate gautamam drutam āyāntam droṇa antikam ariṃdamam tam ācāryaḥ mahā rāja viddhvā pañcabhiḥ āśugaiḥ punar vivyādha viṃśatyā putrāṇām priya kṛt tava mahat yuddham tayoḥ āsīt ghora rūpam viśām pate yathā devāsure yuddhe śambara amararājayoḥ śara jāla āvṛtam vyoma cakratuḥ tau mahā rathau prakṛtyāḥ ghora rūpam tat āsīt ghorataram punar rātriḥ ca bharata śreṣṭha yodhānām yuddha śālinām kālarātri nibhā hi āsīt ghora rūpā bhaya āvahā śikhaṇḍī tu mahā rāja gautamasya mahat dhanuḥ tasya kruddhaḥ kṛpaḥ rājan śaktim cikṣepa dāruṇām svarṇa daṇḍām akuṇṭha agrām karmāra parimārjitām tām āpatatīm ciccheda śikhaṇḍī bahubhiḥ śaraiḥ sā apatat medinīm dīptā bhāsayantī mahā prabhā atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya gautamaḥ rathinām varaḥ prācchādayat śitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ mahā rāja śikhaṇḍinam vyaṣīdata rathopasthe śikhaṇḍī rathinām varaḥ sīdantam ca enam ālokya kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ yudhi vimukham tam raṇe dṛṣṭvā yājñasenim mahā ratham pāñcālāḥ somakāḥ ca eva parivavruḥ samantataḥ rathānām ca raṇe rājan anyonyam abhidhāvatām babhūva tumulaḥ śabdaḥ meghānām nadatām iva dravatām sādinām ca eva gajānām ca viśām pate pattīnām dravatām ca eva pada śabdena medinī nyagṛhṇan bahavaḥ rājan śalabhān vāyasāḥ iva tathā gajān prabhinnān ca su prabhinnāḥ mahā gajāḥ sādī sādinam āsādya padātī ca padātinam samāsādya raṇe anyonyam saṃrabdhāḥ na aticakramuḥ dhāvatām dravatām ca eva punar āvartatām api babhūva tatra sainyānām śabdaḥ su tumulaḥ niśi dīpyamānāḥ pradīpāḥ ca ratha vāraṇa vājiṣu adṛśyanta mahā rāja mahā ulkāḥ iva khāt cyutāḥ sā niśā bharata śreṣṭha pradīpaiḥ avabhāsitā ādityena yathā vyāptam tamaḥ loke praṇaśyati tathā naṣṭam tamaḥ ghoram dīpaiḥ dīptaiḥ alaṃkṛtam divam ca pṛthivīm ca eva diśaḥ ca pradiśaḥ tathā rajasā tamasā vyāptāḥ dyotitāḥ prabhayā punar śastrāṇām kavacānām ca maṇīnām ca mahātmanām antardadhuḥ prabhāḥ sarvāḥ dīpaiḥ taiḥ avabhāsitāḥ putraḥ ca pitaram mohāt sakhāyam ca sakhā tathā saṃbandhinam ca saṃbandhī svasrīyam ca api mātulaḥ uvāca dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā rāja droṇam eva abhyavartata saṃmṛjānaḥ dhanuḥ śreṣṭham jyām vikarṣan punar punar dhṛṣṭadyumnam tadā āyāntam droṇasya anta cikīrṣayā parivavruḥ mahā rāja pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha tathā parivṛtam dṛṣṭvā droṇam ācārya sattamam bala arṇavau tatas tau tu sameyātām niśā mukhe tatas droṇam mahā rāja pāñcālyaḥ pañcabhiḥ śaraiḥ vivyādha hṛdaye tūrṇam siṃhanādam nanāda ca tam droṇaḥ pañcaviṃśatyā viddhvā bhārata saṃyuge tatas kruddhaḥ mahā rāja dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ pratāpavān ādade anyat dhanuḥ śreṣṭham droṇasya anta cikīrṣayā vikṛṣya ca dhanuḥ citram ākarṇāt para vīra hā droṇasya anta karam ghoram vyasṛjat sāyakam tatas sa visṛṣṭaḥ balavatā śaraḥ ghoraḥ mahā mṛdhe bhāsayām āsa tat sainyam divākaraḥ iva uditaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā tu śaram ghoram deva gandharva mānavāḥ karṇaḥ dvādaśadhā rājan ciccheda kṛtahasta vat sa chinnaḥ bahudhā rājan sūtaputreṇa māriṣa nipapāta śaraḥ tūrṇam nikṛttaḥ karṇa sāyakaiḥ chittvā tu samare bāṇam śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam raṇe karṇaḥ vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ śalyaḥ ca navabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ tribhiḥ duḥśāsanaḥ tathā duryodhanaḥ ca viṃśatyā śakuniḥ ca api pañcabhiḥ pāñcālyam tvaritāḥ avidhyan sarve eva mahā rathāḥ sa viddhaḥ sapta vīraiḥ droṇa trāṇa artham āhave droṇam drauṇim ca karṇam ca vivyādha te ca ātmajam te viddhvā dhanvinā tena dhṛṣṭadyumnam punar mṛdhe vivyadhuḥ pañcabhiḥ tūrṇam ekaikaḥ rathinām varaḥ tribhiḥ ca anyaiḥ śaraiḥ tūrṇam tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca bravīt svarṇa puṅkhaiḥ śilā dhautaiḥ prāṇānta karaṇaiḥ yudhi unmamātha śiraḥ kāyāt drumasenasya vīryavān tad śiraḥ nyapatat bhūmau saṃdaṣṭa oṣṭha puṭam raṇe mahā vāta samuddhūtam pakvam tāla phalam yathā dyumatsenam hatam dṛṣṭvā dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ pratāpavān tān ca viddhvā punar vīrān vīraḥ su niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ na tu tat mamṛṣe karṇaḥ dhanuṣaḥ chedanam tathā nikartanam iva ati ugraḥ lāṅgūlasya yathā hariḥ saḥ anyat dhanuḥ samādāya krodha rakta īkṣaṇaḥ śvasan dṛṣṭvā tu karṇam saṃrabdham te vīrāḥ ṣaṭ ratha ṛṣabhāḥ pāñcālya putram tvaritāḥ parivavruḥ jighāṃsayā ṣaṇṇām yodha pravīrāṇām tāvakānām puraskṛtam mṛtyoḥ āsyam anuprāptam dhṛṣṭadyumnam amaṃsmahi etasmin eva kāle tu dāśārhaḥ vikiran śarān dhṛṣṭadyumnam parākrāntam sātyakiḥ pratyapadyata tam āyāntam mahā iṣvāsam sātyakim yuddha durmadam tam sātyakiḥ mahā rāja vivyādha daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ paśyatām sarva vīrāṇām mā gāḥ tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt trāsayan tala ghoṣeṇa kṣatriyān kṣatriya ṛṣabhaḥ rājīva locanam karṇam sātyakiḥ pratyavidhyata kampayan iva ghoṣeṇa dhanuṣaḥ vasudhām balī vipāṭha karṇi nārācaiḥ vatsadantaiḥ kṣuraiḥ api karṇaḥ śara śataiḥ ca api śaineyam pratyavidhyata tathā eva yuyudhānaḥ api vṛṣṇīnām pravaraḥ rathaḥ tāvakāḥ ca mahā rāja karṇa putraḥ ca daṃśitaḥ sātyakim vivyadhuḥ tūrṇam samantāt niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ astraiḥ astrāṇi saṃvārya teṣām karṇasya ca abhibho tena bāṇena nirviddhaḥ vṛṣasenaḥ viśām pate tatas karṇaḥ hatam matvā vṛṣasenam mahā rathaḥ putra śoka abhisaṃtaptaḥ sātyakim pratyapīḍayat pīḍyamānaḥ tu karṇena yuyudhānaḥ mahā rathaḥ vivyādha bahubhiḥ karṇam tvaramāṇaḥ punar punar sa karṇam daśabhiḥ viddhvā vṛṣasenam ca sapta sa hasta āvāpa tayoḥ ciccheda sātvataḥ tau anye dhanuṣī sajye kṛtvā śatru bhayaṃkare yuyudhānam avidhyetām samantāt niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ atīva śuśruve rājan gāṇḍīvasya mahā svanaḥ śrutvā tu ratha nirghoṣam gāṇḍīvasya ca nisvanam eṣa sarvān śibīn hatvā mukhyaśas ca nara ṛṣabhān pauravān ca mahā iṣvāsān gāṇḍīva ninadaḥ mahān śrūyate ratha ghoṣaḥ ca vāsavasya iva nardataḥ eṣā vidīryate rājan bahudhā bhāratī camūḥ viprakīrṇāni anīkāni na avatiṣṭhanti karhi cit dravatām yodha mukhyānām gāṇḍīva preṣitaiḥ śaraiḥ viddhānām śataśas rājan śrūyate ninadaḥ mahān niśīthe rāja śārdūla stanayitnoḥ iva ambare hāhākāra ravān ca eva siṃhanādān ca puṣkalān śṛṇu śabdān bahuvidhān arjunasya ratham prati ayam madhye sthitaḥ asmākam sātyakiḥ sātvata adhamaḥ iha ced labhyate lakṣyam kṛtsnān jeṣyāmahe parān eṣa pāñcāla rājasya putraḥ droṇena saṃgataḥ sātyakim yadi hanyāmaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam ca pārṣatam prayatāmaḥ mahā rāja nihantum vṛṣṇi pārṣatau savyasācī puras abhyeti droṇa anīkāya bhārata saṃsaktam sātyakim jñātvā bahubhiḥ kuru puṃgavaiḥ yāvat pārthaḥ na jānāti sātyakim bahubhiḥ vṛtam te tvaradhvam yathā śūrāḥ śarāṇām mokṣaṇe bhṛśam yathā tūrṇam vrajati eṣa para lokāya mādhavaḥ tathā kuru mahā rāja su nītyā su prayuktayā yathā indraḥ samare rājan prāha viṣṇum yaśasvinam duḥśāsanaḥ durviṣahaḥ subāhuḥ duṣpradharṣaṇaḥ jahi kṛṣṇau mahā bāho dharmarājam ca mātula devānām iva devendre jaya āśā me tvayi sthitā priya artham tava putrāṇām didhakṣuḥ pāṇḍu nandanān tatas pravavṛte yuddham tāvakānām paraiḥ saha prayāte saubale rājan pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm abhyayāt tvaritam yuddhe kiran śara śatān bahūn tathā eva pāṇḍavāḥ sarve sātyakim paryavārayan bhāradvājaḥ tatas gatvā dhṛṣṭadyumna ratham prati dhṛṣṭadyumnena śūreṇa pāñcālaiḥ ca mahātmanaḥ uvāca amṛṣyamāṇāḥ saṃrabdhāḥ yuyudhāna ratham prati atha enam koṣṭhakīkṛtya sarvatas te mahā rathāḥ siṃhanādān tadā cakruḥ tarjayantaḥ sma sātyakim te abhyavarṣan śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ sātyakim satya vikramam tvaramāṇāḥ mahā vīryāḥ mādhavasya vadha eṣiṇaḥ tān dṛṣṭvā patataḥ tūrṇam śaineyaḥ para vīra hā pratyagṛhṇāt mahā bāhuḥ pramuñcan viśikhān bahūn nicakarta śirāṃsi ugraiḥ śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ hasti hastān haya grīvān bāhūn api ca sa āyudhān kṣurapraiḥ pātayām āsa tāvakānām sa mādhavaḥ babhūva dharaṇī pūrṇā nakṣatraiḥ dyauḥ iva prabho teṣām tu yuyudhānena yudhyatām yudhi bhārata babhūva tumulaḥ śabdaḥ pretānām iva krandatām tena śabdena mahatā pūritā āsīt vasuṃdharā rātriḥ samabhavat ca eva tīvra rūpā bhaya āvahā dīryamāṇam balam dṛṣṭvā yuyudhāna śara āhatam śrutvā ca vipulam nādam niśīthe loma harṣaṇam sutaḥ tava abravīt rājan sārathim rathinām varaḥ yatra eṣa śabdaḥ tatra aśvān codaya iti punar punar sūtaḥ saṃcodayām āsa yuyudhāna ratham prati tatas pūrṇa āyata utsṛṣṭaiḥ māṃsa śoṇita bhojanaiḥ śaineyam daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ pratyavidhyat amarṣitaḥ pāñcālānām ca sarveṣām bhāratānām ca dāruṇam sāyakānām aśītyā tu vivyādha urasi bhārata sārathim ca rathāt tūrṇam pātayām āsa pattriṇā hata aśve tu rathe tiṣṭhan putraḥ te viśām pate mumoca niśitān bāṇān śaineyasya ratham prati śarān pañcāśataḥ tān tu śaineyaḥ kṛtahasta vat atha apareṇa bhallena muṣṭideśe mahat dhanuḥ āruroha ratham tūrṇam bhāsvaram kṛtavarmaṇaḥ drāvayām āsa viśikhaiḥ niśā madhye viśām pate śakuniḥ ca arjunam rājan parivārya samantataḥ arjunam yodhayanti sma kṣatriyāḥ kāla coditāḥ tāni arjunaḥ sahasrāṇi ratha vāraṇa vājinām tatas tu samare śūraḥ śakuniḥ saubalaḥ tadā roṣa tāmra īkṣaṇaḥ kruddhaḥ viṃśatyā sāyakaiḥ bhṛśam saṃvārya tān bāṇa gaṇaiḥ yudhi rājan dhanaṃjayaḥ avadhīt tāvakān yodhān vajrapāṇiḥ iva asurān bhujaiḥ chinnaiḥ mahā rāja śarīraiḥ ca sahasraśas samāstīrṇā dharā tatra babhau puṣpaiḥ iva ācitā śirobhiḥ sa kirīṭaiḥ ca su nasaiḥ cāru kuṇḍalaiḥ saṃdaṣṭa oṣṭha puṭaiḥ krodhāt tathā eva uddhṛta locanaiḥ niṣka cūḍāmaṇi dharaiḥ kṣatriyāṇām priyaṃvadaiḥ sa viddhvā śakunim bhūyas pañcabhiḥ nata parvabhiḥ tam ulūkaḥ tathā viddhvā vāsudevam atāḍayat nanāda ca mahā nādam pūrayan vasudhā talam ulūkasya ratham tūrṇam āruroha viśām pate tau eka ratham ārūḍhau pitāputrau mahā rathau pārtham siṣicatuḥ bāṇaiḥ girim meghau iva utthitau tau tu viddhvā mahā rāja pāṇḍavaḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ vidrāvayan te camūm śataśas vyadhamat śaraiḥ vicchinnāni tathā rājan balāni āsan viśām pate tat balam bharata śreṣṭha vadhyamānam tathā niśi pradudrāva diśaḥ sarvāḥ vīkṣamāṇam bhaya arditam saṃbhrāntāḥ paryadhāvanta tasmin tamasi dāruṇe dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā rāja droṇam viddhvā tribhiḥ śaraiḥ ciccheda dhanuṣaḥ tūrṇam jyām śareṇa śitena ha tat nidhāya dhanuḥ nīḍe droṇaḥ kṣatriya mardanaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam tatas droṇaḥ viddhvā sapta āśugaiḥ sārathim pañcabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ rājñ vivyādha saṃyuge tam nivārya śaraiḥ tūrṇam dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā rathaḥ vyadhamat kauravām senām śataśas atha sahasraśas prāvartata nadī ghorā śoṇita ogha taraṃgiṇī yathā vaitaraṇī rājan yama rāṣṭra puram prati drāvayitvā tu tat sainyam dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ pratāpavān atha dadhmuḥ mahā śaṅkhān dhṛṣṭadyumna śikhaṇḍinau yamau ca yuyudhānaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ ca vṛkodaraḥ cakāra kadanam ghoram pāṇḍu sainyeṣu māriṣa jitvā ratha sahasrāṇi tāvakānām mahā rathāḥ siṃhanāda ravān cakruḥ pāṇḍavāḥ jita kāśinaḥ tathā droṇasya śūrasya drauṇeḥ ca eva viśām pate uvāca vidrutam sva balam dṛṣṭvā vadhyamānam mahātmabhiḥ krodhena mahatā āviṣṭaḥ putraḥ te viśām pate abhyetya sahasā karṇam droṇam ca jayatām varam amarṣa vaśam āpannaḥ vākya jñaḥ vākyam abravīt codayām āsa tau tūrṇam amarṣa vaśam īyatuḥ bhavadbhyām iha saṃgrāmaḥ kruddhābhyām saṃpravartitaḥ āhave nihatam dṛṣṭvā saindhavam savyasācinā nihanyamānām pāṇḍūnām balena mama vāhinīm bhūtvā tad vijaye śaktau aśaktau iva paśyataḥ āvām pāṇḍu sutān saṃkhye jeṣyāvaḥ iti mānadau tadā eva aham vacaḥ śrutvā bhavadbhyām anusaṃmatam kṛtavān pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdham vairam yodha vināśanam yadi na aham parityājyaḥ bhavadbhyām puruṣa ṛṣabhau bhavadbhyām pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdham tat ca sarvam nirarthakam prāvartayetām tau yuddham ghaṭṭitau iva pannagau tathā eva sahitāḥ pārthāḥ svena sainyena saṃvṛtāḥ atha droṇaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ daśabhiḥ śini puṃgavam karṇaḥ ca daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ putraḥ ca te sapta daśabhiḥ vṛṣasenaḥ ca saubalaḥ ca api sapta pāñcālān āgatān droṇaḥ preṣayat yama sādanam manaḥ kṛtvā abhyayāt āśu dhṛṣṭadyumna ratham prati dṛṣṭvā ca samare droṇam nighnantam pāṇḍavīm camūm vivyadhuḥ somakāḥ tūrṇam samantāt śara vṛṣṭibhiḥ tatas droṇaḥ aharat prāṇān kṣatriyāṇām viśām pate droṇena vadhyamānānām pāñcālānām viśām pate śuśruve tumulaḥ śabdaḥ krośatām itaretaram putrān anye pitṝn anye bhrātṝn anye ca mātulān bhāgineyān vayasyān ca tathā saṃbandhi bāndhavān pāṇḍavānām raṇe yodhāḥ para lokam tathā apare sā tathā pāṇḍavī senā vadhyamānā mahātmabhiḥ niśi saṃprādravat rājan utsṛjya ulkāḥ sahasraśas tamasā saṃvṛte loke na prājñāyata kim cana kauravāṇām prakāśena dṛśyante tu drutāḥ pare dravamāṇam tu tat sainyam droṇa karṇau mahā rathau jaghnatuḥ pṛṣṭhatas rājan kirantau sāyakān bahūn pāñcāleṣu prabhagneṣu dīryamāṇeṣu sarvaśas droṇa karṇau mahā iṣvāsau etau pārṣata sātyakī pāñcālān ca eva sahitau jaghnatuḥ sāyakaiḥ bhṛśam etayoḥ śara varṣeṇa prabhagnāḥ naḥ mahā rathāḥ vāryamāṇā api kaunteya pṛtanā na avatiṣṭhate tām tu vidravatīm dṛṣṭvā ūcatuḥ keśava arjunau mā vidravata vitrastāḥ bhayam tyajata pāṇḍavāḥ etau āvām sarva sainyaiḥ vyūḍhaiḥ samyak udāyudhaiḥ droṇam ca sūtaputram ca prayatāvaḥ prabādhitum etau hi balinaḥ śūrau kṛtāstrau jita kāśinau upekṣitau balam kruddhau nāśayetām niśām imām tayoḥ saṃvadatoḥ evam bhīma karmā mahā balaḥ eṣa bhīmaḥ abhiyāti ugraḥ punar āvartya vāhinīm vṛkodaram tathā āyāntam dṛṣṭvā tatra janārdanaḥ punar eva abravīt rājñ harṣayan iva pāṇḍavam eṣa bhīmaḥ raṇa ślāghī vṛtaḥ somaka pāṇḍavaiḥ etena sahitaḥ yudhya pāñcālaiḥ ca mahā rathaiḥ āśvāsana artham sarveṣām sainyānām pāṇḍu nandana tatas tau puruṣa vyāghrau ubhau mādhava pāṇḍavau droṇa karṇau samāsādya dhiṣṭhitau raṇa mūrdhani tatas droṇaḥ ca karṇaḥ ca parān mamṛdatuḥ yudhi yathā sāgarayoḥ rājan candra udaya vivṛddhayoḥ tatas utsṛjya pāṇibhyaḥ pradīpān tava vāhinī yuyudhe pāṇḍavaiḥ sārdham unmatta vat ahar kṣaye rajasā tamasā ca eva saṃvṛte bhṛśa dāruṇe kevalam nāma gotreṇa prāyudhyanta jaya eṣiṇaḥ aśrūyanta hi nāmāni śrāvyamāṇāni pārthivaiḥ niḥśabdam āsīt sahasā punar śabdaḥ mahān abhūt kruddhānām yudhyamānānām jayatām jīyatām api tathā saṃyudhyamānānām vigāḍhā abhūt mahā niśā pāṇḍavānām ca rāja indra kauravāṇām ca sarvaśas uvāca tatas karṇaḥ raṇe dṛṣṭvā pārṣatam para vīra hā prativivyādha tam tūrṇam dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ api māriṣa pañcabhiḥ sāyakaiḥ hṛṣṭaḥ tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt tau anyonyam śaraiḥ saṃkhye saṃchādya su mahā rathau punar pūrṇa āyata utsṛṣṭaiḥ vivyadhāte parasparam tatas pāñcāla mukhyasya dhṛṣṭadyumnasya saṃyuge sārathim caturaḥ ca aśvān karṇaḥ vivyādha sāyakaiḥ kārmuka pravaram ca asya praciccheda śitaiḥ śaraiḥ sārathim ca asya bhallena rathanīḍāt apātayat dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ tu virathaḥ hata aśvaḥ hata sārathiḥ avaplutya rathāt tūrṇam gadām ādāya vīryavān sa vidhyamānaḥ karṇena śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ gatvā karṇa samīpam tu jaghāna caturaḥ hayān punar āvṛtya vegena pārṣataḥ para vīra hā dhanaṃjaya ratham kṣipram āruhya rathinām varaḥ prayātu kāmaḥ karṇāya vāritaḥ dharmasūnunā karṇaḥ tu su mahā tejāḥ siṃhanāda vimiśritam dṛṣṭvā vinirjitam yuddhe pārṣatam te mahā rathāḥ amarṣa vaśam āpannāḥ pāñcālāḥ saha somakaiḥ suta putra vadha arthāya śastrāṇi ādāya sarvaśas prayayuḥ karṇam uddiśya mṛtyum kṛtvā nivartanam gṛhītvā parigham ghoram karṇasya aśvān apīpiṣat viddhaḥ ca bahubhiḥ tena śaraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ tatas yudhiṣṭhira anīkam padbhyām eva anvavartata karṇasya api rathe vāhān anyān sūtaḥ nyayojayat śaṅkha varṇān mahā vegān saindhavān sādhu vāhinaḥ labdha lakṣyaḥ tu rādheyaḥ pāñcālānām mahā rathān abhyapīḍayat āyastaḥ śaraiḥ meghaḥ iva acalān sā pīḍyamānā karṇena pāñcālānām mahā camūḥ saṃprādravat su saṃtrastā siṃhena iva arditā mṛgī rathebhyaḥ ca narāḥ tūrṇam adṛśyanta tatas tatas cakāra kadanam ghoram pāṇḍu sainyeṣu bhārata bāhū ciccheda vai karṇaḥ śiraḥ ca eva sa kuṇḍalam ūrū ciccheda ca anyasya gaja sthasya viśām pate vāji pṛṣṭha gatasya api bhūmiṣṭhasya ca māriṣa dhāvamānāḥ bahavaḥ ca mahā rathāḥ saṃchinnāni ātma gātrāṇi vāhanāni ca saṃyuge te vadhyamānāḥ samare pāñcālāḥ sṛñjayaiḥ saha tṛṇa praspandanāt ca api sūtaputram sma menire api svam samare yodham dhāvamānam vicetasaḥ tāni anīkāni bhagnāni dravamāṇāni bhārata abhyadravat drutam karṇaḥ pṛṣṭhatas vikiran śarān avekṣamāṇāḥ te anyonyam su saṃmūḍhāḥ vicetasaḥ na aśaknuvan avasthātum kālyamānāḥ mahātmanā karṇena abhyāhatāḥ rājan pāñcālāḥ parama iṣubhiḥ droṇena ca diśaḥ sarvāḥ vīkṣamāṇāḥ pradudruvuḥ apayāne matim kṛtvā phalgunam vākyam abravīt paśya karṇam mahā iṣvāsam dhanuṣpāṇim avasthitam niśīthe dāruṇe kāle tapantam iva bhāskaram karṇa sāyaka nunnānām krośatām eṣa nisvanaḥ aniśam śrūyate pārtha tvad bandhūnām anātha vat yathā visṛjataḥ ca asya saṃdadhānasya ca āśugān yat atra anantaram kāryam prāpta kālam prapaśyasi evam uktaḥ mahā bāhuḥ pārthaḥ kṛṣṇam atha abravīt bhītaḥ kuntī sutaḥ rājā rādheyasya ati vikramāt evam gam prāp kālam karṇa anīke punar punar bhavān vyavasyatām kṣipram dravate hi varūthinī droṇa sāyaka nunnānām bhagnānām madhusūdana karṇena trāsyamānānām avasthānam na vidyate paśyāmi ca tathā karṇam vicarantam abhīta vat dravamāṇān ratha udārān kirantam viśikhaiḥ śitaiḥ pratyakṣam vṛṣṇi śārdūla pāda sparśam iva uragaḥ sa bhavān atra yātu āśu yatra karṇaḥ mahā rathaḥ aham enam vadhiṣyāmi mām vā eṣa madhusūdana uvāca paśyāmi karṇam kaunteya devarājam iva āhave ṛte tvām puruṣa vyāghra rākṣasāt vā ghaṭotkacāt na tu tāvat aham manye prāpta kālam tava anagha samāgamam mahā bāho sūtaputreṇa saṃyuge dīpyamānā mahā ulkā iva tiṣṭhati asya hi vāsavī saṃyuge rakṣyate śaktiḥ eṣā hi sa hi bhīmena balinā jātaḥ sura parākramaḥ tasmin astrāṇi divyāni rākṣasāni āsurāṇi ca satatam ca anuraktaḥ vaḥ hita eṣī ca ghaṭotkacaḥ vijeṣyati raṇe karṇam iti mama na atra saṃśayaḥ uvāca evam uktvā mahā bāhuḥ pārtham puṣkara locanaḥ ājuhāva atha tat rakṣaḥ tat ca āsīt prādur agratas kavacī sa śarī khaḍgī sa dhanvā ca viśām pate abhivādya tatas kṛṣṇam pāṇḍavam ca dhanaṃjayam abravīt tam tadā hṛṣṭaḥ tu ayam asmi anuśādhi mām tatas tam megha saṃkāśam dīpta āsyam dīpta kuṇḍalam abhyabhāṣata haiḍimbam dāśārhaḥ prahasan iva ghaṭotkaca vijānīhi yat tvām vakṣyāmi putraka sa bhavān majjamānānām bandhūnām tvam plavaḥ yathā vividhāni tava astrāṇi santi māyā ca rākṣasī paśya karṇena haiḍimba pāṇḍavānām anīkinī kālyamānāḥ yathā gāvaḥ pālena raṇa mūrdhani eṣa karṇaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ matimān dṛḍha vikramaḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkeṣu nihanti kṣatriya ṛṣabhān kirantaḥ śara varṣāṇi mahānti dṛḍha dhanvinaḥ na śaknuvanti avasthātum pīḍyamānāḥ śara arciṣā niśīthe sūtaputreṇa śara varṣeṇa pīḍitāḥ ete dravanti pāñcālāḥ siṃhasya iva bhayāt mṛgāḥ mātulānām pitṝṇām ca tejasaḥ astra balasya ca katham naḥ tārayet duḥkhāt sa tvam tāraya bāndhavān tava hi astra balam bhīmam māyāḥ ca tava dustarāḥ pāṇḍavānām prabhagnānām karṇena śita sāyakaiḥ majjatām dhārtarāṣṭreṣu bhava pāram paraṃtapa rātrau hi rākṣasāḥ bhūyas bhavanti amita vikramāḥ balavantaḥ su durdharṣāḥ śūrāḥ vikrānta cāriṇaḥ jahi karṇam mahā iṣvāsam niśīthe māyayā raṇe pārthāḥ droṇam vadhiṣyanti dhṛṣṭadyumna purogamāḥ keśavasya vacaḥ śrutvā bībhatsuḥ api rākṣasam ghaṭotkaca bhavān ca eva dīrgha bāhuḥ ca sātyakiḥ matau me sarva sainyeṣu bhīmasenaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ sa bhavān yātu karṇena dvairatham yudhyatām niśi sātyakiḥ pṛṣṭhagopaḥ te bhaviṣyati mahā rathaḥ jahi karṇam raṇe śūram sātvatena sahāyavān tvayā niyuktaḥ gacchāmi karṇasya vadha kāṅkṣayā alam eva asmi karṇāya droṇāya alam ca sattama anyeṣām kṣatriyāṇām ca kṛtāstrāṇām mahātmanām adya dāsyāmi saṃgrāmam sūtaputrāya tam niśi yam janāḥ saṃpravakṣyanti yāvat bhūmiḥ dhariṣyati na ca atra śūrān mokṣyāmi na bhītān na kṛtāñjalīn sarvān eva vadhiṣyāmi rākṣasam dharmam āsthitaḥ uvāca evam uktvā mahā bāhuḥ haiḍimbaḥ para vīra hā garjatoḥ rāja śārdūla śakra prahrādayoḥ iva uvāca tasmin tathā vartamāne karṇa rākṣasayoḥ mṛdhe dṛṣṭvā ghaṭotkacam rājan sūtaputra ratham prati prayāntam tvararyā yuktam jighāṃsum karṇam āhave abravīt tava putraḥ tu duḥśāsanam idam vacaḥ etat rakṣaḥ raṇe tūrṇam dṛṣṭvā karṇasya vikramam abhiyāti drutam karṇam tat vāraya mahā ratham vṛtaḥ sainyena mahatā yāhi yatra mahā balaḥ rakṣa karṇam raṇe yattaḥ vṛtaḥ sainyena mānada mā karṇam rākṣasaḥ ghoraḥ pramādāt nāśayiṣyati pāṇḍavān hantum icchāmi tvayā ājñaptaḥ saha anugān jaṭāsuraḥ mama pitā rakṣasām agraṇī purā śatru māṃsaiḥ ca rāja indra mām anujñātum arhasi hatvā saṃbhakṣayiṣyāmi sutān anucaraiḥ saha tam abravīt tatas rājā prīyamāṇaḥ punar punar droṇa karṇa ādibhiḥ sārdham paryāptaḥ aham dviṣat vadhe rākṣasam krūra karmāṇam rakṣaḥ mānuṣa sambhavam pāṇḍavānām hitam nityam hasti aśva ratha ghātinam tathā iti vaktvā mahā kāyaḥ samāhūya ghaṭotkacam evam tava suta ādiṣṭaḥ tathā iti uktvā mahā balaḥ jaṭāsuriḥ bhaimasenim nānā śastraiḥ avākirat haiḍimbaḥ pramamātha ekaḥ mahā vātaḥ ambudān iva tatas māyā mayam dṛṣṭvā ratham tūrṇam alaṃbalaḥ ghaṭotkacam śara vrātaiḥ nānā liṅgaiḥ samārdayat vyadrāvayat śara vrātaiḥ pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm tena vidrāvyamāṇāni pāṇḍu sainyāni māriṣa niśīthe viprakīryanta vāta nunnāḥ ghanāḥ iva niśīthe prādravat rājan utsṛjya ulkāḥ sahasraśas tilaśas tasya tat yānam sūtam sarva āyudhāni ca ghaṭotkacaḥ praciccheda prāṇadat ca ati dāruṇam tatas karṇam śara vrātaiḥ kurūn anyān sahasraśas tatas saṃcukṣubhe sainyam kurūṇām rākṣasa arday jaṭāsuriḥ mahā rāja virathaḥ hata sārathiḥ ghaṭotkacam raṇe kruddhaḥ muṣṭinā abhyahanat dṛḍham muṣṭinā abhihataḥ tena pracacāla ghaṭotkacaḥ kṣiti kampe yathā śailaḥ sa vṛkṣa gaṇa gulmavān jaṭāsurim bhaimaseniḥ avadhīt muṣṭinā bhṛśam tam pramathya tatas kruddhaḥ tūrṇam haiḍimbiḥ ākṣipat dorbhyām indra dhvaja ābhābhyām niṣpipeṣa mahī tale jaṭāsuriḥ mokṣayitvā ātmānam ca ghaṭotkacāt ghaṭotkacam raṇe roṣāt niṣpipeṣa mahī tale ājaghāna urasi tadā ghaṭotkaca alaṃbalayoḥ tumulam loma harṣaṇam viśeṣayantau anyonyam māyābhiḥ ati māyinau pāvaka ambunidhī bhūtvā punar garuḍa takṣakau punar kuñjara śārdūlau punar svarbhānu bhāskarau evam māyā śata sṛjau anyonya vadha kāṅkṣiṇaḥ parighaiḥ ca gadābhiḥ ca prāsa mudgara paṭṭiśaiḥ hayābhyām ca gajābhyām ca padāti rathinau punar utpapāta bhṛśam kruddhaḥ śyena vat nipapāta ha gṛhītvā ca mahā kāyam rākṣasa indram alaṃbalam maṇḍala agram pragṛhya tu pātitam bhū tale trastam nādam muktvā muhur muhur keśeṣu tam nijagrāha cakarta kāyāt hi śiraḥ bhīmam vikṛta darśanam piṅga akṣam vikṛtaiḥ dantaiḥ dīptayā jihvayā śubham tad śiraḥ rudhira abhyaktam gṛhya keśeṣu rākṣasaḥ śiraḥ tat ca api saṃgṛhya keśeṣu rudhira ukṣitam yayau ghaṭotkacaḥ tūrṇam droṇa karṇa kṛpān yodhān atītya su mahā balaḥ abhyetya ca mahā bāhuḥ smayamānaḥ sa rākṣasaḥ prāṇadat bhairavam nādam prāvṛṣi iva balāhakaḥ eṣa te nihataḥ bandhuḥ tvayā dṛṣṭaḥ asya vikramaḥ punar draṣṭāsi karṇasya niṣṭhām etām tathā ātmanaḥ karṇasya tu śiraḥ gṛhya punar dṛṣṭvā suyodhanaḥ rikta pāṇiḥ na paśyeta rājānam brāhmaṇam striyam su prītaḥ tāvat tiṣṭhasva yāvat karṇam vadhāmi aham evam uktvā tatas prāyāt karṇam prati janeśvara kiran śara śatān tīkṣṇān vimuñcan karṇa mūrdhani vismāpanam mahā rāja nara rākṣasayoḥ mṛdhe uvāca yatra vaikartanaḥ karṇaḥ rākṣasaḥ ca ghaṭotkacaḥ kīdṛśa ca abhavat yuddham tasya ghora rakṣas rathaḥ ca kīdṛśaḥ tasya māyāḥ sarva āyudhāni ca kīdṛśam varma ca eva asya kaṇṭha trāṇam ca kīdṛśam pṛṣṭaḥ tvam etat ācakṣva kuśalaḥ hi asi saṃjaya uvāca lohita akṣaḥ mahā kāyaḥ tāmra āsyaḥ nimnita udaraḥ ūrdhva romā hari śmaśruḥ śaṅku karṇaḥ mahā hanuḥ ākarṇāt dārita āsyaḥ ca tīkṣṇa daṃṣṭraḥ karālavān su dīrgha tāmra jihvā uṣṭhaḥ lamba bhrūḥ sthūla nāsikaḥ nīla aṅgaḥ lohita grīvaḥ giri varṣmā bhayaṃkaraḥ mahā kāyaḥ mahā bāhuḥ mahā śīrṣaḥ mahā balaḥ vikacaḥ paruṣa sparśaḥ vikaṭa udbaddha piṇḍikaḥ sthūla sphic gūḍha nābhiḥ ca śithila upacayaḥ mahān tathā eva hasta ābharaṇī mahā māyaḥ aṅgadī tathā urasā dhārayan niṣkam agni mālām yathā acalaḥ tasya hema mayam citram bahu rūpa aṅga śobhitam toraṇa pratimam śubhram kirīṭam mūrdhni aśobhata kuṇḍale bāla sūrya ābhe mālām hema mayīm śubhām dhārayan vipulam kāṃsyam kavacam ca mahā prabham tārā jāla nibham rājan pūrṇa candra sama prabham kaṇṭha sūtram mahat ca api tapanīyam adhārayat kiṅkiṇī śata nirghoṣam rakta dhvaja patākinam ṛkṣa carma avanaddha aṅgam nalva mātram mahā ratham tatra mātaṅga saṃkāśāḥ lohita akṣāḥ vibhīṣaṇāḥ kāma varṇa javāḥ yuktāḥ balavantaḥ avahan hayāḥ vahantaḥ rākṣasam raudram balavantaḥ jita śramāḥ vipulābhiḥ saṭābhiḥ te heṣamāṇāḥ muhur muhur rākṣasaḥ asya virūpākṣaḥ sūtaḥ dīpta āsya kuṇḍalaḥ ghora rūpaḥ mahā kāyaḥ karāḷaḥ vikṛta ānanaḥ raśmibhiḥ sūrya raśmi ābhaiḥ saṃjagrāha hayān raṇe saṃsaktaḥ iva ca abhreṇa yathā adriḥ mahatā mahān rakta uttamāṅgaḥ kravya ādaḥ gṛdhraḥ parama bhīṣaṇaḥ vāsava aśani nirghoṣam dṛḍha jyam abhivikṣipan vyaktam kiṣku parīṇāham dvādaśa aratni kārmukam ratha akṣa mātraiḥ iṣubhiḥ sarvāḥ pracchādayan diśaḥ tasyām vīra apahāriṇyām niśāyām karṇam abhyayāt tasya vikṣipataḥ cāpam rathe viṣṭabhya tiṣṭhataḥ aśrūyata dhanuḥ ghoṣaḥ visphūrjitam iva aśaneḥ tam āpatantam saṃprekṣya virūpākṣam vibhīṣaṇam mātaṅgaḥ iva mātaṅgam yūtha ṛṣabhaḥ iva ṛṣabham sa saṃnipātaḥ tumulaḥ tayoḥ āsīt viśām pate prācchādayetām anyonyam takṣamāṇau mahā iṣubhiḥ tatas pūrṇa āyata utsṛṣṭaiḥ śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ nyavārayetām anyonyam kāṃsye nirbhidya varmaṇī saṃchindantau hi gātrāṇi saṃdadhānau ca sāyakān dhakṣyamāṇau śara vrātaiḥ na udīkṣitum aśaknutām na akampayetām anyonyam yatamānau mahā dyutī tat pravṛttam niśā yuddham ciram samam iva abhavat prāṇayoḥ dīvyataḥ rājan karṇa rākṣasayoḥ mṛdhe tasya saṃdadhataḥ tīkṣṇān śarān ca asaktam asyataḥ ghaṭotkacam yadā karṇaḥ viśeṣayati naḥ nṛpa karṇena vihitam dṛṣṭvā divyam astram ghaṭotkacaḥ prāduścakre mahā māyām rākṣasaḥ pāṇḍu nandanaḥ śūla mudgara dhāriṇyā śaila pādapa hastayā rakṣasām ghora rūpāṇām mahatyā senayā vṛtaḥ tam udyata mahā cāpam dṛṣṭvā te vyathitāḥ nṛpāḥ bhūtāntakam iva āyāntam kāla daṇḍa ugra dhāriṇam ghaṭotkaca pramuktena siṃhanādena bhīṣitāḥ prasusruvuḥ gajāḥ mūtram vivyathuḥ ca narāḥ bhṛśam tatas aśma vṛṣṭiḥ ati ugrā mahatī āsīt samantataḥ āyasāni ca cakrāṇi bhuśuṇḍyaḥ śakti tomarāḥ patanti aviralāḥ śūlāḥ śataghnyaḥ paṭṭiśāḥ tathā tat ugram ati raudram ca dṛṣṭvā yuddham narādhipāḥ māyāyām tu prahīṇāyām amarṣāt sa ghaṭotkacaḥ visasarja śarān ghorān sūtaputram te āviśan viviśuḥ dharaṇīm bāṇāḥ saṃkruddhāḥ iva pannagāḥ cakram divyam sahasra aram agṛhṇāt vyathitaḥ bhṛśam kṣura antam bāla sūrya ābham maṇi ratna vibhūṣitam ghaṭotkacaḥ tu saṃkruddhaḥ dṛṣṭvā cakram nipātitam karṇam prācchādayat bāṇaiḥ svarbhānuḥ iva bhāskaram ghaṭotkaca ratham tūrṇam chādayām āsa pattribhiḥ ghaṭotkacena kruddhena gadā hema aṅgadā tadā kṣiptā bhrāmya śaraiḥ sā api tatas māyāvinam karṇaḥ bhīmasena sutam divi mārgaṇaiḥ abhivivyādha ghanam sūryaḥ iva aṃśubhiḥ abhyavarṣat śaraiḥ karṇaḥ parjanyaḥ iva vṛṣṭimān saḥ adṛśyata muhūrtena śvāvidh śalalitaḥ yathā dṛṣṭavantaḥ sma samare śara oghaiḥ abhisaṃvṛtam māyā yuddhena māyāvī sūtaputram ayodhayat saḥ ayodhayat tadā karṇam māyayā lāghavena ca alakṣyamāṇaḥ atha divi śara jāleṣu saṃpatan pracakāra mahā māyām mohayan iva bhārata sa sma kṛtvā virūpāṇi vadanāni aśubha ānanaḥ agrasat sūtaputrasya divyāni astrāṇi māyayā punar ca api mahā kāyaḥ saṃchinnaḥ śatadhā raṇe hatam tam manyamānāḥ sma prāṇadan kuru puṃgavāḥ punar ca api mahā kāyaḥ śata śīrṣaḥ śata udaraḥ vyadṛśyata mahā bāhuḥ mainākaḥ iva parvataḥ aṅguṣṭha mātraḥ bhūtvā ca punar eva sa rākṣasaḥ kṣitim divam ca diśaḥ ca eva māyayā āvṛtya daṃśitaḥ gatvā karṇa ratha abhyāśam vicalat kuṇḍala ānanaḥ prāha vākyam asambhrāntaḥ sūtaputram viśām pate tiṣṭha idānīm na me jīvan sūtaputra gamiṣyasi yuddha śraddhām aham te adya vineṣyāmi raṇa ajire iti uktvā roṣa tāmra akṣam rakṣaḥ krūra parākramam ratha akṣa mātraiḥ iṣubhiḥ abhyavarṣat ghaṭotkacaḥ rathinām ṛṣabham karṇam dhārābhiḥ iva toyadaḥ śara vṛṣṭim ca tām karṇaḥ dūra prāptām aśātayat dṛṣṭvā ca vihatām māyām karṇena bharata ṛṣabha ghaṭotkacaḥ tatas māyām sasarja antarhitaḥ punar śūla prāsa asi musala jala prasravaṇaḥ mahān tam añjana caya prakhyam karṇaḥ dṛṣṭvā mahīdharam prapātaiḥ āyudhāni ugrāṇi udvahantam na cukṣubhe tatas sa toyadaḥ bhūtvā nīlaḥ sa indrāyudhaḥ divi aśma vṛṣṭibhiḥ ati ugraḥ sūtaputram avākirat vyadhamat kāla megham tam karṇaḥ vaikartanaḥ vṛṣā sa mārgaṇa gaṇaiḥ karṇaḥ diśaḥ pracchādya sarvaśas jaghāna astram mahā rāja ghaṭotkaca samīritam prāduścakre mahā māyām karṇam prati mahā ratham sa dṛṣṭvā punar āyāntam rathena rathinām varam ghaṭotkacam asambhrāntam rākṣasaiḥ bahubhiḥ vṛtam siṃha śārdūla sadṛśaiḥ matta dvirada vikramaiḥ nānā śastra dharaiḥ ghoraiḥ nānā kavaca bhūṣaṇaiḥ dṛṣṭvā karṇaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ yodhayām āsa rākṣasam ghaṭotkacaḥ tatas karṇam viddhvā pañcabhiḥ āśugaiḥ nanāda bhairavam nādam bhīṣayan sarva pārthivān bhūyas ca añjalikena atha sa mārgaṇa gaṇam mahat karṇa hasta sthitam cāpam ciccheda āśu ghaṭotkacaḥ atha anyat dhanuḥ ādāya dṛḍham bhāra saham mahat tatas karṇaḥ mahā rāja preṣayām āsa sāyakān suvarṇa puṅkhān śatru ghnān kha carān rākṣasān prati tat bāṇaiḥ arditam yūtham rakṣasām pīna vakṣasām siṃhena iva arditam vanyam gajānām ākulam kulam tat tu dṛṣṭvā mahat karma rādheyasya mahātmanaḥ vidhamya rākṣasān bāṇaiḥ sa aśva sūta gajān vibhuḥ dadāha bhagavān vahniḥ bhūtāni iva yuga kṣaye tatas karṇaḥ mahā rāja rākṣasān vyadhamat śaraiḥ sa sma kṛtvā virūpāṇi vyāttāni vadanāni ca rādheyasya ācchinat bāṇaiḥ astrāṇi vividhāni ca chādayām āsa ca śaraiḥ dhārābhiḥ iva parvatam sa hatvā rākṣasīm senām śuśubhe sūtanandanaḥ teṣu rāja sahasreṣu pāṇḍaveyeṣu māriṣa ṛte ghaṭotkacāt rājñ rākṣasa indrāt mahā balāt mahā ulkābhyām yathā rājan sa arciṣaḥ sneha bindavaḥ ratham āsthāya ca punar māyayā nirmitam punar yuktam gaja nibhaiḥ vāhaiḥ piśāca vadanaiḥ kharaiḥ sa sūtam abravīt kruddhaḥ sūtaputrāya mā vaha dvairatham sūtaputreṇa punar eva viśām pate sa cikṣepa punar krudh sūtaputrāya rākṣasaḥ aṣṭa cakrām mahā ghorām aśanim rudra nirmitām āyasīm nicitām śūlaiḥ kadambam iva kesaraiḥ sa aśva sūta dhvajam yānam bhasma kṛtvā mahā prabhā karṇam tu sarva bhūtāni pūjayām āsuḥ añjasā yat avaplutya jagrāha deva sṛṣṭām mahā aśanim evam kṛtvā raṇe karṇaḥ āruroha ratham punar tatas mumoca nārācān sūtaputraḥ paraṃtapaḥ yat akārṣīt tadā karṇaḥ saṃgrāme bhīma darśane sa hanyamānaḥ nārācaiḥ dhārābhiḥ iva parvataḥ evam sa vai mahāmāyaḥ māyayā lāghavena ca astrāṇi tāni divyāni jaghāna ripu sūdanaḥ nihanyamāneṣu astreṣu māyayā tena rakṣasā cakāra bahudhā ātmānam bhīṣayāṇaḥ narādhipān tatas digbhyaḥ samāpetuḥ siṃha vyāghra tarakṣavaḥ agni jihvāḥ ca bhujagāḥ vihagāḥ ca api ayas mukhāḥ sa kṛ niśā karṇa cāpa cyu śaraiḥ rākṣasāḥ ca piśācāḥ ca yātudhānāḥ śalāvṛkāḥ śālāvṛkāḥ ca bahavaḥ vṛkāḥ ca vikṛta ānanāḥ te karṇam bhakṣayiṣyantaḥ sarvatas samupādravan atha enam vāgbhiḥ ugrābhiḥ trāsayām cakrire tadā teṣām anekaiḥ ekaikam karṇaḥ vivyādha ca āśugaiḥ pratihatya tu tām māyām divyena astreṇa rākṣasīm ājaghāna hayān asya śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ te bhagnāḥ vikṛta aṅgāḥ ca chinna pṛṣṭhāḥ ca sāyakaiḥ sa bhagna māyaḥ haiḍimbaḥ karṇam vaikartanam tatas uvāca tasmin tathā vartamāne karṇa rākṣasayoḥ mṛdhe rākṣasānām virūpāṇām sahasraiḥ parivāritaḥ tasya jñātiḥ hi vikrāntaḥ brāhmaṇa ādaḥ bakaḥ hataḥ kirmīraḥ ca mahā tejāḥ hiḍimbaḥ ca sakhiḥ tathā vijñāya etat niśā yuddham jighāṃsuḥ bhīmam āhave viditam te mahā rāja yathā bhīmena rākṣasāḥ hiḍimba baka kirmīrāḥ nihatāḥ mama bāndhavāḥ parāmarśaḥ ca kanyāyāḥ hiḍimbāyāḥ kṛtaḥ purā kim anyat rākṣasān anyān asmān ca paribhūya ha tam aham sa gaṇam rājan sa vāji ratha kuñjaram haiḍimbam ca saha amātyam hantum abhyāgataḥ svayam nivāraya balam sarvam mad yotsyāma pāṇḍavān tat aham sa gaṇān rājan saṃyotsyāmi ca pāṇḍavān tasya tat vacanam śrutvā hṛṣṭaḥ duryodhanaḥ tadā pratipūjya abravīt vākyam bhrātṛbhiḥ parivāritaḥ tvām puraskṛtya sa gaṇam vayam yotsyāmahe parān evam astu iti rājānam uktvā rākṣasa puṃgavaḥ abhyayāt tvaritaḥ bhīmam sahitaḥ puruṣa aśanaiḥ dīpyamānena vapuṣā rathena āditya varcasā tādṛśeṇa eva rāja indra yādṛśeṇa ghaṭotkacaḥ ṛkṣa carma avanaddha aṅgaḥ nalva mātraḥ mahā rathaḥ tasya api turagāḥ śīghrāḥ hasti kāyāḥ khara svanāḥ śatam yuktāḥ mahā kāyāḥ māṃsa śoṇita bhojanāḥ tasya api akṣa samāḥ bāṇāḥ rukma puṅkhāḥ śilā śitāḥ sa ca api rūpeṇa ghaṭotkacasya śrīmattamaḥ vyākula dīpita āsyaḥ dīpta aṅgadaḥ dīpta kirīṭa mālī gadī bhuśuṇḍī musalī halī ca rathena tena anala varcasā ca vidrāvayan pāṇḍava vāhinīm tām te ca api sarve pravarāḥ narendrāḥ mahā balāḥ varmiṇaḥ carmiṇaḥ ca harṣa anvitāḥ yuyudhuḥ tatra rājan samantataḥ pāṇḍava yodha vīrāḥ uvāca tam āgatam abhiprekṣya bhīma karmāṇam āhave harṣam āhārayām cakruḥ kuravaḥ sarve eva te aplavāḥ plavam āsādya tartu kāmāḥ iva arṇavam punar jātam iva ātmānam manvānāḥ pārthivāḥ tadā alāyudham rākṣasa indram svāgatena abhyapūjayan karṇa rākṣasayoḥ naktam dāruṇa pratidarśane na drauṇiḥ na kṛpaḥ droṇaḥ na śalyaḥ na ca mādhavaḥ ekaḥ eva tu tena āsīt yoddhā karṇaḥ raṇe vṛṣā upapraikṣanta pāñcālāḥ smayamānāḥ sa rājakāḥ tathā eva tāvakāḥ rājan ghūrṇamānāḥ tatas tatas cukruśuḥ na idam asti iti droṇa drauṇi kṛpa ādayaḥ tat karma dṛṣṭvā saṃbhrāntāḥ haiḍimbasya raṇa ajire tava sainyam mahā rāja nirāśam karṇa jīvite duryodhanaḥ tu saṃprekṣya karṇam ārtim parām gatam alāyudham rākṣasa indram āhūya idam atha abravīt eṣa vaikartanaḥ karṇaḥ haiḍimbena samāgataḥ paśya etān pārthivān śūrān nihatān bhaimaseninā nānā śastraiḥ abhihatān pādapān iva dantinā tava eṣa bhāgaḥ samare rāja madhye mayā kṛtaḥ purā vaikartanam karṇam eṣa pāpaḥ ghaṭotkacaḥ māyā balam upāśritya karśayati ari karśanaḥ evam uktaḥ sa rājñā tu rākṣasaḥ tīvra vikramaḥ pratyamitram upāyāntam mardayām āsa mārgaṇaiḥ tam āyāntam an ādṛtya dṛṣṭvā grastam ghaṭotkacam rathena āditya vapuṣā bhīmaḥ praharatām varaḥ tam bhīmaḥ sahasā abhyetya rākṣasa anta karaḥ prabho sa gaṇam rākṣasa indram tam śara varṣaiḥ avākirat tathā eva alāyudhaḥ rājan śilā dhautaiḥ ajihmagaiḥ tathā te rākṣasāḥ sarve bhīmasenam upādravan nānā praharaṇāḥ bhīmāḥ tvad sutānām jaya eṣiṇaḥ sa tāḍyamānaḥ balibhiḥ bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ pañcabhiḥ pañcabhiḥ sarvān tān avidhyat śitaiḥ śaraiḥ te vadhyamānāḥ bhīmena rākṣasāḥ khara yonayaḥ vineduḥ tumulān nādān dudruvuḥ ca diśaḥ daśa tān trāsyamānān bhīmena dṛṣṭvā rakṣaḥ mahā balam tam bhīmasenaḥ samare tīkṣṇa agraiḥ akṣiṇot śaraiḥ alāyudhaḥ tu tān astān bhīmena viśikhān raṇe ciccheda kān cit samare tvarayā kān cit agrahīt sa tam dṛṣṭvā rākṣasa indram bhīmaḥ bhīma parākramaḥ gadām cikṣepa vegena vajra pāta upamām tadā tām āpatantīm vegena gadām jvālā ākulām tatas gadayā tāḍayām āsa sā gadā bhīmam āvrajat sa rākṣasa indram kaunteyaḥ śara varṣaiḥ avākirat tān api asya akarot moghān rākṣasaḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ te ca api rākṣasāḥ sarve sainikāḥ bhīma rūpiṇaḥ śāsanāt rākṣasa indrasya nijaghnuḥ ratha kuñjarān pāñcālāḥ sṛñjayāḥ ca eva vājinaḥ parama dvipāḥ na śāntim lebhire tatra rakṣasaiḥ bhṛśa pīḍitāḥ tam tu dṛṣṭvā mahā ghoram vartamānam mahā āhave abravīt puruṣa śreṣṭhaḥ dhanaṃjayam idam vacaḥ paśya bhīmam mahā bāho rākṣasa indra vaśam gatam padavīm asya gaccha tvam mā vicāraya pāṇḍava dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca yudhāmanyu uttamaujasau sahitāḥ draupadeyāḥ ca karṇam yāntu mahā rathāḥ nakulaḥ sahadevaḥ ca yuyudhānaḥ ca vīryavān itarān rākṣasān ghnantu śāsanāt te pāṇḍava tvam api imām mahā bāho camūm droṇa puraskṛtām evam ukte tu kṛṣṇena yathoddiṣṭāḥ mahā rathāḥ jagmuḥ vaikartanam karṇam rākṣasān ca itarān raṇe atha pūrṇa āyata utsṛṣṭaiḥ śaraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ dhanuḥ ciccheda bhīmasya rākṣasa indraḥ pratāpavān hayān ca asya śitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ sārathim ca mahā balaḥ tatas tām bhīma nirghoṣām āpatantīm mahā gadām tat dṛṣṭvā rākṣasa indrasya ghoram karma bhaya āvaham bhīmasenaḥ prahṛṣṭa ātmā gadām āśu parāmṛśat gadā nipāta saṃhrādaiḥ bhuvam kampayatoḥ bhṛśam mattau iva mahā nāgau akṛṣyetām punar punar tam apaśyat dhṛṣīkeśaḥ pāṇḍavānām hite rataḥ uvāca saṃprekṣya samare bhīmam rakṣasā grastam antikāt vāsudevaḥ abravīt vākyam ghaṭotkacam idam tadā paśya bhīmam mahā bāho rakṣasā grastam antikāt paśyatām sarva sainyānām te ca eva mahā dyute sa karṇam tvam samutsṛjya rākṣasa indram alāyudham jahi kṣipram mahā bāho paścāt karṇam vadhiṣyasi sa vārṣṇeya vacaḥ śrutvā karṇam utsṛjya vīryavān yuyudhe rākṣasa indreṇa baka bhrātrā ghaṭotkacaḥ tayoḥ su tumulam yuddham babhūva niśi rakṣasoḥ alāyudhasya yodhān tu rākṣasān bhīma darśanān vegena āpatataḥ śūrān pragṛhīta śarāsanān ātta āyudhaḥ su saṃkruddhaḥ yuyudhānaḥ mahā rathaḥ sarvān ca samare rājan kirīṭī kṣatriya ṛṣabhān paricikṣepa bībhatsuḥ sarvatas prakṣipan śarān dhṛṣṭadyumna śikhaṇḍi ādīn pāñcālānām mahā rathān tān vadhyamānān dṛṣṭvā tu bhīmaḥ bhīma parākramaḥ abhyayāt tvaritaḥ karṇam viśikhān vikiran raṇe tatas te api āyayuḥ hatvā rākṣasān yatra sūtajaḥ nakulaḥ sahadevaḥ ca sātyakiḥ ca mahā rathaḥ te karṇam yodhayām āsuḥ pāñcālāḥ droṇam eva ca parighena ati kāyena tāḍayām āsa mūrdhani īṣat mūrchā anvitaḥ saṃstambhayata vīryavān tatas dīpta agni saṃkāśām śata ghaṇṭām alaṃkṛtām cikṣepa samare tasmai gadām kāñcana bhūṣaṇām sā hayān sārathim ca eva ratham ca asya mahā svanā cūrṇayām āsa vegena visṛṣṭā bhīma karmaṇā sa bhagna haya cakra akṣaḥ viśīrṇa dhvaja kūbaraḥ utpapāta rathāt tūrṇam māyām āsthāya rākṣasīm sa samāsthāya māyām tu vavarṣa rudhiram bahu vidyut vibhrājitam ca āsīt timira abhra ākulam nabhaḥ tatas vajra nipātāḥ ca sa aśani stanayitnavaḥ mahān caṭacaṭā śabdaḥ tatra āsīt hi mahā āhave tām prekṣya vihitām māyām rākṣasaḥ rākṣaseṇa tu ūrdhvam utpatya haiḍimbaḥ tām māyām māyayā avadhīt saḥ abhivīkṣya hatām māyām māyāvī māyayā eva hi aśma varṣam sa tat ghoram śara varṣeṇa vīryavān āyasaiḥ parighaiḥ śūlaiḥ gadā musala mudgaraiḥ nārācaiḥ niśitaiḥ bhallaiḥ śaraiḥ cakraiḥ paraśvadhaiḥ ayaḥ guḍaiḥ bhindipālaiḥ gośīrṣa ulūkhalaiḥ api utpāṭya ca mahā śākhaiḥ vividhaiḥ jagatīruhaiḥ śamī pīlu karīraiḥ ca śamyākaiḥ ca eva bhārata iṅgudaiḥ badarībhiḥ ca kovidāraiḥ ca puṣpitaiḥ vividhaiḥ parvata agraiḥ ca nānā dhātubhiḥ ācitaiḥ teṣām śabdaḥ mahān āsīt vajrāṇām bhidyatām iva hari indrayoḥ yathā rājan vāli sugrīvayoḥ purā bhujābhyām paryagṛhṇītām mahā kāyau mahā balau rudhiram ca mahā kāyau abhivṛṣṭau iva acalau saḥ apahṛtya śiraḥ tasya kuṇḍalābhyām vibhūṣitam tadā su tumulam nādam nanāda su mahā balaḥ hatam dṛṣṭvā mahā kāyam baka jñātim ariṃdamam pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ ca eva siṃhanādān vinedire tatas bherī sahasrāṇi śaṅkhānām ayutāni ca avādayan pāṇḍaveyāḥ tasmin rakṣasi pātite atīva sā niśā teṣām babhūva vijaya āvahā vidyotamānā vibabhau samantāt dīpa mālinī atha duryodhanaḥ rājā dṛṣṭvā hatam alāyudham jīvitam cira kālāya bhrātṝṇām ca api amanyata sa tam dṛṣṭvā vinihatam bhīmasena ātmajena vai pratijñām bhīmasenasya pūrṇām eva abhyamanyata uvāca nihatya alāyudham rakṣaḥ prahṛṣṭa ātmā ghaṭotkacaḥ nanāda vividhān nādān vāhinyāḥ pramukhe sthitaḥ tasya tam tumulam śabdam śrutvā kuñjara kampanam tāvakānām mahā rāja bhayam āsīt su dāruṇam dṛṣṭvā karṇaḥ mahā bāhuḥ pāñcālān samupādravat daśabhiḥ daśabhiḥ bāṇaiḥ dhṛṣṭadyumna śikhaṇḍinau dṛḍhaiḥ pūrṇa āyata utsṛṣṭaiḥ bibheda nata parvabhiḥ sātyakim ca ratha udāram kampayām āsa mārgaṇaiḥ teṣām abhyasyatām tatra sarveṣām savya dakṣiṇam maṇḍalāni eva cāpāni vyadṛśyanta janādhipa teṣām jyā tala nirghoṣaḥ ratha nemi svanaḥ ca ha jyā nemi ghoṣa stanayitnumān vai dhanuḥ taḍit maṇḍala ketu śṛṅgaḥ śara ogha varṣa ākula vṛṣṭimān ca saṃgrāma meghaḥ sa babhūva rājan vidhvaṃsayām āsa raṇe narendra vaikartanaḥ śatru gaṇa avamardī tatas atulaiḥ vajra nipāta kalpaiḥ śitaiḥ śaraiḥ kāñcana citra puṅkhaiḥ ke cit visūtāḥ vihayāḥ ca ke cid vaikartanena āśu kṛtāḥ babhūvuḥ tān prekṣya bhagnān vimukhīkṛtān ca ghaṭotkacaḥ roṣam atīva cakre āsthāya tam kāñcana ratna citram ratha uttamam siṃhaḥ iva unnanāda tau karṇi nārāca śilīmukhaiḥ ca nālīka daṇḍaiḥ ca sa vatsadantaiḥ varāhakarṇaiḥ sa viṣāṇa śṛṅgaiḥ kṣurapra varṣaiḥ ca vinedatuḥ kham tat bāṇa dhārā āvṛtam antarikṣam tiryak gatābhiḥ samare rarāja atīva tat citram atīva rūpam babhūva yuddham ravi bhīma sūnuvoḥ samākulam śastra nipāta ghoram divi iva rāhu aṃśumantoḥ prataptam ghaṭotkacaḥ yadā karṇam na viśeṣayate nṛpa tadā prāduścakāra ugram astram astra vidām varaḥ tena astreṇa hayān pūrvam hatvā karṇasya rākṣasaḥ uvāca uvāca antarhitam rākṣasam tam viditvā saṃprākrośan kuravaḥ sarve eva katham na ayam rākṣasaḥ kūṭa yodhī hanyāt karṇam samare adṛśyamānaḥ tatas karṇaḥ laghu citra astra yodhī sarvāḥ diśaḥ vyāvṛṇot bāṇa jālaiḥ na ca ādadānaḥ na ca saṃdadhānaḥ na ca iṣudhī spṛśamānaḥ kara agraiḥ adṛśyat vai lāghavāt sūtaputraḥ sarvam bāṇaiḥ chādayānaḥ antarikṣam tatas māyām vihitām antarikṣe ghorām bhīmām dāruṇām rākṣasena saṃpaśyāmaḥ lohita abhra prakāśām dedīpyantīm agni śikhām iva ugrām tatas tasyāḥ vidyutaḥ prādurāsan ulkāḥ ca api jvalitāḥ kaurava indra ghoṣaḥ ca anyaḥ prādurāsīt su ghoraḥ sahasraśas nadatām dundubhīnām tatas śarāḥ prāpatan rukma puṅkhāḥ śaktyaḥ prāsāḥ musalāni āyudhāni paraśvadhāḥ taila dhautāḥ ca khaḍgāḥ pradīpta agrāḥ paṭṭiśāḥ tomarāḥ ca mayūkhinaḥ parighāḥ loha baddhāḥ gadāḥ citrāḥ śita dhārāḥ ca śūlāḥ gurvyaḥ gadāḥ hema paṭṭa avanaddhāḥ śataghnyaḥ ca prādurāsan samantāt mahā śilāḥ ca apatan tatra tatra sahasraśas sa aśanayaḥ sa vajrāḥ cakrāṇi ca aneka śata kṣurāṇi prādurbabhūvuḥ jvalana prabhāni tām śakti pāṣāṇa paraśvadhānām prāsa asi vajra aśani mudgarāṇām vṛṣṭim viśālām jvalitām patatīm karṇaḥ śara oghaiḥ na śaśāka hantum śara āhatānām patatām hayānām vajra āhatānām patatām gajānām śilā āhatānām ca mahā rathānām mahān ninādaḥ patatām babhūva aneka māyā śataśas hatānām su bhīma nānāvidha śastra pātaiḥ ghaṭotkacena abhihatam samantāt hāhākṛta saṃparivartamāna saṃlīyamānam ca viṣad rūpam te tu ārya bhāvāt puruṣa pravīrāḥ parāṅmukhāḥ na babhūvuḥ tadānīm tām rākṣasīm ghoratarām su bhīmām vṛṣṭim mahā śastra mayīm patantīm dṛṣṭvā bala oghān ca nipātyamānān mahat bhayam tava putrān viveśa śivāḥ ca vaiśvānara dīpta jihvāḥ su bhīma nādāḥ śataśas nadantyaḥ rakṣaḥ gaṇān nardataḥ ca abhivīkṣya narendra yodhāḥ vyathitāḥ babhūvuḥ te dīpta jihvā ānana tīkṣṇa daṃṣṭrāḥ vibhīṣaṇāḥ śaila nikāśa kāyāḥ nabhaḥ gatāḥ śakti viṣakta hastāḥ meghāḥ vyamuñcan iva vṛṣṭi mārgam taiḥ āhatāḥ te śara śakti śūlaiḥ gadābhiḥ ugraiḥ parighaiḥ ca dīptaiḥ vajraiḥ pinākaiḥ aśani prahāraiḥ cakraiḥ śataghnī unmathitāḥ ca petuḥ huḍāḥ bhuśuṇḍyaḥ aśma guḍāḥ śataghnyaḥ sthūṇāḥ ca kārṣṇāyasa paṭṭa naddhāḥ avākiran tava putrasya sainyam tathā raudram kaśmalam prādurāsīt niṣkīrṇa antrāḥ vihataiḥ uttamāṅgaiḥ saṃbhagna aṅgāḥ śerate tatra śūrāḥ bhinnāḥ hayāḥ kuñjarāḥ ca avabhagnāḥ saṃcūrṇitāḥ ca eva rathāḥ śilābhiḥ evam mahat śastra varṣam sṛjantaḥ te yātudhānāḥ bhuvi ghora rūpāḥ māyāḥ sṛṣṭāḥ tatra ghaṭotkacena na amuñcan vai yācamānam na bhītam tasmin ghore kuru vīra avamarde kāla utsṛṣṭe kṣatriyāṇām abhāve palāyadhvam kuravaḥ na etat asti sa indrāḥ devāḥ ghnanti naḥ pāṇḍava arthe tathā teṣām majjatām bhāratānām na sma dvīpaḥ tatra kaḥ cit babhūva anīkānām pravibhāge aprakāśe na jñāyante kuravaḥ na itare vā nirmaryāde vidrave ghora rūpe sarvāḥ diśaḥ prekṣamāṇāḥ sma śūnyāḥ tām śastra vṛṣṭim urasā gāhamānam karṇam ca ekam tatra rājan apaśyam tatas bāṇaiḥ āvṛṇot antarikṣam divyām māyām yodhayan rākṣasasya tatas bhītāḥ samudaikṣanta karṇam rājan sarve saindhavāḥ bāhlikāḥ ca asaṃmoham pūjayantaḥ asya saṃkhye saṃpaśyantaḥ vijayam rākṣasasya tena utsṛṣṭā cakra yuktā śataghnī samam sarvān caturaḥ aśvān jaghāna tatas hata aśvāt avaruhya vāhāt antarmanāḥ kuruṣu prādravatsu tatas abruvan kuravaḥ sarve eva karṇam dṛṣṭvā ghora rūpām ca māyām śaktyā rakṣaḥ jahi karṇa adya tūrṇam naśyanti ete kuravaḥ dhārtarāṣṭrāḥ kariṣyataḥ kim ca naḥ bhīma pārthau tapantam enam jahi rakṣaḥ niśīthe yaḥ naḥ saṃgrāmāt ghora rūpāt vimucyet sa naḥ pārthān samare yodhayeta tasmāt enam rākṣasam ghora rūpam jahi śaktyā dattayā vāsavena mā kauravāḥ sarve eva indra kalpāḥ rātrī mukhe karṇa neśuḥ sa yodhāḥ sa vadhyamānaḥ rakṣasā vai niśīthe dṛṣṭvā rājan naśyamānam balam ca mahat ca śrutvā ninadam kauravāṇām matim dadhre śakti mokṣāya karṇaḥ sa tāḍyamānaḥ niśi rākṣaseṇa rājan dṛṣṭvā vidrutam te balam ca śrutvā mahantam ninadam kurūṇām sa vai kruddhaḥ siṃhaḥ iva ati amarṣī na amarṣayat pratighātam raṇe tam śaktim śreṣṭhām vaijayantīm asahyām samādade tasya vadham cikīrṣan yā asau rājan nihitā varṣa pūgān vadhāya ājau satkṛtā phalgunasya yām vai prādāt sūtaputrāya śakraḥ śaktim śreṣṭhām kuṇḍalābhyām nimāya śaktim śreṣṭhām kuṇḍalābhyām gṛhītām puraṃdarāt varmaṇā ādāya rājan tām vai śaktim lelihānām pradīptām pāśaiḥ yuktām antakasya iva rātrim mṛtyoḥ svasāram jvalitām iva ulkām vaikartanaḥ prāhiṇot rākṣasāya tām uttamām para kāya apahantrīm dṛṣṭvā sauteḥ bāhu saṃsthām jvalantīm bhītam rakṣaḥ vipradudrāva rājan kṛtvā ātmānam vindhya pāda pramāṇam dṛṣṭvā śaktim karṇa bāhu antara sthām neduḥ bhūtāni antarikṣe narendra vavuḥ vātāḥ tumulāḥ ca api rājan sa nirghātā gām jagāma sā tām māyām bhasma kṛtvā jvalantī bhittvā gāḍham hṛdayam rākṣasasya ūrdhvam yayau dīpyamānā niśāyām nakṣatrāṇām antarāṇi āviśantī yuddhvā citraiḥ vividhaiḥ śastra pūgaiḥ divyaiḥ vīraḥ mānuṣaiḥ rākṣasaiḥ ca nadan nādān vividhān bhairavān ca prāṇān iṣṭān tyājitaḥ śakra śaktyā idam ca anyat citram āścarya rūpam cakāra asau karma śatru kṣayāya avākśirāḥ stabdha gātraḥ vijihvaḥ ghaṭotkacaḥ mahat āsthāya rūpam sa tat rūpam bhairavam bhīma karmā bhīmam kṛtvā bhaimaseniḥ papāta patat rakṣaḥ svena kāyena tūrṇam priyam kurvan pāṇḍavānām gatāsuḥ akṣauhiṇīm tava tūrṇam jaghāna tatas miśrāḥ prāṇadan siṃhanādaiḥ bheryaḥ śaṅkhāḥ murajāḥ ca ānakāḥ ca dagdhām māyām nihatam rākṣasam ca dṛṣṭvā hṛṣṭāḥ prāṇadan kauraveyāḥ tatas karṇaḥ kurubhiḥ pūjyamānaḥ yathā śakraḥ vṛtra vadhe marudbhiḥ anvārūḍhaḥ tava putram ratha stham hṛṣṭaḥ ca api prāviśat svam sa sainyam dhṛtarāṣṭraḥ amarṣitāḥ pāṇḍaveyāḥ kim akurvan mahā raṇe marditāḥ ca bhṛśam yuddhe kim akurvata saṃjaya ye ca te abhyadravan droṇam vyūḍha anīkāḥ prahāriṇaḥ sṛñjayāḥ saha pāñcālaiḥ te akurvan kim mahā raṇe amarṣāt jīvitam tyaktvā gāhamānam varūthinīm jṛmbhamāṇam iva vyāghram vyātta ānanam iva antakam katham pratyudyayuḥ droṇam ajayyam kuru sṛñjayāḥ ācāryam ye ca rakṣanti duryodhana purogamāḥ drauṇi karṇa kṛpāḥ tāta te hi akurvan kim āhave bhāradvājam jighāsantau savyasāci vṛkodarau māmakān yuddhe katham saṃjaya śaṃsa me amarṣitāḥ ca saṃkruddhāḥ raṇam cakruḥ katham yudhi uvāca haiḍimbam nihatam dṛṣṭvā vikīrṇam iva parvatam pāṇḍavāḥ dīna manasaḥ sarve bāṣpa ākula īkṣaṇāḥ hatam ghaṭotkacam jñātvā vāsudevaḥ pratāpavān sa vinadya mahā nādam abhīśūn saṃniyamya ca nanarta harṣa saṃvītaḥ vāta uddhūtaḥ iva drumaḥ tatas vinirbhrāmya punar pārtham āsphoṭya ca asakṛt prahṛṣṭa manasam jñātvā vāsudevam mahā balam abravīt arjunaḥ rājan na ati hṛṣṭa manāḥ iva praharṣam tasya tam jñātvā keśavasya dhanaṃjayaḥ vimukhāni ca sainyāni hatam dṛṣṭvā ghaṭotkacam vayam ca bhṛśam āvignāḥ haiḍimbasya nipātanāt tat adya śaṃsa me pṛṣṭaḥ satyam satyavatām vara harṣasya sati api sthāne na ulbaṇam yānti paṇḍitāḥ uvāca ati harṣam imam prāptam śṛṇu me tvam dhanaṃjaya śaktim ghaṭotkacena imām vyaṃsayitvā mahā dyute śakti hastam punar karṇam kaḥ loke asti pumān iha diṣṭyā apanīta kavacaḥ diṣṭyā apahṛta kuṇḍalaḥ diṣṭyā ca vyaṃsitā śaktiḥ amoghā asya ghaṭotkace sa amarān api lokān trīn ekaḥ karṇaḥ jayet balī vāsavaḥ vā kuberaḥ vā varuṇaḥ vā jaleśvaraḥ gāṇḍīvam āyamya bhavān cakram vā mama sudarśanam tvad hita artham tu śakreṇa māyayā hṛta kuṇḍalaḥ vihīna kavacaḥ ca ayam kṛtaḥ parapuraṃjayaḥ prādāt śakrāya karṇaḥ vai tena vaikartanaḥ smṛtaḥ āśīviṣaḥ iva kruddhaḥ stambhitaḥ mantra tejasā tathā adya bhāti karṇaḥ me śānta jvālaḥ iva analaḥ yadā prabhṛti karṇāya śaktiḥ dattā mahātmanā vāsavena mahā bāho prāptā yā asau ghaṭotkace kuṇḍalābhyām nimāya atha divyena kavacena ca tām prāpya amanyata vṛṣā satatam tvām hatam raṇe ṛte tvā puruṣa vyāghra śape satyena ca anagha ripuṣu api dayāvān ca tasmāt karṇaḥ vṛṣā smṛtaḥ yuddha śauṇḍaḥ mahā bāhuḥ nitya udyata śarāsanaḥ vimadān ratha śārdūlān kurute raṇa mūrdhani śara jāla sahasra aṃśuḥ śaradi iva divākaraḥ divya astra jaladaḥ karṇaḥ parjanyaḥ iva vṛṣṭimān tridaśaiḥ api ca asyadbhiḥ śara varṣam samantataḥ aśakyaḥ tat ayam jetum sravadbhiḥ māṃsa śoṇitam kavacena vihīnaḥ ca kuṇḍalābhyām ca pāṇḍava tena ādityam nirudhyet yaḥ śara varṣaiḥ ca vṛṣṭimān saḥ adya mānuṣa tām prāptaḥ vimuktaḥ śakra dattayā kṛcchra prāptam ratha cakre nimagne hanyāḥ pūrvam tvam tu saṃjñām vicārya jarāsaṃdhaḥ cedi rājaḥ mahātmā mahā balaḥ ca ekalavyaḥ niṣādaḥ atha apare nihatāḥ rākṣasa indrāḥ hiḍimba kirmīra baka pradhānāḥ jarāsaṃdha prabhṛtayaḥ ghātitāḥ pṛthivīṣvarāḥ uvāca jarāsaṃdhaḥ cedi rājaḥ naiṣādaḥ ca mahā balaḥ yadi syuḥ na hatāḥ pūrvam idānīm syuḥ bhayaṃkarāḥ suyodhanaḥ tān avaśyam vṛṇuyāt ratha sattamān te asmābhiḥ nitya saṃduṣṭāḥ saṃśrayeyuḥ ca kauravān te hi vīrāḥ mahātmānaḥ kṛtāstrāḥ dṛḍha yodhinaḥ dhārtarāṣṭrām camūm kṛtsnām rakṣeyuḥ amarāḥ iva sūtaputraḥ jarāsaṃdhaḥ cedi rājaḥ niṣāda jaḥ suyodhanam samāśritya taperan pṛthivīm imām yogaiḥ api hatāḥ yaiḥ te tān mama śṛṇu dhanaṃjaya ekaikaḥ hi pṛthak teṣām samastām sura vāhinīm jarāsaṃdhaḥ hi ruṣitaḥ rauhiṇeya pradharṣitaḥ mad vadha artham cikṣepa gadām vai lohitāmukhīm sīmantam iva kurvāṇām nabhasaḥ pāvaka prabhām vyadṛśyata āpatatī sā śakra muktā yathā aśaniḥ tām āpatantīm dṛṣṭvā eva gadām rohiṇinandanaḥ pratighāta artham astram vai sthūṇākarṇam avāsṛjat dārayantī dharām devīm kampayantī iva parvatān tatra sma rākṣasī ghorā jarā nāma āśu vikramā saṃdhayām āsa tam jātam jarāsaṃdham ariṃdamam dvābhyām jātaḥ hi mātṛbhyām ardha dehaḥ pṛthak pṛthak tayā sa saṃdhitaḥ yasmāt jarāsaṃdhaḥ tatas smṛtaḥ sā tu bhūmi gatā pārtha hatā sa suta bāndhavā gadayā tena ca astreṇa sthūṇākarṇena rākṣasī vinābhūtaḥ sa gadayā jarāsaṃdhaḥ mahā mṛdhe yadi hi syāt gadā pāṇiḥ jarāsaṃdhaḥ pratāpavān sa indrāḥ devāḥ na tam hantum raṇe śaktāḥ narottama tvad hita artham hi naiṣādaḥ aṅguṣṭhena viyojitaḥ droṇena ācāryakam kṛtvā chadmanā satya vikramaḥ sa tu baddha aṅguli trāṇaḥ naiṣādaḥ dṛḍha vikramaḥ ekalavyam hi sa aṅguṣṭham aśaktāḥ deva dānavāḥ kim u mānuṣa mātreṇa śakyaḥ syāt prativīkṣitum dṛḍha muṣṭiḥ kṛtī nityam asyamānaḥ divāniśam tvad hita artham tu sa mayā hataḥ saṃgrāma mūrdhani sa ca api aśakyaḥ saṃgrāme jetum sarvaiḥ sura asuraiḥ sa hi jātaḥ catur bāhuḥ dhṛta jāmbūnada srajaḥ ajeyaḥ sarva bhūtānām jayet api divaukasaḥ vadha artham tasya jātaḥ aham anyeṣām ca suradviṣām tvad sahāyaḥ nara vyāghra lokānām hita kāmyayā hiḍimba baka kirmīrāḥ bhīmasenena pātitāḥ rāvaṇena sama prāṇāḥ brahmayajña vināśanāḥ hataḥ tathā eva māyāvī haiḍimbena api alāyudhaḥ haiḍimbaḥ ca api upāyena śaktyā karṇena ghātitaḥ yadi hi enam na ahaniṣyat karṇaḥ śaktyā mahā mṛdhe mayā na nihataḥ pūrvam eṣa tvad priya īpsayā eṣa hi brāhmaṇa dveṣī yajña dveṣī ca rākṣasaḥ dharmasya loptā pāpa ātmā tasmāt eṣa nipātitaḥ vyaṃsitā ca api upāyena śakra dattā mayā anagha dharma saṃsthāpana artham hi pratijñā eṣā mama avyayā brahma satyam damaḥ śaucam dharmaḥ hrīḥ śrīḥ dhṛtiḥ kṣamā na viṣādaḥ tvayā kāryaḥ karṇam vaikartanam prati upadekṣyāmi upāyam te yena tam prasahiṣyasi suyodhanam ca api raṇe haniṣyati vṛkodaraḥ tasya ca api vadha upāyam vakṣyāmi te pāṇḍava dahati eṣa ca vaḥ sainyam droṇaḥ praharatām varaḥ uvāca eka vīra vadhe moghā śaktiḥ sūta ātmaje yadā kasmāt sarvān samutsṛjya sa tām pārthe na muktavān tasmin hate hatāḥ hi syuḥ sarve pāṇḍava sṛñjayāḥ na jaghāna vṛṣā kasmāt tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya nūnam buddhi vihīnaḥ ca api asahāyaḥ ca me sutaḥ sā śaktiḥ vāsudevena vyaṃsitā asya ghaṭotkace tathā śaktiḥ amoghā sā moghībhūtā ghaṭotkace ghaṭotkacaḥ yadi hanyāt hi karṇam paraḥ lābhaḥ sa bhavet pāṇḍavānām vaikartanaḥ vā yadi tam nihanyāt tathā api kṛtyam śakti nāśāt kṛtam syāt iti prājñaḥ prajñayā etat vicārya ghaṭotkacam sūtaputreṇa yuddhe ayodhayat vāsudevaḥ nṛ siṃhaḥ priyam kurvan pāṇḍavānām hitam ca uvāca etat cikīrṣitam jñātvā karṇe madhunihā nṛpa niyojayām āsa tadā dvairathe rākṣasa īśvaram ghaṭotkacam mahā vīryam mahā buddhiḥ janārdanaḥ tadā eva kṛta kāryāḥ hi vayam syāma kuru udvaha na rakṣet yadi kṛṣṇaḥ tam pārtham karṇāt mahā rathāt sa aśva dhvaja rathaḥ saṃkhye dhṛtarāṣṭra patet bhuvi vinā janārdanam pārthaḥ yogānām īśvaram prabhum taiḥ taiḥ upāyaiḥ bahubhiḥ rakṣyamāṇaḥ sa pārthiva jayati abhimukhaḥ śatrūn pārthaḥ kṛṣṇena pālitaḥ sa viśeṣam tu amoghāyāḥ kṛṣṇaḥ arakṣata pāṇḍavam hanyāt kṣiptā hi kaunteyam śaktiḥ vṛkṣam iva aśaniḥ uvāca virodhī ca kumantrī ca prājña mānī mama ātmajaḥ sa vā karṇaḥ mahā buddhiḥ sarva śastrabhṛtām varaḥ na muktavān katham sūta tām amoghām dhanaṃjaye uvāca preṣya vat pāṇḍu pāñcālān upabhokṣyāmahe tatas atha vā nihate pārthe pāṇḍuṣu anyatamam tatas sthāpayet yudhi vārṣṇeyaḥ tasmāt kṛṣṇaḥ nipātyatām kṛṣṇaḥ hi mūlam pāṇḍūnām pārthaḥ skandhaḥ iva udgataḥ śākhāḥ iva itare pārthāḥ pāñcālāḥ pattra saṃjñitāḥ kṛṣṇa āśrayāḥ kṛṣṇa balāḥ kṛṣṇa nāthāḥ ca pāṇḍavāḥ kṛṣṇaḥ parāyaṇam ca eṣām jyotiṣām iva candramāḥ tasmāt parṇāni śākhāḥ ca skandham ca utsṛjya sūtaja kṛṣṇam nikṛndhi pāṇḍūnām mūlam sarvatra sarvadā hanyāt yadi hi dāśārham karṇaḥ yādava nandanam kṛtsnā vasumatī rājan vaśe te syāt na saṃśayaḥ sā tu buddhiḥ kṛtā rājan kṛṣṇam prati nareśvara viṣṇoḥ tejaḥ pramūḍhānām yuddha kāle praṇaśyati yadi hi sa nihataḥ śayīta bhūmau yadu kula pāṇḍava nandanaḥ mahātmā sā tu buddhiḥ kṛ api evam jāgrati tridaśeśvare arjunam ca api kaunteyam sadā rakṣati keśavaḥ anyān ca asmai ratha udārān upasthāpayat acyutaḥ amoghām tām katham śaktim moghām kuryām iti prabho yaḥ ca evam rakṣate pārtham karṇāt kṛṣṇaḥ mahā manāḥ ātmānam sa katham rājan na rakṣet puruṣottamaḥ tatas kṛṣṇam mahā bāhuḥ sātyakiḥ satya vikramaḥ ayam ca pratyayaḥ karṇe śaktyā ca amita vikrama uvāca duḥṣāsanaḥ ca karṇaḥ ca śakuniḥ ca sa saindhavaḥ karṇa karṇa mahā iṣvāsa raṇe amita parākrama na anyasya śaktiḥ eṣā te moktavyā jayatām vara ṛte mahā rathāt pārthāt kuntī putrāt dhanaṃjayāt sa hi teṣām ati yaśāḥ devānām iva vāsavaḥ tasmin vinihate sarve pāṇḍavāḥ sṛñjayaiḥ saha bhaviṣyanti gata ātmānaḥ surāḥ iva niragnayaḥ ṛte mahātmanaḥ pārthāt karṇena nihatāḥ dhruvam tathā iti ca pratijñātam karṇena śini puṃgava hṛdi nityam tu karṇasya vadhaḥ gāṇḍīvadhanvanaḥ yatas na avasṛjat śaktim pāṇḍave śvetavāhane ghaṭotkace vyaṃsitām tu dṛṣṭvā tām śini puṃgava mṛtyoḥ āsya antarāt muktam paśyāmi adya dhanaṃjayam na pitā na ca me mātā na yūyam bhrātaraḥ tathā na ca prāṇāḥ tathā rakṣyāḥ yathā bībhatsuḥ āhave na iccheyam sātvata aham tat vinā pārtham dhanaṃjayam mṛtam pratyāgatam iva dṛṣṭvā pārtham dhanaṃjayam atas ca prahitaḥ yuddhe mayā karṇāya rākṣasaḥ na hi anyaḥ samare rātrau śaktaḥ karṇam prabādhitum yasya tvam puruṣa vyāghra śivāya satatam sthitaḥ uvāca uvāca karṇa duryodhana ādīnām śakuneḥ saubalasya ca apanītam mahat tāta tava ca eva viśeṣataḥ yat ājānīta tām śaktim eka ghnīm satatam raṇe anivāryām asahyām ca devaiḥ api sa vāsavaiḥ uvāca saṃgrāmāt vinivṛttānām sarveṣām naḥ viśām pate prabhāta mātre śvobhūte keśavāya arjunāya vā śaktiḥ eṣā vimoktavyā karṇa karṇa iti nityaśas anyeṣām ca eva yodhānām sā buddhiḥ naśyate punar na jaghāna raṇe pārtham kṛṣṇam vā devakī sutam kṛṣṇe vā devakīputre mohitaḥ deva māyayā pārthe vā śakra kalpe vai vadha artham vāsavīm prabho uvāca gatā hi vāsavī hatvā tṛṇa bhūtam ghaṭotkacam karṇaḥ ca mama putrāḥ ca sarve ca anye ca pārthivāḥ kurūṇām pāṇḍavānām ca haiḍimbe nihate tadā ye ca te abhyadravan droṇam vyūḍha anīkāḥ prahāriṇaḥ sṛñjayāḥ saha pāñcālaiḥ te api akurvan katham raṇam amarṣāt jīvitam tyaktvā gāhamānam varūthinīm jṛmbhamāṇam iva vyāghram vyātta ānanam iva antakam katham pratyudyayuḥ droṇam asyantam pāṇḍu sṛñjayāḥ ācāryam ye ca te arakṣan duryodhana purogamāḥ drauṇi karṇa kṛpāḥ tāta te api akurvan kim āhave bhāradvājam jighāṃsantau savyasāci vṛkodarau samārchat māmakāḥ yuddhe katham saṃjaya śaṃsa me amarṣitāḥ su saṃkruddhāḥ raṇam cakruḥ katham niśi uvāca hate ghaṭotkace rājan karṇena niśi rākṣase praṇadatsu ca hṛṣṭeṣu tāvakeṣu yuyutsuṣu vigāḍhāyām rajanyām ca rājā dainyam param gataḥ abravīt ca mahā bāhuḥ bhīmasenam paraṃtapaḥ āvāraya mahā bāho dhārtarāṣṭrasya vāhinīm haiḍimbasya abhighātena mohaḥ mām āviśat mahān evam bhīmam samādiśya sva rathe samupāviśat aśru pūrṇa mukhaḥ rājā niḥśvasan ca punar punar kaśmalam prāviśat ghoram dṛṣṭvā karṇasya vikramam tam tathā vyathitam dṛṣṭvā kṛṣṇaḥ vacanam abravīt vaiklavyam bharata śreṣṭha yathā prākṛta pūruṣe śrutvā kṛṣṇasya vacanam dharmarājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ vimṛjya netre pāṇibhyām kṛṣṇam vacanam abravīt vid tvad mahat bāhu dharmāṇām paramā gatiḥ naḥ hi vana sthānām haiḍimbena mahātmanā bālena api satā tena kṛtam sāhyam janārdana astra hetoḥ gatam jñātvā pāṇḍavam śvetavāhanam āgamya sa sahāyena kṛtā rakṣā mahātmanā saḥ adya karṇena nihataḥ paśyatām pāpa cetasām asya pāpasya mokṣam hi katham yāsyāmi mādhava asau kṛṣṇa mahā iṣvāsaḥ kāmyake mām upasthitaḥ uṣitaḥ ca saha asmābhiḥ yāvat na āsīt dhanaṃjayaḥ gandhamādana yātrāyām durgebhyaḥ ca sma tāritāḥ pāñcālī ca pariśrāntā pṛṣṭhena ūḍhā mahātmanā diśām hi vijaye kṛṣṇa sahadevasya ca ājñayā laṅkām tu gatvā paulastyaḥ karam vai dāpitaḥ balāt ārambhāt ca eva yuddhānām yat eṣa kṛtavan prabho mad artham duṣkaram karma kṛtam tena mahātmanā svabhāvāt yā ca me prītiḥ sahadeve janārdana sā eva me dviguṇā prītiḥ rākṣasa indre ghaṭotkace bhaktaḥ ca me mahā bāhuḥ priyaḥ asya aham priyaḥ ca me yena vindāmi vārṣṇeya kaśmalam śoka tāpitaḥ paśya sainyāni vārṣṇeya drāvyamāṇāni kauravaiḥ niśīthe pāṇḍavam sainyam ābhyām paśya pramarditam gajābhyām iva mattābhyām yathā naḍavanam mahat an ādṛtya balam bāhvoḥ bhīmasenasya mādhava eṣa droṇaḥ ca karṇaḥ ca rājā ca eva suyodhanaḥ nihatya rākṣasam yuddhe hṛṣṭāḥ nardanti saṃyuge haiḍimbaḥ prāptavan mṛtyum sūtaputreṇa saṃgataḥ kadarthīkṛtya naḥ sarvān paśyataḥ savyasācinaḥ nihataḥ rākṣasaḥ kṛṣṇa bhaimaseniḥ mahā balaḥ yadā abhimanyuḥ nihataḥ dhārtarāṣṭraiḥ durātmabhiḥ na āsīt tatra raṇe kṛṣṇa savyasācī mahā rathaḥ upadiṣṭaḥ vadha upāyaḥ karṇasya guruṇā svayam vyāyacchataḥ ca khaḍgena dvidhā khaḍgam cakāra ha vyasane vartamānasya kṛtavarmā nṛśaṃsa vat aśvān jaghāna sahasā tathā ubhau pārṣṇisārathī alpe ca kāraṇe kṛṣṇa hataḥ gāṇḍīvadhanvanā yadi śatru vadhe nyāyyaḥ bhavet kartum ca pāṇḍavaiḥ droṇa karṇau raṇe pūrvam hantavyau iti mama matiḥ etau mūlam hi duḥkhānām asmākam puruṣa ṛṣabha etau raṇe samāsādya parāśvastaḥ suyodhanaḥ tatra avadhīt mahā bāhuḥ saindhavam dūra vāsinam avaśyam tu mayā kāryaḥ sūtaputrasya nigrahaḥ tatas yāsyāmi aham vīra svayam karṇa jighāṃsayā bhīmasenaḥ mahā bāhuḥ droṇa anīkena saṃgataḥ evam uktvā yayau tūrṇam tvaramāṇaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ vṛtaḥ śikhaṇḍī tvaritaḥ rājānam pṛṣṭhatas anvayāt tatas bherīḥ samājaghnuḥ śaṅkhān dadhmuḥ ca daṃśitāḥ śaṅkha śabda ravān ca eva bāṇa śabdān ca daṃsitāḥ pāñcālāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ ca eva yudhiṣṭhira purogamāḥ eṣa prayāti krodha āviṣṭaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ evam uktvā hṛṣīkeśaḥ śīghram aśvān acodayat dūram ca yātam rājānam anvagacchat janārdanaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā sahasā yāntam sūtaputra jighāṃsayā śoka upahata saṃkalpam dahyamānam iva agninā karṇam āsādya saṃgrāme diṣṭyā jīvati phalgunaḥ savyasāci vadha ākāṅkṣī śaktim rakṣitavan hi saḥ na ca agāt dvairatham jiṣṇuḥ diṣṭyā tam bharata ṛṣabha sṛjetām spardhinau etau divyāni astrāṇi sarvaśas vadhyamāneṣu ca astreṣu pīḍitaḥ sūtanandanaḥ vāsavīm samare śaktim dhruvam muñcet yudhiṣṭhira diṣṭyā rakṣaḥ hatam yuddhe sūtaputreṇa mānada vāsavīm kāraṇam kṛtvā kālena apahataḥ hi asau tava eva kāraṇāt rakṣaḥ nihatam tāta saṃyuge mā krudhaḥ bharata śreṣṭha mā ca śoke manaḥ kṛthāḥ prāṇinām iha sarveṣām eṣā niṣṭhā yudhiṣṭhira bhrātṛbhiḥ sahitaḥ sarvaiḥ pārthivaiḥ ca mahātmabhiḥ ānṛśaṃsyam tapaḥ dānam kṣamām satyam ca pāṇḍava iti uktvā pāṇḍavam vyāsaḥ tatra eva antaradhīyata uvāca ghaṭotkace tu nihate sūtaputreṇa tām niśām duḥkha amarṣa vaśam prāptaḥ dharmaputraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ dṛṣṭvā bhīmena mahatīm vāryamāṇām camūm te dhṛṣṭadyumnam uvāca idam kumbhayonim nivāraya tvam hi droṇa vināśāya samutpannaḥ hutāśanāt sa śaraḥ kavacī khaḍgī dhanvī ca para tāpanaḥ abhidrava raṇe hṛṣṭaḥ na ca te bhī katham cana janamejayaḥ śikhaṇḍī ca daurmukhiḥ ca yaśodhanaḥ abhidravantu saṃhṛṣṭāḥ kumbhayonim samantataḥ sātyakiḥ kekayāḥ ca eva pāṇḍavaḥ ca dhanaṃjayaḥ pādātāḥ ca raṇe droṇam prāpayantu mahā ratham tathā ājñaptāḥ tu te sarve pāṇḍavena mahātmanā āgacchataḥ tān sahasā sarva udyogena pāṇḍavān pratijagrāha samare droṇaḥ śastrabhṛtām varaḥ tatas duryodhanaḥ rājā sarva udyogena pāṇḍavān pāṇḍavānām kurūṇām ca garjatām itaretaram nidrā andhāḥ te mahā rāja pariśrāntāḥ ca saṃyuge na abhyapadyanta samare kām cit ceṣṭām mahā rathāḥ tri yāmā rajanī ca eṣā ghora rūpā bhayānakā sahasra yāma pratimā babhūva prāṇa hāriṇī vadh ca tathā teṣām kṣatānām ca viśeṣataḥ aho rātriḥ samājajñe nidrā andhānām viśeṣataḥ sarve hi āsan nirutsāhāḥ kṣatriyāḥ dīna cetasaḥ tava ca eva pareṣām ca gata astrāḥ vigata iṣavaḥ te tathā pārayantaḥ ca hrīmantaḥ ca viśeṣataḥ śastrāṇi anye samutsṛjya nidrā andhāḥ śerate janāḥ nidrā andhāḥ naḥ bubudhire kām cit ceṣṭām narādhipāḥ ātmānam samare jaghnuḥ svān eva ca parān api nānā vācaḥ vimuñcantaḥ nidrā andhāḥ te mahā raṇe asmākam ca mahā rāja parebhyaḥ bahavaḥ janāḥ jaghnuḥ śūrāḥ raṇe rājñ tasmin tamasi dāruṇe hanyamānam tathā ātmānam parebhyaḥ bahavaḥ janāḥ na abhyajānanta samare nidrayā mohitāḥ bhṛśam teṣām etādṛśīm ceṣṭām vijñāya puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ uvāca vākyam bībhatsuḥ uccais saṃnādayan diśaḥ śrāntāḥ bhavantaḥ nidrā andhāḥ sarve eva sa vāhanāḥ saṃsādhayiṣyatha anyonyam svargāya kuru pāṇḍavāḥ upāramata pāṇḍūnām viratā hi varūthinī upāramata pāṇḍūnām senā te ca bhārata tām asya vācam devāḥ ca ṛṣayaḥ ca mahātmanaḥ sarva sainyāni ca akṣudrāḥ prahṛṣṭāḥ pratyapūjayan muhūrtam asvapan rājan śrāntāni bharata ṛṣabha sā tu saṃprāpya viśrāmam dhvajinī tava bhārata dharmaḥ tvayi mahā bāho dayā bhūteṣu ca anagha yat ca āśvastāḥ tava icchāmaḥ śarma pārtha tat astu te iti te tam nara vyāghram praśaṃsantaḥ mahā rathāḥ nidrayā samavākṣiptāḥ tūṣṇīm āsan viśām pate aśva pṛṣṭheṣu ca api anye rathanīḍeṣu ca apare gaja skandha gatāḥ ca anye śerate ca apare kṣitau sa āyudhāḥ sa gadāḥ ca eva sa khaḍgāḥ sa paraśvadhāḥ sa prāsa kavacāḥ ca anye narāḥ suptāḥ pṛthak pṛthak gajāḥ te pannaga ābhogaiḥ hastaiḥ bhū reṇu rūṣitaiḥ nidrā andhāḥ vasudhām cakruḥ ghrāṇa niḥśvāsa śītalām gajāḥ śuśubhire tatra niḥśvasantaḥ mahī tale viśīrṇāḥ girayaḥ yadvat niḥśvasadbhiḥ mahā uragaiḥ samām ca viṣamām cakruḥ khura agraiḥ vikṣatām mahīm hayāḥ kāñcana yoktrāḥ ca kesara ālambibhiḥ yugaiḥ suṣupuḥ tatra rāja indra yuktāḥ vāheṣu sarvaśas evam hayāḥ ca nāgāḥ ca yodhāḥ ca bharata ṛṣabha yuddhāt viramya suṣupuḥ śrameṇa mahatā anvitāḥ te kṣatriyāḥ kuṇḍalinaḥ yuvānaḥ parasparam sāyaka vikṣata aṅgāḥ kumbheṣu līnāḥ suṣupuḥ gajānām kuceṣu lagnāḥ iva kāminīnām vīrāḥ vāraṇa kumbheṣu suṣupuḥ yuddha karśitāḥ rātrau rati pariśrāntāḥ kāminīnām kuceṣu iva tatas kumudanāthena kāminī gaṇḍa pāṇḍunā netra ānandena candreṇa māhendrī diś alaṃkṛtā daśa śata akṣaka kubdari niḥsṛtaḥ timira vāraṇa yūtha vidāraṇaḥ smara śarāsana pūrṇa sama prabhaḥ pravisṛtaḥ kumudākara bāndhavaḥ tatas muhūrtāt bhagavān purastāt śaśalakṣaṇaḥ aruṇam darśayām āsa grasan jyotiḥ prabham prabhuḥ paryagacchan śanais sarvāḥ diśaḥ kham ca kṣitim tathā aprakhyam aprakāśam ca jagāma āśu tamaḥ tathā pratiprakāśite loke divābhūte niśākare bodhyamānam tu tat sainyam rājan candrasya raśmibhiḥ bubudhe śatapattrāṇām vanam mahat iva ambhasi tathā candra udaya uddhūtaḥ sa babhūva bala arṇavaḥ tatas pravavṛte yuddham punar eva viśām pati loke loka vināśāya param lokam abhīpsatām uvāca na marṣaṇīyāḥ saṃgrāme viśramantaḥ śrama anvitāḥ sapatnāḥ glāna manasaḥ labdha lakṣyāḥ viśeṣataḥ te ete pariviśrāntāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ balavattarāḥ divyāni astrāṇi sarvāṇi brahmāstra ādīni yāni api tāni sarvāṇi tiṣṭhanti bhavati eva viśeṣataḥ na pāṇḍaveyāḥ na vayam na anye loke dhanurdharāḥ sa bhavān marṣayati enān tvattaḥ bhītān viśeṣataḥ śiṣya tvam vā puraskṛtya mama vā mandabhāgya tām atas param mayā kāryam kṣudram vijaya gṛddhinā yat bhavān manyate ca api śubham vā yadi vā aśubham nihatya sarva pāñcālān yuddhe kṛtvā parākramam tasya vīryam mahā bāho śṛṇu satyena kaurava tam na devāḥ na gandharvāḥ na yakṣāḥ na ca rākṣasāḥ khāṇḍava yena bhagavant pratyudyā sureśvara sāyakaiḥ vāritaḥ ca api varṣamāṇaḥ mahātmanā yakṣāḥ nāgāḥ tathā daityāḥ ye ca anye bala garvitāḥ nihatāḥ puruṣa indreṇa tat ca api viditam tava gandharvāḥ ghoṣa yātrāyām citrasena ādayaḥ jitāḥ yūyam taiḥ hriyamāṇāḥ ca mokṣitāḥ dṛḍhadhanvanā nivāta kavacāḥ ca api devānām śatravaḥ tathā suraiḥ avadhyāḥ saṃgrāme tena vīreṇa nirjitāḥ dānavānām sahasrāṇi hiraṇyapura vāsinām vijigye puruṣa vyāghraḥ sa śakyaḥ mānuṣaiḥ katham kṣapitam pāṇḍu putreṇa ceṣṭatām naḥ viśām pate aham duḥśāsanaḥ karṇaḥ śakuniḥ mātulaḥ ca me haniṣyāmaḥ arjunam saṃkhye dvaidhīkṛtya adya bhāratīm tiṣṭha sa tvam mahā bāho nityam śiṣyaḥ priyaḥ te kaḥ hi gāṇḍīvadhanvānam jvalantam iva tejasā akṣayam kṣapayet kaḥ cit kṣatriyaḥ kṣatriya ṛṣabham na asura uraga rakṣāṃsi kṣapayeyuḥ saha āyudham mūḍhāḥ tu etāni bhāṣante yāni imā āttha bhārata tvam tu sarva ati śaṅki tvāt niṣṭhuraḥ pāpa niścayaḥ imān kim pārthivān sarvān ghātayiṣyasi anāgasaḥ eṣa te mātulaḥ prājñaḥ kṣatra dharmam anuvrataḥ dūrdyūta devī gāndhāriḥ prayātu arjunam āhave eṣaḥ akṣa kuśalaḥ jihmaḥ dyūta kṛt kitavaḥ śaṭhaḥ devitā nikṛti prajñaḥ yudhi jeṣyati pāṇḍavān asakṛt śūnya vat mohāt dhṛtarāṣṭrasya śṛṇvataḥ aham ca tāta karṇaḥ ca bhrātā duḥśāsanaḥ ca me pāṇḍu putrān haniṣyāmaḥ sahitāḥ samare trayaḥ anutiṣṭha pratijñām tām satya vāc bhava taiḥ saha eṣa te pāṇḍavaḥ śatruḥ aviṣahyaḥ agratas sthitaḥ kṛtakṛtyaḥ anṛṇaḥ ca asi mā bhaiḥ yudhyasva pāṇḍavam dvaidhīkṛtya tatas senām yuddham samabhavat tadā uvāca tri bhāga mātra śeṣāyām rātryām yuddham avartata kurūṇām pāṇḍavānām ca saṃhṛṣṭānām viśām pate atha candraprabhām muṣṇan ādityasya puraḥsaraḥ prācyām diśi sahasrāṃśoḥ aruṇena aruṇīkṛtam tāpanīyam yathā cakram bhrājate ravi maṇḍalam tatas ratha aśvān ca manuṣya yānāni utsṛjya sarve kuru pāṇḍu yodhāḥ saṃdhyā gatāḥ prāñjalayaḥ babhūvuḥ tatas dvaidhīkṛte sainye droṇaḥ somaka pāṇḍavān dvaidhībhūtān kurūn dṛṣṭvā mādhavaḥ arjunam abravīt sa mādhavam anujñāya kuruṣva iti dhanaṃjayaḥ abhiprāyam tu kṛṣṇasya jñātvā parapuraṃjayaḥ āji śīrṣa gatam dṛṣṭvā bhīmasenam samāsadat uvāca arjuna arjuna bībhatso śṛṇu mama tattvataḥ vacaḥ yad artham kṣatriyā sūte tasya kālaḥ ayam āgataḥ asaṃbhāvita rūpaḥ san ānṛśaṃsyam kariṣyasi satya śrī dharma yaśasām vīryeṇa ānṛṇyam āpnuhi bhindhi anīkam yudhām śreṣṭha savyasācin imān kuru uvāca tam āji śīrṣam āyāntam dahantam kṣatriya ṛṣabhān parākrāntam parākramya yatantaḥ kṣatriya ṛṣabhāḥ na aśaknuvan vārayitum vardhamānam iva analam atha duryodhanaḥ karṇaḥ śakuniḥ ca api saubalaḥ abhyavarṣan śara vrātaiḥ kuntī putram dhanaṃjayam teṣām astrāṇi sarveṣām uttama astra vidām varaḥ sarvān avidhyat niśitaiḥ daśabhiḥ daśabhiḥ śaraiḥ uddhūtā rajasaḥ vṛṣṭiḥ śara vṛṣṭiḥ tathā eva ca na dyauḥ na bhūmiḥ na diśaḥ prājñāyanta tathā gate śabda mātreṇa jānīmaḥ vayam te ca parasparam hata aśvāḥ hata sūtāḥ ca niśceṣṭāḥ rathinaḥ tadā hatān gajān samāśliṣya parvatān iva vājinaḥ tatas tu abhyavasṛtya eva saṃgrāmāt uttarām diśam atiṣṭhat āhave droṇaḥ vidhūmaḥ iva pāvakaḥ tam āji śīrṣāt ekāntam apakrāntam niśāmya tu samakampanta sainyāni pāṇḍavānām viśām pate bhrājamānam śriyā yuktam jvalantam iva tejasā droṇam dṛṣṭvā arayaḥ tresuḥ celuḥ mamluḥ ca māriṣa āhvayantam para anīkam prabhinnam iva vāraṇam na enam śaśaṃsire jetum dānavāḥ vāsavam yathā vismitāḥ ca abhavan ke cid ke cid āsan amarṣitāḥ vidhūya anye karān kruddhāḥ kareṣu eva nyapīḍayan apare daśanaiḥ oṣṭhān adaśan krodha mūrchitāḥ vyākṣipan āyudhān anye mamṛduḥ ca apare bhujān pāñcālāḥ tu viśeṣeṇa droṇa sāyaka pīḍitāḥ dṛṣṭvā droṇam mahā rāja samakampata pāṇḍavāḥ tatas pāṇḍavānām mahātman dṛṣṭvā droṇam dīpyamānam śara oghaiḥ tatas sarve sṛñjayāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ ca tatas virāṭa drupadau droṇam pratiyayuḥ raṇe tathā carantam saṃgrāme bhṛśam samara durjayam cedayaḥ ca mahā iṣvāsāḥ droṇam eva abhyayus yudhi teṣām drupada pautrāṇām trayāṇām niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ matsyān ca eva ajayat sarvān bhāradvājaḥ mahā rathaḥ droṇam prati mahā rāja virāṭaḥ ca eva saṃyuge tam nihatya iṣu varṣam tu droṇaḥ kṣatriya mardanaḥ tau śaraiḥ chādayām āsa virāṭa drupadau ubhau tatas droṇaḥ mahā rāja krodha amarṣa samanvitaḥ bhallābhyām bhṛśa tīkṣṇābhyām ciccheda tayoḥ tatas virāṭaḥ kupitaḥ samare tomarān daśa daśa cikṣepa ca śarān droṇasya vadha kāṅkṣayā śaktim ca drupadaḥ ghorām āyasām svarṇa bhūṣitām tatas bhallaiḥ su niśitaiḥ chittvā tān tomarān daśa śaktim kanaka vaiḍūryām droṇaḥ ciccheda sāyakaiḥ sa tābhyām arditaḥ vṛddhaḥ vṛddhābhyām krodha mūrchitaḥ tatas droṇaḥ su pītābhyām bhallābhyām ari mardanaḥ drupadam ca virāṭam ca praiṣīt vaivasvata kṣayam hateṣu triṣu vīreṣu drupadasya ca naptṛṣu pāñcāla rāja pautreṣu triṣu ca adbhuta karmasu droṇasya karma tat dṛṣṭvā kopa duḥkha samanvitaḥ śaśāpa rathinām madhye dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā manāḥ iṣṭāpūrtāt tathā kṣātrāt brāhmaṇyāt ca sa naśyatu droṇaḥ yasya adya mucyeta yaḥ vā droṇāt parāṅmukhaḥ āyāt droṇam saha anīkaḥ pāñcālyaḥ para vīra hā pāñcālāḥ tu ekatas droṇam abhyaghnan pāṇḍavāḥ anyatas duryodhanaḥ ca karṇaḥ ca śakuniḥ ca api saubalaḥ sodaryāḥ ca yathā mukhyāḥ te arakṣan droṇam āhave rakṣyamāṇa tathā droṇam samare taiḥ mahātmabhiḥ yatamānā api pāñcālāḥ na śekuḥ prativīkṣitum tatra akrudhyat bhīmasenaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnasya māriṣa viśeṣataḥ tu śapatham śapitvā rāja saṃsadi śara cāpa indhanaḥ droṇaḥ kṣatram dahati tejasā purā karoti niḥśeṣām pāṇḍavānām anīkinīm iti uktvā prāviśat kruddhaḥ droṇa anīkam vṛkodaraḥ dṛḍhaiḥ pūrṇa āyata utsṛṣṭaiḥ drāvayan tava vāhinīm atha udyamya gadām bhīmaḥ kāla daṇḍam iva antakaḥ sa aśva sūta dhvajam rājan droṇasya apothayat tadā sva bahūn yodhān vāyu vṛkṣān iva ojasā anyam tu ratham āsthāya droṇaḥ praharatām varaḥ vyūha dvāram samāsthāya yuddhāya samavasthitaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ api pāñcālyaḥ praviśya mahatīm camūm āsasāda raṇe droṇam tadā āsīt tumulam mahat na eva naḥ tādṛśam yuddham dṛṣṭa pūrvam na ca śrutam saṃsaktāni vyadṛśyanta ratha vṛndāni māriṣa hatāni ca vikīrṇāni śarīrāṇi śarīriṇām vimukhāḥ pṛṣṭhatas ca anye tāḍyante pārśvatas apare tathā saṃsakta yuddham tat abhavat bhṛśa dāruṇam atha saṃdhyā gataḥ sūryaḥ kṣaṇena samapadyata uvāca te tathā eva mahā rāja daṃśitāḥ raṇa mūrdhani saṃdhyā gatam sahasrāṃśum ādityam upatasthire dvaṃdvāni yāni tatra āsan saṃsaktāni purā udayāt rathaiḥ hayāḥ hayaiḥ nāgāḥ pādātāḥ ca api kuñjaraiḥ hayāḥ hayaiḥ samājagmuḥ pādātāḥ ca padātibhiḥ saṃsaktāḥ ca viyuktāḥ ca yodhāḥ saṃnyapatan raṇe te rātrau kṛta karmāṇaḥ śrāntāḥ sūryasya tejasā kṣudh pipāsā parīta aṅgāḥ visaṃjñāḥ bahavaḥ abhavan śaṅkha bherī mṛdaṅgānām kuñjarāṇām ca garjatām visphārita vikṛṣṭānām kārmukāṇām ca kūjatām dravatām ca padātīnām śastrāṇām vinipātyatām hayānām heṣatām ca eva rathānām ca nivartatām krośatām garjatām ca eva tat āsīt tumulam mahat nānā āyudha nikṛttānām ceṣṭatām āturaḥ svanaḥ bhūmau aśrūyata mahān tadā āsīt kṛpaṇam mahat patatām patitānām ca patti aśva ratha hastinām teṣu sarveṣu anīkeṣu vyatiṣakteṣu anekaśas sve svān jaghnuḥ pare svān ca sve parān ca parān pare vīra bāhu visṛṣṭāḥ ca yodheṣu ca gajeṣu ca asayaḥ pratyadṛśyanta vāsasām nejaneṣu iva udyata pratipiṣṭānām khaḍgānām vīra bāhubhiḥ saḥ eva śabdaḥ tad rūpaḥ vāsasām nijyatām iva nikṛṣṭa yuddham saṃsaktam mahat āsīt su dāruṇam gaja aśva kāya prabhavām nara deha pravāhinīm śastra matsya su saṃpūrṇām māṃsa śoṇita kardamām ārta nāda svanavatīm patākā vastra phenilām nadīm prāvartayan vīrāḥ para loka pravāhinīm śara śakti arditāḥ klāntāḥ rātri mūḍha alpa cetasaḥ viṣṭabhya sarva gātrāṇi vyatiṣṭhan gaja vājinaḥ saṃśuṣka vadanāḥ vīrāḥ śirobhiḥ cāru kuṇḍalaiḥ kravyāda saṃghaiḥ ākīrṇam mṛtaiḥ ardha mṛtaiḥ api katham cit avahan śrāntāḥ vepamānāḥ śara arditāḥ kula sattva bala upetāḥ vājinaḥ vāraṇa upamāḥ balam āsīt tadā sarvam ṛte droṇa arjunau ubhau tau eva āstām nilayanam tau ārta ayanam eva ca pāñcālānām ca saṃsaktam na prājñāyata kim cana antaka ākrīḍa sadṛśe bhīrūṇām bhaya vardhane pṛthivyām rāja vaṃśānām utthite mahati kṣaye na tatra karṇam na droṇam na arjunam na yudhiṣṭhiram na bhīmasenam na yamau na pāñcālyam na sātyakim na kṛpam madra rājam vā kṛtavarmāṇam eva ca na ca anyān na eva ca ātmānam na kṣitim na diśaḥ tathā paśyāma rājan saṃsaktān sainyena rajasā āvṛtān dvitīyām iva saṃprāptām amanyanta niśām tadā na jñāyante kauraveyāḥ na pāñcālāḥ na pāṇḍavāḥ na diśaḥ na divam na urvīm na samam viṣamam tathā aśobhanta yathā meghāḥ śāradāḥ cala vidyutaḥ hasta saṃsparśam āpannān parān vā api atha vā svakān nyapātayan tadā yuddhe narāḥ sma vijaya eṣiṇaḥ praśaśāma rajaḥ bhaumam śīghra tvāt anilasya ca tatra nāgāḥ hayāḥ yodhāḥ rathinaḥ atha padātayaḥ pārijāta vanāni iva vyarocan rudhira ukṣitāḥ tatas duryodhanaḥ karṇaḥ droṇaḥ duḥśāsanaḥ tathā pāṇḍavaiḥ samasajjanta caturbhiḥ caturaḥ rathāḥ vṛkodareṇa rādheyaḥ bhāradvājena ca arjunaḥ ratha ṛṣabhāṇām ugrāṇām saṃnipātam amānuṣam yatamānāḥ parākrāntāḥ paraspara jigīṣavaḥ jīmūtau iva gharma ante śara varṣaiḥ avākiran te rathān sūrya saṃkāśān āsthitāḥ puruṣa ṛṣabhāḥ aśobhanta yathā meghāḥ śāradāḥ samupasthitāḥ yodhāḥ te tu mahā rāja krodha amarṣa samanvitāḥ spardhinaḥ te mahā iṣvāsāḥ kṛta yatnāḥ dhanurdharāḥ abhyagacchan tathā anyonyam mattāḥ gaja vṛṣāḥ iva bāhubhiḥ caraṇaiḥ chinnaiḥ śirobhiḥ cāru kuṇḍalaiḥ kārmukaiḥ viśikhaiḥ prāsaiḥ khaḍgaiḥ paraśu paṭṭiśaiḥ nālīka kṣura nārācaiḥ nakharaiḥ śakti tomaraiḥ citraiḥ ca vividha ākāraiḥ śarīra āvaraṇaiḥ api amanuṣyaiḥ hayaiḥ trastaiḥ kṛṣyamāṇaiḥ tatas tatas vātāyamānaiḥ asakṛt hata vīraiḥ alaṃkṛtaiḥ vyajanaiḥ kaṅkaṭaiḥ ca eva dhvajaiḥ ca vinipātitaiḥ hāraiḥ kirīṭaiḥ mukuṭaiḥ uṣṇīṣaiḥ kiṅkiṇī gaṇaiḥ urasyaiḥ maṇibhiḥ niṣkaiḥ cūḍāmaṇibhiḥ eva ca āsīt āyodhanam tatra nabhaḥ tārā gaṇaiḥ iva apasavyam cakāra atha mādrī putraḥ te ātmajam kiran śara śataiḥ hṛṣṭaḥ tatra nādaḥ mahān abhūt apasavyam kṛtaḥ saṃkhye bhrātṛvyena ati amarṣiṇā sarvatas vinivārya enam śara jālena pīḍayan tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti nakulaḥ babhāṣe tanayam tava uvāca tasya apatata eva āśu bhallena amitra karśanaḥ mādrī sutaḥ śiraḥ yantuḥ sa śirastrāṇam acchinat na enam duḥśāsanaḥ sūtam na api kaḥ cana sainikaḥ hṛta uttamāṅgam āśu tvāt sahadevena buddhavan yadā tu a saṃgṛhīta tvāt prayānti aśvāḥ yathāsukham tatas duḥśāsanaḥ sūtam buddhavan gata cetasam sa hayān saṃnigṛhya ājau svayam haya viśāradaḥ yuyudhe rathinām śreṣṭhaḥ citram laghu ca suṣṭhu ca sahadevaḥ tu tān aśvān tīkṣṇaiḥ bāṇaiḥ avākirat pīḍyamānāḥ śaraiḥ ca āśu prādravan te tatas tatas sa raśmiṣu viṣakta tvāt utsasarja śarāsanam chidreṣu teṣu tam bāṇaiḥ mādrī putraḥ abhyavākirat vṛkodaraḥ tatas karṇam tribhiḥ bhallaiḥ samāhitaiḥ saṃnyavartata tam karṇaḥ saṃghaṭṭitaḥ iva uragaḥ bhīmam āvārayām āsa vikiran niśitān śarān abhisaṃśliṣṭayoḥ tatra tayoḥ āhava śauṇḍayoḥ bibheda āśu tadā rājñ tat adbhutam iva abhavat tatas bhīmasya rādheyaḥ gadām ādāya vīryavān avāsṛjat rathe tām tu bibheda gadayā gadām tatas bhīmaḥ punar gurum cikṣepa ādhiratheḥ gadām tām śaraiḥ daśabhiḥ karṇaḥ su puṅkhaiḥ su samāhitaiḥ pratyavidhyat punar ca anyaiḥ sā bhīmam punar āvrajat vyālī iva mantra abhihatā karṇa bāṇaiḥ abhidrutā papāta sārathiḥ ca asya mumoha gadayā hataḥ sa karṇe sāyakān aṣṭau vyasṛjat krodha mūrchitaḥ dhvaje śarāsane ca eva śarāvāpe ca bhārata karṇaḥ api anyat dhanuḥ gṛhya hema pṛṣṭham durāsadam ṛṣya varṇān jaghāna āśu tathā ubhau pārṣṇisārathī hariḥ yathā gireḥ śṛṅgam samākrāmat ariṃdamaḥ ācārya śiṣyau rāja indra kṛta praharaṇau yudhi laghu saṃdhāna yogābhyām rathayoḥ ca raṇena ca mohayantau manuṣyāṇām cakṣūṃṣi ca manāṃsi ca a dṛṣṭa pūrvam paśyantaḥ tat yuddham guru śiṣyayoḥ vicitrān pṛtanā madhye ratha mārgān udīryataḥ parākramam tayoḥ yodhāḥ dadṛśuḥ tam su vismitāḥ āmiṣa artham mahā rāja gagane śyenayoḥ iva yat yat cakāra droṇaḥ tu kuntī putra jigīṣayā tat tat pratijaghāna āśu prahasan tasya pāṇḍavaḥ mṛdu pūrvam abhūt yuddham divya astra vidvasoḥ dvayoḥ yadā droṇaḥ na śaknoti pāṇḍavasya viśeṣaṇe tatas prāduścakāra astram astra mārga viśāradaḥ aindram pāśupatam tvāṣṭram vāyavyam atha vāruṇam muktam muktam droṇa cāpāt tat jaghāna dhanaṃjayaḥ astrāṇi astraiḥ yadā tasya vidhivat dhanti pāṇḍavaḥ yat yat astram sa pārthāya prayuṅkte vijigīṣayā mene ca ātmānam adhikam pṛthivyām api bhārata tena śiṣyeṇa sarvebhyaḥ śastra vidbhyaḥ samantataḥ vāryamāṇaḥ tu pārthena tathā madhye mahātmanām tatas antarikṣe devāḥ ca gandharvāḥ ca sahasraśas ṛṣayaḥ siddha saṃghāḥ ca vyatiṣṭhanta didṛkṣayā tat
