apsarobhiḥ ākīrṇam yakṣa rākṣasa saṃkulam śrīmat ākāśam abhavat bhūyas megha ākulam yathā droṇasya stava saṃyuktāḥ pārthasya ca mahātmanaḥ visṛj astreṣu jvālayatsu diśaḥ daśa abruvan tatra siddhāḥ ca ṛṣayaḥ ca samāgatāḥ na eva idam mānuṣam yuddham na āsuram na ca rākṣasam vicitram idam āścaryam na naḥ dṛṣṭam na ca śrutam ati pāṇḍavam ācāryaḥ droṇam ca api ati pāṇḍavaḥ na anayoḥ antaram draṣṭum śakyam astreṇa kena cit jñānam ekastham ācārye jñānam yogaḥ ca pāṇḍave droṇe sauṣṭhavam ācārye lāghavam sauṣṭhavam tathā lakṣam ekastham ācārye lakṣam vedhaḥ ca pāṇḍave śaighryam ekastham ācārye śaighryam vedhaḥ ca pāṇḍave gatam ekastham ācārye gatam vedhaḥ ca pāṇḍave śauryam ekastham ācārye balam śauryam ca pāṇḍave na imau śakyau mahā iṣvāsau raṇe kṣepayitum paraiḥ iti abruvan mahā rāja dṛṣṭvā tau puruṣa ṛṣabhau antarhitāni bhūtāni prakāśāṇi ca saṃghaśas yadā droṇam mahā rāja viśeṣayati pāṇḍavaḥ tatas droṇaḥ brāhmam astram prāduścakre mahāmatiḥ tat astram saṃdhitam rājan ghora rūpam mahā āhave saṃtāpayan raṇe pārtham bhūtāni antarhitāni ca vavau ca viṣamaḥ vāyuḥ sāgarāḥ ca api cukṣubhuḥ tatas trāsaḥ mahān āsīt kuru pāṇḍava senayoḥ sarveṣām ca eva bhūtānām udyate astre mahātmanā brahmāstreṇa eva rāja indra tatas sarvam aśīśamat na ajñāyata tatas kim cit punar eva viśām pati droṇaḥ tyajya raṇe pārtham pāñcālān anvadhāvata arjunaḥ api raṇe droṇam tyaktvā prādrāvayat kurūn śara oghaiḥ atha tābhyām tu chāyā bhūtam mahā mṛdhe śara jālaiḥ samākīrṇe megha jālaiḥ iva ambare uvāca tasmin tathā vartamāne nara aśva gaja saṃkṣaye duḥśāsanaḥ mahā rāja dhṛṣṭadyumnam ayodhayat sa tu rukma ratha āsaktaḥ duḥśāsana śara arditaḥ amarṣāt te putrasya śaraiḥ vāhān avākirat na adṛśyata mahā rāja pārṣatasya śaraiḥ citaḥ duḥśāsanaḥ tu rāja indra pāñcālyasya mahātmanaḥ na aśakat pramukhe sthātum śara jāla prapīḍitaḥ sa tu duḥśāsanam bāṇaiḥ vimukhīkṛtya pārṣataḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ api rāja indra bhagnam dṛṣṭvā te ātmajam kiran śara sahasrāṇi droṇam eva abhyayāt raṇe sodaryāṇām trayaḥ ca eva te enam paryavārayan tam yamau pṛṣṭhatas anvaitām rakṣantau puruṣa ṛṣabhau droṇāya abhimukham yāntam dīpyamānam iva analam amarṣitāḥ sattvavantaḥ kṛtvā maraṇam agratas śuddha ātmānaḥ śuddha vṛttāḥ rājan svarga puraskṛtāḥ śukla abhijana karmāṇaḥ matimantaḥ janādhipāḥ na atra karṇī na nālīkaḥ na liptaḥ na ca vastakaḥ na sūcī kapiśaḥ na atra na gavāsthiḥ gajāsthikaḥ na cūlī baliśas tatra na yamī na api pāvakaḥ iṣuḥ āsīt na saṃśliṣṭaḥ na pūtiḥ na ca jihma gaḥ ṛjūni eva viśuddhāni sarve śastrāṇi adhārayan caturṇām te yodhānām taiḥ tribhiḥ pāṇḍavaiḥ saha dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ tu tān hitvā te rājan ratha ṛṣabhān yamābhyām vāritān dṛṣṭvā śīghra astraḥ droṇam abhyayāt nivāritāḥ tu te vīrāḥ tayoḥ puruṣa siṃhayoḥ dvābhyām dvābhyām yamau sārdham rathābhyām ratha puṃgavau dṛṣṭvā droṇāya pāñcālyam vrajantam yuddha durmadam yamābhyām tān ca saṃsaktān tad antaram upādravat duryodhanaḥ mahā rāja kiran śoṇita bhojanān tam sātyakiḥ śīghrataram punar eva abhyavartata hasamānau nṛ śārdūlau abhītau samagacchatām bālye vṛttāni sarvāṇi prīyamāṇau vicintya tau anyonyam prekṣamāṇau ca hasamānau punar punar atha duryodhanaḥ rājā sātyakim pratyabhāṣata priyam sakhim satatam garhayan vṛttam ātmanaḥ yat tvam mām abhisaṃdhatse tvām ca aham śini puṃgava tvam hi prāṇaiḥ priyataraḥ mama aham ca sadā tava smarāmi tāni sarvāṇi bālye vṛttāni yāni āvayoḥ tāni sarvāṇi jīrṇāni sāṃpratam āvayoḥ raṇa ajire tam tathāvādinam rājan sātyakiḥ pratyabhāṣata prahasan viśikhān tīkṣṇān udyamya parama astra vid na iyam sabhā rāja putra na ca ācārya niveśanam yatra krīḍitam asmābhiḥ tadā rājan samāgataiḥ kva sā krīḍā gatā mama bālye vai śini puṃgava uvāca tam tathāvādinam tatra rājānam mādhavaḥ abravīt evaṃvṛttam sadā kṣatram yat hanti iha gurūn api yadi te aham priyaḥ rājan jahi mām mā ciram kṛthāḥ tvad kṛte su kṛtān lokān gaccheyam bharata ṛṣabha na icchāmi etat aham draṣṭum mitrāṇām vyasanam mahat iti evam vyaktam ābhāṣya pratibhāṣya ca sātyakiḥ abhyayāt tūrṇam avyagraḥ nirapekṣaḥ viśām pate tam āyāntam abhiprekṣya pratyagṛhṇāt tava ātmajaḥ śaraiḥ ca avākirat rājan śaineyam tanayaḥ tava tatas pūrṇa āyata utsṛṣṭaiḥ sātvatam yuddha durmadam pañcāśatā punar ca ājau triṃśatā daśabhiḥ ca ha ākarṇa muktaiḥ niśitaiḥ vivyādha triṃśatā śaraiḥ tatas asya sa śaram cāpam kṣurapreṇa dvidhā karot sātyakiḥ vyasṛjat ca api śara śreṇīm sutasya te tām āpatantīm sahasā śara śreṇīm jighāṃsayā sātyakim ca trisaptatyā pīḍayām āsa vegitaḥ svarṇa puṅkhaiḥ śilā dhautaiḥ ākarṇāpūrṇa niḥsṛtaiḥ tasya saṃdadhataḥ ca iṣūn saṃhita iṣum ca kārmukam acchinat sātyakiḥ tūrṇam śaraiḥ ca eva abhyavīvṛṣat duryodhanaḥ mahā rāja dāśārha śara pīḍitaḥ visṛjan iṣu jālāni yuyudhāna ratham prati tatra iṣubhiḥ kṣipyamāṇaiḥ patadbhiḥ ca samantataḥ agamya rūpam ca śaraiḥ ākāśam samapadyata na tu tam marṣayām āsa bhīmasenaḥ mahā balaḥ abhyayāt tvaritaḥ karṇam visṛjan sāyakān bahūn tasya karṇaḥ śitān bāṇān pratihanya hasan iva dhanuḥ śarān ca ciccheda sūtam ca abhyahanat śaraiḥ bhīmasenaḥ tu saṃkruddhaḥ gadām ādāya pāṇḍavaḥ dhvajam dhanuḥ ca sūtam ca saṃmamarda āhave ripoḥ eka cakram ratham tasya tam ūhuḥ su ciram hayāḥ amṛṣyamāṇaḥ karṇaḥ tu bhīmasenam ayudhyata vividhaiḥ iṣu jālaiḥ ca nānā śastraiḥ ca saṃyuge pāñcālānām nara vyāghrān matsyānām ca nara ṛṣabhān ye naḥ prāṇāḥ śiraḥ ye naḥ ye naḥ yodhāḥ mahā balāḥ te ete dhārtarāṣṭreṣu viṣaktāḥ puruṣa ṛṣabhāḥ kim tiṣṭhata yathā mūḍhāḥ sarve vigata cetasaḥ jayantaḥ vadhyamānāḥ vā gatim iṣṭām gamiṣyatha jitvā ca bahubhiḥ yajñaiḥ yakṣyadhvam bhūri dakṣiṇaiḥ hatāḥ vā devasāt bhūtvā lokān prāpsyatha puṣkalān te rājñā coditāḥ vīrāḥ yotsyamānāḥ mahā rathāḥ caturdhā vahinīm kṛtvā tvaritāḥ droṇam abhyayus pāñcālāḥ tu ekatas droṇam abhyaghnan bahubhiḥ śaraiḥ āsan tu pāṇḍu putrāṇām trayaḥ ajihmāḥ mahā rathāḥ abhidrava arjuna kṣipram kurūn droṇāt apānuda tatas enam haniṣyanti pāñcālāḥ hata rakṣiṇam kauraveyān tatas pārthaḥ sahasā samupādravat pāñcālān eva tu droṇaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumna purogamān sasṛjuḥ tarasā vīrān pañcame ahani bhārata pāñcālānām tatas droṇaḥ api akarot kadanam mahat yathā kruddhaḥ raṇe śakraḥ dānavānām kṣayam purā droṇa astreṇa mahā rāja vadhyamānāḥ pare yudhi na atrasanta raṇe droṇāt sattvavantaḥ mahā rathāḥ vadhyamānāḥ mahā rāja pāñcālāḥ sṛñjayāḥ tathā tad tu utsāday pāñcālānām samantataḥ vadh saṃgrāme pāñcāleṣu mahātmanā udīryamāṇe droṇa astre pāṇḍavān bhayam āviśat dṛṣṭvā aśva nara saṃghānām vipulam ca kṣayam yudhi dṛṣṭvā ca nara nāga aśva pattīnām vipulam kṣayam pāṇḍaveyāḥ mahā rāja na āśaṃsuḥ vijayam tadā samiddhaḥ śiśira apāye dahan kakṣam iva analaḥ trastān kuntī sutān dṛṣṭvā droṇa sāyaka pīḍitān matimān śreyase yuktaḥ keśavaḥ arjunam abravīt na eṣa yuddhena saṃgrāme jetum śakyaḥ katham cana sa dhanuḥ dhanvinām śreṣṭhaḥ devaiḥ api sa vāsavaiḥ api vṛtrahanā yuddhe ratha yūthapa yūthapaḥ āsthīyatām jaye yogaḥ dharmam utsṛjya pāṇḍava yathā vaḥ saṃyuge sarvān na hanyāt rukmavāhanaḥ tam hatam saṃyuge kaḥ cit asmai śaṃsatu mānavaḥ jaghāna gadayā rājan aśvatthāmānam iti uta aśvatthāmā hataḥ iti śabdam uccais cakāra ha kṛtvā manasi tam bhīmaḥ mithyā vyāhṛtavan tadā śaṅkamānaḥ sa tat mithyā vīrya jñaḥ sva sutasya vai sa labdhvā cetanām droṇaḥ kṣaṇena eva samāśvasat sa pārṣatam abhidrutya jighāṃsuḥ mṛtyum ātmanaḥ avākirat sahasreṇa tīkṣṇānām kaṅka pattriṇām tam vai viṃśati sāhasrāḥ pāñcālānām nara ṛṣabhāḥ tathā carantam saṃgrāme sarvatas vyakiran śaraiḥ taiḥ śaraiḥ āvṛtam droṇam na apaśyāma mahā ratham bhāskaram jaladaiḥ ruddham varṣāsu iva viśām pate vidhūya tān bāṇa gaṇān pāñcālānām mahā rathaḥ tatas prāduṣkarot droṇaḥ brāhmam astram paraṃtapaḥ vadhāya teṣām śūrāṇām pāñcālānām amarṣitaḥ śirāṃsi apātayat ca api pāñcālānām mahā mṛdhe tathā eva parigha ākārān bāhūn kanaka bhūṣaṇān te vadhyamānāḥ samare bhāradvājena pārthivāḥ medinyām anvakīryanta vāta nunnāḥ iva drumāḥ kuñjarāṇām ca patatām haya oghānām ca bhārata agamya rūpā pṛthivī māṃsa śoṇita kardamā hatvā viṃśati sāhasrān pāñcālānām ratha vrajān vasudānasya bhallena śiraḥ kāyāt apāharat punar pañcaśatān matsyān ṣaṣ sahasrān ca sṛñjayān hastinām ayutam hatvā jaghāna aśva ayutam punar kṣatriyāṇām abhāvāya dṛṣṭvā droṇam avasthitam ṛṣayaḥ abhyāgaman tūrṇam havyavāha purogamāḥ vasiṣṭhaḥ kaśyapaḥ atriḥ ca brahma lokam ninīṣavaḥ sikatāḥ pṛśnayaḥ gargāḥ bālakhilyāḥ marīcipāḥ bhṛgavaḥ aṅgirasaḥ ca eva sūkṣmāḥ ca anye mahā ṛṣayaḥ nyasya āyudham raṇe droṇa sametya asmān avasthitān nyasya āyudham amogha iṣo tiṣṭha vartmani śāśvate paripūrṇaḥ ca kālaḥ te vastum loke adya mānuṣe brahmāstreṇa tvayā dagdhāḥ an astra jñāḥ narāḥ bhuvi yat etat īdṛśam vipra kṛtam karma na sādhu tat nyasya āyudham raṇe kṣipram droṇa mā tvam ciram kṛthāḥ mā pāpiṣṭhataram karma kariṣyasi punar dvija iti teṣām vacaḥ śrutvā bhīmasena vacaḥ ca tat dhṛṣṭadyumnam ca saṃprekṣya raṇe sa vimanāḥ bhavat trayāṇām api lokānām aiśvarya arthe katham cana tasmāt tam paripapraccha na anyam kam cit viśeṣataḥ tasmin tasya hi satya āśā bālyāt prabhṛti pāṇḍave tatas niṣpāṇḍavām urvīm kariṣyantam yudhām patim droṇam jñātvā dharmarājam govindaḥ vyathitaḥ abravīt satyam bravīmi te senā vināśam samupaiṣyati sa bhavān trātu naḥ droṇāt satyāt jyāyaḥ anṛtam bhavet anṛtam jīvitasya arthe vadan na spṛśyate anṛtaiḥ kāminīṣu vivāheṣu gavām arthe tathā dhane brāhmaṇa abhyavapattau ca anṛte na asti pātakam śrutvā eva tam mahā rāja vadha upāyam mahātmanaḥ gāhamānasya te senām mālavasya indravarmaṇaḥ aśvatthāmā iti vikhyātaḥ gajaḥ śakra gaja upamaḥ nūnam na aśraddadhat vākyam eṣa me puruṣa ṛṣabhaḥ sa tvam govinda vākyāni mānayasva jaya eṣiṇaḥ droṇāya nihatam śaṃsa rājñ śāradvatī sutam tasya tat vacanam śrutvā kṛṣṇa vākya pracoditaḥ tasya pūrvam rathaḥ pṛthvyāḥ catur aṅgulaḥ uttaraḥ babhūva evam tu tena ukte tasya vāhaḥ aspṛśat mahīm yudhiṣṭhirāt tu tat vākyam śru droṇaḥ mahā rathaḥ āgaskṛtam iva ātmānam pāṇḍavānām mahātmanām ṛṣi vākyam ca manvānaḥ śrutvā ca nihatam sutam yoddhum na aśaknuvat rājan yathāpūrvam ariṃdama tam dṛṣṭvā parama udvignam śoka upahata cetasam pāñcāla rājasya sutaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ samādravat labdhaḥ droṇa vināśāya samiddhāt havyavāhanāt dṛḍha jyam ajaram divyam śarān ca āśīviṣa upamān saṃdadhe kārmuke tasmin śaram āśīviṣa upamam droṇam jighāṃsuḥ pāñcālyaḥ mahā jvālam iva analam tasya rūpam śarasya āsīt dhanuḥ jyā maṇḍala antare pārṣatena parāmṛṣṭam jvalantam iva tat dhanuḥ anta kālam iva prāptam menire vīkṣya sainikāḥ tam iṣum saṃhitam tena bhāradvājaḥ pratāpavān dṛṣṭvā amanyata dehasya kāla paryāyam āgatam tatas sa yatnam ātiṣṭhat ācāryaḥ tasya vāraṇe na ca asya astrāṇi rāja indra prādurāsan mahātmanaḥ tasya tu ahāni catvāri kṣapā ca ekā asyatas gatā tasya ca ahnaḥ tri bhāgena kṣayam jagmuḥ patatriṇaḥ sa śara kṣayam āsādya putra śokena ca arditaḥ vividhānām ca divyānām astrāṇām aprasanna tām utsraṣṭu kāmaḥ śastrāṇi vipra vākya abhicoditaḥ tejasā preryamāṇaḥ ca yuyudhe saḥ ati mānuṣam atha anyat sa samādāya divyam āṅgirasam dhanuḥ śarān ca brahmadaṇḍa ābhān dhṛṣṭadyumnam ayodhayat tatas tam śara varṣeṇa mahatā samavākirat vyaśātayat ca saṃkruddhaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam amarṣaṇaḥ tatas ca pārṣataḥ rājan samākṛṣya dhanuḥ mahat śaram mumoca niśitam bhāradvāja jighāṃsayā tam śaram śatadhā ca asya droṇaḥ ciccheda sāyakaiḥ dhvajam dhanuḥ ca niśitaiḥ sārathim ca api apātayat dhṛṣṭadyumna prahas anyat punar ādā kārmuka yat ca asya bāṇam vikṛtam dhanūṃṣi ca viśām pate sarvam saṃchidya durdharṣaḥ gadām khaḍgam atha api ca dhṛṣṭadyumnam tatas avidhyat navabhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ jīvitānta karaiḥ kruddhaḥ kruddha rūpam paraṃtapaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumna rathasya aśvān sva ratha aśvaiḥ mahā rathaḥ te miśrāḥ bahu aśobhanta javanāḥ vāta raṃhasaḥ pārāvata savarṇāḥ ca śoṇāḥ ca bharata ṛṣabha tathā rejuḥ mahā rāja miśritāḥ raṇa mūrdhani praṇāśayat ameya ātmā dhṛṣṭadyumnasya sa dvijaḥ uttamām āpadam prāpya gadām vīraḥ parāmṛśat tā asya viśikha tīkṣṇaiḥ kṣip mahat ratha nijaghāna śaraiḥ droṇaḥ kruddhaḥ satya parākramaḥ tām dṛṣṭvā tu nara vyāghraḥ droṇena nihatām śaraiḥ asaṃśayam tathābhūte pāñcālyaḥ sādhu amanyata vadham ācārya mukhyasya prāpta kālam mahātmanaḥ cikīrṣuḥ duṣkaram karma dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ mahā rathaḥ iyeṣa vakṣaḥ bhettum ca bhāradvājasya saṃyuge śoṇānām jaghana ardheṣu tat sainyāḥ samapūjayan tiṣṭhataḥ yuga pālīṣu śoṇān api adhitiṣṭhataḥ kṣipram śyena car yathā eva āmiṣa gṛddhin tadvat āsīt abhīsāraḥ droṇam prārthayataḥ raṇe tasya aśvān ratha śaktyā asau tadā kruddhaḥ parākramī sarvān ekaikaśas droṇaḥ kapota ābhān ajīghanat te hatāḥ nyapatan bhūmau dhṛṣṭadyumnasya vājinaḥ śoṇāḥ ca paryamucyanta ratha bandhāt viśām pate tān hayān nihatān dṛṣṭvā dvijāgryeṇa sa pārṣataḥ na amṛṣyata yudhām śreṣṭhaḥ yājñaseniḥ mahā rathaḥ virathaḥ sa gṛhītvā tu khaḍgam khaḍgabhṛtām varaḥ tasya rūpam babhau rājan bhāradvājam jighāṃsataḥ yathā rūpam param viṣṇoḥ hiraṇyakaśipoḥ vadhe saḥ acarat vividhān mārgān prakārān ekaviṃśatim darśayām āsa kauravya pārṣataḥ vicaran raṇe bhrāntam udbhrāntam āviddham āplutam prasṛtam sṛtam parivṛttam nivṛttam ca khaḍgam carma ca dhārayan saṃpātam samudīrṇam ca darśayām āsa pārṣataḥ bhāratam kauśikam ca eva sātvatam ca eva śikṣayā carataḥ tasya tān mārgān vicitrān khaḍga carmiṇaḥ vyasmayanta raṇe yodhāḥ devatāḥ ca samāgatāḥ khaḍgam carma ca saṃbādhe dhṛṣṭadyumnasya sa dvijaḥ te tu vaitastikāḥ nāma śarāḥ hi āsanna ghātinaḥ nikṛṣṭa yuddhe droṇasya na anyeṣām santi te śarāḥ ṛte śāradvatāt pārthāt droṇeḥ vaikartanāt tathā pradyumna yuyudhānābhyām abhimanyoḥ ca te śarāḥ atha asya iṣum samādhatta dṛḍham parama saṃśitam antevāsinam ācāryaḥ jighāṃsuḥ putra saṃmitam tam śaraiḥ daśan tīkṣṇaiḥ ciccheda śini puṃgava paśyataḥ tasya tān mārgān vicitrān khaḍga carmaṇi droṇa karṇa antara gatam kṛpasya api ca bhārata apaśyetām mahātmānau viṣvaksena dhanaṃjayau apūjayetām vārṣṇeyam bruvāṇau sādhu sādhu iti dhanaṃjayaḥ tatas kṛṣṇam abravīt paśya keśava ācārya vara mukhyānām madhye krīḍan madhūdvahaḥ ānandayati mām bhūyas sātyakiḥ satya vikramaḥ mādrī putrau ca bhīmam ca rājānam ca yudhiṣṭhiram mahā rathān upakrīḍan vṛṣṇīnām kīrti vardhanaḥ ajayyam samare dṛṣṭvā sādhu sādhu iti sātvatam uvāca sātvatasya tu tat karma dṛṣṭvā duryodhana ādayaḥ śaineyam sarvatas kruddhāḥ vārayām āsuḥ añjasā kṛpa karṇau ca samare putrāḥ ca te māriṣa śaineyam tvarayā abhyetya vinighnan niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tatas rājā mādrī putrau ca pāṇḍavau bhīmasenaḥ ca balavān sātvatam paryavārayan karṇaḥ ca śara varṣeṇa gautamaḥ ca mahā rathaḥ tām vṛṣṭim sahasā rājan utthitām ghora rūpiṇīm vārayām āsa śaineyaḥ yodhayan tān mahā rathān teṣām astrāṇi divyāni saṃhitāni mahātmanām saṃprahṛṣṭa acyutaḥ dṛṣṭvā sādhu sādhu iti pūjayan tam yaudhāḥ ca abhavan sarve karmaṇā anena pūjayan evam uktvā mahā rāja vāsudevam dhanaṃjayaḥ prāyāt tava balam jiṣṇuḥ bhāradvāja ratham prati tatra āsīt bhairavaḥ nādaḥ tāvakānām jaya eṣiṇām samabhidravatām pārtham daityānām iva vāsavam tatra akarot mahā rāja mahīm śoṇita kardamām prācchinat ca uttamāṅgāni pārthaḥ aśva nara dantinām krūram āyodhanam jajñe tasmin rāja samāgame hastānām uttamāṅgānām kārmukāṇām ca bhārata chatrāṇām ca apaviddhānām cāmarāṇām ca saṃyuge rāśayaḥ sma vyadṛśyanta tatra tatra raṇa ajire sādibhiḥ ca hataiḥ śūraiḥ saṃkīrṇā vasudhā bhavat bāṇa pāta nikṛttāḥ tu yodhāḥ te kuru sattama ceṣṭantaḥ vividhāḥ ceṣṭāḥ vyadṛśyanta mahā āhave abravīt kṣatriyān tatra dharmarājaḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ abhidravata saṃyattāḥ kumbhayonim mahā rathāḥ eṣa vai pārṣataḥ vīraḥ bhāradvājena saṃgataḥ ghaṭate ca yathāśakti bhāradvājasya nāśane yādṛśāni hi rūpāṇi dṛśyante naḥ mahā raṇe adya droṇam raṇe kruddhaḥ pātayiṣyati pārṣataḥ te yūyam sahitāḥ bhūtvā kumbhayonim parīpsata yudhiṣṭhira samājñaptāḥ sṛñjayānām mahā rathāḥ abhyadravanta saṃyattāḥ bhāradvājam jighāṃsavaḥ tān samāpatataḥ sarvān bhāradvājaḥ mahā rathaḥ vavuḥ vātāḥ sa nirghātāḥ trāsayantaḥ varūthinīm dīpayatī iva tāpena śaṃsatī iva mahat bhayam jajvaluḥ ca eva śastrāṇi bhāradvājasya māriṣa rathāḥ svananti ca atyartham hayāḥ ca aśrūṇi avāsṛjan hata ojāḥ iva ca api āsīt bhāradvājaḥ mahā rathaḥ prāsphurat nayanam ca asya dakṣiṇaḥ bāhuḥ eva ca vimanāḥ ca abhavat yuddhe dṛṣṭvā pārṣatam agratas ṛṣīṇām brahma vādānām svargasya gamanam prati tatas caturdiśam sainyaiḥ drupadasya abhisaṃvṛtaḥ hatvā viṃśati sāhasrān kṣatriyān ari mardanaḥ daśa ayutāni tīkṣṇa agraiḥ avadhīt viśikhaiḥ śitaiḥ saḥ atiṣṭhat āhave yattaḥ vidhūmaḥ iva pāvakaḥ kṣatriyāṇām abhāvāya brāhmam ātmānam āsthitaḥ pāñcālyam viratham bhīmaḥ hata sarva āyudham vaśī aviṣaṇṇam mahātmānam tvaramāṇaḥ samabhyayāt saṃrabdhaḥ ca śarān asyan droṇam durvāraṇam raṇe vivārayiṣuḥ ācāryam śara varṣaiḥ avākirat tau nyavārayatām śreṣṭhau saṃrabdhau raṇa śobhinaḥ udīrayetām brāhmāṇi divyāni astrāṇi anekaśas sa mahā astraiḥ mahā rāja droṇam ācchādayat raṇe nihatya sarvāṇi astrāṇi bhāradvājasya pārṣataḥ sa vasātīn śibīn ca eva vāhlīkān kauravān api rakṣiṣyamāṇān saṃgrāme droṇam vyadhamat acyutaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ tadā rājan gabhastibhiḥ iva aṃśumant babhau pracchādayan āśāḥ śara jālaiḥ samantataḥ tasya droṇaḥ dhanuḥ chittvā viddhvā ca enam śilīmukhaiḥ marmāṇi abhyahanat bhūyas sa vyathām paramām agāt tatas bhīmaḥ dṛḍha krodhaḥ droṇasya āśliṣya tam ratham sva karmabhiḥ asaṃtuṣṭāḥ na sma kṣatram kṣayam vrajet ahiṃsā sarva bhūteṣu dharmam jyāyastaram viduḥ tasya ca brāhmaṇaḥ mūlam bhavān ca brahma vittamaḥ śvapāka vat mleccha gaṇān hatvā ca anyān pṛthagvidhān bharanti hi sutān dārān tvad vat ajñāna mohitāḥ ajñānāt mūḍha vat brahman putra dāra dhana īpsayā idānīm tiṣṭha durbuddhe na me jīvan gamiṣyasi yasya arthe śastram ādāya yam apekṣya ca jīvasi sa ca adya patitaḥ śete pṛṣṭena āveditaḥ tava dharmarājena tat vākyam na atiśaṅkitum arhasi saṃnyāsāya śarīrasya yokṣyamāṇaḥ sa vai dvijaḥ sarvāṇi astrāṇi dharma ātmā hātu kāmaḥ abhyabhāṣata karṇa duryodhanau rājñ tvaramāṇaḥ parākramī saṃgrāme kriyatām yatnaḥ bravīmi eṣa punar punar raṇe kṛtaḥ mayā yatnaḥ yat mā brūtha sadā sadā pāṇḍavebhyaḥ śivam vaḥ astu śastram abhyutsṛjāmi aham utsṛjāmi eva vai prāṇān divam gacchāmi sāṃpratam tasya tat chidram ājñāya dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ samutthitaḥ hāhākṛtāni bhūtāni mānuṣāṇi itarāṇi ca droṇam tathāgatam dṛṣṭvā dhṛṣṭadyumna vaśam gatam hāhākāram bhṛśam cakruḥ aho dhik iti ca bruvan droṇaḥ api śastrāṇi utsṛjya paramam sāmyam āsthitaḥ tathā uktvā yogam āsthāya jyotiḥ bhūtaḥ mahā tapāḥ purāṇam puruṣam viṣṇum jagāma manasā param nimīlita akṣaḥ sattva sthaḥ nikṣipya hṛdi dhāraṇām om iti ekākṣaram brahma jyotiḥ bhūtaḥ mahā tapāḥ nirāvaraṇam ācāryam paśyāmaḥ tad anantaram divam ākrāmat ācāryaḥ sadbhiḥ saha durākramam mūrdhānam yasya nirbhidya jyotiḥ rājan mahātmanaḥ ekāgram iva ca āsīt hi jyotirbhiḥ pūritam nabhaḥ samapadyata ca arka ābhe bhāradvāja niśākare āsīt kilakilā śabdaḥ prahṛṣṭānām divaukasām vayam eva tadā adrākṣma pañca mānuṣa yonayaḥ yoga yuktam mahātmānam gacchantam paramām gatim aham dhanaṃjayaḥ pārthaḥ kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ dvijaḥ vāsudevaḥ ca vārṣṇeyaḥ dharmarājaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ gatim paramikām prāptam a jānantaḥ nṛ yonayaḥ na apaśyan gacchamānam hi tam sārdham ṛṣi puṃgavaiḥ ācāryam yogam āsthāya brahma lokam ariṃdamam vitunna aṅgam śara śataiḥ nyasta āyudham asṛj kṣaram vikṛṣya pārṣataḥ khaḍgam krodha amarṣa vaśam gataḥ prākrośan pāṇḍavāḥ sarve phalgunaḥ ca āplutaḥ rathāt krośatsu pāṇḍaveyeṣu anudhāvati phalgune vikṛtaḥ sarva bhūtasya brahma bhūtam parāmṛśat dhikkṛtaḥ pārṣataḥ tam tu sarva bhūtaiḥ parāmṛśat kim cit abruvataḥ kāyāt vicakarta asinā śiraḥ harṣeṇa mahatā yuktaḥ bhāradvāje nipātite ākarṇa palitaḥ śyāmaḥ vayasā aśīti pañcakaḥ uktavan ca mahā bāhuḥ kuntī putraḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ vāhayitvā ratham tatra mā droṇam ghātayiṣyasi jīvantam ānaya ācāryam mā vadhīḥ drupada ātmaja krośamāne arjune ca eva pārthiveṣu ca sarvaśas dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ avadhīt droṇam ratha talpe nara ṛṣabham śoṇitena pariklinnaḥ rathāt bhūmim ariṃdamaḥ evam tam nihatam saṃkhye dadṛśe sainikaḥ janaḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ tu tat rājan bhāradvāja śiraḥ mahat tāvakānām mahā iṣvāsaḥ pramukhe tat samākṣipat te tu dṛṣṭvā śiraḥ rājan bhāradvājasya tāvakāḥ rathāt nipatitam droṇam ācāryam brāhmaṇam gurum palāyana kṛta utsāhāḥ dudruvuḥ sarvatodiśam aham eva tadā adrākṣam droṇasya nidhanam nṛpa ṛṣeḥ prasādāt kṛṣṇasya satyavatyāḥ sutasya ca catvāraḥ te ca mānuṣāḥ agneḥ iva śikhām dīptām ulkām prajvalitām iva apaśyāma divam stabdhvā mahimānam mahātmanaḥ vidhūmām iva saṃyāntam ulkām prajvalitām iva apaśyāma divam stabdhvā gacchantam tam mahā dyutim hate droṇe nirutsāhān kurūn pāṇḍava sṛñjayāḥ nihatāḥ haya bhūyiṣṭhāḥ saṃgrāme niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ ubhayena eva te hīnāḥ na avindan dhṛtim ātmanaḥ anvicchantaḥ śarīram tu bhāradvājasya pārthivāḥ udatiṣṭhan uruṇḍānām sahasrāṇi ekaviṃśatiḥ ācchinnāḥ paṭṭasaiḥ khaḍgaiḥ prāsaiḥ ca bharata ṛṣabha hāhākāreṇa mahatā śastra saṃtāpa tāpitān pradhāna hata bhūyiṣṭhāḥ kṛta cintāḥ palāyane te ca yaudhāḥ mahā rāja nirutsāhāḥ tadā abhavan rathinaḥ aśva gaja sthāḥ ca pādātāḥ ca viśām pate nihatāḥ hata bhūyiṣṭhāḥ mṛtāḥ iva hata prabhāḥ tāvakānām ratha śreṣṭhāḥ udhvastāḥ iva bhasmanā pāṇḍavāḥ tu jayam labdhvā paratra ca mahat yaśaḥ bāṇa śabda ravān cakruḥ siṃhanādān ca puṣkalān bhīmasenaḥ tatas rājan dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ ca pārṣataḥ abravīt ca tadā bhīmaḥ pārṣatam śatru tāpanam bhūyas aham tvām vijayinam pariṣvakṣyāmi pārṣata sūtaputre hate pāpe dhārtarāṣṭre ca saṃyuge etāvat uktvā bhīmaḥ tu harṣeṇa mahatā yutaḥ bāhu śabdena pṛthivīm kampayām āsa pāṇḍavaḥ tasya śabdena vitrastāḥ prādravan tāvakāḥ yudhi pāṇḍavāḥ tu mudā yuktāḥ siṃhanādam pracakrire prādravan te sutān dṛṣṭvā sumukham ca eva pārṣatam kṣatra dharmam samutsṛjya palāyana parāyaṇāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ tu jayam labdhvā hṛṣṭāḥ hi asan viśām pate tatas droṇe hate rājan kuravaḥ śastra pīḍitāḥ hata pravīrāḥ vidhvastāḥ bhṛśam śoka parāyaṇāḥ udīrṇān ca parān dṛṣṭvā hṛṣyamāṇān punar punar aśru pūrṇa īkṣaṇāḥ trastāḥ dīnāḥ hi āsan viśām pate vicetasaḥ hata utsāhāḥ kaśmala abhihata ojasaḥ rajasvalā vepamānā vīkṣamāṇā diśaḥ daśa aśru kaṇṭhāḥ yathā daityāḥ hiraṇyākṣe purā hate sa taiḥ parivṛtaḥ rājā trastaiḥ kṣudra mṛgaiḥ iva kṣudh pipāsā pariśrāntāḥ te yodhāḥ te bhārata ādityena ca saṃtaptāḥ bhṛśam vimanasaḥ abhavan amarṣaṇīyam tat dṛṣṭvā bhāradvājasya pātanam trasta rūpatarāḥ rājan kauravāḥ prādravan bhayāt hatam rukmaratham dṛṣṭvā prādravat sahitaḥ rathaiḥ varūthinīm vegavatīm vidrutām sa patākinīm parigṛhya mahā senām sūtaputraḥ apayāt bhayāt ratha nāga aśva kalilām puraskṛtya tu vāhinīm madrāṇām īśvaraḥ śalyaḥ vīkṣamāṇaḥ apayāt bhayāt hata pravīraiḥ bhūyiṣṭham dvipaiḥ bahu padātibhiḥ vṛtaḥ śāradvataḥ agacchat kaṣṭam kaṣṭam iti bruvan bhoja anīkena śiṣṭena kaliṅga āraṭṭa bāhlikaiḥ kṛtavarmā vṛtaḥ rājan prāyāt su javanaiḥ hayaiḥ ulūkaḥ prādravat tatra dṛṣṭvā droṇam nipātitam darśanīyaḥ yuvā ca eva śaurye ca kṛta lakṣaṇaḥ duḥśāsanaḥ bhṛśa udvignaḥ prādravat gaja saṃvṛtaḥ rathānām ayutam gṛhya tri sāhasrān ca dantinaḥ vṛṣasenaḥ apayāt tūrṇam dṛṣṭvā droṇam nipātitam gaja aśva ratha saṃyuktaḥ vṛtaḥ ca eva padātibhiḥ duryodhanaḥ mahā rāja prāyāt tatra mahā rathaḥ saṃśaptaka balam gṛhya hata śeṣam kirīṭinā suśarmā prādravat rājan dṛṣṭvā droṇam nipātitam gajān rathān samāruhya parasya api hayān janāḥ prādravan sarvatas saṃkhye dṛṣṭvā rukmaratham hatam codayantaḥ ca sainyāni svasrīyān ca tathā apare tatas duryodhanaḥ rājā aśvatthāmānam abravīt prakīrṇa keśāḥ vidhvastāḥ na dvau ekatra dhāvataḥ na idam asti iti puruṣāḥ hata utsāhāḥ hata ojasaḥ utsṛjya kavacān anye prādravan tāvakāḥ vibho dhuryān pramucya tu rathāt hata sūtān su alaṃkṛtān tasya āsīt su mahat yuddham śikhaṇḍi pramukhaiḥ gaṇaiḥ prabhadrakaiḥ ca pāñcālaiḥ cedibhiḥ ca sa kekayaiḥ hatvā bahuvidhām senām pāṇḍūnām yuddha durmadaḥ dravamāṇam balam dṛṣṭvā palāyana kṛtakṣaṇam dravamāṇām ca rāja indra na avasthāpayase raṇe tvam ca api na yathāpūrvam prakṛti sthaḥ narādhipa karṇa prabhṛtayaḥ ca ime na avatiṣṭhanti pārthivāḥ etām avasthām saṃprāptam tat mama ācakṣva kaurava ghoram apriyam ākhyātum na aśakat pārthiva ṛṣabhaḥ bāṣpeṇa pihitaḥ dṛṣṭvā droṇaputram rathe sthitam tatas śāradvatam rājā sa vrīḍam idam abravīt atha śāradvataḥ rājan ārtim gacchan punar punar śaśaṃsa droṇaputrāya yathā droṇaḥ nipātitaḥ uvāca vayam droṇam puraskṛtya pṛthivyām pravaram ratham prāvartayāma saṃgrāmam pāñcālaiḥ eva kevalaiḥ tatas pravṛtte saṃgrāme vimiśrāḥ kuru somakāḥ vartamāne tathā yuddhe kṣīyamāṇeṣu saṃyuge dhārtarāṣṭreṣu saṃkruddhaḥ pitā te astram udairayat tatas droṇaḥ brāhma astram vikurvāṇaḥ nara ṛṣabhaḥ ahanat śātravān bhallaiḥ śataśas atha sahasraśas pāṇḍavāḥ kekaya matsya pāñcālāḥ ca viśeṣataḥ saṃkhye droṇa ratham prāpya vyanaśan kāla coditāḥ sahasram ratha siṃhānām dvi sāhasram ca dantinām droṇaḥ brahmāstra nirdagdham preṣayām āsa mṛtyave ākarṇa palitaḥ śyāmaḥ vayasā aśīti pañcakaḥ raṇe paryacarat droṇaḥ vṛddhaḥ ṣoḍaśa varṣa vat kliśyamāneṣu sainyeṣu vadhyamāneṣu rājsu amarṣa vaśam āpannāḥ pāñcālāḥ vimukhāḥ abhavan divyam astram vikurvāṇaḥ babhūva arkaḥ iva uditaḥ sa madhyam prāpya pāṇḍūnām śara raśmiḥ pratāpavān te dahyamānāḥ droṇena sūryeṇa iva virājatā dagdha vīryāḥ nirutsāhāḥ babhūvuḥ gata cetasaḥ tān dṛṣṭvā pīḍay bāṇaiḥ droṇena madhusūdanaḥ jaya eṣī pāṇḍu putrāṇām idam vacanam abravīt na eṣa jātu paraiḥ śakyaḥ jetum śastrabhṛtām vara api vṛtrahanā saṃkhye ratha yūthapa yūthapaḥ te yūyam dharmam utsṛjya jayam rakṣata pāṇḍavāḥ jaye hi yatamānānām śrīḥ dharmaḥ ca pravartate yathā vaḥ saṃyuge sarvān na hanyāt rukmavāhanaḥ hatam tam saṃyuge kaḥ cit ākhyātu asmai mṛṣā naraḥ hatam vā api ahatam vā ājau tvām pitā putra vatsalaḥ aśvatthāmānam āha idam hataḥ kuñjaraḥ iti uta bhīma giri varṣman mālava indravarman putraḥ te dayitaḥ nityam śaḥ aśvatthāmā nipātitaḥ śete vinihataḥ bhūmau vane siṃha śiśuḥ yathā sa tvām nihatam ākrandan kṛtvā tvad nāma pīḍitaḥ tam dṛṣṭvā parama udvignam śoka upahata cetasam pāñcāla rājasya sutaḥ krūra karmā samādravat tad dṛṣṭvā vihita mṛtyum loka tattva vicakṣaṇa divyāni astrāṇi atha utsṛjya raṇe prāyas upāviśat tatas asya keśān savyena gṛhītvā pāṇinā tadā pārṣataḥ krośamānānām vīrāṇām acchinat śiraḥ udyam bāhū tvaritaḥ bruvāṇaḥ ca punar punar jīvantam ānaya ācāryam mā vadhīḥ iti dharma vid sainikāḥ ca tatas sarve prādravanta bhaya arday uvāca krodham āhārayat tīvram pada āhataḥ iva uragaḥ tatas kruddhaḥ raṇe drauṇiḥ bhṛśam jajvāla māriṣa uvāca adharmeṇa hatam śrutvā dhṛṣṭadyumnena saṃjaya brāhmaṇam pitaram vṛddham aśvatthāmā kim abravīt śūraḥ ca kṛta vidyaḥ ca tejasā jvalana upamaḥ yat abravīt tadā sūta tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya yaḥ veda divyāni astrāṇi sarva śastrabhṛtām varaḥ mānuṣam vāruṇa āgneyam brāhmam astram ca vīryavān aindram nārāyaṇam ca eva yasmin nityam pratiṣṭhitam tam adharmeṇa dharmiṣṭham dhṛṣṭadyumnena saṃjaya śrutvā nihatam ācāryam aśvatthāmā kim abravīt yena rāmāt avāpya iha dhanurvedam mahātmanā proktāni astrāṇi divyāni putrāya guru kāṅkṣiṇe ācāryāṇām bhavanti eva rahasyāni mahātmanām tāni putrāya vā dadyuḥ śiṣyāya anugatāya vā sa śilpam prāpya tat sarvam sa viśeṣam ca saṃjaya śūraḥ śāradvatī putraḥ saṃkhye droṇāt anantaraḥ rāmasya anumataḥ śāstre puraṃdara samaḥ yudhi asyatā yena saṃgrāme dharaṇī abhinipīḍitā mahā udadhiḥ iva akṣobhyaḥ rāmaḥ dāśarathiḥ yathā tam adharmeṇa dharmiṣṭham dhṛṣṭadyumnena saṃyuge śrutvā nihatam ācāryam aśvatthāmā kim abravīt dhṛṣṭadyumnasya yaḥ mṛtyuḥ sṛṣṭaḥ tena mahātmanā tam nṛśaṃsena pāpena krūreṇa ati alpa darśinā śrutvā nihatam ācāryam aśvatthāmā kim abravīt uvāca chadmanā nihatam śrutvā pitaram pāpa karmaṇā bāṣpeṇa apūryata drauṇiḥ roṣeṇa ca nara ṛṣabha antakasya iva bhūtāni jihīrṣoḥ kāla paryaye aśru pūrṇe tatas netre apamṛjya punar punar uvāca kopāt niḥśvasya duryodhanam idam vacaḥ asatya vākyam yat tena lobhāt uktam durātmanā rājya hetoḥ nṛśaṃseṇa tat ca api viditam mayā na sa duḥkhāya bhavati tathā dṛṣṭaḥ hi sa dvijaḥ gataḥ sa vīra lokāya pitā mama na saṃśayaḥ na śocyaḥ puruṣa vyāghraḥ tathā sa nidhanam gataḥ paśyatām sarva sainyānām tat me marmāṇi kṛntati mayi jīvati yat tātaḥ keśa graham avāptavān kāmāt krodhāt avajñānāt darpāt bālyena vā punar tat idam pārṣatena iha mahat ādharmikam kṛtam avajñāya ca mām nūnam nṛśaṃsena durātmanā tasya anubandham sa draṣṭā dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ su dāruṇam anāryam paramam kṛtvā mithyāvādī ca pāṇḍavaḥ yaḥ hi asau chadmanā ācāryam śastram saṃnyāsayat tadā tasya adya dharmarājasya bhūmiḥ pāsyati śoṇitam śape satyena kauravyaḥ iṣṭāpūrtena ca anagha a hatvā sarva pāñcālān jīveyam na katham cana sarva upāyaiḥ yatiṣyāmi pāñcālānām aham vadhe dhṛṣṭadyumnam ca samare hantā aham pāpa kāriṇam karmaṇā yena tena iha mṛdunā dāruṇena vā pāñcālānām vadham kṛtvā śāntim labdhāsmi kaurava pretya ca iha ca saṃprāptam trāṇāya mahataḥ bhayāt pitrā tu mama sā avasthā prāptā nirbandhunā yathā mayi śaila pratīkāśe putre śiṣye ca jīvati dhik mama astrāṇi divyāni dhik bāhū dhik parākramam yat mām droṇaḥ sutam prāpya keśa grahaṇam āptavān para loka gatasya api gamiṣyāmi anṛṇaḥ pituḥ āryeṇa tu na vaktavyā kadā cit stutiḥ ātmanaḥ adya paśyantu me vīryam pāṇḍavāḥ sa janārdanāḥ na hi devāḥ na gandharvāḥ na asurāḥ na ca rākṣasāḥ adya śaktāḥ raṇe jetum ratha stham mām nara ṛṣabha aham hi jvalatām madhye mayūkhānām iva aṃśumant prayoktā deva sṛṣṭānām astrāṇām pṛtanā gataḥ kṛśāśva tanayāḥ hi adya mad prayuktāḥ mahā mṛdhe darśayantaḥ vīryam pramathiṣyanti pāṇḍavān adya sarvāḥ diśaḥ rājan dhārābhiḥ iva saṃkulāḥ āvṛtāḥ pattribhiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ draṣṭāraḥ māmakaiḥ iha śatrūn nipātayiṣyāmi mahā vātaḥ iva drumān na bhīmasenaḥ na yamau na ca rājā yudhiṣṭhiraḥ na pārṣataḥ durātmā asau na śikhaṇḍī na sātyakiḥ nārāyaṇāya me pitrā praṇamya vidhi pūrvakam vavre pitā me paramam astram nārāyaṇam tatas gṛhāṇa astram idam vipra nārāyaṇam anuttamam vadhaḥ saṃkhye dravaḥ ca eva śastrāṇām ca visarjanam prayācanam ca śatrūṇām gamanam śaraṇasya ca sarvathā pīḍitaḥ hi syāt avadhyān pīḍayan raṇe tvam varṣiṣyasi divyāni śastra varṣāṇi anekaśas anena astreṇa saṃgrāme tejasā ca jvaliṣyasi etat nārāyaṇāt astram tat prāptam mama bandhunā tena aham pāṇḍavān ca eva pāñcālān matsya kekayān vidrāvayiṣyāmi raṇe śacīpatiḥ iva asurān yathā yathā aham iccheyam tathā bhūtvā śarāḥ mama iccheyam yadi dūra sthān nihaniṣyanti mama śarāḥ yatheṣṭam aśma varṣeṇa pravarṣiṣye raṇe sthitaḥ paraśvadhān ca vividhān prasakṣye aham asaṃśayam saḥ aham nārāyaṇa astreṇa mahatā śatru tāpana śatrūn vidhvaṃsayiṣyāmi kadarthīkṛtya pāṇḍavān pāñcāla apasadaḥ ca adya na me jīvan vimokṣyate evam uktvā tatas drauṇiḥ śaṅkham dadhmau sa māriṣaiḥ pūrayan pṛthivīm sarvām sa śaila vana kānanām tasya śaṅkha svanam śrutvā tava sainyāni māriṣa nyavartanta raṇāya eva bhayam tyaktvā mahā rathāḥ tatas sarve mahā śaṅkhān dadhmuḥ puruṣa sattamāḥ bherīḥ ca abhyahanan hṛṣṭāḥ ḍiṇḍimān ca sahasraśas tathā nanāda vasudhā khura nemi prapīḍitā sa śabdaḥ tumulaḥ kham dyām pṛthivīm ca vyanādayat tam śabdam pāṇḍavāḥ śrutvā parjanya ninada upamam sametya rathinām śreṣṭhāḥ sahitāḥ saṃnyamantrayan prāduścakāra tat divyam astram nārāyaṇam tadā uvāca prāvāt sa pṛṣataḥ vāyuḥ anabhre stanayitnumān cacāla pṛthivī ca api cukṣubhe ca mahā udadhiḥ pratisrotas pravṛttāḥ ca gantum tatra samudragāḥ śikharāṇi vyadīryanta girīṇām tatra bhārata apasavyam mṛgāḥ ca eva pāṇḍu putrān pracakrire tamasā ca avakīryanta sūryaḥ ca kaluṣaḥ abhavat saṃpatanti ca bhūtāni kravyādāni prahṛṣṭa vat deva dānava gandharvāḥ trastāḥ āsan viśām pate katham kathā bhavat tīvrā dṛṣṭvā tat vyākulam mahat vyathitāḥ sarva rājānaḥ tadā hi āsan vicetasaḥ tat dṛṣṭvā ghora rūpam tu drauṇeḥ astram bhaya āvaham petuḥ ākāśa gāḥ tatra vimanaskāḥ viśām pate rodasī ca viyat ca eva sarvam jvālā samāvṛtam uvāca bhṛśam śoka abhitaptena pituḥ vadham a mṛṣyatā kurūn āpatataḥ dṛṣṭvā dhṛṣṭadyumnasya rakṣaṇe kaḥ mantraḥ pāṇḍaveṣu āsīt tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya uvāca prāk eva vidrutān dṛṣṭvā dhārtarāṣṭrān yudhiṣṭhiraḥ punar ca tumulam śabdam śrutvā arjunam abhāṣata ācārye nihate droṇe dhṛṣṭadyumnena saṃyuge na aśaṃsanta jayam yuddhe dīna ātmānaḥ dhanaṃjaya ātma trāṇe matim kṛtvā prādravan kuravaḥ yathā ke cit bhrāntaiḥ rathaiḥ tūrṇam nihata pārṣṇiyantṛbhiḥ vipatāka dhvaja chatraiḥ pārthivāḥ śīrṇa kūbaraiḥ bhagna nīḍaiḥ ākula aśvaiḥ āruhya anye vicetasaḥ bhītāḥ pādaiḥ hayān ke cid tvarayantaḥ svayam rathaiḥ yuga cakra akṣa bhagnaiḥ ca drutāḥ ke cid bhaya āturāḥ rathān viśīrṇān utsṛjya padbhiḥ ke cit ca vidrutāḥ haya pṛṣṭha gatāḥ ca anye kṛṣyante ardha cyuta āsanāḥ gaja skandheṣu saṃsyūtāḥ nārācaiḥ calita āsanāḥ śara ārtaiḥ vidrutaiḥ nāgaiḥ hṛtāḥ ke cit diśaḥ daśa viśastra kavacāḥ ca anye vāhanebhyaḥ kṣitim gatāḥ saṃchinnāḥ nemiṣu gatāḥ mṛditāḥ ca haya dvipaiḥ na abhijānanti ca anyonyam kaśmala abhihata ojasaḥ putrān pitṝn sakhīn bhrātṝn samāropya dṛḍha kṣatān palāyana pare ca anye yodhāḥ śata sahasraśas avasthām tādṛśīm prāpya hate droṇe drutam balam avasthānam avindan vai vikṣatam śara pīḍitam punar āvartitam kena yadi jānāsi śaṃsa me hayānām heṣatām śabdaḥ kuñjarāṇām ca bṛṃhatām ratha nemi svanaḥ ca atra vimiśraḥ śrūyate mahān ete śabdāḥ bhṛśam tīvrāḥ pravṛttāḥ kuru sāgare yaḥ eṣa tumulaḥ śabdaḥ śrūyate loma harṣaṇaḥ sa indrān api eṣa lokān trīn bhañjyāt iti matiḥ mama prahṛṣṭa lomakūpāḥ sma saṃvigna ratha kuñjarāḥ dhanaṃjaya gurum śrutvā tatra nādam su bhīṣaṇam kaḥ eṣa kauravān dīrṇān avasthāpya mahā rathaḥ udyamya ātmānam ugrāya karmaṇe dhairyam āsthitāḥ dhamanti kauravāḥ śaṅkhān yasya vīryam upāśritāḥ dhārtarāṣṭrān avasthāpya kaḥ eṣa nadati iti ha hrīmantam tam mahā bāhum matta dvirada gāminam vyākhyāsyāmi ugra karmāṇam kurūṇām abhayaṃkaram yasmin jāte dadau droṇaḥ gavām daśa śatam dhanam brāhmaṇebhyaḥ mahārhebhyaḥ saḥ aśvatthāmā eṣa garjati jāta mātreṇa vīreṇa yena uccaiḥśravasā iva heṣatā kampitā bhūmiḥ lokāḥ ca sakalāḥ trayaḥ tat śrutvā antarhitam bhūtam nāma ca asya akarot tadā aśvatthāmā iti saḥ adya eṣa śūraḥ nadati pāṇḍava yaḥ adya anāthaḥ iva ākramya pārṣatena hataḥ tathā karmaṇā su nṛśaṃsena tasya nāthaḥ vyavasthitaḥ gurum me yatra pāñcālyaḥ keśapakṣe parāmṛśat tat na jātu kṣamet drauṇiḥ jānan pauruṣam ātmanaḥ upacīrṇaḥ guruḥ mithyā bhavatā rājya kāraṇāt dharma jñena satā nāma saḥ adharmaḥ su mahān kṛtaḥ rāme vāli vadhāt yadvat evam droṇe nipātite sarva dharma upapannaḥ ayam mama śiṣyaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ na ayam vakṣyati mithyā iti pratyayam kṛtavan tvayi sa satya kañcukam nāma praviṣṭena tatas anṛtam āsīt sa vihvalaḥ rājan yathā dṛṣṭaḥ tvayā vibhuḥ sa tu śokena ca āviṣṭaḥ vimukhaḥ putra vatsalaḥ śāśvatam dharmam utsṛjya guruḥ śiṣyeṇa ghātitaḥ rakṣatu idānīm sa amātyaḥ yadi śaknoṣi pārṣatam sarve vayam paritrātum na śakṣyāmaḥ adya pārṣatam sauhārdam sarva bhūteṣu yaḥ karoti atimātraśaḥ vikrośamāne hi mayi bhṛśam ācārya gṛddhini avakīrya svadharmam hi śiṣyeṇa nihataḥ guruḥ yadā gatam vayaḥ bhūyas śiṣṭam alpataram ca naḥ tasya idānīm vikāraḥ ayam adharmaḥ yad kṛtaḥ mahān saḥ alpa kālasya rājyasya kāraṇāt nihataḥ guruḥ dhṛtarāṣṭreṇa bhīṣmāya droṇāya ca viśām pate visṛṣṭā pṛthivī sarvā saha putraiḥ ca tad paraiḥ sa prāpya tādṛśīm vṛttim satkṛtaḥ satatam paraiḥ avṛṇīta sadā putrān mām eva abhyadhikam guruḥ akṣīyamāṇaḥ nyasta astraḥ tvad vākyena āhave hataḥ kṛtaḥ hi anāryaiḥ asmābhiḥ rājya arthe laghu buddhibhiḥ aho bata mahat pāpam kṛtam karma su dāruṇam putrān bhrātṝn pitṝn dārān jīvitam ca eva vāsaviḥ sa mayā rājya kāmena hanyamānaḥ api upekṣitaḥ tasmāt avākśirāḥ rājan prāptaḥ asmi narakam vibho brāhmaṇam vṛddham ācāryam nyasta śastram yathā munim ghātayitvā adya rājya arthe mṛtam śreyaḥ na jīvitam uvāca apriyam vā priyam vā api mahā rāja dhanaṃjayam nyasta daṇḍaḥ yathā pārtha brāhmaṇaḥ saṃśita vrataḥ kṣatāt trātā kṣatāt jīvan kṣāntaḥ triṣu api sādhuṣu kṣatriyaḥ kṣitim āpnoti kṣipram dharmam yaśaḥ śriyam a vipaścit yathā vākyam vyāharan na adya śobhase amarṣam pṛṣṭhatas kṛtvā dharmam eva abhikāṅkṣase aham āvārayiṣyāmi gadayā sarva kauravān tvayā vinā yadi mahīm dharmaputrāya dhīmate na dadyām pañcame prāpte divase na asmi kṣatriyaḥ ānṛśaṃsye ca te diṣṭyā buddhiḥ satatam acyuta draupadī ca parāmṛṣṭā sabhām ānīya śatrubhiḥ katham vṛddheṣu tiṣṭhatsu dhārmikeṣu mahatsu ca draupadī prāpnuyāt kleśam veśyā yoṣā iva bhārata kim u teṣām bilva phalam mukhe hi āsīt mahātmanām uta aho badhirāḥ hi āsan mūkāḥ vā api dhanaṃjaya andhāḥ vasan tadā te tu yaiḥ ca na uktam hitam vacaḥ anurūpam kṛtam ca api bhīṣma droṇa kṛpa ādibhiḥ putraiḥ śiṣyaiḥ ca yat sārdham saṃnaddhāḥ yoddhum āhave vanam pravrājitāḥ ca āsma valkala ajina vāsasaḥ an arhamāṇāḥ tam bhāvam trayodaśa samāḥ paraiḥ bahūni kṣāmya śatrūṇām satya dharma ratāḥ vayam etāni amarṣa sthānāni marṣitāni tvayā anagha sa anubandhān haniṣyāmi kṣudrān rājya harān aham tvayā tu kathitam pūrvam yuddhāya abhyāgatāḥ vayam bhaya arditānām asmākam vācā marmāṇi kṛntasi vapan vraṇe kṣāram iva kṣatānām śatru karśana vidīryate me hṛdayam tvayā vāc śalya pīḍitam yat tvam ātmānam asmān ca praśaṃsyān na praśaṃsasi vāsudeve sthite ca api droṇaputram praśaṃsasi yaḥ kalām ṣoḍaśīm tvattaḥ na arhate tam praśaṃsasi mama nāga ayutam pārtha balam bāhvoḥ vidhīyate prapātayeyam ca śaraiḥ sa indrān devān samāgatān sarākṣasa gaṇān pārtha sa asura uraga mānavān dārayeyam mahīm krodhāt vikireyam ca parvatān āvidhya ca gadām gurvīm bhīmām kāñcana mālinīm giri prakāśān kṣitijān bhañjeyam anilaḥ yathā sa tvam evaṃvidham jānan bhrātaram mām nara ṛṣabha aham enam gadā pāṇiḥ jeṣyāmi ekaḥ mahā āhave tatas pāñcāla rājasya putraḥ pārtham atha abravīt bībhatso vipra karmāṇi viditāni manīṣiṇām yājana adhyāpane dānam tathā yajña pratigrahau ṣaṣṭham adhyayanam nāma teṣām kasmin pratiṣṭhitaḥ apakrāntaḥ svadharmāt ca kṣatra dharmam upāśritaḥ amānuṣeṇa hanti asmān astreṇa kṣudra karma kṛt tathā māyām prayuñjānam asahyam brāhmaṇabruvam tasmin tathā mayā śaste yadi drauṇāyaniḥ ruṣā yat ca mām dhārmikaḥ bhūtvā bravīṣi guru ghātinam yasya kāryam akāryam vā yudhyataḥ syāt samam raṇe tam katham brāhmaṇam brūyāḥ kṣatriyam vā dhanaṃjaya viśeṣāt pitṛ hantā mama na sa vadhyaḥ katham mayā yaḥ ayam pāpaḥ su durmedhāḥ bāndhavān yudhi jaghnivān vidharmiṇam dharma vidbhiḥ proktam teṣām viṣa upamam nṛśaṃsaḥ sa mayā ākramya rathaḥ eva nipātitaḥ kṛte raṇe katham pārtha jvalana arka viṣa upamam bhīmam droṇa śiraḥ chede praśasyam na praśaṃsasi niṣāda viṣaye kṣiptam jayadratha śiraḥ yathā avadhaḥ ca api śatrūṇām adharmaḥ śiṣyate arjuna sa śatruḥ nihataḥ saṃkhye mayā dharmeṇa pāṇḍava yathā tvayā hataḥ śūraḥ bhagadattaḥ pituḥ sakhā pitāmaham raṇe hatvā manyase dharmam ātmanaḥ saṃbandha avanatam pārtha na mām tvam bahu manyase sva gātra kṛta sopānam niṣaṇṇam iva dantinam draupadyāḥ draupadeyānām kṛte na anyena hetunā kula krama āgatam vairam mama ācāryeṇa viśrutam tathā jānāti ayam lokaḥ na yūyam pāṇḍu nandanāḥ na anṛtaḥ pāṇḍavaḥ jyeṣṭhaḥ na aham vā adhārmikaḥ arjuna pitaram vā gurum vā api jighāṃsum putra śiṣyayoḥ iti vac brahmaṇā pūrvam kṣatriyāṇām dviṣat vadhe tasmāt śiṣyeṇa nihataḥ śatruḥ mama brāhmaṇabruvaḥ yaḥ kṣatriya sutaḥ hanyāt pitaram vā gurum ca vā uvāca sa aṅgāḥ vedāḥ yathānyāyam yena adhītāḥ mahātmanā yasmin sākṣāt dhanurvedaḥ hrī niṣedhe pratiṣṭhitaḥ nīca ātmanā nṛśaṃsena kṣudreṇa guru ghātinā yasya prasādāt karmāṇi kurvanti puruṣa ṛṣabhāḥ amānuṣāṇi saṃgrāme devaiḥ asukarāṇi ca tasmin ākruśyati droṇe samakṣam pāpa karmiṇaḥ pārthāḥ sarve ca rājānaḥ pṛthivyām ye dhanurdharāḥ śrutvā kim āhuḥ pāñcālyam tat mama ācakṣva saṃjaya uvāca śrutvā drupada putrasya tāḥ vācaḥ krūra karmaṇaḥ tūṣṇīm babhūvuḥ rājānaḥ sarve eva viśām pate arjunaḥ tu kaṭākṣeṇa jihmam prekṣya ca pārṣatam yudhiṣṭhiraḥ ca bhīmaḥ ca yamau kṛṣṇaḥ tathā apare āsan su vrīḍitāḥ rājan sātyakiḥ idam abravīt na iha asti puruṣaḥ kaḥ cit yaḥ imam pāpa pūruṣam bhāṣamāṇam akalyāṇam śīghram hanyāt nara adhamam ete tvām pāṇḍavāḥ sarve kutsayanti vivitsayā karmaṇā tena pāpena śvapākam iva brāhmaṇāḥ etat kṛtvā mahat pāpam ninditam sarva sādhubhiḥ katham ca śatadhā jihvā na te mūrdhā ca dīryate gurum ākrośataḥ kṣudra na ca adharmeṇa pātyase yāpyaḥ tvam asi pārthaiḥ ca sarvaiḥ ca andhaka vṛṣṇibhiḥ yat karma kaluṣam kṛtvā ślāghase jana saṃsadi akāryam tādṛśam kṛtvā punar eva gurum kṣipan nigṛhya keśeṣu vadham guroḥ dharma ātmanaḥ sataḥ sapta avarāḥ tathā pūrve bāndhavāḥ te nipātitāḥ yaśasā ca parityaktāḥ tvām prāpya kula pāṃsanam uktavan ca api yat pārtham bhīṣmam prati nara ṛṣabham na anyaḥ pāñcāla putrebhyaḥ vidyate bhuvi pāpa kṛt sa ca api sṛṣṭaḥ pitrā te bhīṣmasya anta karaḥ kila śikhaṇḍī rakṣitaḥ tena sa ca mṛtyuḥ mahātmanaḥ pāñcālāḥ calitāḥ dharmāt kṣudrāḥ mitra guru druhaḥ tvām prāpya saha sodaryam dhikkṛtam sarva sādhubhiḥ punar ced īdṛśīm vācam mad samīpe vadiṣyasi śiraḥ te pātayiṣyāmi gadayā vajra kalpayā tvām ca brahma haṇam dṛṣṭvā janaḥ sūryam avekṣate brahmahatyā hi te pāpam prāyaścitta artham ātmanaḥ tiṣṭha tiṣṭha sahasva ekam gadā pātam imam mama tava ca api sahiṣye aham gadā pātān anekaśas sātvatena evam ākṣiptaḥ pārṣataḥ paruṣa akṣaram śrūyate śrūyate ca iti kṣamyate ca iti mādhava na ca anārya śubham sādhum puruṣam kṣeptum arhasi kṣamā praśasyate loke na tu pāpaḥ arhati kṣamām kṣamāvantam hi pāpa ātmā jitaḥ ayam iti manyate sa tvam kṣudra samācāraḥ nīca ātmā pāpa niścayaḥ varam hi te mṛtam pāpa na ca te vṛttam īdṛśam śrotum vaktavyatā mūlam nīcāḥ vakṣyanti mānavāḥ parān kṣipanti doṣeṇa sveṣu doṣeṣu adṛṣṭayaḥ yaḥ sa bhūriśravāḥ chinne bhuje prāya gataḥ tvayā vāryamāṇena nihataḥ tatas pāpataram nu kim vyūhamānaḥ mayā droṇaḥ divyena astreṇa saṃyuge visṛṣṭa śastraḥ nihataḥ kim tatra krūra duṣkṛtam nihatya tvām yadā bhūmau sa vikrāmati vīryavān kim tadā na nihaṃsi enam bhūtvā puruṣa sattamaḥ tvad punar anāryeṇa pūrvam pārthena nirji yadā tadā hataḥ śūraḥ saumadattiḥ pratāpavān yatra yatra tu pāṇḍūnām droṇaḥ drāvayate camūm sa tvam evaṃvidham kṛtvā karma cāṇḍāla vat svayam vaktum icchasi vaktavyaḥ kasmāt mām paruṣāṇi atha kartā tvam karmaṇā ugrasya na aham vṛṣṇi kula adhama pāpānām ca tvam āvāsaḥ karmaṇām mā punar vada atha vakṣyasi mām maurkhyāt bhūyas paruṣam īdṛśam gamayiṣyāmi bāṇaiḥ tvām yudhi vaivasvata kṣayam teṣām api hi adharmeṇa ceṣṭitam śṛṇu yādṛśam vañcitaḥ pāṇḍavaḥ pūrvam adharmeṇa yudhiṣṭhiraḥ draupadī ca parikliṣṭā tathā adharmeṇa sātyake pravrājitāḥ vanam sarve pāṇḍavāḥ saha kṛṣṇayā sarva svam apakṛṣṭam ca tathā adharmeṇa bāliśa adharmeṇa apakṛṣṭaḥ ca madra rājaḥ paraiḥ itas adharmeṇa tathā bālaḥ saubhadraḥ vinipātitaḥ itas api adharmeṇa hataḥ bhīṣmaḥ kuru pitāmahaḥ bhūriśravāḥ hi adharmeṇa tvayā dharma vidā hataḥ evam paraiḥ ācaritam pāṇḍaveyaiḥ ca saṃyuge rakṣamāṇaiḥ jayam vīraiḥ dharma jñaiḥ api sātvata yudhyasva kauravaiḥ sārdham mā gāḥ pitṛ niveśanam evamādīni vākyāni krūrāṇi paruṣāṇi ca śrāvitaḥ sātyakiḥ śrīmān ākampitaḥ iva abhavat tat śrutvā krodha tāmra akṣaḥ sātyakiḥ tu ādade gadām viniḥśvasya yathā sarpaḥ praṇidhāya rathe dhanuḥ tatas abhipatya pāñcālyam saṃrambhena idam abravīt na tvām vakṣyāmi paruṣam haniṣye tvām vadha kṣamam tam āpatantam sahasā mahā balam amarṣaṇam pāñcālyāya abhisaṃkruddham antakāya antaka upamam avaplutya rathāt tūrṇam bāhubhyām samavārayat dravamāṇam tathā krudh sātyakim pāṇḍavaḥ balī praskandamānam ādāya jagāma balinam balāt sthitvā viṣṭabhya caraṇau bhīmena śini puṃgavaḥ nigṛhītaḥ pade ṣaṣṭhe balena balinām varaḥ tathā api bhīmāt ātmānam āmucya balinā ucchritaḥ bhīmena atha āśu mahatā vegam āsthāya madhyamam avaruhya rathāt tam tu hriyamāṇam balīyasā uvāca ślakṣṇayā vācā sahadevaḥ viśām pate param andhaka vṛṣṇibhyaḥ pāñcālebhyaḥ ca mādhava tathā eva andhaka vṛṣṇīnām tava ca eva viśeṣataḥ pāñcālānām ca vārṣṇeya samudrāntām vicinvatām na anyat asti param mitram yathā pāṇḍava vṛṣṇayaḥ sa bhavān īdṛśam mitram manyate ca yathā bhavān bhavantaḥ ca yathā asmākam bhavatām ca tathā vayam niyaccha manyum pāñcālyāt praśāmya śini puṃgava pārṣatasya kṣama tvam vai kṣamatām te pārṣataḥ praśāmyamāne śaineye sahadevena māriṣa pāñcāla rājasya sutaḥ prahasan idam abravīt muñca muñca śineḥ pautram bhīma yuddha mada anvitam āsādayatu mām eṣa dharādharam iva anilaḥ yāvat asya śitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ saṃrambham vinayāmi aham kim nu śakyam mayā kartum kāryam yat idam udyatam su mahat pāṇḍu putrāṇām āyānti ete hi kauravāḥ atha vā phalgunaḥ sarvān vārayiṣyati saṃyuge aham api asya mūrdhānam pātayiṣyāmi sāyakaiḥ manyate chinna bāhum mām bhūriśravasam āhave utsṛja enam aham vā enam eṣa mām vā haniṣyati śṛṇvan pāñcāla vākyāni sātyakiḥ sarpa vat śvasan tau vṛṣau iva nardantau balinaḥ bāhu śālinaḥ tvarayā vāsudevaḥ ca dharmarājaḥ ca māriṣa yatnena mahatā vīrau vārayām āsatuḥ tatas yuyutsavaḥ parān saṃkhye pratīyuḥ kṣatriya ṛṣabhāḥ uvāca tatas sa kadanam cakre ripūṇām droṇa nandanaḥ yuga ante sarva bhūtānām kāla sṛṣṭaḥ iva antakaḥ dhvaja drumam śastra śṛṅgam hata nāga mahā śilam aśva kiṃpuruṣa ākīrṇam śarāsana latā āvṛtam śūla kravyāda saṃghuṣṭam bhūta yakṣa gaṇa ākulam pratijñām śrāvayām āsa punar eva te ātmajam yasmāt yudhyantam ācāryam dharma kañcukam āsthitaḥ muñca śastram iti prāha kuntī putraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ tasmāt saṃpaśyataḥ tasya drāvayiṣyāmi vāhinīm vidrāvya satyam hantāsmi pāpam pāñcālyam eva tu sarvān etān haniṣyāmi yadi yotsyanti mām raṇe satyam te pratijānāmi parāvartaya vāhinīm bherīḥ ca avādayan hṛṣṭāḥ paṭahān dundubhīn ca ha āḍambarān mṛdaṅgān ca jharjharīḥ ca ānakān api maḍḍukān paṇavān vīṇāḥ ḍiṇḍimān ca sahasraśas sarve ca eva mahā iṣvāsāḥ dadhmuḥ śaṅkhān mahā svanān sa śabdaḥ tumulaḥ kham ca pṛthivīm ca vyanādayat kurūṇām atha tam śabdam śrutvā ghoram samutthitam pāṇḍavāḥ somakaiḥ sārdham samapadyanta vismi te tu dṛṣṭvā kurūn rājan nadataḥ bhairavān ravān tatas samāgamaḥ rājan kuru pāṇḍava senayoḥ punar eva abhavat tīvraḥ pūrṇa sāgarayoḥ iva saṃrabdhāḥ hi sthirībhūtāḥ droṇaputreṇa kauravāḥ udagrāḥ pāṇḍu pāñcālāḥ droṇasya nidhanena ca teṣām parama hṛṣṭānām jayam ātmani paśyatām saṃrabdhānām mahā vegaḥ prādurāsīt raṇa ajire yathā śiloccaye śailaḥ sāgare sāgaraḥ yathā rāja indra tathā āsan kuru pāṇḍavāḥ tatas śaṅkha sahasrāṇi bherīṇām ayutāni ca avādayanta saṃhṛṣṭāḥ kuru pāṇḍava sainikāḥ cukṣubhe pṛthivī sarvāḥ diśaḥ ca pratisasvanuḥ saṃbhrāntāni ca bhūtāni jala jāni api māriṣa te ca sarve tathā yaudhāḥ saṃprahṛṣṭāḥ yuyutsavaḥ saṃpatatsu ratha ogheṣu te teṣām ca bhārata prāduścakre tatas drauṇiḥ astram nārāyaṇam tadā abhisaṃdhāya pāṇḍūnām pāñcālānām ca vāhinīm prādurāsan tatas bāṇāḥ dīpta agrāḥ khe sahasraśas pāṇḍavān bhakṣayiṣyantaḥ dīpta āsyāḥ iva pannagāḥ te diśaḥ kham ca sainyam ca samāvṛṇvan mahā āhave tatas antarikṣam kha gamaiḥ nānā liṅgaiḥ su bhairavaiḥ muhūrtāt bhāskarasya iva rājan lokam gabhastayaḥ tathā apare dyotamānāḥ jyotīṃṣi iva ambare amale prādurāsan mahīpāla kārṣṇāyasa mayāḥ guḍāḥ caturdiśam vicitrāḥ ca śataghnyaḥ atha hutāśa dāḥ cakrāṇi ca kṣura antāni maṇḍalāni iva bhāsvataḥ pāśāḥ ca vividha ākārāḥ nārāca añjalikāḥ tathā saṃpatantaḥ sma dṛśyante śataśas atha sahasraśas tadvat āsīt tadā rājan jyotiḥ bhūtam nabhaḥ sthalam śastra ākṛtibhiḥ ākīrṇam atīva bharata ṛṣabha dṛṣṭvā antarikṣam āvignāḥ pāṇḍu pāñcāla sṛñjayāḥ yathā yathā hi ayudhyanta pāṇḍavānām mahā rathāḥ vadhyamānāḥ tathā astreṇa tena nārāyaṇena vai prapetuḥ kuñjarāḥ tatra śastra saṃghaiḥ nipātitāḥ vyadīryamāṇāḥ girayaḥ vajra nunnāḥ yathā purā aparaiḥ ca tathā bāṇaiḥ kuntaiḥ ca kanaka ujjvalaiḥ saṃkīrṇā pṛthivī jajñe māṃsa śoṇita kardamā gajebhyaḥ cyavamānānām yantṝṇām tatra bhārata vibhujānām viśīrṇānām nyasta kārmuka varmaṇām pūrṇam āyodhanam jajñe preta rāja pura upamam alaṃkāraiḥ ca nāgānām graiveyaiḥ ca sa kaṅkaṭaiḥ kakṣyābhiḥ agnikuṇḍaiḥ ca yantraiḥ ca eva patākibhiḥ śaktibhiḥ ca mahā rāja bāṇaiḥ ca nata parvabhiḥ tūṇīraiḥ apaviddhaiḥ ca cāpaiḥ ca su mahādhanaiḥ anukarṣaiḥ patākābhiḥ yoktraiḥ ca eva viśām pate raśmibhiḥ ca pratodaiḥ ca kiṅkiṇībhiḥ ca māriṣa chattraiḥ ca candra saṃkāśaiḥ vṛṣṭi ātapa nivāribhiḥ aṅgulitraiḥ sa keyūraiḥ dīptaiḥ niṣkaiḥ ca kāñcanaiḥ karṇa sūtraiḥ kirīṭaiḥ ca mukuṭaiḥ ca mahādhanaiḥ citraiḥ vastraiḥ alaṃkāraiḥ kuṇḍalaiḥ ca api bhārata apaviddhaiḥ tathā śīrṣaiḥ bāhubhiḥ ca mahātmanām uraśchadaiḥ tathā citraiḥ ghaṇṭā jālaiḥ ca bhāsvaraiḥ nānā aṅga avayavaiḥ hīnāḥ yaudhāḥ sasruḥ bhaya arditāḥ cukruśuḥ tāta tāta iti hā hā putra iti ca asakṛt nūnam te nidhanam prāptāḥ pāṇḍaveyāḥ mahā rathāḥ vāsudevaḥ ca vārṣṇeyaḥ tathā somaka sṛñjayāḥ jīvatsu samare teṣu na hi vīreṣu sainikāḥ iti abruvan tathā yaudhāḥ hanyamānāḥ tadā raṇe hanyamānāḥ tathā astreṇa tena nārāyaṇena te yathā hi śiśira apāye dahet kakṣam hutāśanaḥ tathā tat astram pāṇḍūnām dadāha dhvajinīm prabho āpūryamāṇena astreṇa sainye kṣīyati ca abhibho jagāma paramam trāsam dharmaputraḥ yudhiṣṭhiraḥ dravamāṇam tu tat sainyam dṛṣṭvā vigata cetanam dhṛṣṭadyumna palāyasva saha pāñcāla senayā sātyake tvam ca gacchasva vṛṣṇi andhaka vṛtaḥ gṛhān vāsudevaḥ api dharma ātmā kariṣyati ātmanaḥ kṣamam upadeṣṭum samarthaḥ ayam lokasya kim uta ātmanaḥ bhīṣma droṇa arṇavam tīrtvā saṃgrāmam bhīru dustaram kāmaḥ saṃpadyatām asya bībhatsoḥ āśu mām prati kalyāṇa vṛttaḥ ācāryaḥ mayā yudhi nipātitaḥ yena bālaḥ sa saubhadraḥ yuddhānām a viśāradaḥ yena a vibruvatā praśnam tathā kṛṣṇā sabhām gatā upekṣitā sa putreṇa dāsa bhāvam niyacchatī arjunasya vighāta artham pratijñā yena rakṣitā vyūha dvāri vayam ca eva dhṛtāḥ yena jigīṣavaḥ jighāṃsuḥ dhārtarāṣṭraḥ ca śrānteṣu aśveṣu phalgunam yena brahmāstra vidvasā pāñcālāḥ satyajit mukhāḥ kurvāṇāḥ mad jaye yatnam sa mūlāḥ vinipātitāḥ yena pravrājyamānāḥ ca rājyāt vayam adharmataḥ nivāryamāṇena asmābhiḥ anugantum tat eṣitāḥ vana vāsāt nivṛttānām samaye ca tathā kṛte snehaḥ ca darśitaḥ nityam pratyakṣam vaḥ mahā rathāḥ yaḥ asau atyantam asmāsu kurvāṇaḥ sauhṛdam param śīghram nyasyata śastrāṇi vāhebhyaḥ ca avarohata rāmeṇa pṛthivī sarvā niḥkṣatriya gaṇā kṛtā anena astreṇa bhīmena kṣatram utsāditam purā tat astram nirmitam pūrvam viṣṇunā prabhaviṣṇunā yadā nipātitaḥ daityaḥ hiraṇyākṣaḥ mahā asuraḥ tadā nārāyaṇa astram hi pūrva sṛṣṭam hi viṣṇunā tam nipātya mahā daityam dvāpara ante nṛpa uttama rāmeṇa tapaḥ āsthāya labdham pūrvam mahātmanā devadevam samārādhya viṣṇum tribhuvana īśvaram tasmāt droṇam anuprāptam sarva astra prativāraṇam nārāyaṇa astrasya nṛpāḥ eṣa yogaḥ nivāraṇe ye añjalim kurvate vīrāḥ namanti ca vivāhanāḥ tān na etat astram saṃgrāme nihaniṣyati mānavān īṣuḥ sarve astram utsraṣṭum manobhiḥ karaṇena ca tatas utsraṣṭu kāmān tān astrāṇi ālakṣya pāṇḍavaḥ bhīmasenaḥ abravīt rājñ idam saṃharṣayan vacaḥ na katham cana śastrāṇi moktavyāni iha kena cid aham āvārayiṣyāmi droṇaputra astram āśugaiḥ kāla vat vicariṣyāmi drauṇeḥ astram viśātayan paśyadhvam me dṛḍhau bāhū nāga rāja kara upamā adya paśyata me vīryam bāhvoḥ pīna aṃsayoḥ yudhi adya enam pratiyotsyāmi paśyatsu kuru pāṇḍuṣu arjuna arjuna bībhatso na nyasyam gāṇḍivam tvayā śaśāṅkasya iva te paṅkaḥ nairmalyam pātayiṣyati bhīma nārāyaṇa astre mama goṣu ca brāhmaṇeṣu ca kampayan medinīm sarvām trāsayan ca camūm te śaṅkha śabdam mahat kṛtvā bhuja śabdam ca pāṇḍavaḥ tasya śaṅkha svanam śrutvā bāhu śabdam ca tāvakāḥ samantāt koṣṭhakīkṛtya śara vrātaiḥ avākiran samakampanta vitrastāḥ śakṛt mūtram prasusruvuḥ nimeṣa mātreṇa āsādya kuntī putraḥ abhyavākirat avakīrṇaḥ abhavat pārthaḥ sphuliṅgaiḥ iva kāñcanaiḥ pāṇḍu sainyam ṛte bhīmam su mahat bhayam āviśat tatas śastrāṇi te sarve samutsṛjya mahī tale teṣu nikṣipta śastreṣu vāhanebhyaḥ cyuteṣu ca gṛhīta śastrān ārūḍhān vāhaneṣu mahātmasu yatra yatra prayāti sma kramamāṇam raṇa ajire tatra tatra vimuktāḥ tāḥ sarve adṛśyanta saṃghaśas tatas apaśyat raṇe bhīmam gadā hastam ariṃdamam asambhrāntam samāyāntam droṇaputra ratham prati hāhākṛtāni bhūtāni pāṇḍavāḥ ca viśeṣataḥ bhīmasenam apaśyanta tejasā saṃvṛtam tadā uvāca bhīmasenam samākīrṇam dṛṣṭvā astreṇa dhanaṃjayaḥ tejasaḥ pratighāta artham vāruṇena samāvṛṇot na alakṣayata tam kaḥ cit vāruṇa astreṇa saṃvṛtam sa aśva sūta rathaḥ bhīmaḥ droṇaputra astra saṃvṛtaḥ agnau agniḥ iva nyastaḥ jvālā mālī su durdṛśaḥ yathā rātri kṣaye rājan jyotīṃṣi asta girim prati samāpetuḥ tathā bāṇāḥ bhīmasena ratham prati tat astram vāruṇam bhaktāḥ nārāyaṇa samudbhavam prajajvāla punar bhīmam saṃvṛtya tu raṇa ajire sa hi bhīmaḥ rathaḥ ca asya hayāḥ sūtaḥ ca māriṣa saṃvṛtāḥ droṇaputreṇa pāvaka antargatāḥ abhavan gacchet agniḥ vibhoḥ āsyam tathā astram bhīmam āvṛṇot sūryam agniḥ praviṣṭaḥ syāt yathā ca agnim divākaraḥ tathā praviṣṭam tat tejaḥ na prājñāyata kim cana tat astram bhīma huṃkārāt apayāti punar punar punar punar tam āyāti huṃkārāt tam vimuñcati tatas devāḥ sa gandharvāḥ bhīmam dṛṣṭvā su vismitāḥ vikīrṇam astram tat dṛṣṭvā tathā bhīma ratham prati udīryamāṇam drauṇim ca niṣpratidvaṃdvam āhave sarva sainyāni pāṇḍūnām nyasta śastrāṇi acetasaḥ yudhiṣṭhira purogān ca vimukhān tān mahā rathān arjunaḥ vāsudevaḥ ca tvaramāṇau mahā dyutī avaplutya rathāt vīrau bhīmam ādravatām tatas vigāhya tau su balinau māyayā āviśatām tadā vāruṇa astra prayogāt ca vīryavat tvāt ca kṛṣṇayoḥ tatas cakṛṣatuḥ bhīmam tasya sarva āyudhāni ca nārāyaṇa astra śānti artham nara nārāyaṇau balāt pātayām āsatuḥ punar bhīmasenam raṇe balāt bhīmam nirāyudham kṛtvā tadā kṛṣṇa dhanaṃjayau apakṛṣyamāṇaḥ kaunteyaḥ nadati eva mahā rathaḥ tam abravīt vāsudevaḥ kim idam pāṇḍu nandana evam uktvā tatas kṛṣṇaḥ rathāt bhūmim apātayat niḥśvasantam yathā nāgam krodha saṃrakta locanam yadā apakṛṣṭaḥ sa rathāt nyāsitaḥ ca āyudham bhuvi tatas nārāyaṇa astram tat praśāntam śatru tāpanam babhūvuḥ vimalāḥ sarvāḥ diśaḥ pradiśaḥ eva ca pravavuḥ ca śivāḥ vātāḥ praśāntāḥ mṛga pakṣiṇaḥ vāhanāni ca hṛṣṭāni yodhāḥ ca manuja īśvara babhau bhīmaḥ niśā apāye dhīmān sūryaḥ iva uditaḥ hata śeṣam balam tatra pāṇḍavānām atiṣṭhata astra vyuparamāt dhṛṣṭam te putra jighāṃsayā vyavasthitāḥ hi pāñcālāḥ punar eva jaya eṣiṇaḥ aśvatthāmā tathā uktaḥ tu tava putreṇa māriṣa su dīnam abhiniḥśvasya rājānam idam abravīt eṣa ca astra pratīghātam vāsudevaḥ prayuktavān tat etat astram praśamam yātam kṛṣṇasya mantrite parājayaḥ vā mṛtyuḥ vā śreyaḥ mṛtyuḥ na nirjayaḥ nirjitāḥ ca arayaḥ hi ete śastra utsargāt mṛta upamāḥ uvāca dṛṣṭvā pārthān ca saṃgrāme yuddhāya samavasthitān nārāyaṇa astra nirmuktān carataḥ pṛtanā mukhe uvāca jānan pituḥ sa nidhanam siṃha lāṅgūla ketanaḥ abhidrutya ca viṃśatyā kṣudrakāṇām nara ṛṣabhaḥ tam tu dṛṣṭvā su saṃkruddham kāla anala yama upamam vimuñcan viśikhān tūrṇam pārṣataḥ abhyadravat raṇe tau drauṇiḥ krodha tāmra akṣaḥ didhikṣan iva tejasā chādayām āsa bāṇa oghaiḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam samantataḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ api saṃbhrāntaḥ śareṇa ānata parvaṇā tasya drauṇiḥ dhanuḥ chittvā sthūṇena para vīra hā dhṛṣṭadyumnam trisaptatyā vivyādha niśitaiḥ nadan tat apāsya dhanuḥ chinnam dhṛṣṭadyumnaḥ pratāpavān anyat kārmukam ādāya saḥ aśvatthāmānam ārdayat tam ca api avākirat bāṇaiḥ dhṛṣṭadyumnam paraṃtapaḥ tatas sa pārṣataḥ tūrṇam śaktim hema pariṣkṛtām tām āpatatīm sahasā vyālī kāle iva āhave tām nikṛttām tatas dṛṣṭvā drauṇinā pārṣataḥ tatas tatas avidhyat su tīkṣṇābhyām śarābhyām drauṇim āhave tatas dvābhyām su tīkṣṇābhyām bhallābhyām tatra kārmukam tam ca bāṇaiḥ mahā tejāḥ punar anyaiḥ samāvṛṇot sa aśva sūta ratham tūrṇam chādayām āsa saṃyuge tasya ca anucarān sarvān dīpta astrān pārśvatas sthitān vyadrāvayata saṃkruddhaḥ śaraiḥ saṃnata parvabhiḥ brahmadattam tatas bāṇam dhṛṣṭadyumna jighāṃsayā sātyakiḥ tu tam ādāya rāja putram śara arditam aṣṭabhiḥ niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ aśvatthāmānam ārdayat aśītyā punar āhatya nānā rūpaiḥ amarṣaṇaḥ vivyādha asya tribhiḥ sūtam caturbhiḥ caturaḥ hayān evam uktvā śaraiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ sātyakim tūrṇam āvṛṇot saṃrabdhaḥ krodha tāmra akṣaḥ droṇaputraḥ pratāpavān sātyakiḥ tu tatas kruddhaḥ śareṇa ānata parvaṇā tatas drauṇiḥ mahā rāja bāṇaiḥ saṃchādya sātyakim dhanuḥ krodha parīta ātmā ciccheda āśu mahā astra vid tatas śaktim mahā ghorām hema daṇḍām ayasmayīm cikṣepa sātyakiḥ tūrṇam droṇaputra jighāṃsayā tām āpatantīm sahasā śakra muktām iva aśanim aprāptām eva ciccheda drauṇiḥ sapta āśugaiḥ tām nikṛttām śaraiḥ dṛṣṭvā drauṇinā sāyakaiḥ bhṛśam tat vikṛṣya mahat cāpam sātyakiḥ sātvatām varaḥ sāyakaiḥ bahubhiḥ tūrṇam aśvatthāmānam ārdayat tatas drauṇiḥ su saṃrabdhaḥ śara jālena mādhavam chādayām āsa samare sātyakim krodha mūrchitaḥ tāni asya śara jālāni antarikṣe viśām pate tatas pūrṇa āyata utsṛṣṭaiḥ hema puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ vivyādha su dṛḍham droṇaputram amarṣitaḥ tathā sa viddhaḥ su bhṛśam droṇaputraḥ atyamarṣaṇaḥ avākirat ameya ātmā bāṇa varṣaiḥ samantataḥ parvatam vāri dhārābhiḥ tapānte jaladaḥ yathā droṇaputram triṣaṣṭyā tu rājan vivyādha pattriṇām sārathim ca asya viṃśatyā svarṇa puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ hayān ca caturaḥ avidhyat caturbhiḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ ādadat sarva lokasya prāṇān iva mahā raṇe pārṣataḥ tu balī rājan kṛtāstraḥ kṛta niśramaḥ drauṇim eva abhidudrāva kṛtvā mṛtyum nivartanam tatas bāṇa mayam varṣam droṇaputrasya mūrdhani avāsṛjat ameya ātmā pāñcālyaḥ rathinām varaḥ tad drauṇiḥ samara krudh chādayām āsa pattrin dvābhyām ca su vikṛṣṭābhyām kṣurābhyām dhvaja kārmuke chittvā pāñcāla rājasya drauṇiḥ anyaiḥ samārdayat vyaśva sūta ratham ca enam drauṇiḥ cakre mahā āhave pradrudrāva tatas sainyam pāñcālānām viśām pate saṃbhrānta rūpam ārtam ca śara varṣa parikṣatam dṛṣṭvā ca vimukhān yodhān dhṛṣṭadyumnam ca pīḍitam śaineyaḥ acodayat tūrṇam raṇam drauṇi ratham prati aṣṭabhiḥ niśitaiḥ ca eva saḥ aśvatthāmānam ārdayat viṃśatyā punar āhatya nānā rūpaiḥ amarṣaṇam sa sa aśvam vyadhamat ca api ratham hema pariṣkṛtam hṛdi vivyādha samare triṃśatā sāyakaiḥ bhṛśam evam sa pīḍitaḥ rājan aśvatthāmā mahā balaḥ śara jālaiḥ parivṛtaḥ kartavyam na anvapadyata kṛpa karṇa ādibhiḥ sārdham śaraiḥ sātvatam āvṛṇot duryodhanaḥ tu viṃśatyā kṛpaḥ śāradvataḥ tribhiḥ kṛtavarmā atha daśabhiḥ karṇaḥ pañcāśatā śaraiḥ duḥśāsanaḥ śatena eva vṛṣasenaḥ ca sapta sātyakim vivyadhuḥ tūrṇam samantāt niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ tatas sa sātyakiḥ rājan sarvān eva mahā rathān virathān vimukhān ca eva kṣaṇena eva akarot nṛpa aśvatthāmā tu saṃprāpya cetanām bharata ṛṣabha cintayām āsa duḥkha ārtaḥ niḥśvasan ca punar punar tatas ratha antaram drauṇiḥ samāruhya paraṃtapaḥ sātyakim vārayām āsa kiran śara śatān bahūn tam āpatantam saṃprekṣya bhāradvāja sutam raṇe tatas te pāṇḍavāḥ rājan dṛṣṭvā sātyaki vikramam śaṅkha śabdān bhṛśam cakruḥ siṃhanādān ca nedire evam tam viratham kṛtvā sātyakiḥ satya vikramaḥ jaghāna vṛṣasenasya tri sāhasrān mahā rathān ayutam dantinām sārdham kṛpasya nijaghāna saḥ pañca ayutāni ca aśvānām śakuneḥ nijaghāna ha tatas drauṇiḥ mahā rāja ratham āruhya vīryavān punar tam āgatam dṛṣṭvā śaineyaḥ niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ saḥ atividdhaḥ mahā iṣvāsaḥ nānā liṅgaiḥ amarṣaṇaḥ śaineya abhyavapattim te jānāmi ācārya ghātinaḥ śape śape ātmanā aham śaineya satyena tapasā tathā a hatvā sarva pāñcālān yathā śāntim avāpnuyām yat balam pāṇḍaveyānām vṛṣṇīnām api yat balam evam uktvā arka raśmi ābham su parvāṇam śara uttamam vyasṛjat sātvate drauṇiḥ vajram vṛtre yathā hariḥ sa tam nirbhidya tena astaḥ sāyakaḥ sa śarāvaram vimucya sa śaram cāpam bhūri vraṇa parisravaḥ sūtena apahṛtaḥ tūrṇam droṇaputrāt ratha antaram atha anyena su puṅkhena śareṇa nata parvaṇā ājaghāna bhruvoḥ madhye dhṛṣṭadyumnam paraṃtapaḥ sa pūrvam atividdhaḥ ca bhṛśam paścāt ca pīḍitaḥ javena abhyadravan śūrāḥ pañca pāṇḍavāt rathāḥ kirīṭī bhīmasenaḥ ca vṛddhakṣatraḥ ca pauravaḥ yuvarājaḥ ca cedīnām mālavaḥ ca sudarśanaḥ ete hāhākṛtāḥ sarve pragṛhīta śarāsanāḥ vīram drauṇāyanim vīrāḥ sarvatas paryavārayan āśīviṣa ābhaiḥ viṃśadbhiḥ pañcabhiḥ ca api tān śaraiḥ ciccheda yugapad drauṇiḥ pañcaviṃśati sāyakān sapta ca śitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ pauravam drauṇiḥ ārdayat mālavam tribhiḥ ekena pārtham ṣaḍbhiḥ vṛkodaram tatas te vivyadhuḥ sarve drauṇim rājan mahā rathāḥ yugapad ca pṛthak ca eva rukma puṅkhaiḥ śilā śitaiḥ yuvarājaḥ tu viṃśatyā drauṇim vivyādha pattriṇām tatas arjunam ṣaḍbhiḥ atha ājaghāna drauṇāyaniḥ daśabhiḥ vāsudevam bhīmam daśārdhaiḥ yuvarājam caturbhiḥ dvābhyām chittvā kārmukam ca dhvajam ca dvābhyām dvābhyām mālava pauravau ca sūtam viddhvā bhīmasenasya ṣaḍbhiḥ punar pārtham śara varṣeṇa viddhvā drauṇiḥ ghoram siṃhanādam nanāda tasya asyataḥ su niśitān pīta dhārān drauṇeḥ śarān pṛṣṭhatas ca agratas ca dharā viyant dyauḥ pradiśaḥ diśaḥ ca channāḥ bāṇaiḥ abhavan ghora rūpaiḥ āsīnasya sva ratham tu ugra tejāḥ sudarśanasya indra ketu prakāśau sa pauravam ratha śaktyā nihatya chittvā ratham tilaśas ca api bāṇaiḥ yuvānam indīvara dāma varṇam cedi priyam yuvarājam prahasya bāṇaiḥ tvarāvān jvalita agni kalpaiḥ viddhvā prādāt mṛtyave sa aśva sūtam dṛṣṭvā samakṣam nihatam droṇaputreṇa pāṇḍavaḥ bhīmasenaḥ mahā bāhuḥ krodham āhārayat param tatas śara śataiḥ tīkṣṇaiḥ saṃkruddha āśīviṣa upamaiḥ chādayām āsa samare droṇaputram paraṃtapaḥ tatas drauṇiḥ mahā tejāḥ śara varṣam nihatya tam vivyādha niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ bhīmasenam amarṣaṇaḥ tatas bhīmaḥ mahā bāhuḥ drauṇeḥ yudhi mahā balaḥ kṣurapreṇa dhanuḥ chittvā drauṇim vivyādha pattriṇā tat apāsya dhanuḥ chinnam droṇaputraḥ mahā manāḥ anyat kārmukam ādāya bhīmam vivyādha pattribhiḥ avarṣatām śara varṣam vṛṣṭimantau iva ambudau bhīma nāma aṅkitāḥ bāṇāḥ svarṇa puṅkhāḥ śilā śitāḥ drauṇim saṃchādayām āsuḥ ghana oghāḥ iva bhāskaram avākīryata sa kṣipram śaraiḥ śata sahasraśas sa chādyamānaḥ samare drauṇinā raṇa śālinā tatas bhīmaḥ mahā bāhuḥ kārtasvara vibhūṣitān nārācān daśa saṃpraiṣīt yama daṇḍa nibhān śitān te jatru deśam āsādya droṇaputrasya māriṣa nirbhidya viviśuḥ tūrṇam valmīkam iva pannagāḥ saḥ atividdhaḥ bhṛśam drauṇiḥ pāṇḍavena mahātmanā dhvaja yaṣṭim samāśritya nyamīlayata locane sa muhūrtāt punar saṃjñām labdhvā drauṇiḥ narādhipa dṛḍham saḥ abhihataḥ tena pāṇḍavena mahātmanā tatas ākarṇapūrṇānām śarāṇām tigma tejasām śatam āśīviṣa ābhānām preṣayām āsa bhārata tūrṇam prāsṛjat ugrāṇi śara varṣāṇi pāṇḍavaḥ ājaghāna urasi kruddhaḥ pāṇḍavam niśitaiḥ śaraiḥ tatas anyat dhanuḥ ādāya bhīmasenaḥ atyamarṣaṇaḥ vivyādha niśitaiḥ bāṇaiḥ drauṇim pañcabhiḥ āhave jīmūtau iva gharma ante tau śara ogha pravarṣiṇau ayudhyetām su saṃrabdhau kṛta pratikṛta eṣiṇau bhīmam praikṣata sa drauṇiḥ śarān asyantam antikāt ādadānasya viśikhān saṃdadhānasya ca āśugān vikarṣataḥ muñcataḥ ca na antaram dadṛśuḥ janāḥ drauṇeḥ āsīt mahā rāja bāṇān visṛjataḥ tadā dhanuḥ cyutāḥ śarāḥ tasya śataśas atha sahasraśas ākāśe pratyadṛśyanta śalabhānām iva āyatīḥ te tu drauṇi dhanuḥ muktāḥ śarāḥ hema vibhūṣitāḥ balam vīryam prabhāvam ca vyavasāyam ca bhārata tām sa meghāt iva udbhūtām bāṇa vṛṣṭim samantataḥ jala vṛṣṭim mahā ghorām tapānte iva cintayan amuñcat śara varṣāṇi prāvṛṣi iva balāhakaḥ tat rukma pṛṣṭham bhīmasya dhanuḥ ghoram mahat raṇe vikṛṣyamāṇam vibabhau śakra cāpam iva aparam tasmāt śarāḥ prādur āsan śataśas atha sahasraśas tayoḥ visṛjatoḥ evam śara jālāni māriṣa tathā drauṇiḥ mahā rāja śarān hema vibhūṣitān taila dhautān prasanna agrān prāhiṇot vadha kāṅkṣayā viśeṣayan droṇa sutam tiṣṭha tiṣṭha iti ca abravīt punar ca śara varṣāṇi ghorāṇi ugrāṇi pāṇḍavaḥ tatas astra māyayā tūrṇam śara vṛṣṭim nivārya tām sa chinna dhanvā balavān ratha śaktim su dāruṇām tām āpatantīm sahasā mahā ulkā ābhām śitaiḥ śaraiḥ etasmin antare bhīmaḥ dṛḍham ādāya kārmukam drauṇim vivyādha viśikhaiḥ smayamānaḥ vṛkodaraḥ lalāṭe dārayām āsa śareṇa ānata parvaṇā vyāmoham agamat rājan raśmīn utsṛjya vājinām tatas aśvāḥ prādravan tūrṇam mohite ratha sārathau tam dṛṣṭvā pradrutaiḥ aśvaiḥ apakṛṣṭam raṇa ajirāt tān nihatya raṇe vīraḥ droṇaputraḥ yudhām patiḥ dadhmau pramuditaḥ śaṅkham bṛhantam aparājitaḥ tatas sarve ca pāñcālāḥ bhīmasenaḥ ca pāṇḍavaḥ pāñcālāḥ tu tatas sarve droṇaputra śara arditāḥ dhṛṣṭadyumna ratham bhītāḥ tyaktvā saṃprādravan diśaḥ tān prabhagnān tathā drauṇiḥ pṛṣṭhatas vikiran śaraiḥ abhyavartata vegena kāla vat pāṇḍu vāhinīm te vadhyamānāḥ samare droṇaputreṇa kṣatriyāḥ uvāca tān dṛṣṭvā dravataḥ śūrān bībhatsuḥ aparājitaḥ tat prabhagnam balam dṛṣṭvā kuntī putraḥ dhanaṃjayaḥ savyasācī mahā iṣvāsam aśvatthāmānam abravīt yā śaktiḥ yat ca te vīryam yat jñānam yat ca pauruṣam dhārtarāṣṭreṣu yā prītiḥ pradveṣaḥ asmāsu yaḥ ca te samāsādaya pāñcālyam mām ca api saha keśavam uvāca ācārya putraḥ māna arhaḥ balavān ca api saṃjaya prītiḥ dhanaṃjaye ca asya priyaḥ ca api sa vāsaveḥ na bhūta pūrvam bībhatsoḥ vākyam paruṣam īdṛśam atha kasmāt sa kaunteyaḥ sakhāyam rūkṣam abravīt uvāca dhṛṣṭadyumne sātyakau ca bhīme ca api parājite mānyam ācārya tanayam rūkṣam kāpuruṣaḥ yathā evam uktaḥ śvasan krodhāt mahā iṣvāsatamaḥ nṛpa pārthena paruṣam vākyam sarva marma ghnayā girā drauṇiḥ cukopa pārthāya kṛṣṇāya ca viśeṣataḥ dṛśya adṛśyān ari gaṇān uddiśya ācārya nandanaḥ sarvatas krodham āviśya cikṣepa para vīra hā tatas tumulam ākāśe śara varṣam ajāyata pāvaka arciḥ parītam tat pārtham eva abhipupluve ulkāḥ ca gaganāt petuḥ diśaḥ ca na cakāśire tamaḥ ca sahasā raudram camūm avatatāra tām rakṣāṃsi ca piśācāḥ ca vineduḥ abhisaṃgatāḥ vavuḥ ca śiśirāḥ vātāḥ sūryaḥ na eva tatāpa ca cukruśuḥ dānavāḥ ca api dikṣu sarvāsu bhairavam pakṣiṇaḥ paśavaḥ gāvaḥ munayaḥ ca api suvratāḥ śara tejaḥ abhisaṃtaptāḥ nāgāḥ bhūmiśayāḥ tathā diśaḥ kham pradiśaḥ ca eva bhuvam ca śara vṛṣṭayaḥ uccāvacāḥ nipetuḥ vai garuḍa anila raṃhasaḥ pradagdhāḥ śatravaḥ petuḥ agni dagdhāḥ iva drumāḥ kṛṣṇa arjunau hatau adya droṇaputrasya māyayā dahyamānāḥ mahā nāgāḥ petuḥ urvyām samantataḥ apare pradrutāḥ tatra dahyamānāḥ mahā gajāḥ tresuḥ tathā apare ghore vane dāva agni saṃvṛtāḥ drumāṇām śikharāṇi iva dāva dagdhāni māriṣa aśva vṛndāni adṛśyanta ratha vṛndāni ca abhibho yuga ante sarva bhūtāni saṃvartakaḥ iva analaḥ dṛṣṭvā tu pāṇḍavīm senām dahyamānām mahā āhave prahṛṣṭāḥ tāvakāḥ rājan siṃhanādān vinedire tatas tūrya sahasrāṇi nānā liṅgāni bhārata tūrṇam ājaghnire hṛṣṭāḥ tāvakāḥ jita kāśinaḥ hāhākāre tatas sainye pāṇḍaveyeṣu bhārata ratha saṃghāḥ ca dahyanta hayānām prayutāni ca tathā hayānām vṛndāni pattayaḥ ca api analpakāḥ na a dahyamānaḥ pāṇḍūnām kaḥ cit sainye vyadṛśyata udīrṇam droṇaputram ca dṛṣṭvā pārthaḥ paraṃtapaḥ gāṇḍīvam jyām ca bāṇān ca saḥ anumantrya mahā balaḥ kṛtsnā hi akṣauhiṇī rājan savyasācī ca pāṇḍavaḥ tamasā saṃvṛte loke na adṛśyata mahā āhave na eva naḥ tādṛśam rājan dṛṣṭa pūrvam na ca śrutam yādṛśam droṇaputreṇa sṛṣṭam astram amarṣiṇā pravavau ca anilaḥ śītaḥ diśaḥ ca vimalāḥ abhavan tatra adbhutam apaśyāma kṛtsnām akṣauhiṇīm hatām an abhijñeya rūpām ca pradagdhām astra māyayā sahitau saṃpradṛśyetām nabhasi iva tamonudau tatas gāṇḍīvadhanvā ca keśavaḥ ca akṣatau ubhau sa patāka dhvaja hayaḥ sa anukarṣa vara āyudhaḥ tatas kilakilā śabdaḥ śaṅkha bherī ravaiḥ saha pāṇḍavānām prahṛṣṭānām kṣaṇena samajāyata pāṇḍavān muditān dṛṣṭvā sarvān eva sva sainikān ittham drauṇi mahā iṣvāsam pārtham apratimam raṇe āvṛṇvānam diśaḥ sarvāḥ bāṇa jālaiḥ samantataḥ dṛṣṭvā gāṇḍīva nirmuktaiḥ śaraiḥ āśīviṣa upamaiḥ ādityam iva duṣprekṣyam dahantam ahitān raṇe tarasā abhyāgatau dṛṣṭvā vimuktau keśava arjunau dṛṣṭvā pramuditān pārthān tvadīyāḥ vyathitāḥ abhavan vimuktau ca mahātmanau dṛṣṭvā drauṇiḥ su duḥkhitaḥ muhūrtam cintayām āsa kim tu etat iti māriṣa cintayitvā tu rāja indra dhyāna śoka parāyaṇaḥ niḥśvasan dīrgham uṣṇam ca vimanāḥ ca bhavat tadā tatas snigdha ambuda ābhāsam vedavyāsam akalmaṣam āvāsam ca sarasvatyāḥ sa vai vyāsam dadarśa ha tam drauṇiḥ agratas dṛṣṭvā sthitam kuru kula udvaha bho bho māyā yadṛcchā vā na vidmaḥ kim idam bhavet pṛcchāmi tvām aham tāta saṃdeham tam vadasva mama adhara uttaram etat vā lokānām vā parābhavaḥ yat imau jīvataḥ kṛṣṇau kālaḥ hi duratikramaḥ na asura amara gandharvāḥ na piśācāḥ na rākṣasāḥ na sarpa yakṣa patagāḥ na manuṣyāḥ katham cana tat idam kevalam hatvā yuktām akṣauhiṇīm jvalat uvāca tatas samāyayau vyāsaḥ dṛṣṭvā astram samudīritam tam prāptam pūjayitvā tu drauṇiḥ papraccha saṃśayam uvāca mahāntam etam artham mām yam tvam pṛcchasi vismayāt tat pravakṣyāmi te sarvam samādhāya manaḥ śṛṇu yaḥ asau nārāyaṇaḥ nāma pūrveṣām api pūrvajaḥ tasmāt imam jetu kāmaḥ ajñāna tamasā vṛtaḥ viśveśvaraḥ atha lokādiḥ paramātmā hi adhokṣajaḥ sahasra saṃmitāt aṃśāt eka aṃśaḥ ayam ajāyata devānām hita kāma artham lokānām ca eva sattama ūrdhvabāhuḥ mahā tejāḥ jvalana āditya saṃnibhaḥ ṣaṣṭim varṣa sahasrāṇi tāvanti eva śatāni ca aśoṣayat tadā ātmānam vāyubhakṣaḥ ambuja īkṣaṇaḥ dyāvāpṛthivyoḥ vivaram tejasā samapūrayat dadarśa bhṛśa durdarśam sarva devaiḥ api īśvaram aṇīyasām aṇīyāṃsam bṛhadbhyaḥ ca bṛhattaram astāvīt samanudhyāyan mahādevam bṛhattaram rudram īśānam ṛṣabham cekitānam ajam param haram śambhum kapardinam durvāraṇam durdṛśam tigma manyum mahātmānam sarva haram pracetasam divyam cāpam iṣudhī ca ādadānam hiraṇya varmāṇam ananta vīryam durvāraṇam su durdharṣam durnirīkṣyam durāsadam tam devadevam paramāṇum īḍyam saṃkhye divyau iṣudhī ādadānam pinākinam vajriṇam dīpta śūlam paraśvadhim gadinam su āyata asim subhrum jaṭā maṇḍala candra maulim vyāghra ajinam parigham daṇḍapāṇim śubha aṅgadam nāga yajña upavītim viśvaiḥ gaṇaiḥ śobhitam bhūta saṃghaiḥ ekībhūtam tapasām saṃnidhānam vayotigaiḥ suṣṭutam iṣṭa vāgbhiḥ jalam divam kham kṣitim candra sūryau tathā vāyu agnī pratimānam jagat ca na alam draṣṭum yama jam bhinna vṛttā brahma dviṣa ghnam amṛtasya yonim ye ca anṛtāḥ nāstikāḥ pāpa śīlāḥ yam paśyanti brāhmaṇāḥ sādhu vṛttāḥ kṣīṇe pāpe manasā ye viśokāḥ sa tad niṣṭhaḥ tapasā dharmam īḍyam tad bhaktyā vai viśvarūpam dadarśa devam dṛṣṭvā ca enam vāc manaḥ buddhi dehaiḥ saṃhṛṣṭa ātmā mumude devadevam akṣa mālā parikṣiptam jyotiṣām paramam nidhim tatas nārāyaṇaḥ dṛṣṭvā vavande viśva saṃbhavam vara dam pṛthu cāru aṅgayā pārvatyā sahitam prabhum krīḍamānam mahātmānam bhūta saṃgha gaṇaiḥ vṛtam ajam īśānam avyagram kāraṇa ātmānam acyutam sa jānubhyām mahīm gatvā kṛtvā śirasi ca añjalim padmākṣaḥ tam virūpākṣam abhituṣṭāva bhaktimān tvad saṃbhū bhūta kṛt vareṇya goptāraḥ adya bhuvanam pūrvadevāḥ āviśya imām dharaṇīm ye abhyarakṣan purā purāṇām tava deva sṛṣṭim sura asurān nāga rakṣaḥ piśācān narān suparṇān atha gandharva yakṣān pṛthagvidhān bhūta saṃghān ca viśvān tvad saṃbhūtān vidma sarvān tathā eva aindram yāmyam vāruṇam vaittapālyam maitram tvāṣṭram karma saumyam ca tubhyam rūpam jyotiḥ śabdaḥ ākāśa vāyu sparśaḥ svādyam salilam gandhaḥ urvī kāmaḥ brahmā brahma ca brāhmaṇāḥ ca tvad saṃbhūtam sthāsnu cariṣṇu ca idam adbhyaḥ stokāḥ yānti yathā pṛthaktvam tābhiḥ ca aikyam saṃkṣaye yānti bhūyas evam vidvān prabhavam ca api ayam ca hitvā bhūtānām tatra sāyujyam eti divya āvṛtau mānasau dvau suparṇau avāk śākhaḥ pippalaḥ sapta gopāḥ daśa api anye ye puram dhārayanti tvayā sṛṣṭāḥ te hi tebhyaḥ paraḥ tvam vācaḥ ca arthāḥ devatāḥ lokapālā bhūtam bhavyam bhavitā ca api adhṛṣyam tvad saṃbhūtā bhuvanāni iha viśvā tvattaḥ bhāvāḥ sarve eva abhivṛttāḥ bhaktam ca mām bhajamānam bhajasva mā rīriṣaḥ mām ahita ahitena ātmānam tvām ātmanaḥ ananya bhāvaḥ astauṣam tvām tava saṃmānam icchan vicinvan vai sa vṛṣam deva varya su durlabhān dehi varān mama iṣṭān abhiṣṭutaḥ pratikārṣīḥ ca mā mām tasmai varān acintya ātmā nīlakaṇṭhaḥ pinākadhṛk uvāca aprameya bala ātmā tvam nārāyaṇa bhaviṣyasi na piśācāḥ na gandharvāḥ na narāḥ na ca rākṣasāḥ na suparṇāḥ tathā nāgāḥ na ca viśve viyoni jāḥ na śastreṇa na vajreṇa na agninā na ca vāyunā na ārdreṇa na ca śuṣkeṇa traseṇa sthāvareṇa vā na hastena na pādena na kāṣṭhena na loṣṭunā uvāca evam ete varāḥ labdhāḥ purastāt viddhi śauriṇā tasya eva tapasā jātam naram nāma mahā munim tau etau pūrvadevānām parama upacitau ṛṣī lokayātrā vidhāna artham saṃjāyete yuge yuge dānavānām vadhāya ca dharma saṃsthāpana arthāya sa bhavān deva vat prājñaḥ jñātvā bhava mayam jagat śubham aurvam navam kṛtvā mahā puruṣa vigraham ījivāḥ tvam japaiḥ homaiḥ upahāraiḥ ca mānada sa tathā pūjyamānaḥ te pūrvadevaḥ api atūtuṣat puṣkalān ca varān prādāt tava vidvas hṛdi sthitān tābhyām liṅge arcitaḥ devaḥ tvayā arcāyām yuge yuge saḥ eṣa viṣṇu rudraḥ ca śaṃkaraḥ viṣṇu sambhavaḥ śarīram ekam etābhyām yogāt arthe dvidhā kṛtam sarve viṣṇu mayāḥ devāḥ sarva viṣṇu mayāḥ gaṇāḥ sarvam vai viṣṇunā vyāptam trailokyam sacarācaram mūrtayaḥ tasya devasya brahma a viṣṇu maheśvarāḥ sarva rūpam bhavam jñātvā liṅge yaḥ arcayati prabhum ātma yogāḥ ca tasmin vai śāstra yogāḥ ca śāśvatāḥ evam devāḥ yajantaḥ hi siddhāḥ ca parama ṛṣayaḥ kṛṣṇaḥ eva hi yaṣṭavyaḥ yajñaiḥ ca eṣa sanātanaḥ matsyaḥ kūrmaḥ varāhaḥ ca nṛsiṃhaḥ vāmanaḥ hariḥ sādhyaḥ nārāyaṇaḥ viṣṇuḥ kaśyapasya ātmasaṃbhavaḥ rāmaḥ rāmaḥ ca rāmaḥ ca vāsudevaḥ ca yādavaḥ kalkī bhaviṣyate vipraḥ yuge kṣīṇe punar hariḥ ekena eva ātmanā viśvam sthāvaram jaṅgamam ca yat tat sarvam viṣṇunā sṛṣṭam anantena mahātmanā tapaḥ eṣa prakurute lokānām hita kāmyayā varān ca prārthayati asmāt pradhānāt deva sattamāt badarīm samupāgamya viṣṇunā viṣṇunā saha tapaḥ cīrṇam viśālāyām etat te kathitam mayā sarva bhūta bhavam jñātvā liṅge arcayati yaḥ prabhum tasmin abhyadhikām prītim karoti vṛṣabhadhvajaḥ uvāca hṛṣṭa lomā ca vaśya ātmā namaskṛtya mahā ṛṣaye tatas pratyavahāraḥ abhūt pāṇḍavānām viśām pate kauravāṇām ca dīnānām droṇe yudhi nipātite yuddham kṛtvā dinān pañca droṇaḥ hatvā varūthinīm brahma lokam gataḥ rājan brāhmaṇaḥ vedapāragaḥ uvāca māmakāḥ pāṇḍavāḥ ca eva kim akurvan atas param uvāca dṛṣṭvā su mahat āścaryam ātmanaḥ vijaya āvaham munim snigdha ambuda ābhāsam vedavyāsam akalmaṣam saṃgrāme nighnataḥ śatrūn śara oghaiḥ vimalaiḥ aham agratas lakṣaye yāntam puruṣam pāvaka prabham jvalantam śūlam udyamya yām diśam pratipadyate tasyām diśi viśīryante śatravaḥ mama mahā mune na padbhyām spṛśate bhūmim na ca śūlam vimuñcati śūlāt śūla sahasrāṇi niṣpetuḥ tasya tejasā śūla pāṇiḥ mahān kṛṣṇa tejasā sūrya saṃnibhaḥ uvāca prajāpatīnām prathamam taijasam puruṣam vibhum īśānam vara dam pārtha dṛṣṭavan asi śaṃkaram tam gaccha śaraṇam devam sarva ādim bhuvaneśvaram mahādevam mahātmānam īśānam jaṭilam śivam tryakṣam mahā bhujam rudram śikhinam cīra vāsasam devadevam haram sthāṇum vara dam bhuvaneśvaram viśvātmānam viśvasṛjam viśvamūrtim yaśasvinam viśveśvaram viśvayonim viśvakarmāṇam īśvaram śaṃbhum svayambhum bhūteśam bhūta bhavya bhava udbhavam sarva śreṣṭham jagat śreṣṭham variṣṭham parameṣṭhinam jñāna ātmānam jñāna gamyam jñāna jñeyam su durvidam śuddha ātmānam varam bhīmam vaśinam viśvaretasam śāśvatam bhūdharam devam sarva vāc īśvara īśvaram dātāram ca eva bhaktānām prasāda vihitān varān tasya te pārṣadāḥ divyāḥ rūpaiḥ nānāvidhaiḥ vibhoḥ vāmanāḥ jaṭilāḥ muṇḍāḥ hrasva grīvāḥ mahā udarāḥ mahā kāyāḥ mahā utsāhāḥ mahā karṇāḥ tathā apare ānanaiḥ vikṛtaiḥ pādaiḥ pārtha veṣaiḥ ca vaikṛtaiḥ īdṛśaiḥ sa mahādevaḥ pūjyamānaḥ maheśvaraḥ sa śivaḥ tāta tejasvī prasādāt yāti te agratas droṇa karṇa kṛpaiḥ guptām mahā iṣvāsaiḥ prahāribhiḥ kaḥ tām senām tadā pārtha manasā api pradharṣayet ṛte devāt mahā iṣvāsāt bahu rūpāt maheśvarāt visaṃjñāḥ hata bhūyiṣṭhāḥ vepanti ca patanti ca ye bhaktāḥ vara dam devam śivam rudram umāpatim saṃgrāmeṣu jayam prāpya pālayanti mahīm imām rudrāya śitikaṇṭhāya kaniṣṭhāya suvarcase yāmyāya avyakta keśāya sat vṛtte śaṃkarāya ca kāmyāya hari netrāya sthāṇave puruṣāya ca harikeśāya muṇḍāya kṛśāya uttaraṇāya ca bhāskarāya sutīrthāya devadevāya raṃhase bahurūpāya śarvāya priyāya priya vāsase uṣṇīṣiṇe su vaktrāya sahasrākṣāya mīḍhuṣe namaḥ vṛkṣāya senānye madhyamāya namaḥ namaḥ giriśāya praśāntāya pataye cīra vāsase diśām digdantinām ca eva dikkāla pataye namaḥ vṛkṣāṇām pataye ca eva apām ca pataye tathā vṛkṣaiḥ āvṛta kāyāya senānye madhyamāya ca umāpatim virūpākṣam dakṣa yajña nibarhaṇam prajānām patim avyagram bhūtānām patim avyayam kapardinam vṛṣāvartam vṛṣanābham vṛṣadhvajam vṛṣa darpam vṛṣa patim vṛṣa śṛṅgam vṛṣa ṛṣabham vṛṣāṅkam vṛṣabha udāram vṛṣabham vṛṣabha īkṣaṇam vṛṣa āyudham vṛṣa śaram vṛṣa bhūtam maheśvaram mahodaram mahā kāyam dvīpi carma nivāsinam loka īśam vara dam muṇḍam brahmaṇyam brāhmaṇa priyam triśūla pāṇim vara dam khaḍga carma dharam prabhum pinākinam khaṇḍaparaśum lokānām patim īśvaram niṣaṅginam paraśu hastam dharmāṇām ca prakāśakam prapadye śaraṇam devam śaraṇyam cīra vāsasam vanaspatīnām pataye narāṇām pataye namaḥ mātṝṇām pataye ca eva gaṇānām pataye namaḥ apām ca pataye nityam yajñānām pataye namaḥ pūṣṇaḥ danta vināśāya tryakṣāya vara dāya ca nīlakaṇṭhāya piṅgāya svarṇakeśāya vai namaḥ karmāṇi ca eva divyāni mahādevasya dhīmataḥ tāni te kīrtayiṣyāmi yathāprajñam yathāśrutam na surāḥ na asurāḥ loke na gandharvāḥ na rākṣasāḥ dhanuṣā bāṇam utsṛjya sa ghoṣam vinanāda ca te na śarma kutas śāntim lebhire sma surāḥ tadā tena jyā tala ghoṣeṇa sarve lokāḥ samākulāḥ babhūvuḥ vaśa gāḥ pārtha nipetuḥ ca sura asurāḥ apaḥ cukṣubhire sarvāḥ cakampe ca vasuṃdharā parvatāḥ ca vyaśīryanta diśaḥ nāgāḥ ca mohitāḥ andhāḥ ca tamasā lokāḥ na prakāśanta saṃvṛtāḥ jaghnivān saha sūryeṇa sarveṣām jyotiṣām prabhāḥ cukruśuḥ bhaya bhītāḥ ca śāntim cakruḥ tathā eva ca ṛṣayaḥ sarva bhūtānām ātmanaḥ ca sukha eṣiṇaḥ pūṣāṇam abhyadravata śaṃkaraḥ prahasan iva puroḍāśam bhakṣayataḥ daśanān vai vyaśātayat tatas niścakramuḥ devāḥ vepamānāḥ natāḥ sma tam punar ca saṃdadhe dīptam devānām niśitam śaram tam dṛṣṭvā tu surāḥ sarve praṇipatya maheśvaram rudrasya yajña bhāgam ca viśiṣṭam te nu akalpayan bhayena tridaśāḥ rājan śaraṇam ca prapedire yattāḥ ca api surāḥ āsan yattāḥ ca adya api tam prati asurāṇām purāṇi āsan trīṇi vīryavatām divi āyasam rājatam ca eva sauvarṇam aparam mahat āyasam tārakākṣasya kamalākṣasya rājatam sauvarṇam paramam hi āsīt vidyunmālinaḥ eva ca atha sarve amarāḥ rudram jagmuḥ śaraṇam arditāḥ te tam ūcuḥ mahātmānam sarve devāḥ sa vāsavāḥ pīḍayanti adhikam lokam yasmāt te vara darpitāḥ tvat ṛte devadeveśa na anyaḥ śaktaḥ katham cana hantum daityān mahādeva tvam hantā ca suradviṣām śalyam agnim ca vai kṛtvā puṅkhe somam apām patim sa kṛtvā dhanuḥ oṃkāram sāvitrīm jyām maheśvaraḥ pṛthvīm sa sāgara vanām ratham kṛtvā tu śaṃkaraḥ akṣam kṛtvā tu nāga indram śeṣam nāgam trilocanaḥ cakram kṛtvā tu candra arkau devadevaḥ pinākadhṛk kṛtvā elapatram ca puṣpadantam ca tryambakaḥ yūpam kṛtvā ca malayam avanāham ca takṣakam yoktra aṅgāni ca catvāri kṛtvā śarvaḥ pratāpavān vedān kṛtvā atha caturaḥ caturaḥ aśvān maheśvaraḥ upavedān khalīnān ca kṛtvā lokatraya īśvaraḥ gāyatrīm pragraham kṛtvā sāvitrīm ca maheśvaraḥ kṛtvā oṃkāram pratodam ca brahmāṇam ca eva sārathim gāṇḍīvam mandaram kṛtvā guṇam kṛtvā ca vāsukim viṣṇum śara uttamam kṛtvā śalyam agnim tathā eva ca vāyum kṛtvā atha vājābhyām puṅkhe vaivasvatam yamam vidyut kṛtvā atha merum kṛtvā atha vai dhvajam āruhya sa ratham divyam sarva deva mayam śivaḥ tripurasya vadha arthāya sthāṇuḥ praharatām varaḥ asurāṇām anta karaḥ śrīmān atula vikramaḥ stūyamānaḥ suraiḥ pārtha ṛṣibhiḥ ca tapodhanaiḥ sthānam māheśvaram kṛtvā divyam apratimam prabhuḥ atiṣṭhat sthāṇu bhūtaḥ sa sahasram parivatsarān yadā trīṇi sametāni antarikṣe purāṇi vai purāṇi na ca tam śekuḥ dānavāḥ prativīkṣitum śaram kālāgni saṃyuktam viṣṇu soma samāyutam purāṇi dagdhavantam tam devī yātā pravīkṣitum mumoca bhagavant śambhuḥ purāṇi ādiśya vīryavān tatas daityāḥ mahābhāga sa putrāḥ sa parigrahāḥ bhasmībhūtāḥ durātmānaḥ bhinnāḥ ca tripure purā hatvā daityān mahādevaḥ sarva devaiḥ sabhājitaḥ ṛṣibhiḥ saṃstutaḥ ca eva parām mudam upāgamat devyāḥ svayaṃvare vṛttam śṛṇuṣva anyat dhanaṃjaya bālam aṅka gatam kṛtvā svayam pañcaśikham punar umā jijñāsamānā vai kaḥ ayam iti abravīt surān asūyataḥ ca śakrasya vajreṇa prahariṣyataḥ prahasya bhagavant tūrṇam sarva loka īśvaraḥ śivaḥ tatas saṃstambhita bhujaḥ śakraḥ deva gaṇaiḥ vṛtaḥ jagāma śaraṇam tūrṇam brahmānam prabhum avyayam te tam praṇamya śirasā procuḥ prāñjalayaḥ tadā bāla rūpa dharam dṛṣṭvā na asmābhiḥ tat ca lakṣitam tasmāt tvām praṣṭum icchāmaḥ nirjitāḥ yena vai vayam a yudhyatā hi bālena līlayā sa puraṃdarāḥ teṣām tat vacanam śrutvā brahmā brahma vidām varaḥ dhyātvā sa śaṃbhum bhagavant bālam ca amita tejasam uvāca bhagavān brahmā śakra ādīn ca sura uttamān yaḥ dṛṣṭaḥ hi umayā sārdham yuṣmābhiḥ amita dyutiḥ sa pārvatyāḥ kṛte devaḥ kṛtavān bāla rūpa tām atha anyena sva rūpeṇa brahmā dṛṣṭvā tam avyayam sa prajāpatayaḥ sarve bāla arka sadṛśa prabham atha abhyetya tatas brahmā dṛṣṭvā ca sa maheśvaram ayam śreṣṭhaḥ iti jñātvā vavande tam pitāmahaḥ tvam yajñaḥ bhuvanasya asya tvam gatiḥ tvam parāyaṇam uvāca padmayoneḥ vacaḥ śrutvā tatas prītaḥ maheśvaraḥ prasāda abhimukhaḥ bhūtvā ca aṭṭahāsam atha akarot tatas prasādayām āsuḥ umām rudram ca te surāḥ teṣām prasannaḥ bhagavant sa patnīkaḥ vṛṣadhvajaḥ devānām tridaśa śreṣṭhaḥ dakṣa yajña vināśanaḥ sa candramāḥ sa ca īśānaḥ sa sūryaḥ varuṇaḥ ca saḥ sa kālaḥ saḥ antakaḥ mṛtyuḥ sa yamaḥ rātri ahāni ca māsa ardha māsāḥ ṛtavaḥ saṃdhye saṃvatsaraḥ ca saḥ sa ca dhātā vidhātā ca viśvātmā viśva karma kṛt sarvāsām devatānām ca dhārayati avapuḥ vapuḥ dve tanū tasya devasya veda jñāḥ brāhmaṇāḥ viduḥ ghorā ca anyā śivā ca anyā te tanū bahudhā punar soma ardham punar eva asya āpaḥ jyotīṃṣi candramāḥ vedāṅgāḥ sa upaniṣadaḥ purāṇa adhyātma niścayāḥ īdṛśaḥ sa mahādevaḥ bhūyas ca bhagavant ajaḥ na hi sarve mayā śakyāḥ vaktum bhagavataḥ guṇāḥ api varṣa sahasreṇa satatam pāṇḍu nandana sa mocayati su prītaḥ śaraṇyaḥ śaraṇa āgatān āyuḥ ārogyam aiśvaryam vittam kāmān ca puṣkalān sa dadāti manuṣyebhyaḥ sa ca eva ākṣipate punar sa ca eva vyāhṛte loke manuṣyāṇām śubha aśubhe aiśvaryāt ca eva kāmānām īśvaraḥ punar ucyate maheśvaraḥ ca bhūtānām mahatām īśvaraḥ ca saḥ eṣa ca eva śmaśāneṣu devaḥ vasati nityaśas asya dīptāni rūpāṇi ghorāṇi ca bahūni ca vede ca asya samāmnātam śatarudrīyam uttamam nāmnā ca anantarudra iti upasthānam mahātmanaḥ sa kāmānām prabhuḥ devaḥ ye divyāḥ ye ca mānuṣāḥ jyeṣṭham bhūtam vadanti enam brāhmaṇāḥ munayaḥ tathā teṣām adhipatiḥ yat ca tasmāt paśupatiḥ smṛtaḥ ṛṣayaḥ ca eva devāḥ ca gandharva apsarasaḥ tathā urdhvaliṅgaḥ tatas ca uktaḥ bhagavān brāhmaṇaiḥ sadā sukhī prītaḥ ca bhavati prahṛṣṭaḥ ca eva śaṃkaraḥ sthāvaram jaṅgamam ca eva bahurūpaḥ tatas smṛtaḥ eka akṣaḥ jājvalan āste sarvatas akṣi mayaḥ api vā krodhāt yaḥ ca aviśat lokān tasmāt śarvaḥ iti smṛtaḥ viśve devāḥ ca yat tasmin viśvarūpaḥ tatas smṛtaḥ dyām apaḥ pṛthivīm ca eva tryambakaḥ ca tatas smṛtaḥ śivam icchan manuṣyāṇām tasmāt eśa śivaḥ smṛtaḥ sahasrākṣaḥ ayuta akṣaḥ vā sarvata ukṣi mayaḥ api vā yat ca viśvam mahat pāti mahādevaḥ tatas smṛtaḥ sthita liṅgaḥ ca yat nityam tasmāt sthāṇuḥ iti smṛ sūryācandramasoḥ loke prakāśanti aṃśavaḥ ca ye te keśāḥ saṃjñitāḥ tasya vyomakeśaḥ tatas smṛtaḥ kapiḥ śreṣṭhaḥ iti proktaḥ dharmaḥ ca vṛṣaḥ ucyate sa devadevaḥ bhagavān kīrtyate vai vṛṣākapiḥ nimīlitābhyām netrābhyām bālyāt devyāḥ maheśvaraḥ bhūtam bhavyam bhaviṣyat ca sarvam sarvam aśeṣatas viṣama sthaḥ śarīreṣu samaḥ ca prāṇinām iha sa vāyuḥ viṣama stheṣu prāṇa apāna śarīriṣu liṅgam pūjayitā nityam mahatīm śriyam aśnute ūrubhyām ardham āgneyam soma ardham ca śivā tanuḥ taijasī mahatī dīptā devebhyaḥ ca śivā tanuḥ brahmacaryam carati eṣa śivā yā asya tanuḥ tayā yā asya ghoratarā mūrtiḥ sarvān atti tayā īśvaraḥ saṃgrāme śātravān nighnan tvayā dṛṣṭaḥ pinākadhṛk eṣa vai bhagavān devaḥ saṃgrāme yāti te agratas yena dattāni te astrāṇi yebhiḥ tvayā dānavāḥ hatāḥ dhanyam yaśasyam āyuṣyam puṇyam vedaiḥ ca saṃjñitam sarva artha sādhakam puṇyam sarva kilbiṣa nāśanam iṣṭasya phalam āpnoti durācāraḥ api mānavaḥ gavām koṭi śatasya api dānasya phalam aśnute caturvidham idam stotram yaḥ śṛṇoti naraḥ sadā caritam mahātmanaḥ divyam sāṃgrāmikam idam śubham paṭhan vai śatarudrīyam śṛṇvan ca satata utthitaḥ yaḥ śṛṇoti naraḥ bhaktyā yaḥ ca api parikīrtayet divā vā yadi vā rātrau brahmahatyām vyapohati bhaktaḥ viśveśvaram devam mānuṣeṣu tu yaḥ sadā uvāca evam uktvā arjunam saṃkhye parāśara sutaḥ tadā jagāma bharata śreṣṭha yathāgatam ariṃdama uvāca yuddham kṛtvā mahā ghoram pañca ahāni mahā balaḥ kṣatriyāṇām abhīrūṇām viśuddham khyāpyate yaśaḥ yaḥ idam paṭhate parva śṛṇuyāt vā api nityaśas idam paṭhet sarva mahā artha saṃyutam raṇe jayam pāṇḍava vṛṣṇi siṃhayoḥ sadā śubham yaḥ śṛṇuyāt tathā naraḥ yajña avāptiḥ brāhmaṇasya iha nityam yuddhe nityam kṣatriyāṇām jayaḥ ca śeṣau varṇau kāmam iṣṭam labhete putrān pautrān nityam iṣṭān tathā eva etat ākhyāya vai sūtaḥ rājñaḥ sarvam tu saṃjayaḥ prayātaḥ śibirāya eva draṣṭum karṇasya vaiśasam
